ovr gracyous god moost magnyfycece mercyful eyen casteth fro heue hi seynge creature deedly vyolence hym selfe complayneth pyte full ru fully sayenge deus man deuoyde intellygence open thyne eeres vnto call crye tell yf haue done offence thou forsakest wyllyngly man suche loue dyde take world seuen dayes wha wrought thou laste thynge dyd make bycause wolde thou wanted nought thynge myght helpe dyd lake thy nede yf sought fowle fysshe thynge thy sake thy comforte forth brought ouer gaue dygnyte beestes bowe vntyll made also lyke vnto gaue connynge freewyll serue thou sholde se chose good leue yll aske nothynge agayne loue thy souerayne skyll vnto takest thou none entente thou tournest fro full vnkyndly loues vnlefull thy loue lente thy herte beholdeth heuen hye goodes haue sente lysteth one saye gramercye tyme come thou repente man make amendes thou dye crysten soule conceyued synne receyued conscyence thus complanynge fell downe flatte delefull dynne sayd homo lorde mercy souerayne kynge moost vnkynde wretche man kynne knowe thy traytour vntrue lyuynge wycked lyfe lyue may nought hyde frome thy knowynge want wordes also wytte thy kyndnesse speke cause haue thou gaue thy goodnes withouten cause thoughe haue greued yet thy benefaytes thou nought withdrawse haue deserued haue hell pytte haue lyued ayenst thy lawse lorde thou knowest mannes feblenesse frayle hath ben aye thoughe soule haue thy lykenesse man fulsome erthe claye synne conceyued wretchednesse soule rebell alwaye fyrst man groweth dooth gresse wasteth floures haye syth man frayle thynge thy power grete kynde worlde twynkelynge thou mayst destroye myght fynde thy ryght lorde mercy mynge sore salue thou sende sore repenteth slyuynge mercy lorde wyll amende deus man gaue bodyly hele thou sholde spende seruyce fayrenes also fetures fele man doost thou thyse thou delytes deuyll doost dele whiche great despyse thou lyuest lecherous lyfe vnlele fro yere yere thou lyst ryse thou studyest nyce araye makest great cost thy clothynge make semely sholde saye thou coudest amende makynge thou purposed daye daye set people synnynge thy wretched wyll thou folowest alwaye ende synne hathe yu thynkest nothynge no tyme bycause synne lecherye especyall vengeauce came mane kynne saue viii persones drowned sodome gomor men wtin made fyre brymstone fall fro heuen bode therin synne destroyed bothe great small man wenest thou myght lesse elles thou hast moche wyckednesse whan smote moost pyteously yf thou wyll thy fautes redresse thought spare mercy man thynke ryghtwysnesse make amendes rose couetyse grounde roote wo myschaunce vayne reporte selfe auaunce whiche put selfe ieopardye without rescue lykely dye helpe ne sleyghte armes vayle myght agayne cursyd charmes stronge colchos wrought sondry nacions pursued auntres conquere tyll pelleus ferfoth gan enquere knewe hooly trouthe herte anone gan compas myght sleyght make neuewe iason vnder take hye empryse colchos wende whiche waye beste myght hym shende pand gan pretende coloure fresshe hewe gylt outwarde lusty newe treason hydde within sawe tyme begyn purpose thofirst made queynte began asour golde peynte gaye wordes sownynge gloryous knowynge iason yonge desyrous vnto suche thynge lyghtly wolde enclyne therfore thought wolde fyne playnly werke conclusion made anone conuocacion lordes baronye aboute enuyron londe thesalye assemble estate degree realme within chefe cytee holde counsayle vtterly caste therby acheue desyre faste court contynued dayes thre laste hyd myquyte gan rake hath hyd longe ne myght longer forth prolonge venym hyd frete herte slye wyse man myght auerte vpon syde mente well treason cured euerydell curtyned vnder trecherye thynge slyghly gan gye pryme face man myght deme worde wolde seme chere port sygne dalyaunce caste knyghtly auaunce yonge neuewe lyklynesse hye honour manhode prowesse entent whiche gan purpose man cowde spye theffecte dyde glose texte conueyed flaterye people cowde nat espye lytell nought entent within whiche anone preyse hym begyn suche honour neuewe wolde suche chere began vnfolde tofore entencion hath voyded suspeccion assembled place towarde iason tourne gan face full louyngly countenaunce cher hym sayde myghte thorughout court wha maked sylence thus worde worde platly sentence phow pelleus counsayled neuewe iason malyce go conquere golden lee toke vpon hym ca iii cosyn iaso take hede shal sayn inly glad fayn supprised myrthe thorugh herte enchasyth voydeth smerte consyder myn inspeccion thy youthe disposicion whiche shortly comprehende saue vertue thynge dothe entende vnto worshyp gentylnesse manly fredom hye largesse verrayly wake wynke ioye oonly thynke selfe holde passynge fortunate londe hye lowe estate lykely honour flete tolyue reste quyete thorugh thy supporte supportayle whose man hode may moche v auayle lykelyhod moche amende verray sothe saue v defende agayne tho descryue malys wolde agaynst v stryue rebell maner waye surquedrye pryde werraye worthynesse assuryd tranquylle assaute wolde v ylle perturbe noble estate royall agaynst whan thou art wall myghty shyeld proteccion thus deme fully myn oppynyon pfor thyne age thy wyt thy prouydence thy knyghtly herte thy manly excellence reported ben thyne hye renowne many londe many regyowne rounde worlde aboute circuyte myght stonde better plyte thyne honour lyke founde worshyp hyghly dothe rebounde wolde playnely nat cease coude helpe encrease thyne hygh renowne wy euery hour therupon spenden treasour hygh desyre withouten fayle entyer loue dothe sore assayle nyght daye may haue rest shall tourne hope beste enhaunce thyn honour heuen aboue pool sterrys seuen whiche thynge haue awaye espyed wyt therto haue applyed mene shuld lenger dwelle dere cosyn shall telle manhode souereyne thy knyghthode thou durst atteyne flees golde conquere thy strengthe whiche spoke fer brede lengthe retourne home body saufand sounde conquest myght founde thou durst achieue empryse hertis wye kowde nat deuyse worlde sothly beste realme reste thy manhode wolde v drede wherfore cosyne knyghthode manhede take vpon prayer requeste pand trouthe take beheste euer nedeth meygne costage wyll selfe towarde vyage ordeyney ioughe harneyse araye nought shall fayle thy paye moreouer playnely ensure se thou thy besycure hygh empryse brynge aboute thou shalt fere eke ben doute daye succession kynge region hooly haue sceptre regalye wherfore iason lyfte vp thyne hert eye thynke thy name shalbe longe recorded thurgh worlde wherfore accorded within thy selfe playnly nat ne spare thyne entent somme declare whan iason vncle vnderstande reioyseth take hande dredfull laboure withoute auysement nought aduertith meuynge fraudulent pryue poyson vnder sugre cured howe galle hony lured derke deceyte clowdy fals engyne ygy without vnder venyme wherto iason hath noon aduertence kynge wende clene conscyence without fraude hadde thynge iment wherfore anon yeueth full assent wordes fewe playnly gan seye vncles wyll wolde obeye accordyd conclusion humble herte hoole entencion wherof kynge receyueth suche gladnesse vuneth myght expresse right faste dyde besy payne iourney haste ordayne asmoche colchos countree enclosed aboute see man longe stryue without shyp thyder may arryue prelence anone dyde call famous argus cowde moste make shyp firste art yfonde sayle see f londe londe hath wrought ship sotyl craft whiche firste euer wawe raft haue entre argon bare name gramariens recorde yet eche great shyp firste meruayle callyd whiche proudely bare hir sayle hercules force myght strengthe pereles bygette vpon almene somly fayre aud womanly sene iubiter full louge agon takynge lyknesse amphitrion downe fro heuen deyte rauysshed thurgh luste hir beaute hir loued herte hole entente two sothly discente came hercules worthy famous knyght moste renomed manhode myght whiche tyme meruaylous excellent victoryous ouyde lyst recorde hym sylue methamorphoseos famous dedys twelue whiche ben remembred inspecyall honour memoryall pand reherse ordre ye lyst purpose viterly slough antheon eyer hyght many geaut myght eyght outrayed theyr lymes rude serpent ydre sloughe eke pallude serberus hounde bonde sore helle gate brake made hym voyde venym stryfe vpwarde gaue hym suche laxatyfe worlde brethe contagyous infectyd hath venymous wynde wolde renne ascadye catchyd arpyes byrdys archadye slough centaurus best monstruous firste lyon brast hous fayne whan slawe skynne hath hym strypt flawe cruell herte thorugh hye renowne golden applys barefro dragone firye catte slough without archadye cruell tuskye bore laste shuldres square veray myght firmament hebare may nat reken passynge dedys whiche ben hystoryall rede ouyde ye shall fynde tryumphes howe maketh mynde thorugh world hym honour fet pylers gades set whiche alysaundre macedoyne kynge worthy lyuynge rood conquest guydolyst wryte hoost proudely visyte beyonde whiche londe habytable see sayle sothely couenable ferre beyonde occian shypmen skyll sibilles streyghtes maryners call boundes named eke hercules hym selfe sette markes lette ferther passe guy maketh mynde place callyd fynde siracenyca fyne labour longa saphy recorde myne auctour pof mater shuld sayne vnto iason wyll retourne agayne haste doth hym redy make vncle whan hath leue take towarde see hercules yfere men anoneas ye shall tyme yere whan shene sonne spere ferre vp ronne passyd gemyny hath chare whyrlyd vp hy thorough draught pirous reed made crabbys heed mansion see royall halowed stondyng escynall fresshe appollo golden wayne whan herde men herte fayne hete shroude shade vnder thyse braunches thyse bowys glade whan phebus bemys bryght shyne descendyd ben right lyne cause eyer refleccion full hoote lusty fresshe season whan cornys gynne felde sede grassys grene mede fro yere yere ben custome mowe playne caste leyde full lowe tyll moysture consumed awaye holte hethe merye somers daye whiche tyme yonge knyght iason hercules shyp gon eke reherse grekes eke many lusty man shypped echon royall apparayle whan crossyd vnder fayle within shyp whiche argus made whiche stauche myght water lade gan sayle wynde wyll shyp gan breke sturdy wawes yll vpon see bothe daye nyght colchos warde helde waye ryght gydynge theyr cours lode sterre sayle costes nyghe ferre philotetes theyr alder guyde coude afore prudently prouyde insyght caste afore se tempest wynde bothe londe see whan shulde trouble stormes fall mayster playnly shypman craft chose theyr gouernour coude warne afore euery shour shulde falle whan sterres dyde appere specyally guydo doth v lere philotetes whiche fole moste syght erecte vnto pole aduertence clere inspeccion sterres constellacion axtre rounde aboute gon clerkes call septemtryon pole ycallyd arthycus euer oon apperyth vnto v ryght sothe loke aryght antharticus shrouded syght shypmen discrete wyse lyste theyr cours prudently deuyse vpon see haue suffysaunce ynoughe gye theyr passage arthourys ploughe direccion vnto costes euery region helpe oonly nedle stone may erre costes gone maryners discrete sage expert theyr lodmanage str ge costes sayle ferre gynne theyr cours oonly sterre pwhiche arthur compasseth enuyron whiche cercle constellacion called cercle artophilax knoweth nedeth ax shypmen sterry nyght suffysaunt whan se lyght pand poetis thyse poolys twayne theyr bokes lyketh fayne theyr dytees declare vnto v calixto e archadius hir owne sone istellyfyed heuen deyfyed iune hir hadde enuye iubiter whan dyde hir espye pfor whiche bere tourned hir gylt hath erthe mourned tyll heuen nason tell translatyd eternally dwell amonge sterres stalled vrsa maior clerkes called hir sone worthy fame pof vria minor beryth name suche cours myght nat asterte philotetes moste experte shypmen euer herde tell connynge myght bere bell pand whan grekes hadde longe fordryue caste saylynge see forweryed trauayle caste aryue wolde auayle refresshe disporte ioye vpon boundes londe troye phow iason g ynge conquere golden flees toke lande refresshe hym felawshyp besyde troye ca iiii whan hercules iason honde shyp taken haue londe wt eke theyr knyghtes euerychone fro see londe gone forweryed theyr trauayle sothe come aryuayle symeounte hauen great renowne lytell besyde troye towne gladde sykernesse storme tempest werynesse ne mente treason harme gyle stronde resten whyle hyndre wyght maner age yle damage man beest euer go abyde day two refresshe repayre anone whan rage see gone whyles vpon stronde laye thynge dyde disporte playe bathe wasshe fresshe ryuere dronke water soote clere sprange lyke cristall colde welle toke right nought selle thynge theyr entencion vnto wyght offension moleste greue wyght ordre fortune myght hath euer enuye men lyue ese whose coursenhasteth vnwarely dysese cause god wote causeles gery fortune lady recheles blynde goddesse transmutacion tourne hir whele reuolucion make troyens vniustly wene grekes aryued tene cause suspicion hath many brought vnto destruccion full many worthy kynges prynces thorughout worlde rekened prouynces sclaundre vnto myscheif brought thynge ala neuer thought cause occasiowne cyte royall towne distroyed playnly founde whose walles hye bete downe groude many man many worthy knyght slayne many lady bryght wedowe made duresshe werre kouthe reported ferre many mayde grene tendre age lefte sool great rage behynde theyr fadres ala fall sholde thynge fortune wolde shewe hir myght hir crueltee vengeaunce takynge vpon cytee palas euer worthy estate shulde lytell falle debate whan gon nat lyke staunche graffynge lytell braunche full sturdy tree growe vp full ofte clymbeth hye may nat fall softe sparkes syght small fyre engendred deuoureth gnast firste lytell hate encauseth flawme contek debate enuye sprede brode full ferre thus ala realmes mortall werre firste bygonne men may rede se sparke lytell enmytee nat stauchyd first wha gone whan fyre fer yronne embraseth hertes hatrede make brenne hoote glede partye thorughe cruell tene staunche sharpe swerdes kene whiche ala consumeth slethe thus fyne enmyte dethe thoughe gynnynge casuell frete abydynge passyngly cruell voyde realmes reste pea ioye fyll whylom worthy troy dothe wepe caas sodayne euery wyght ought complayne lytell gylt shuld haue suche vengeaunce except parcaas thorugh goddes pourueaunce myscheyf shulde folowynge parchaunce great felycyte troye brought vnto destruccion gynnynge occasion myn auctour specyfyed worthy rome edyfyed ofsprynge worthy eneas whylom fro troy whan exyled whiche rome rede ye may se worlde hede cheyf cyte passynge famous worthynesse eke wha troye brought distresse walles caste broke downe cause many regyowne begonne many great cytee troyan manly man enee sondry see gan longe sayle tyll fortune came ytayle wan londe bookes telle v eke sone askanius ence doth lyne succeede lande italye iustly possede hym sone syluyus came brute passyngly famous shall nat fayne whylom lande called bretayne geauntes thorugh manhode wan noble yle firste began pfrom troye also ylke enee came worthy francus lorde hye degree whiche vpon rome encrease renowne bylded tyme fall royall towne whiche sothely honour auaunce name made calle fraunce thus began vnderstande name firste worthy lande authenor departynge fro troyens began firste cyte venycyens sycanus within alytell whyle began enhabyte lande cecyle partynge sycanus worthy brother called syculus fynde reygned yle hym called cecyle pbut eneas tuscy gone enhabyte people right anone cecyle naplys firste began whiche full many neopolytane longeth day full ryche great myght pand dyomedes noble worthy knyght whan troye falle toures fayre reygne caste repayre lyeges began feyne quarell agaynst hym shope rebell malys conspiracy owne hym withhelde bothe sceptre crowne theyr deuty olde lygeaunce hym denye trouthe obeyssaunce wherfore anone bokes telle l folke went dwelle vnto calabre began possede knyghtes dyomede tro troye haue hym thyder sewed fourme byrdes anone trasmewed circe crafte doughter sonne eyre flee one gonne called ben ysydre rede amonge grekes brydes dyomede bokes bere wytnesse chaunge made venus goddesse wrathe yt hadde worthy knyght oonly sawe hym one fyght eneas hir owne sone dere whiche tyme faughte yfere dyomede darte grounde ame hym deedly mortall wounde pthis moder venus began anone hym shroude vnder skye mystye cloude saue hym tyme fro myschaunce skyl venus toke vengaunce byrdes tourne meyne fourme yere yere fle vnto tombe graue vpon hym mynde haue custome remembraunce aryte holde obseruaunce exequyes thyse brydes euerychone dayes space thennys nat ne gone ouer dewe loue grekes platly eschewe latynes nought may betyde present anone fice asyde eche bokes v assure byrdes knowe oonly nature grekes latynes kyndely assonder whan se wonder vnto wyt nat aspye cause hydde suche sorcerye well wote though wyt blent roote fals enchauntement faythe ought defye suche apparences shewed eye whiche fende illusion thereof thus whan troye towne euersed brought nought full many cyte ybyld wrought pand many lande many ryche towne edefyed occasiowne werre ye haue herde telle whiche declare nowe maye nat dwelle poynt poynt lyke bokes sayne iason wyll resorte agayne landyd worthy hercules symeounte hauen ches haue tolde reste comforte nat elles oonly disporte kynge reygnynge troye towne tyme called lamedowne fals enuye reported tolde certayne grekes herte bolde entrete lande whiche nat knewe well arayed vessell newe whiche aryue hadde lycence purpose done offence lyklyheed lande greue pryde without leue sauf conduyte haue stronde ytake suche maystryes lande make theyr power maner thynge hauynge regarde playnely kynge pof estate take none hede suche straungers great drede men laches outher neclygent fully wete theyr entent forthe prolonge peryll caste suche sodayne thynge wolde wyst faste nat differred tyll harme wysdom se men may longe suffre abyde neclygence lete slyde enquere theyr gouernaunce speche dalyaunce eueryche reuelaciowne euery strete thorugh troye towne rownynge spake brode speche longe bode one another sothely sowne reported kynge lamedowne ye haue herde whiche wylfulnesse without counsayle vysynesse hastely maked hath sonde wyt hardy londe besyde leue presumpcion wherfore bad conclusion without bode soone remewe fynally shulde nat eschewe compelled maugre sayth nay kynge vpon certayne day haste hath sent embassatoure vnto jason grekes gouernoure nouther thoughte harme villanye innocent companye disportyd hym endlonge stronde euer hath sythe came londe charge hym layde worde worde iason sayde effect euery circumstaunce playnely substaunce phow kyng lamedone troyesent messenger vnto iason byd hym auoyde countre theyr langage betwene capitulo v wyse worthy famous renown myghty kyg ye noble lamedown hath vnto message sent whiche theffect sentement sothe hath meruayle lande aryuayle bryngynge grekes nat afewe haue conduyte shewe proteccion playnly lycence preiudyce magnyfycence wherfore hath charge layde wyll platly sayde ye anone without delaye without noyse affraye troye lande bondes ye leue youres casteth greue better ease departe folye lyues ieoparte wyse lacke prouydence agaynst wyll make resystence outher pryde wylfulnesse bolde without vysynesse interrupte felycyte desyreth tranquyllyte holde reygne without perturbaunce whose parsone made suche allyaunce wene manhode royall mageste wyll nat suffre none degre enpugne quyete maner wyse wherfore counsayle ye seme wyse take hede vnto seye byddynge nat disobeye pleste ye offende knyghtly excellence ye shall fynde experyence without feynynge sothe telle take hede therfore may lenger dwelle poynt poynt syth ye wyse sage hool effect message whan iason herde messagere thyse word gan chauge kepte hym close sobre coutenaunce nat hasty irene greuaunce rancoure caughte tale saue face began wex pale longe abydynge aughte wolde sayne spake worde agayne vnto hym fro kynge sent began disclose entent vnto folke stondynge rounde aboute vnto discured oute message hool firste whan abreyde worde worde thus seyde syres sayth knowe take hede praye bothe hye lowe lamedone kynge troye hath sent v wonderfull enuoye chargynge haste hye londe axeth vpon stronde aryue hadde hardynesse without leue se gentylnesse fredom whiche nat alyte lyke kynge hym quyte vnto straungers entre yle nought god wote lytell whyle refresshe departe anoon lyke ye recorde euerychon bere wytnesse ala fredom become pwhere manhode gentylnesse also whiche kynge togyder bothe two shulde custome haue theyr restyng place honour shuld also embrace alordes herte whiche kyngly ryght manly fredome full myght shulde straungers refresshe recomforte afterwarde myght hym reporte plarges experte manhode gentyllesse haue founde worthynesse noblesse allye fredom eke knyt regallye longeth honoure kynge shulde haue charged firste thynge worthy lyeges myght please haue shewed comforte ease theyr myght theyr besy cure vnto straungers venture see dryuen dismayed comforte nat euyll apayed caas semblable outher fortune varyable sort hap may nat withstande aryued hadde grekes lande honestly lyke degre sholde v haue receyued lyke longeth vnto gentrye syth ought espy hath fredom honoure humanyte one made courte fle chose dyshonour let worshyp gone shall euery chone hath chose helpe fulfyll whan power shall nat belyke wyll saye sothe shalbe founde dede shall hym selfe rebounde syth malys hath werke begonne perauenture somer sonne sodyak hath thryes gone aboute lete hym truste thynge doute shall hym serue wt suche hath sought lyue shalbe dere bought therof sette tyde lande wyll lenger byde tyll haue leyser better soiourne yt worde gan anone tourne manly face sterne chere sodaynly vnto messagere fro kynge vnto hym sent wyse sheweth entent frende quod haue well vnderstande message hool thou toke hande thy kynge brynge vnto v right vnwarely syth stondeth thus haue menynge euerydele poynt poynt vnderstonde wele word word haue playnly coteyned gyftes haue receyued behalfe great nede wyll remembre take right good hede euery thynge thou haste v brought truste well forgete nought emprente well suerly mynde goodly fynde great bounte maner thynge within lande lamedone kynge welcomynge great chere goodly sonde thou bryngest nat accordynge nat entent god well wote neuer ment harme vnto hym playnly damage none maner age vpon goddes inmortall kynde ben celestyall vnto recorde myn herte take touching borowes make wytnessynge ment none offence ne toke nat violence within realme woman childe man thou mayste reporte thou dryuen see compelled necessyte aryue thou haste harde sayne oonly reste v vpon playne without vnto certayne daye afterwarde holde forthe waye vpon iourney make taryenge lyke thou mayste recorde thy kynge saye hym eke shall tyme e paraunter shall mowe thanked whan tyme cometh v go forthe thy way say hym thus brother anone ialon pe manly knyght worthy hercules wha herd thyng fro poyt poynt anone brought suche disioynt hasty rancoure sodayne ire whiche herte almoste sette fyre sodaynly abreyde bake hye disdeyne euen thus spake chere askoyne vnto messagere sayde felawe thynge abydynge right well certayne tytan bemes reyse agayne shall departe shyp gone men shall nat leue one within lande god toforne morowe vpon haue fayth borowe lenger shall holde soioure elles shall make retoure morowe erely dawnynge vpon payne repref go say thy kynge thre yere god v graunt lyfe maugre grutcheth make stryfe vnto lande shall agayne retourne caste anker whyle soiourne take hede therof note well tyme newe chaunge shall folowe pryme power shall nat large streche sauf conduyte lytell shall reche saye platly entent wyll nat haue vnto maundement lytell regarde day abyde takynge leue shalbe sette syde bycause hath begonne playe whiche shall quyte god maye tourne shall owne shame spare nat saye thy kynge messager gan agayne replye sayde syr ye maye nat denye honeste message declare auyse wyll nat spare kynges sonde playnely telle ye lyste go dwelle ye may yet chese leef lothe ye haue cause wrothe syt nat vnto worthynesse ye take hede waye gentyllesse manassynge suche arowes shete honeste thretynge lete kepe secrete tyll ye large certaynely parcell charge stryue debate better tymes late ye beware harme myght falle parte say vnto alle pytee ye destroyed man hyndre shulde dere worthy parsones maner wyse whiche ben lykly discrete wyse lest wordes greue saye take leue nyght ypassed sprigyng daye whan arke blessed laye began salue lusty rowes rede phebus chare fresshely sprede vpon bordure oryente aurora herte hool entente swetnesse hir syluer shoures bedewed hadde fresshe somer floures made rose newe bawme flete soote lylye margarete vnclose theyr tendre leues whyte oppressed hertes gladnesse delyte drery afore myghtes tene hony souklys amonge busshes grene enbawmed hadde enuyron eyre longe tytan began make repeyre bryghtnesse bemys merye reioyse emysperye longe aforne dyde aryse worthy iason full hasty wyse felowe hercules also chargyd haue theyr shypmen haue ado hale vp anker redy make bad haste euery man take right waye vnto shyp anoon sothenesse manly man iason thought nat stuffed meyne begyn werre troye cyte nat shortly conclude egall noumbre multitude tyme werre begynne nat lykly shulde wynne victorye tho fewe nat holsome man hewe aboue heed whan ouer hye leste chyppes wyll falle eye wherfore frygye leue costes blyue drewe vp sayle shyp began dryue wynde good goddes fauorable fortune theyr frende though varyable thus colchos sauf ben come vnto lande bothe ben aryued lytell space see haue founde grace neptunus caused blyue sayde ere colchos aryue yle lytell lande colchos hyghte ye shall vnderstande ryall cheyf cyte reygne moost dignyte worthynesse rychesse fame iachonytes tyme bare name cheuest speke buyldynge stretes large coryous housynge therwith dyched well withoute stronge walled toured rounde aboute huge heyght aboue batayled magecolde also leste assayled many paleys stately royall sete moost pryncypall kynge abyde better elles tyme happed hym called cethes rede full renomed knyghode manhede aboute hym well besene meyne lyke syttynge vnto degre euery landes enuyrowne spradde hye renowne aboute myghty cheyfcytee cethes helde royall see fresshe ryuers water clene lyke cristall shone agayne sonne shene fayre playnes guydo bereth wytnesse holsom hylles full lustynesse many lay many lusty welle eke myn aucto r telle full many parke full fayre fresshe sene many wode many medowe grene sondry floures amonge herbes meynt whiche theyr stalke nature hath depeynt sondry hewes within withoute season yt somer came aboute fysshynge foulynge haukynge also venerye huatynge bothe two place ly delytable corne greyne passyngly greable plenteuous maner thynge men herde byrdes fresshely synge tyme yere theyr armonye noyse soote melodye fresshe braunches full delycyous reioyse wolde folkes amerous loues bronde fyred herte adawen theyr paynes sinerte certaynely whan grene vere ypassed aye fro yere yere may come monthe gladnesse fresshe flora floures emperesse hadde cladde soyle newe hir deuyse noble place lyke paradyse cere goddesse largesse foyson suche plente gaue vnto regyon flesshe fysshe wyne vytayle corne lycoure hir full horne vpon lande began rayne snowe astates bothe hyghe lowe lad theyr lyfe soueraygne suffysaunce nature cowde myght auaunce lytell yle hir gyftes greate lyke toforne ye haue herde treate plente habundauce myght pleasaunce herte comodytee besell cytee iason come hym hercules foloweth pres full well arayed ryally sayne army senclosyd togyder twayne twayne people chose none therwith brawnes bone eueryche makynge facyon full well complete proporcyon yonge age good stature countenaunce sad full demure euery wyghte hadde great plesaunce se maner theyr gouernaunce yonge fresshe hardy meke also one paleys go suche chere eueryche hath disporte se maner theyr noble porte gentylmanly demenyd people gan prese euery tose thyse straungers lyke grekes gyse demene selfe thryfty wyse desyre people ne wolde ceesse aboute gader empreesse enquere myght newe suche ryalte ben sodenly entred towne thus eueryche wolde felawe rowne rude stare gase gape loke mase townysshe folke comonly euery thynge falleth sodeynly cethes lyke worthy kynge whan herde firste theyr comynge receyueth hooly matere ye lyste one ye shall whan ye kyng hath sothly vnderstade grekes come lande iason also therwith borne dyssent blode royall thesalye lykly heyre grace haue agayne repeyre auentures achyeued colchos kynge anone see aroos gentyllesse haste may goodly wyse mete way receyueth chere full benynge vnto one dothe assygne offycers awayte nyght daye chargynge maner waye euer may ese thynge may queme plese haue foyson plente eueryche lyke degre thus comaunded maner thynge anone noble worthy kynge fredom myroure thorughe many halle many ryche toure many tourne many dyuers waye many gree made marbyll graye hath conueyed full easy pa tyll brought hambre helde dalyaunce anone euery circumstaunce manly fredom made chere chambre englased bryght clere shone full shene golde asure many ymage pycture hath comaunded offycers oonly honour straugers sp ce wyne anoon yonge fresshe lusty man iason faste gan lycence kynge declare cause comynge firste kynge great tyaltee assendyd royall see clothes golde hanged enuyron custome regyon beholde noble syght stondynge aboute many worthy knyght many squyre many gentylman full well besene kynge right vnto iason stondynge presence comaundyd hath magnyfycence hercules sytte downe besyde iason lenger lyste abyde comynge cause shewe effect whiche wordes fewe saue iason tale began full well auysed chered lyke man conceyued hath noted wonder well poynt poynt mater euerydell nat forgat worde speche euen lyke rethoryk dothe teche gan tale crafte conueye make kynge wolde seye condescende rather enclyne assente myght fyne comynge knyghtly hye empryse thus worde worde shal deuyse right worthy prynce present place oonly supporte hye grace goodnesse moste excellent dygne pacyence fauour benyngne displease nat may saye shewe declare wordes fewe fynall grounde cause comynge ye lyste whiche ben noble kynge goodly wyse without offence benyngly gyue audyence request ye nat disdeyne goodly graunte may atteyne yle may auayle slees golde frely assayle goddes auenture lyste ordayne fatall eure lyeth playnly fortune gouerne thynges comune pea conquest victorye army renowne glorye discomfyture bryngynge outraunce lyeth hyndre auaunte ayen whose myght mortal man may ches wynne lese lyfe deth befyne labour ye lyste fauour gyue leue delaye accorded fully assaye lyke statute maketh mencyon lyste make none excepcyon vpon syde fauour fynde rytys playnly make mynde euer falle shall vnder fonge lowly besechynge ye nat prolonge purpose make delaye grace sette daye myne empryse may achyeue myne abode stant vpon leue seyth one worde grauntynge leste haue fyne requeste whan kynge herde ceryously entent iason sayde manfully stynt alyte kepte hym close whyle tyll laste goodly gan smyle towardes iason sayde vnto hym thus iason quod though thou desyrous vnderfonge passynge hye empryse counsayle lyke shall deuyse full prudently caste aforne mortal peryle thou lorne thynge lawe sette bychauntement may nat belette remedyed fauour mede deth sothe taketh hede guerdon platly twynne fall yt caste flees golde wynne helpe none manhode fortune streyghte waye importune dredfull eke full rage saue deth passage victorye palme conquere sothly iason shall lere founded olde meruaylous workynge statute mortall thynge sore bounde vnder regalye rygour may nat modefye wherfore iason thou thynge tame leste afterwarde layde blame thy lesynge destruccion feythfull herte trewe entencion warne selfe quyte man iustely shall wyte though thou youthe wylfulnesse thy lyfe destroye without vysynesse syth iason perylous caas poynt poynt haue tolde caas auysed put faute surplus frely lyeth thynge sythe thou mayst chese thou wynne lese man iustly may arecte lawe mar hym selfe sette mortall man dewe right may passe hye lowe gette noon grace goddes lyste hym ordeyne euer caste hym darreyne dyuers thynge moste furyous drede wherfore iason euer thou spede haue openly declared hooly peryle fauour spared fer sothe reason wyll ryght thou wotest well lyeth myght declare man lette manhode knyghtly caste sette vpon thynge thou haste herde tell shulde ilenger mater dwell vayne thou knowest beware hir tourneth ball tyme thou gettest thou lyste put choys worde kynge rose vp anone vpon tyme whan shulde gone vnto mete iason syde ye shall ye lyste abyde tyme aprocheth gan neygh fast offycers full besely cast make redy theyr full cure halle bordes cure dyall hour began marke phebus shouthward reysed arke hye lofte drewe noone tyme kynge gone vnto mete entre halle cethes lordes alle knyght hym euerychon hercules also iason sette mete royall see euery lorde lyke degree firste worthy man iason assygned kynge anoon sytte owne borde hercules great lorde set also faste syde marshall lenger lyste abyde assygne estate shulde lyke hye lowe degree scaffolde hye lofte noyse gan loude thynge sof e bothe trompers claryoners noble offycers full thryftely serued haue halle lyke season tyme dyde falle deyntes may rekened sothfastly foyson plente kyngly fredom vnto hye lowe fulsomly gan reygne snowe thorugh hall manhode preysed kynge renowne reysed gestes sothely sye whan hym lyste chere fe ey lyke kynge thryfty wyse deynte man deuyse feste solempnyte grekes myght great nobley see kyng cethes worthynesse reporte therof bere wytnesse come theyr lyue wante connynge ordre discryue euery cours dyuersytees straunge sewes sotyltees day serued place haue excused thoughe lyghtly passe though nat ordre sayne myn englysshe rude eke playne endyte hye thynge forthe wyll reherse kynge shewe gestes nobley ouer hathe doughter sent specyall bad shulde forth anoon brought whiche sothe though men sought world thrugh playn assure men myght founde fayrer creature womanly porte manere demure sadder hir chere whose beaute nat lykely fade whan came grekes glade halle sooth walketh vp downe woman hede pure affeccy owne make chere vnto gestes newe thus medca hir rosen hewe fresshenesse lyllye whyte enter medled kynde delyte nature made hir face spr de egally whyte rede medlynge conclusion ennewed proporcion fynally excesse none one bothe two one ioyned longe endure emperesse called nature hir made lyke hir deuyse beholde paradyse sothe bothe one olde yonge syttynge hall therto successyon borne heyre regyon hir fader discent lyne abyde dure fyne syth e right succede noon heyre male rede also boke maketh mencyon vnto yeres discrecyon able age maryed withstondynge also eke beaute womanheed one fayrest reed yet none bothe haue hir youthe let clergye hir desyre set passyngly specyall artes called lyberall expert knowynge beste hir vre konne hir leste suche woman herde neuer telle elycon dranke welle hir tyme none semblable founde sothe ne none able conceyue studye doctryne nature dispute termyne koude also cause fynde thynges formed kynde lernynge hir tyme spent knewe fyrmament trewe cours sterres theyr meuynge shulde fall expert astronomye moste wrought nygromanyce exorsismes coniurisons vsed also make illusion hir charmes sayde sondry wyse rytes dyuers sacrifyse encens rechelys caste fyre shewe thynges lyke hir desyre gootes horne mylke blode whan mone equat stode fyfthe syxte hous fortuned lokynge gracious chese houre conuenyent fortunat enchauntement make werke sondry apparences well knewe heuenly influence aspectes bothe wrothe glade hir thynges made appartene suche experymentes whan hir lyste hir enchauntementes cowde make wyndes blowe thondre lyghte hayle snowe frese also greue men payne sodeynly cowde make rayne shewe weder hir lyste haue gasten men sodeyne erthe quaue turne daye vnwarely vnto nyght anone make sonne bryght shewe bemes full persynge full shene golden horne voyde nyghtes tene reyse floodes many dredfull wawe whan hir lyst cowde eft wtdrawe eke yonge tree sere roote rynde afterwarde make ageyne kynde lusty braunches blosme budde newe also wynter floures flresshe hewe aray erthe tappte hym grene beholde ioye sene many coloure shewynge full dyuers whyte rede grene ynde pers dayesye hir ryche crowne floures wynter made frown vpon theyr stalke fresshely appere sodeynly dedely chere cowde somer wynter tourne causynge daye mystes morne olde men cowde make yonge eft agayne spronge cowde shewe bothe heed berde full hore graye crafte lerede tree wt fruyte cowde eke make bare rynde leef men stare clypse mone bryght sonne naturelly hadde theyr cours yronne apropred whiche may nat passe tytan cours kynde trase whan meueth vnder clyptyk lyne clypse nat folowe auctours lyst diffyne theyr discripcion bothe twayne full coniunccion sonne bemes reed haue dwellynge dragon heed mone set eke tayle nature may nat fayle must falle eclips nede sondry bokes lyke ye may rede bycause certayne intersecacions dyuers clerkes reuolucions maked ben heuen lofte whiche cause v fayle ofte fresshe comfortable stremes v shadde phebus bemes mone hath made dyuysion sodayne interposicion syght stremes visuall may nat beholde sene luste fully comprehende appollo chare chyuende wonte aforehande se great tholome kynge egypt telleth great cause within boke full compendyously bothe eclyps coniunccion falle naturell mocion medee though clerke suyde encrease hir name vpon euery syde lest fable suche thynges telle thoughe poetes sprynge welle yet god forbede ye shulde gyue credence suche feynynge hygh offence syth nature muste denyed suche affermynge also diffyed euery cristen stedfast byleue certaynly wolde hyghly greue conscience wyse wene agaynst kynde whiche hye quene wyght orlyuynge creature shulde haue power playne ure cursyd thynges supersticious werke kynde contraryous pfor god almyghty iuge iuges alle hath set lawe whiche may nat falle amonge planettes perpetuelly endure afore ordeyned eternall cure whiche may nat clerkes lyst termyne vpon syde bowe declyne discorde debate eternally yformed create thorugh fynger sapyence alway meue theyr intellygence lyke lordshyp bounde neuer yet ne eclyps yfounde mone nat beynge coniunccion haue tolde saue passyon whiche eclips agaynst kynde nature hir knot tyme dyde vnbynde whan goddes sone starfe vpon roode sonne lyfe dyrked goode whan heuen erthe wt hye compunccion haue sygnes shewed lamentacion erthe quaues lyght tourned dyrkenesse deed bodyes vpwarde gan dresse theyr tombes agayne deth lyue stone rocke sonder ganne ryue temple veyll kut two sygnes many yshewed tho wonder token meruaylous great worthy dyonysyous whiche athene clerkes hym wryte called scolys ariopagyte whan sawe noble famous clerke bryght daye sodaynly derke though apaynym tho dayes infect right theyr layes moost cheyf pryncypall phylosophers reken yet tyme astoned mynde sayde platly outher god kynde suffreth dethe outher doute rounde worlde whiche large aboute shalbe dissolued ybrought nought sodayne chaunge hasty thought pby clergye knewe better skyll god may chaunge wyll hath power suche coaccion vnder whose myght disposicion lawe kynde constreyned sothe seye poynt poynt lowely obeye euery thynge hym lyst ordeyne element may cours restreyne hooly wryt wytnesseth ye may se requeste worthy iosue bryght sonne stode gabaon adayes space one degre shon shewynge token trewe knyght fynally gyue hym lyght myght hye prowesse cruell foon manfully oppresse whan faught knyght iosue kynges fyue reygnynge amoree longe laste pursute chaas tyll take theyr trespaas dempt dede bible telle syth god thus hyghly lyst fulfylle knyght request orison wonder though passion criste ihesu incarnat sake sonne bemes though wex blake syth hath lordshyp planettes alle hym lyst nedes must falle medea though ouydius fable reherseth wryte thus lyst hir name exalte yet trouthe whyle doth alte passynge sorceresse ferthest name chaunteresse wyll passe ouer agayne matere came mete ye shall whan hir fader hadde hir sent came anone comaundement came fynde tofore make hir beaute seme hir closet toke hir beste araye encrease euer maye nature werke royall apparayle woman gladly wyll nat fayle wha beaute haue plenteuous largesse embellysshe theyr besynesse ryche tyre vpon euery syde fought mysse close hyde foule shall couertly wryed defaute outwarde espyed pbut bothe fayre well besayne hir porte womanly certayne hir comynge gladeth halle ioye vnto one alle se maner tho hir entree hir fader bad take hir see besyde iason hym disporte womanhode recomforte pbut oo ala lacked hye prudence discrete auyse inwarde prouydence wysdome also perell caste afore truste mayde tendre yeres bore vnhappy fonde wylfulnesse kynge gentylnesse comaunded hath confusion dishonour destruccion owne donghter borne heyre also womanly feyre sodaynly downe discende consydred nat myscheif ende ala durst hir affye make hir sytte curtesye myght casuell mocion full lyghtly catche haue occasion amysse ala dyde lyst hym nat take hede therto auerte discrecion wysely caste afore reason vnware chaunge womanhede whiche euery wyse man oughte drede euer yet mad wood ought reason konne ryght good gyue fayth hastely credence woman without experyence nouther truste sykernesse ben double full brytylnesse harde assure vnto longeth nature theyr byrthe haue allyaunce doublenesse varyaunce theyr hertes freell vnstable namely youthe meuynge mutable clerkes lyst endyte sory wryte saye chaunge mutabylyte apropred ben femynyte affermed full sage specyally whyle tendre age theyr wexynge whan yt yonge whose herte accordeth full selde wt tonge trouthe inwardely sought surplus remenaunt theyr thought men may trewe patron fynde inconstaunce whose flaskysable kynde fro meuynge wynde hercules nat stronge bynde nouther sampson beleue woman herte make nat remeue blase whyrleth afyre fro flee theyr desyre tyll accomplysshe fully theyr delyte matere naturell appetyte kyndely desyreth fourme tyll cours processe may perfourme woman refrayne ne sewe theyr luste fro man man wyll nat cease tyll assayed wolde god matere apayed one fourme holdeth hym content whan boundes hath terme went nat desyre ferther procede styll abyte wyll nat excede example woman wolde reste one dewely sholde holde payde stylle abyde vnsure fotynge dothe ofte slyde nat content vnytee pursue aye pluralytee nature meuynge thewed though amoge signes outward shewed pretende maner stabylnesse vnder hyd doublensse secrely outwarde eye full harde treason espye vnder curtyn veyle honeste closed chaunge mutabylyte theyr desyre kepte full close mewe thynge hadde leuest sewe outwarde haue lawde declyne wt faynynge frawde pwherfore cethes thy wyt barayne thou afore prudence naddyst sayne shulde folowe vnhappy ca thou bolde suffre ala thyn owne doughter fayre fresshe hewe straunge gestys entred newe folylye lete hir dele wher thrugh thy hono thy worship thy hele loste haste myscheif brought straunge lande wt sorowe moche thought great sclaundre great myserye aduersyte ende made thou lefte sole thou myghtest wel complayne make dole ala whyle thy prudent syght thou haddest grace remembre ryght haue cast discrete purueaunce weyed wysely mesure balaunce fraude woman freelte full selde sykerte latyn guydo doth expresse wherfore thou cethes rechelesnesse thou haste one augment thy wo without recure bothe two forgo firste thy treasoure thy doughter dere passyngly entere eke thyne heyre whan yt gone sayth myn auctour none thy daye occupye thy royall ceptre thy lande gye pbut worthe great prouydence waker kepynge besy dylygence myghty mar god batayle myght helpe diffende auayle agayne wyt woman sleyghte whose fraudes huge aweyghte lyste aye game gothe theyr purpose holde lyef lothe slye prudent wyse storye playnly doth deuyse medea hir engyne crafte hir fader treasour hath berafte thorugh worchynge hir sleyght gyle ye shall within lytell whyle sat mete tyde next hir fader iason hir syde sodaynly hir fresshe rosen hewe full ofte tyme gan chaunge renewe hondreth fythe alytell space blood hir goodly face vnto hir herte vnwarely gan bale therwithall wexeth dede pale efte anone take hede hir hewe chaungeth goodly rede euer amonge ennewe hir coloure rose meynt lylye f oure though rose delegan pace yet lylye abydeth place tyll nature made efte mete thus colde sodayne hete medea hir selfe assayled passyngly bexed trauayled brent gan colde aye gan beholde yonge iason gan desyr loke hym set afyre beaute semelynesse euery thynge inly gan inpresse sawe bothe mynde thought emprenteth forgat right nought considereth euery circumstaunce bothe porte gouernaunce sonnysshe heer crisped lyke golde knyghtly loke manly chere countenaunce many noble sygne face also moste gracious benygne moste acceptable vnto hir plesaunce thought suffisaunce without vnto hir alone consyder loke parsone tyme without drede mete drynke toke lytell hede foode hath loste hir appetyte loke hym hath great delyte prynted hir remembraunce loue hathe hir caught newly traunce marked fury bronde may nat escape honde noreschewe stroke speciall yolde body herte vnto iason platly seye euer amonge hym cast hir eye whan fonde aleyser opportune wysdom woldenat contune hir loke longe lest men dempte amys maner woman kepte hir close wonderly secree hir chere man myght see mente none occasion put suspeccion openly token sene caste rather men shulde wene encheson hir abstynence sat sylence oonly womanhede honeste shame chaste drede togyder hir herte mette whiche twayne mayde lette fro mete drynke wolde seme thus wysdome made deme caste theyr oppynyon thus blent discrecion hir chere cowde euery thynge excuse gaue mater fooles muse pno chere vnbrydeled tyme hir asterte one enclosed hir herte another hir chere declared maydens hath ofte sythes spared shewe desyre dede falleth take hede whyle flouren virgynyte youthe haue lyberte specefye theyr herte wolde kepe close nat bolde shewe sume theyr sentence thus medea kepynge aye sylence ne lette worde hir lyppes pace couertly obre chere face mente sheweth hir eye secretly man cowde espye hote fyre hir brest yreke hir selfe right thus gan speke sothe moche wolde god yonge lusty man whiche fayre semely syght assured myn owne kynght whiche moste plesaunt enteer berde yspronge shynynge lyke gold weer well ilymed compact measure well growe heyght good stature lyketh euery parte wele assent fortune hir whele iewred stonde grace semeth vpon knyghtly face heuen beholde therwith herte fele colde yet sothe may none ala ne hath wopyte leste knewe entente moche trouthe hym mente whiche ala taketh maner hede hym brenne dothe glede deed dare nat discure ala pytous wofull auenture rewefull mortall payne murdred dare complayn frende foo chaunce ala fynde helpe socour ca trewely yet shall deuyse thynge mene honest wyse lyke shall openly founde desyre knyt bounde hym wedlok neuer hym twyn menynge withouten syn grounded sette vpon clenlynesse without fraude doubylnesse clene pure myne entencion lo aye maner condycion woman well fayne shewe one though thynke twayne couertly thynge sayne humble chere face playn enclose theyr lustes suche sotylte vnder boundes honeste theyr entent though trecherye withall surplus vnder iurye though fayth afore pretende fraude wt florisshing wel defede flaterye oonly worlde blende doubylnesse enclosed ende yet aye deceyt benethe ment vnder sugre fayned clene entent sothe existence truste well apparence shewe one another mene whose blewe lyghtly dyed grene vnder floures depeynt stabylnesse serpent dareth newfangelnesse playne seme wt wordes fayre glosed vnderneth theyr couert wyles closed thyngr moste theyr paye wyll denye rathest swere naye lyketh guydo wome endyte ala wolde cursydly wryte agaynst debate right sory englysshe translate repreef euyll seye leuer theyr loue deye wherfore praye take pacyence purpose nat offence good parfyte euerychone reken trowe nat one wyll herte trewe though amonge chese loues newe consydereth thynge blame ofte tyme se men must puruaye wha refuse cowde wolde excuse sytteth nat woman lyue alone store haue mo one prayeng grace hope trespace though makynge guydo wryte origynall myssayth lete hym bere wyte syt well vengaunce byte hym woman hath offended myght shulde amended shulde receyue duely penaunce deyed without repentaunce dispeyred sauacion shulde euer haue remyssion contryte synne redresse may nat ben clerkes bere wytnesse pand trouthe alyue mene guydo shulde hym shryue bytter penaunce playnly shulde haue tyme ygraue shulde remembre platly nat sterte repente hym hole herte spake confusion wyll lenger make disgression matere lete gnydo tell forthe workynge medee hath lycence hir fader nome hir chaumbre alone come whan halle withdrawen pres whan iason also hercules lyke kynge mete hadde theyr chambres conueyed ladde full royally arayed besayne euery walle couered certayne clothe golde full stately wyse whyle ye haue herde deuyse medea hir chaumbre gone wherby selfe complaynynge euer one gaue yssue hir paynes smerte hir sore haue wounded herte loue hath brought hir sodayne rage nat lykly soone aswage sothenesse furyous god cupyde hath suche fyre kynled hir syde neuer lykly lete violent feruent hete encrease gan hir payne hir brest wixe twayne great debate stronge batayle feruently eche dyde assayle contek erne game inparted betwyxt loue shame metynge togydre vnset steuen felde nat parted euen loue sothe full hye renowne bolde hardy lyke fyerse lyowne nat ferefull spere swerde knyfe hote hasty auntre lyfe eke surquydous stoute full pryde chefe champyon god cupyde causeth ofte bothe f e bonde full many peryll take honde caused hath full many man deth many one yelde vp breth made theyr woundes largely blede peryll loue taketh none hede gete hym honour excellence fame pbut contrary enmye called shame lyke cowarde faynt hertles neuer dare put hymselfe pres lacke manhode draweth hy euer bake dredfull ferefull wrake lyke childe yonge tendre age hath nouther herte corage assayle febyll myght yet full ofte hath stonde syght many louer lete hym spede thorugh false cospyrynge brother drede drede shame whan allyed one assent haue pytously denyed vnto loue herte hardynesse ne durst worde expresse whan loue manhode wolde speke woode fyre brest vnreke vpon poynt whan shulde assay cometh shame anone vtterly fayth nay causeth loue horne shrynke abasshe chere pytously wynke cowardely cause appayre thus shame frowarde contrayre thorugh helpe drede louers folke fere doutlesse shame nought ne kouthe bothe nyghe ferre loue lawes often shulde erre wynde honestes cheyne bondes brydell breke reyne right hors tray large lytell nought louers wolde charge folowe theyr wyll theyr lust sewe whyle shame kept mewe within brest none knowe outwarde porte loue bereth hym lowe ne shame clerkes haue compyled theyr hertes daunger exyled straungenesse feyned fals disdayne ne shame playnly wardayne woman wrytynge olde without assaute castell yolde nede sege layne suche caas longe tretye vayne nature loue processe pbut ala drede shamefastnesse haue daunted loue full lowe manere made hym full humble porte chere haue eke theyr vyolence manhode put hym sylence ben great cause mornyng payne amyddes ylke twayne loue shame euen vpon poynt stode medea full great disioynt ne may payne nat endure hoote brente wofull creature betwyxe bothe mene loue shame whan loue wolde thynge attame desyres declare oute came shame anone put hym doute drede redy lust denye thus stode iupardye loue shame maner traunce vn euenly hanged balaunce shame great loue yet well knewe hir syghes sore hir stormy cruell auenture drede shame durste nat discure fyre loue hath hir brest enclosed whiche full harde deposed thus henge euen wixe two shene wyste beste tyll fortune hir double face vnhappely hath wrought gete hir grace whyrlynge hir whele aboute causeth wretch ful lowe dowe loute whan beste wene sytte hye lofte experyence men may se full ofte hir gery reuolucion lady transmutacion full ofte tyme fals full vnstable enhasteth thynges foolys full greable whiche ende theyr confusion vndre sugre shrowde hir poyson aye fortune hir maner wretch sheweth fayre chere face flaterye benyngne eye fully foolys parfourme thentent thorugh great myscheif shent ende crafte eschewe vnware harme hir tayle doth sewe right fell whylome medee gynnyge grounde hir aduersyte pfor lady called fortune graunted hath leyser opportune shewe iason hooly hir herte whiche made hir full sore wepe smerte daye merydyene whan appollo bemes shene southe plage gan westre faste cethes hir fader hath sent haste medea come hym anone bad hir shulde gone vnto iason hercules make chere amonge pres whan kaught oportune space hir desyre sawe eke place hir fader moost occupyed thought nat espyed apparceyuynge great besynesse towarde iason anone gan hir dresse haste full knyghtly chere curteys wyse gan drawe nere towardes hir sawe let whan togyder met medea syghynge firste abrayde iason euen thus sayde phowe medea shewed iason maner conquest golden flees wan ca vi iason quod thyne hye noblesse thy manhode thy gentylnesse bothe assembled thy parsone yfere knyghthode firste requere thy conceyte oppynyon nat arecte presumpcyon doubylnesse inconstaunce womanhede varyaunce bolde thynge spare menynge clerely declare without eynynge wordes plat playne besechynge firste shall sayne without goodlyhede benyngnely take hede pacyently wordes leste saye take beste entent thynge greue thynges two myne herte sore meue saye loue gentylnesse mene clerely expresse persone thynge counsele parte lyke ye shall fele semeth firste curtesye soth fastnesse genterye straungers euery maner wyght bounde holde due ryght make chere trewely bycause iason se moche manhode great worthynesse wyll nat fayne besynesse helpe al may lyke worde herte gan syke sake sayde ouer fele full great anoy sore meued without auysenesse oonly youthe wylfull hardynesse flees golde gete ye may whiche empryse euer assay peryllous playnly achyeue sothe ye cowdelyeue douteles well assure fynall mede auenture nat deth saue report shame ye wene gete name ende playnly shall tourne contrarye gynnynge fyne shall varye wyt man nouther engyne myght though neuer expert fyght haue armes passynge excersyse sleyghtes olde newe empryse though beste brethed endure deuyse armure wepen also brynge harded stele trenchaunt persynge yet laste whan hath sought without vayle may right nought pwherfore iason haue compassion youthe pure affeccion wylfulnesse ye shall thus lorne ben blood lyne hygh yborne certaynly may none ye counsayle take none may helpe ese ala iason wyll ye nat appese manly corage caas yblent counsayle ben obedyent durst swere ye shulde haue victory ben remembred put memorye perpetuelly thorugh knyghthod wyn flees golde whiche yonde within yle standes besyde whiche mar gouernour gyde wherfore one selfe assente counsayle fully consente fewe wordes ye lyste spede leue lust worke rede iason wt full humble chere answered sayd myn owne lady dere thanke best wyse right fet forthe may suffyse power platly may attayne myne hertes quene lady souerayne ye may hooly ensure whyle lyfe may dure truste right well lyst nat fayne lyue dye luste restrayne hym owne trewe man obeye euer without chaunge doubylnesse whyle lyue sothfastnesse lyste trewe affeccion vpon lyfe haue compassion gentyllesse ye lyste haue suche cherte body saue good fayth due ryght ybounde owne knyght vnto myn ende specially grace benyngnely ye lyst selfe counsayle neuer afore degre ne dyde seruyse womanhede wordes full goodlyhede owne man lysteth recomforte whiche sothe reporte thousande folde plesaunt neuer afore meryte gat hym graunt ne desert request prayere frely herte full entere lyst vnrequyred wo rewe vndisserued trewe ensure vpon fayth faste seruyse shall vnto laste parseuer sothely shalbe slouthe varyaunce therto trouthe fynally withouten wene fewe wordes saye right mene lyste nat fayne flatre delude beheste dethe shall conclude whan parcas lyues threde rende thus make ende quod ful wysely herte ye muste afore consydre aud aduerte aduenture ye take hande prudently peryll vnderstande full warely caste haue mynde mortall harme tayle behynde well credyble leue well impossyble gynne honour also fyne thylke flees hye power dyuyne preserued eke marcys myght entreth therfore fyght full harde hym escape fyrye flawme whan bulles gape ben brasse trapped leuen drede lyghtnynge heuen tofore dynt great thonder seuered hath many toure asonder asshes must man consume wherfore rede ye nat presume ram assayle leste ye labour lese withdrawe foote yet sythe ye may chese good aduyse discreciowne honour sauf hye renowne ye lyste wylfulnesse oonly folye hastynesse empryse heed procede ye lyst lyke rede saue selfe wo myschaunce lyke ye shall myn ordenaunce ye commytte lowely lyste obeye without fraude seye iason syttynge borde medea emprentynge euery worde waxe ire almoste vnpacyent sayde ala entent counsayle leue empryse certes foule cowardyse gynne thynge myght nat cheue euery man wolde repreue reporte confusion pryde presumpcion toke whan large hye thynge great charge durst doute myschefe accomplysshe whan cam prefe leuer myn owne lady dere iuparte put selfe one wordes fewe smale pecys hewe shulde cowardely forsake thylke empryse haue vndertake ye well knowe leue thus ala let counsayle playnely ca euer happe falle trusteth right well shall none cowarde herte fro purpose shulde dyuerte without lawde lyfe shulde lede shame eternall shulde mede worlde noted ouer euery lande spoke speciall iason hath hyghly vndertake fere dare none ende make thynketh right well shall betyde lyfe dethe myscheif abyde vpon trouthe ensure ferforthe lyfe may endure shall parfourme haue begonne though may nat wonne muste deth beye wyll nat leue leuer haue deye lyue ashamed cowardyse slouthe semeth hygh routhe man appere dare shewe hede whan hath honour vyllanede tyme whan name slayne eueryman shulde rather fayne dye honour lyue wretche though thynge deth stretche welcome shall well abyde betyde quod sythe ye algates desyre haue ado ther nomore ought espy ye leuer shortly dye rather lyue haue shame yet ernest game suche monstres vnwarely dele lyke dede ye shall fele wherfore meued pyte greatly stered ye volunte without aduyse discrecion counsayle good delyberacion lyste take meruaylous vyage youthe also corage gouerned ben matere luste bothe two yfere inparded ben ye purpose sewe unpossyble eschewe sodayne dethe nouther fre bonde crafte man hath power withstonde pwherfore thynke herte good entent caste awaye yet ye shent tourne shape remedye suche routhe haue ye shulde dye fader loue moste rather ye shulde thus loste shall offende vtterly displease frendes may ease shall fynde suche amene weye leste ye shall nat deye caas thynke gyde shall sette asyde byrthe firste stok royall pand ouer myn heritage withall myn honour shalbe put backe helpe shalbe lacke founde ye wyll kynde ye lyste haue mynde disserne goodly quyte consyderynge firste nat alyte saue lyfe stande ieopardye peryllous ye espye shall ordayne thorugh crafte oonly wyxe v twayne parte hope shalbe wele vpon poynt may fele faythfully ioye wo smerte full accorde body wyll herte desyre ye condecende vndertake make good ende sothly lady sayde iason tho assented without wordes mo fulfyll euery circumstaunce euer may pleasaunce quod sayne firste wt fayth herte playne myght besy cure menynge hole ye meassure ye hereafter shall take wyfe holde kepe lyfe dede accorde hest fyne sume requeste excepte oonly ye shall ordeyne repayre faders reygne faythfully ye shall led whan ye succede daye herytage herte aye one one corage ye shall lyke trewe cherysshe chaunge newe lyke myn estate without varyaunce whyle ye lyue haue remembraunce kyndenesse great nede none lyue may spede creature mortall assayle force marcy dragon bulles bothe fere lere hooly manere shall hym gye lyke thynke specifye whan happeth mete agayne none may helpe certayne caas platly ye shall fynde nat aske ye kynde sothly quod iason shalbe ye deuyse wyll fayth assure goodlyest creature euer yet sawe vnto paye fayrest eke sothe naye bounte ye ben comparable dethe ye ben merciable whyle lyue saye fayth myn herte meneth tunge ayth wyll founde owne trewe man lyfe deth euer grace pleasaunt parfourme hestes graunnt worke fully sauacion ye haue sayde full conclusion trewely ye bere lyfe beaute haue prerogatyfe passynge echone lyst nat glose amonges floures dothe rede rose whiche somer amyd leuys soote veer hath made roote humydyte kyndly ascende barayne foyle clothe amende braunches wynter made bare sote blosmes fresshely repare medowes many sondry hewe tapited ben dyuers floures newe sondry motlees moste lusty sene holsome bawme shad amonge ye grene pright rose fayrest echone right nature sette alone whan made firste hir deuyse aboue haue pryse ye ben bounte sprynge welle therto beuute sothly ye excelle lyue comparison ne may made discrecion ye passe euery man may se fynde vnto moste goodly euer yet borne without lorne helpe socour fully destitute ne founde refute fro al fredo mewarde doth haboude somoche euer bounde fer forthe lyue may streche sake deth ne reche therwithall myght agrene helpe goodly lyste sene neclygence sholde thynge refuse ye wolde myght reason full well merked noted eke wylfull nycetee folylye voyde away grace arage man hym chace wylfull fortune whan benyngne wherfore hooly resygne herte body lyfe eke dethe hande whyle lasteth brethe othes afferme may perseruer myn endynge day youre trewe spouse haue sayd sworne behested playnly toforne vpon euery thynge obeye may please tyll tyme deye shuld lenger tarye beheste shall neuer varye whan sawe great stedefastnesse upprysed hye gladnesse great ioye pleynly hir herte voyde euery wo smerte lowly hir lust obeyde wente thus hym seyde iason quod shall ordayne amene waye bothe twayne may efte agayne leyser mete sone parfourme done matere lyke entent shalbe made fynall sacrament desyre man shall vnbynde though therto may leyser fynde towarde eue shall nat escape truste right well tyme shape secretly may mete yfere shall sende pryue chambrere myne whiche shall conueye vnto chamber pryue weye certayne houre without fable entent moste greable vpon poynt whan phebus wt lyght westryd eke derke nyght hath dymnesse shadowes blake emysperye fully ouer take ofte gyueth fauour fortune vnto louers leyser opportune parfourme theyr lustes achyeue right anone draweth eue shall closet sende euery thynge make ende shall good leyser speke eueryche hertes breke declare sume wylle whan haue spoken fylle good leyser fully byhete shall ordayne whan v lust mete sette tyme euer saye nay alway nyght whan passed day myghty ioue wysely socoure hence forth wyll hooly youre whyle lyue wakynge slepe ye hestys kepe iosan lowly gan enclyne said fer man may ymagyne wyght may clerely comprehende wyll lyues ende seruaunt faythfully quyte though nat say lyte trewe herte wyll nat neuerthelasse though nat peynte compasse gay processe soueraygne hertes quene tyll deed trewely shall mene haue trouth whyle haue lyf myde ende trewely ye shall fynde theyr speche ende thus make medea shope hir take hir leue anone amonges pres first hir fader hercules bode lenger forth anone vnto hir chambre haste gone vp downe made many wente none hir meyne wetynge mente castynge wayes hir purpose chyeue hir wyttes gan besyly meue rometh hir habytacle syde obstacle lettynge whiche wolde hir sore greue hir studye tyll drewe eue hir leue complaynynge hir wo many thought walkynge fro pthe myddaye houre gone ouer slyde tytan faste hath chare ryde dayes arke est west compassed fyry stedes haue almoste passed oryzonte drawe downe full lowe golden wayne man myght knowe hydde fyry bemes bryght descence full fer syght pand herynes hir cope myrke euenynge begonne dyrke twylyght whan day gan fade esperus stremes glade ben fresshe lusty merye gan recomforte emysperye pwhan medea hir selfe alone hygh desyre gan make hir mone longe abode hir knyght alway accountynge houres nyght full trouble full thought whiche hath full streytly serched sought redy waye vnto hir purpose kept full close amyd hir herte quappynge awawe drede fere tyll hope gan adawe bad shulde right merye gladde tyll drede agaynward made hir sobre sadde lest hir desyre troubled lette thus abay ysette amyd hope drede also ne wyste beste pfor hir desyre hye affeccion sobre brente hir oppynyon luste hadde mete iason agaynst drede came anoon made hir ferefull lest espyed hir sorowe holpe remedyed oonly fortune dyrke nyght whiche made full glade lyght recomforted oonly thyse two good hope made hir glade also began anone caste deuyse whan mone heuen wolde ryse whan hir horne pale wolde shede hir lyght vpon hylle vale gan acounte caste well tyme founde quarter passed pryme well knowynge art sawe sothe fourth part mone shadde newe lyght passed hir cours full ryght tyme coniunccion thre sygnes full computacion complet seuen dayes hir age pat whiche tyme brennynge hir rage thorugh darted cupides arowe gan loke beholde narowe euery dore lysten besely ony wyght myghtespy court outher walke go man romyn fro sore shedradde goynge vp downe whan herde noyse sowne whan hereth sprynge venym sothly hir ere wysshed hadde ben bedde pytouslyfe longe nyght ledde wtout respyte though wyght coude knowe tyll hye mydnyght cokkes crowe whiche tyme whan huste stylle accomplysshe ye remenaunt hir wylle euery made sylence clepyd anone vnto hir presence aged vecke fer yeres ronne suche crafte moche helpe konne thriftely bryng thynge aboute afore caste euery doute pof yeres passed olde experyence hath gyue passynge hye prudence loue sleyghtes knowe made dogge bowe medea discureth hir thought poynt poynt forgat right nought charged hir reles hir smerte recomforte hir troubled herte haste hir anone vpon hir waye vnto hir chaumbre iason conuaye anone nat rekles caas gone hym full softe paas newe nat lere brought hym anone ye shall whan cok comon astrologere mydnyght hour wt voyce ful clere began sowne dyde besy payne bete breste wynges twayne tyme mynute wyll nat pace warne place tydes season nyght medea awayte vpon hir knyght full redy entre kepe lyste full lytell slepe ne parcell hir thought wha iason hir chambre brought without espyeng maner wyght anone conueyeth hym full right hir closet haste maye full well besene great ryche arraye hir syde made hym take see firste ylke lee three hir moste expert caas sodeynly tourned braas vecke stare vpon mone walked hath lefte alone whan medea dores shette downe iason anone hath hir sette firste fynde hir besy myght aboute chambre set vp lyght great torch cyerges full ryall aboute pyllers euery wall whiche gaue alyght lyke sonne shene cheste wrought crystall clene firste taketh hir passage whiche toke aryche ymage pure golde full lusty beholde custome rytes olde myghty ioue eterne creat halowed also consecrat whiche ymage deuoutly ought humble herte iason first brought made hym lowly theron take othe vnto laste outher lyef orlothe hir shulde take vnto wyfe fro daye forthe durynge lyfe herte vnfayned fayth inuyolate cherysshe hir lyke hir estate fro tyme fynde hadde euer floured virgynyte myn auctour well reherce aye kept hir clene touche man thought dede neuer dyde amys herte holly gyuen vnto iason euer mo anone hath put hande vnto swore fully ye haue herde saye hir requestes without delaye kepe whyle lyfe may laste ala soone ouer caste hest fayth wt whiche assured hadde fraude flaterye yeured couertly hir innocence hir trewe menynge hir dylygence euer deuyse deceyued falshede man though yt trouthe apparent aboue doubylnesse slyghly shoue though sothly allyed trewe menyng thynge espyed vnder fayre chere faynynge failas myght wrought ca thy sake ceptre regalye lordes eke hir alye forsoke one toke hede pyte goodlyhede loste hir frendes hir good fame oonly iason saue froshame yet moreouer forsoke hir herytage borne hye parage shulde haue successyon heyre dissent regyon womanly wolde hir quyte yfere set nat amyte one hour hath forsake vnto hath hir holly take oonly truste thou shuldest haue kynde rychesse honour hath lefte behynde ches exyle gone hir kynne cely mayde alone ala wepe thyne vnkyndnesse hath nat fro deth fro distresse preserued yet thou takest none hede shulde haue deyed ne thy rede thy conquest cause may nat shortly clause wryte hir bounte breifly comprehende effectuelly parfourmed ende wordes fewe may nat tolde thorugh hast ryche f ee golde manly conquered whiche without doute vnlyaly brought aboute whan thou helpe destytute thy comforte synguler refute thou mayst nat denye erthely honour gan defye conserue heuynesse hir fader hath rychesse emperysshed pyte ensample whiche woman myght lere shulde truste man ala medea moche bothe sterres astronomye yet sawe nat afore hir desten ye loue hath hir put gouernayle hir crafte ne myght hir natauayle slowe calculacion caste afore constellacion hir byrthe hir wofull fate rekleshed sawe late suppose hir connynge fallyble doutles semeth nat credyble hadde wyste toforne pytously hadde nat lorne ye shall se hastely storye reherseth befell iason medee firste ye shall ordre maner se wrought swore nyght ala hathe forbore hir mayden hede great pyte yet mente nat honeste suppose went haue wyfe touchynge holde stryfe yet one thynge dare aferme fayne menynge ylke twayne ne nat one wonder fer atwene trewely gan mene honeste thynkynge outrage lyke mayde innocent age accomplysshe flesshely false appetyte parfourme foule appetyte wrought euery thynge hir entent contrayre ala debonayre truste vpon curtesye quyte hir hir genterye hastely rewe vpon sinerte woman tendre herte wyll gladly routhe pyte whan man aduersyte saue lyfe rather shulde deye medea shortly seye castynge peryll shall fall desyres lustes hooly obeyeth hir full myght longe almoste nyght hath course rounde aboute gon whiche tyme hir spake iason lowly sayde lady tyme aryse soone wyll pryme ye may se well daye begynneth sprynge may byrdes synge prayenge beste wyse shall werke ye lyste deuyse ceryously euery thynge dispose beseche goodly fresshe rose myne empryse brynge ende erst hense wyll wynde saue thynke firste wt trete wyse countre ye shall lete grece repayre agayne whiche lande great felycyte truste well thynge drede reyne shall lede conquest wynne wherfore praye goodly begynne shall werke haste ye maye good fayth anone wyll daye spake fayeng ye shall myn owne iason vnto dere myselfe conclusion assented full affeccion wyttes hole herte enfourme ye shall asterte euery daunger lytell yle ye lyste abyde whyle vp rose haste maye cofre hir treasour laye went anone brought hym hir honde ryche ymage syluer fonde whiche sothely meruaylous entayle whose power vertue auayle effectuelly hir bothe entent agayne magyk enchauntement sytte force sorcerye made astronomye houre chose equat none clerkes olde full longe agone whylom wha flouryng age vsed make suche ymages dyde kynge called tholomee iason comaunded hath medee bere ymage hym pryuely ye haue herde worke effectuelly euery thynge dyde assygne toke hym medecyne made maner oynement ennoynte hym nat brent ryche precious bawme agayne malys euery fyre flawme toke hym anone ryche rynge sette stone vertue hadde venym destroye syde myght hym noye whiche stone also myght man cowde bere ryght within hande next skyn enclosed strengthe syght shulde deposed wolde gase beholde euer hande holde vertue infallyble storye sayth shulde vysyble whiche stone wyse clerkes calle achates moste vertuous alle founde sothely cecyle whiche stone whylom wrote virgyle venus eneas sente firste whan cartage wente iason toke certayne bylle wryten lyke boke iourney myght moche auayle bad hym wysely nat ne fayle caste hym graciously spede firste scripture rede ram touche wyse hym chargynge eke afore hye empryse humble herte deuocyon knelynge saye oryson vp downe wryten bylle prayenge goddes lowely fulfylle requeste mercy haue pyte myscheif hym saue cheif socoure toke hym vyoll lycoure bad hym manly without fere drede whan come vnto bully rede hym shape knyghtly escape faste seeth gape theyr goles lycour caste hym nat lytell gaste theyr iowes togyder shall glyewe syde shall nat eschewe beye luste hym lyste costreyne doutles maugre theyr peyne shall daunte make tame hym lyste ernest game myght make louten enclyne bowe bothe backe chyne lycour shall chawles coharte sonder shall nat departe offende noye wyght whan thus vnto hir knyght euery thynge gaue instruccion playne doctryne informacion shall scape daungers take hede werke auysely accorded thought ye best parte men theyr rest waked drewe daye well sawe morowe graye leste men hadde suspecion hye prudence discrecion twene twelyght rody morowe toke theyr leue wt seynt iohn ye borowe oft kyssynge louers wha twynne wente lefte withinne beynge hope mete agayne daye iason faste euer maye gan ordayne hym iourney acheue thought wolde anone go take leue wyse within lytell whyle maner rude style purpose sothely nat spare supporte playnly declare whan rowes rayes rede estwarde v full erely gonne sprede euen twelyght ye damnynge whan larke custome gynneth synge salue hir heuenly laye lusty goddesse morowe graye mene aurora whiche afore sonne wonte enchase blacke skyes donne derkenesse dymme nyght fresshe phebus coforte lyght bryghtnesse bemes shene hadde ouer gylte hye hylles grene floures eke agayne morowe tyde vpon theyr stalk gan playn leues wyde whan iason companye towarde kynge full faste gan hym hye fonde lyke estate sceptre hande full pompous elate hye see regalye syttynge full kyngly amyd chyualrye lordes aboute enuyron whiche tyme yonge champyon vnder vowe stondyng ram sterne face tofore kynge cam besechynge hym magnyfycence day graunte hym lycence armes make delayes concludynge playnly assayes wyll daye felde founde achieue lyke bounde olde byheste nat poynt declyne lyfe deth tyll parfourme fyne hooly auntres vnto flees longe kynge requeryng lenger hym prolonge goodly graunte fyn empryse kynge full sobre wyse consyderynge sume demaunde iason spake sayde shall comaunde requeste parfourmed haste quod full sore gaste wylfulnesse thou shuldest destruyde leste men thy deth arected vnto therupon wolde blame sette ryall power nat ne lette thy manly youthe suche iupartye whiche sothe great vylanye preiudyce myn estate name afterwarde men put blame thorugh fals reporte wronge opynyon withstode nat thy destruccion pwherfore rede yet thou auysed counsayle lete nat dispysed better honoure certayne thy countre repayre agayne wylfully take honde mortall thynge man may wtstonde rede fully myn aduyse take hede therto fythe thou art wyse leste thou repente whan late thou wylt algate thy purpose holde nat rede almyghty mar praye spede gyde euer falle eke praye goddes alle saufe sounde thy body restore thou gettest whan iason herde kynge nat dismayed stoned thynge knyghtly wyse dyde hym reuerence thankynge hyghly royall excellence grace benyngnyte vpon deth hym lyste haue pyte fully concludynge touchynge batayle nouther rede counsayle wyse purpose shulde withdrawe lyke statute playnly lawe right fer forthe fortune wyll hym eure tyde auenture settynge asyde euery feer drede sayde platly wyll procede parfourme hath vndertake ydell mo skylles make allegge agayne iason full openly playne touchynge surplus dredfull thynge departynge sayde kynge audyence lordes alle euer falle euer malys theron muse worlde firste excuse goddes platly quyte though deye ye nothynge wyte ne man shall arecte skylle werke frely wylle agayne aduyse hye prudence lyfe deth presence hooly herte neuer f ytte goddes fortune comytte lyste ordayne agayne whose wyll shall neuer playne put blame betyde honour ioye shame thynge thus ende make tyme leue take tho aboute stonde one one toke honde wyse forthe gan hym dresse anone thynke expresse whan tytan wt feruent hete drawe vp ye dewe leues wete towarde myd morowe diffyne vpon houre whan clocke nyne iason full manly full lyke knyght armed stele chere full glad lyght ganoresse hym forth hap euer fall sayde dieu vnto feres boote vpon stronde alone whan came londe water hadde vessell lafte firste remembrynge crafte medea circumstaunces shulde kepe obseruaunces euery thynge hadde well mynde anone full manly fynde shope hym forth went knyghtly pa towarde bulles forged bra poynt whan iourney gan hym medea wexed full pale wan ore agast thynge myght hir glade routhe se woshe made teres hir chekes twayne full pyteously distylle ayne fordewed hir wedes blake aye sorowe made sake lyke woman ferefull doute whyle armes ful maly brought aboute sobbe syghe nat pe leste haste oughte rekles poynt poynt lyke badde lyfe hym hath ladde pand se shulde hym defende gan anone grecys assende toure hye pynacle myght haue none obstacle lettynge nouther haue syght hym hir owne chosen knyght euer amonge wordes brake stoundemell thus hir selfe spake thou iaso souerayne hertes hele thou knewe wo forthe fele sothly trowe shulde nat asterte trewe thy hole herte god praye iourney leste may tyme tourne beste kepe saufe sounde euery membre yefe myght fully remembre taughte fourme euery thynge fully parfourme oonly daye thyn honoure auaunce whiche se hole pleasaunce certes iason fylle ought amysse fare well helthe worldly blysse fare well myrthe solace welfare fortune grace one hertely suffysaunce plo hym hir gouernaunce tyme lande hath ome firste whan come bulles fell dispytous caste theyr fyre frawme f ryous theyr mouthes wonder large huge agayne whiche chefe refuge hym saue nat brent enoynted oyntement body kept hym damage thylke fyre full rage smoke derke full horryble whiche escape almoste impossyble man estate without comforte counsayle medee whose doctryne iason werke scaped mystes derke fyre blases blake eyer cludy dyde make hadde hym made discret sage oonly vertue thylke ymage whiche aboute necke bare wherby prudent ware whan ye bulles haue feersly gaped hath theyr malys auysely escaped enfeccion theyr troubled eyre hath venquysshed disspeyre effecte agayne foule fume wolde man vnto deth consume ymage preseruatyfe hym diffende saue lyfe surely kepe hym drede full ofte sythe wrytte dyde rede vertue oryson vnto hym full proteccion nat fell distresse sykernesse hym preserue mortall ca toke lycour vyell therwithall full lyke manly man one toke bulles forgat nat warely cast therwithal chawes made fast vertue myghtely englewed thorugh hath vtterly eschewed enfeccion sinoky leuen whan eyre gan clere heuen mystes wasted hym toforne manly herte raughte horne sterne bulles vyolence drewe forth defence yoketh maner ploughe made go pa vp n w downe eere londe lyste buxom fonde soyle smothe bare playne made redy bere grayne renges tourned vp downe th rebellyowne humble meke redy wylle desyres playnly fulfylle pand iason lyke champyon gan hym enhaste towarde dragon beest great monstruous foule horryble ryght venymous enarmed scale large thycke brethe peryllous wycke heyre pestylence venym suche vyolence full deedly mortall throte yssued flawme fyre fournes mouthe lyke leuene downe southe gest wont tempest smyte right dragon sothely wryte mouthe hadde flawme blased wherof iason fyrste lytell mased herte dredefull thynge whan remembred rynge fere drede layde asyde gone rynge sette stone full ryche noble ryght vertuous whiche techeth great ysydorus myn auctor also fynde moste comenly comyth ynde must kept chaste wonder clene colour surmounteth euery grene whose vertue venym destroye withstande may nat anoye dragon serpent adder snake specially take holden opposyte worme euen agayne syte without abode sothe may nat chese venym force muste lese stronge vyolent rage stone dothe full great damage whan hath vertue blyue pecys smale gynneth ryue selfe hole abydes whyle lande called cecyle worme bufo bereth name wha men wyll malys make hym tame venym vtterly expresse take quyll myn auctor bereth wytnesse whan wyll worke large ende stone lette lyne right agayne wromes hede holde tyll dede sothly vertue nature venym may laste endure presence ryche stone fynde bufo right anone
