thorugh myght therof bresteth euen twayn oonly kynde whiche man may restrayn goddesse called nature whiche next hir lorde thynge cure hath vertue gyue herhe gras stone whiche man knoweth hir selfe alone cause hyd closed hir hande wytte man nat vnderstande openly myght hir workynge iason vertue rynge thrugh stone yt might hy auauce hath dragon brought vnto vttraunce fonde maner resystence hym withstande force diffence nouther venym none stryfe wherfore hath berafte hym lyfe manly wyse felde outrayed iason full glad well apayed hath wt swerde spent hy many stroke layde hym men hewe oke bryght skales harde dur well vnneth ne myght endure hym dismembre smyte hede anone stede sede gan tethe hede arace ryght forthwith selfe place gan sowe ryght men corne vpon lande ered aforne whiche sede sprange wonder grayne bryght armed knyght stondinge playne whiche anone wt sharpe swerdes grounde eueryche gan hurte wounde tyll eche felowe hath cruelly slawe theyr fate fynall lawe none shulde victorye dethe reioyse memorye yfere thus made ende iason gan wende vnto ram dylygence whiche fonde power diffence maner stryfe rebellyowne myghtely ram draweth downe sette honde vpon eueryche horne slewe firste hath shorne flees golde passynge ryche world tresour lyche made delay take boote haste may roweth forthe tother yle hercules mene whyle vpon brynke many nother mo ode iason tyll euerychone fynde blyue oonly ioye whan dyde aryue gan thanke cheyr goddes graciously hath fall flees hath knyghtly wonne shone clere somer sonne whiche brought wt hym vnto londe feres abydynge stronde whan appollo dayes arke ye west almost ronne marke faste gan downwarde declyne wawes full watrye gan shyne yet passed occian iason come many manly man feres presence kynge hadde acheued euery thynge whiche longeth conquest ram cethes soone euer cam make hym chere outward hath hy payned herte fayned sory without drede expleyte good spede iason flees hath wonne lyke sothe feyners konne whan lyste craftly compace shewe outwarde faythfull trewe face venym enclosed hole within menynge maner syn ryght kynge loke forheed clere made vnto iason outward ryght good chere gan hym speke wordes fewe frendlyhede many sygnes shewe though conquest euery dele poynt poynt lyked wonder wele befull glad fortuned vnto ende hath contuned reioyseth speche countenaunce fortune lyste hym auaunce paleys gan goodly hym conueye daye daye full rychely festeye thynge done herte le felte full great smerte treasour despoyled hath ryche flees forgo damage confucion thus great dyuysion twixe chere menynge thought fareth ofte well sought many man menynge fals double calme couer trouble hye malys hyd desyre rake falsly wycked couert fyre full hoote brennynge inwarde enuye well hym cowde espye knewe theyr menynge fals fraudelent thorugh ala full many innocent deceyued wote nat mene namely suche nat trouthe wene euery chere men make innocence beste take wyse thynke nat wele ryght certayne iason euery dele hath take gre ye kynge hath wrought nat aduertynge ye grutchynge thought doutles sat kynge full sore ram hath loste euermore whan hath vtterly sayne though grutche gayne fynally necessyte tyme myght none outher playnely sawe may nat chese algate flees must lese whether lefe lothe fayneth chere nat wrothe oonly gentylnesse sygne outward grutchyng dyd expresse daye daye curtesye chereth iason companye whiche tyme aboute enuyrowne euery partye regyowne people came stare gase vpon ram mase loke wondre deme lyste whose dome lytell tryste ofte vary tourne fro wysely taketh hede therto comon people chaungeth phane daye wexe morowe wane dothe mone flaskysable trusteth shal fynde ful vnstable glad iason hath sped wele sory lyke neuer adele sayde wonder myght agayne dragon bulles fyght agayne force marte ile alyue myght parte another sayde parauenture crafte wrought discomfyture outher charme sorcerye thus eche theyr fantasye gan deme hym longe day laste makynge delay full glad lyght medea downe descendeth hir chambre outwarde pretendeth sadnesse chere thynge ne knewe men coude nat conceyue hir hewe hir secrete menynge womanly mened hir prudently auoyded discrecion fantasye suspeccion man coude hir workynge deme thynge well dyde seme porte chere cause processe drewe hir pryuely towarde iason nat lere secretly badde hym ere alwyse nat ne leue hir chambre come eue mater hadde trete shal know leyser whan mete anone whan entred nyght sool hym selfe without torche lyght medea hath way take abode slepeles sake wonder deuoutly desyrynge gesse hym trete holynesse touchynge materes contemplacion smytte deuocion freshe venus holde memorye hym alone hir oratorye nat openly ypocrytes praye dyuers angle ioynge waye people comended nat hath nyght dispended vayneglorye none laude themselfe thynkyng fraude secretly ylke twayne alone without lyght outher sonne mone longe nyght haue ladde without reste thought nat beste speke slepe tyll pryme caste lese tho tyme thus nyght togyder dispende dull comprehende obseruaunces suche relygyous prolix werkynge compendyous deme selfe ye gete nomore well ye wote euery faculte hath knowynge experyence men wyll hym rather gyue credence wherfore saye ye wyse axe nat whiche rude man deme thynge namely whan passeth knowynge also wit dulled myn ymagenatyfe deme practyke speculatyfe wherfore passe lete ouer slyde forthe thynke ye lyste abyde playnely tell iason ee whiche accorded assented hym shall grece wende whan gothe shortly ende vnwyste hir fader euery wyght saue alone hath trouthe plyght trewe bothe well woo vnto laste hir moo phowe iason toke shyppynge loue medea sayled awaye hir ca vij whan iason iournee full rychely lyke degree refresshed colchos kynge withall myght lykynge amoneth passed gone grekes assented one purposed hath shortly myght medea stele awaye nyght moche treasour ryche flees full accorde also herculees medea thou hastest faste thou slowe wysely caste shulde falle whan yu thy iourney toke myscheif forsoke false eke vnkynde othes fynde thou bothe eue morowe thy fatall chaunce thy pytous sorowe weptest gan thy selfe rende tyll dethe made wofull ende vayne make rehersayle wote thynge myght auayle iason vnkynde none receyued hath penam talliones goddes disnaturelnesse myscheif wretchednesse made eke ende thorugh cruell hate felle mar loo mortall fate twayne made theyr ende trowe lyke wryte guydo theyr gynnynge nat vertuous ende foloweth full contagyous ala hadde take hede aforne nat myscheif lorne wyll nat afore myscheif se may nat eschewe haue aduersyte ende platly deuyne euen lyke ryght medecyne auayleth nat whan syke deed may helpe stomake heed letuarye emplaystre pocyon resseyt confeccyon herbe stone lech knowe whan corp layde erthe lowe por whan beest tourned careyne myne auctor sayth veyne recure vpon halowe ere leyne salowe veryly fantasye helpeth nat doth remedye thynge parfourmed due date vertue hath whan cometh late rightsom case veryly semblable worldly truste false full mutable caste peryll tyll falle stede sugre ofte casteth galle blended luste whiche present future slouthe neclygent ne lyste afore myscheif caste tyll snare englued faste prouyde graceles full vnprudent wylfull recheles caste peryll tyde sewe theyr luste reason goth asyde befelle whylom two medea iason also pbut euer iason ynde playnly harme alone great damage fynall smerte lacke wysdome ne wolde aduerte shulde falle whan hir iourney toke hir fader folyly forsoke sythe wrought oonly wylfulnesse without counsayle auysenesse lyste hir harmes bewayle lytell nought myght auayle lete hir alone complayne hir damage well wote touchynge hir passage nat take good plyte moone hastynesse began soone chesynge houre nat fortunat alone frendes desolat colchos forsoke shyp gon haste byddynge iason hercules companye hym came thesalye without taryeng one worde yentred ben within shyppes borde oonly cause wynde gode euery thynge theyr luste tho stode assent stale awaye nyght treasoure catche myght ladde plente vytayle forthe anone began sayle many coste many sondry ile towardes grece mene whyle medea glad good chere iason syttynge bothe yfere hercules gentylnesse comforte dyde besynesse faynyngly maner sake louers full queynte make tyll haue hadde hooly theyr pleasaunce theyr luste fulfylled vttreth varyaunce preued iason vtterly hath forsake full vnkyndely medea payne sorowe wo hir guydo ne wryte wordes mo maketh hir none mencyon bycause trowe myn opynyon hir sorowes ende euery dele rehersed full openly wele methamorphoseos wryte full playne naso recordeth certayne hir deth nat oonly hir heuynesse parcell eke vnkyndenesse iason telleth playnely howe medea hir bothe sone slowe lyke theyr fader vysage telleth eke put hir moste rage falsly hym nat excuse loued nother called ceruse eke pysteles taketh hede hir deedly sorowe may beholde rede hir trouthe boughte sore medea ye gete boke hir auenture wyll besy cure hooly tourne style iason werre made lamedon lyke guydo openly descryued grece aryued fi rste whan iason hercules also londed many nother mo lande reygne thesalye kynge pelleus cheualrye caste hym playnely wyll nat fayle mete neuewe aryuayle whan mette countenaunce made outwarde hole entere hadde soueraygne gladnesse kynghthode heyprowesse renowne manly hede expleyte good spede fortune encrease name hath caused hym noble fame colchos honour repayre chere vtterly contrayre entent euer came agayne face hole playne welcomed hym agaynst herte full sore astoned euer asterte auentures colchos peryllous retourned victoryous couertly treason hyde delaye gan sette asyde iason chere full benyngne herytage firste gan resygne septre crowne kyngdome leste parfourme sume beheste lyke assured bonde iason toke honde gan vncle full lowe manere firste thanke herte entere ful knyghtly gan hym praye goodly wolde saye matere fret herte sore daye daye encresynge euer besechynge hym graunte hym audyence tochynge wronge vyolence done vnto hym whan harme ne mente torye lande colchos wente saye kynge troye towne within bondes regyon whan myne great aduersyte wynde weder dryue see v refresshe lande dyde aryue purpose hym stryue rest v wo lytell whyle forth anone go sothe maner harme ne thought vnkyngly malys sought agaynst v firste occasion byddynge haste voyde regyon nat withstondynge come pe lyke brother knoweth hercules vnto myght doynge distresse wherfore praye hye noblesse purpose condescende whiche platly fynall ende sette full conclusion hooly werke destruccion lyke auowe whan thense went ye goodly lyste assent one strongly nat spare maugre myght troye fare may fynde fauoure v refresshe golde creasoure oonly eke curtesye v strengthe also cheualrye pelleus without abode anone mater vnderstode assented herte wyll also vyage go worthy regyowne kynges duke lordes renowne accorded nat one sayth nay go helpe may iourney chyeue solycytour hercules worthy conquerour haste retenewe make towarde sparthos hath way take whiche yle grekes pertynent fully obeyeng theyr comaundement whiche pollux castor eke also worthy kyng myghty brother two wereas fynde tyme gouernours bare theyr crowne lyke noble werreours brothren also eleyne poetes lyketh feyne iubiter deyte vpon dyane begat thre beaute dyde excelle eleyne lyke bokes telle conceyued tyndarys yle vnto londe ioynynge cecyle therfore fynde yle called tyndarys theyr byrthe lyste endyte forthe thynke hercules wryte hath besought noble k g twayne myghty hande theyr besy payne oonly graunte hym wende troye warde shortly ende assente saye nat one nay power catche may agayne tyme hym lyste assygne hercules cherefull benyngne thanked hym behyght forthe wente haste myght towarwe messene stronge myghty londe within whiche noble kynge fonde knyghtly man worthy thelamon lorde prynce regyon armes one manlyest lyue egall beste whan knewe hercules come oye hath hym armes e receyued maner thynge lyke sat worthy kynge whan wyste sothely mente without anone dyde assente hym gone troyens greue hercules goodly toke leue hym enhasteth thesalye agayne pelleus telleth hym certayne hath spedde besechynge hym also haste may sende letter lordes call assemble worthy knyghtes thorugh lande nygh ferre suche knewe expert werre also counsayle sage wyt ronne age force without experyence whan manhode mente sapyence consydereth may double auayle longe haue vsed trauayle lyke playnely suppose may helpe moste iourney dispose vnto age experyence wytte youthe force hardynesse sytte whan bothe one entent fully accorded worke assent quarell grounded vpon ryght thorugh helpe grace hath treble myght nat drede spere wt shelde knyghtly wyse holde felde knyghthode fame glorye armes conquest victorye nat assured vpon multytude manhode grace lyste conclude therfore lete v auenge wronge firste ryght make selfe stronge force manly shewe knyghtes chose taken fewe deuoyde encombraunce nombre shall foe beste encombre hercules hath sayde kynge pelleus right well apayde hym thought cousayle right gode hercules without abode great haste meyne gon aprouynce called phylon whiche duke noble fame fynde nestor name full renowmed stronge chyualrye eke full nye allye hercules blode whan playnely vnderstode purpose hole cause comynge graunted hym without tariynge go hymselfe hym vyage worthy baronage redy agayne certayne daye hercules faste euer maye repayred home thesalye gadred hooly nauye lordes full redy apparayled well enarmed rychely vytayled pelleus hath taken firste see euery lorde lyke degree shypped redy gon hercules also iason theyr behestes manly fulfylle towardes troye cyte spylle sothely fynde nat abyde vpon wynde phow iason hercules prynces grece toke theyr shyppynge go destroye cyte troye ca viii whan sote stormes aprylle vnto roote full lowe gan distylle lusty lycoure many holsome shoure reyse vertue vpon floure phebus ascendynge spere brest smote bemes clere ram full coleryke halowynge veer equynoxiall whan may kalendes entre sothe zephyrus full ageable smothe tendre brauches enspyreth doth sprynge euery busshe lusty blossomynge hylle water reuolued snowes whyte phebus hath dissolued bawme vapoureth vp lofte eyre herbes softe rote vertue wt colde wynter hydde hath hole myght forse kydde erthe herbe euery tree shade braunches humydytee areysed oonly sonnes hete moysture raynes swete whan syluer welles shedeth theyr stremes ryuers gylte sonne bemes hadde newe grene agayne hir lyner shad vpon euery playne nyghtyngalys wooed ronge full amorously welcomed songe lusty season fresshe desyrous namely hertes amerous see calour blaundysshynge trouble wynde wawy bollynge tempest sure escape season grekes forth shape towardes troye erles duke kynges shyppes stuffed al maner thynges werre myght moste auayle right anone began sayle whan redy without abode eche shyppe water rode whan wynde theyr luste gan blowe ioye se go rowe whiche made faste hast theyr waye shorte tyme come ben troye hauen called symeonte whan phebus fer vnder theyr orysonte westred men ne myght hym se grekes escaped peryll see caste theyr ancres thought beste theyr shyppes nyght reste morowe whan larke songe worthy grek maly stronge began lande haste myghte troye grounde theyr tentys pyght afore towne great dylygence ne founde maner resystence whyle sette good awayte euery syde leste deceyte tyll houre sonne bryghte hadde morowe shade rody lyghte amyd felde vpon euery tente whiche tyme one assente grekes assembled euerychon byddynge kynge anone iason firste hym hercules many worthy beynge pres ben ten e pelleus come whan lordes ogyder place met eche degre set pelleus whan al whyste styll began ryght thus declare wyll noble worthy hye estate lowe whose knyghtly fame thrugh world yknow reported fer shyneth sonne grekes yet neuer thynge begonne ne hadde victorye ende lawrer fer men may wende crowned ben toke hande suche theyr happe se lande pwherfore ye lord moste worthy renowne ye remembre kynge lameoow e wronge vpon rought whan harme hym none ne thought whiche muste quyt shortly ende come stroye shende wherfore anone haste may lete v set without delay firste rede take hede thynges thre moste helpynge nede pfirste aduyse good discrecion defence sauacion prudently wardes make none oures myscheif take ylke daye lacke prouydence seconde dylygence myght hole entencion laboure full destruccion four foe owne glorye thirde may victorye reioyse platly laste ye maye afore well caste knyghthod thorugh hardynesse may venquysshe shal hyerychesse conquere possessiowne knowen troye towne plente shalbe founde golde treasour passyngly habounde shyppes sothly wene receyue ne shall nat mow sustene habundaunce yonder within cyte wyn god v graunte wyll pand also faste kynge styll noble knyght stronge hercules presence worthy pres sayd counsayle hyghly comende wyse begynnynge preysed ende effect purpose brynge counsayle mornynge tofore discured ben daye v arme haste maye felde payne deuyde mayne twayne tone shall kynge thelamowne gouernour hye renowne kynge pelleus shall haue gouernaunce wysely saue myselfe iason brother shall secretly go vnder cyte sonneshynes busshayle thycke vynes shall v hyde kepe v full koye lamedon kynge troye anone may espye grekes chyualrye cyte wyll issue anone fyghte venge hym fone whan cometh shyppes warde nestor duke shall firste warde mete hym castor shall also whan seeth tyme knyghtly haue ado helpe nestor nede thirde warde pelleus shall lede whyles ye thus hym occupye iason shall v faste hye cyte vnwyst echone doute nat shall wynne anone dothe counsayle wyll auayle trouthe ye may nat fayle conquere cyte yonder afore ye gete accorde wt al theyr stregth myght arme stele shone full bryght agayne sonne morowe whan ryseth wrought fully hercules deuyseth phow grekes armed vpon morowe fought troyens discomfyte toke theyr cyte distroyed capitulo ix lamedon whan herde tell comyng h lyst leger dwell went many noble knyght flourynge youthe desyrous fyght tho myght armes bere coude sho e durste handell spere whan assembled felde eueryche armes depeynt vpon shelde brouded bete vpon coote armure lamedone besy cure set inordre wardes maketh felde forthe way taketh towarde grekes lyneryght fully purposynge abyde fyght nat ware behynde nat aduerteth casteth mynde great sleyghte trecherye hym shape coude nat espye forthe went wardes set grekes anone hym hath met herte bolde astoned nat alle duke nestor firste sturdy walle whose manhod neuer founde lacke full knyghtly vpon hors backe herte men knyghtes eke gan prese many worthy greke lamedon sturdely mete whiche tyme felte full vnswete pand frountell ful many manly man sharpe speres firste togyder ran swerdes sharpe kene grounde thylke daye gyuen many wounde mette vpon euery syde thrugh plate mayle theyr woud bled wyde basenettes ryue crowne noyse stroke eyre gan sowne blode shad newe grene soyle chaunged hath dyed playnly reed vpon whiche full many man lay deed many worthy lost lyfe certaynly mortall stryfe grekes hadde discomfyted echone ne castor socoured anone troye manly haue bore many knyght grekes lore whan castor entreth batayle knyghtes sore dyde assayle worthy troyans spere shelde grekes agayne recouerde haue felde many one lyeth slayne grene gyrt thorugh body wt sharpe speres kene troye mortall stoure dryue backe tyll came socoure haste worthy lamedowne whiche entrede lyke wood lyowne made waye vpon euery syde made swerde glyd deth manly hym bare well vnneth none dare abyde stroke rydynge vp downe made waye aboute hym enuyrowne renges hath foen sought day armes meruailes hath wrought manhod worthynesse grekes hath brought suche distresse swerde fledde deth mercyles many sleeth whiche slaughter grekes confuse tyll pelleus came theyr rescuse irous wood fall rage thought wolde great pompe aswage troye dyde one vnhorseth many one felly slough stode hym aforne many harneys hath day torne made sheldes ryue sondre beholde wondre tyll lamedone people sawe go backe pelleus brought wracke wherof herte felte full great payne besechynge repayre agayne kythe theyr myght lyke men endure felde made recure tyll duke nestor knewe lamedowne amyd felde kynge troye towne right anone without abode agaynst hym full great pase rode whan kynge dyde hym firste espye hye dispyte rancour enuye knyghtly wyse gan tourne agayne thynge agast hye disdayne irous herte enbolled pryde hor fyersly gan take syde tyll ranne rede blode nestor lyke woode rode anone spere brake full knyghtly kept hors bake full delyue ly hym agayne quyte w th spere full sharpe whette byte thorugh sheld brest gaue hym woude fro hors felde h downe groude whiche falle kynge thynge ferde ro e hym vp drewe swerde angre fret hym herte rote vnhorsed fyghte muste fote wherof party full confuse tyll one cedar came rescuse made knyght selfe yere yonge fresshe lusty noble chere syttynge tyme noble stede whan gan take hede sawe kynge fote myscheif fyght gan pryke haste myght towarde nestor spere hymhytte sadell made hym f ytte downe grounde afore kynge lamedon anone lyke champion recured vp hym selfe diffendeth many stroke eche spendeth sharpe swerdes kene byte eueryche gan foyne smyte tyll lamedone dispytous chere face rased viser force one smet ryche cercle basenet large perle goynge enuyrowne creste fyersly bete downe whyles nestor thus afore hym stode face depeynt blode certaynly sothe conclude hadde nat grekes great multytude rescued hym lamedowne beslayne faste bore downe vnto erthe amonge hors f te castor thought ne wolde lete helpe byhelde fere irously toke myghty spere cedar spake late gan ryde prycke great hate came toke hym douteles troyan knyght called segnerides cosyn cedar whan hath sene courser rode anone bytwene spere smote castor stroke brake euen two castor without areste hath spere amyddes breste segnerides gyue mortall wounde lykly neuer sounde wherfore cedar caughte suche enuye anone melancolye despyte boylynge herte segnerides whan sawe smerte maugre grutcheth amyddes felde myght castor toke shelde thorugh vyser rancour rage wounded hym amyddes vysage hors fro hym also caughte squyer manfully raughte certaynly stode suche disioynt worthy castor poynt haue taken troye tho fote hym must haue go ne hadde pollux many manly knyght mo vii hondred stele armed bryght rather come castor rescewe whiche soregan sewe maugre castor whan fonde force toke hym fro theyr honde hors restored hym agayne pollux certayne anger feruent ire agayne troyens rancour set fyre one vpon sette mode fortune mette troyan knyght called elyatus armes yonge fresshe desyrous wonder semely tendre age kynges sone also cartage neuewe eke vnto lamedon whan pollux hath lyke fyers lyon without routhe pyte mercy renges slayne cruelly lamedone whan gan take hede inwarde dole felte herte blede whan hym sawe euen vpon dethe full pytously yelde vp brethe vpon playne lay hym beforne whiche anone made sowne horne whiche tyme came full ryche araye seuen knyght haste maye vpon dethe auenged whiche mercyles great cruelte grekes haue grounded lyeth one dede another wounded myght haue take mortally made go abake gan tourne theyr confusion fynally day lamedon tryumphe hadde felde gone saue ala towne anone vnto kynge came messangere hath hym tolde full pytous chere grekes haue cyte take pthan se wo dyde make wolde haue made pytous herte blyue dole sondre ryue sore gan within hym selfe morne wyste nat partye may torne weer abydynge longe afore hym sawe myghty grekes stronge cyte another hoost behynde almoste wo went mynde sodeynly bakwarde behelde towarde cyte sawe come felde firste hercules hym iason theyr sleyghte wonne towne pand haste cruell hercules myghty gyaunt force pereles lyke lyon wood despytous tygre rage furyous gan newe troye assayle swerde perce plate mayle whiche labour full mate feynt longe fyghte werynesse atteynt came lusty fresshe grene force myght nat sustene rode amonge yonder cruell wyse seuered sonder put hooly hye myschaunce reule gouernaunce kynge oppressed dole wardes destytute sole myscheif left infortunat comforte fully disconsolat hercules despytous loke sharp spore stede felly toke cruelly rode lamedowne erthe fyersly bare hym downe vpon hym haste myght downe hors sodeynly lyghte myghtely rent basenette swerde sharp grounde whette smote hede none grace caste forthe selfe place amonge hors cruell vyolence without pyte reuerence arage raughte hors agayne lyke alyon rennynge playne baredowne sloughe came weye many troyan day made deye lyke shepe skatered wyde destytute gouernour guyde ne rede shortly conclude grekes double multytude gan enchace dethe full blyue well vnneth lefte none lyue felde haue victours tryumphe lyke conquerours cyte toke theyr waye ende downe bothe spa ce rafter treasour rychesse towne toke anone theyr possessy owne euer grutche lefe lothe founde playnely wt gothe temple dyde great offence goddes doynge reuerence spoyle without drede fere vnto shyppe euery thynge bere yles croked olde lame werdes made cruelly tame child soukynge theyr moders breste murdre sle without areste yonge maydens wepynge distresse gentyll borne great fayrenesse ladde may nat excuse fresshe beaute falsly mysuse waste brenne consume without brake downe wall exyone kynges doughter dere hym passyngly entere lyfe meane lamedon meke benyngne condycion hercules hath anone hir take drede pyteously gan quake delyuered vnto wne firste towne gyfte receyued hath gree bycause surmountynge beautee tretyde hir wolde lyke kynges doughter sholde sythe gat hir day victorye worshyp owne glorye hauynge regarde hir hye degree shulde rather knyghtly honestee knyghthode haue wedded hir therfore blode gentyll bore wan false luste agayne goodlyhede hir beaute hir womanhede dishonestly synfull wyse royall blode nat lyke hye empryse doctryne nature ryght lyke nurture gentyll knyght consydred firste hir byrthe hir kynrede hir grene youthe hir maydenhede good fayre womanly therto kynges doughter byrthe also ben name thou blame thorugh thy gouernaunce kynled full hye vengaunce hote sparke enuye thorugh ye world fyre gan multeply whiche nat lyght quenche hete ha olde brenne nat lete newe flawme taketh hede smoke drede storye hereafter shalbe knowe wha towne brent brought lowe bothe toure wall wt soyle made pleyn thynge stode myght vtterly grekes oppresse makynge waste lyke wyldernesse pfor good tresour rychesse many iewell full plesynge delyte theyr shyppes towne lede short tyme homwarde spede treasour stuffed habundaunce gode whan sawe weder stode wynde also theyr lust hadde gan sayle wt home ladde exyone many mayde moo troye grece goo saylynge forth within lytell space escaped fro see grace vnto londe aryued merely whose comynge grekes vtterly ioyfull theyr good spede specially guydo rede theyr shyppes wt golde lade wherof herte wexe wonder glade hadde well conquere fewe lorne theyr meyne thanke theyr goddes grace fall wt treasour yt haue home brought full many pore made vp nought thrugh ye lande ther habundace moche good great su ysaunce wyghte amonges nede many day blessydfull lyfe lede frome yere yere reuoluciowne theyr manhode theyr hye renowne theyr honour ran rounde worlde aboute offende many lande hath doute theyr knyghthode wyse pand tyll storye lyste agayne deuyse manere ferther procede fauour goodlyhede wyll reste lytell space vp borne wt supporte grace accomplysshe vndertoke ende firste boke make quakynge hande drede fere shall rede lyste ye ala hasty mocyon ne wyll nat haue compassyon pyte routhe vpon rudenesse lowly besechynge gentylnesse mercy oonly bothe nyghe ferre ye fynde fayle erre correcte ye ferther flytte grace hooly commytte lydgate complayneth hym fortune firste dystruccyon cyte troye begynneth seconde boke folowynge mater sayde storye capitulo x enuyous ordre fortunat meuyge worldly thynge false flykerynge ne wyll nat suffre v psent lyfe reste without werre stryfe blynde fykell vnstable hir course false full mutable sytte hyest downe hym enclyne leest weneth brynge hym ruyne ay e gladly ben sodayne hir face parted twayne shewe moost hole whan leest tryste tha well hym hir disceytes wyste engynes hir trappes knewe euery daye hir courte newe whiche sothe well afferme dare mortall man may lyfe beware vneuen peysynge balaunce countrefete fayned countenaunce lokynge playne chere flaterye vnwarely blere mannes eye hym begyle sothe face blandysshynge smothe wha hath hym fro hye degre brought lowe full falsly smyle make hym mowe yet somwhyle moost varyaunt hewe vnto pretendeth trewe whylom fauourable false deceyuable reyse one brynge another downe false lady transmutaciowne gyueth renowne victorye dothe floure honour glorye apayre false fame gyltles put man blame goodly benyngne disdayne also malygne agayne another make hym lowte lowe theyr see kynges throwe auayle theyr hye toures plonge worthy emperours hylle hye prosperyte vale aduersyte ryche emporysshe rancoure disdayne pore enhaunce agayne false goddesse hir eyen blynde set one afore nother gothe behynde dothe one renne nother halte one rychesse hye exalte nother plonge pouerte man may haue sykerte sugre hony distylleth botell fylleth bytter galle myrre ale thus lady wylfull recheles frowarde peruers hath hir seler drynkes dyuers fraude falla mynystreth pyment bawme ypocras sodaynly whan soote paste custome gyue hym caste conclude falsly fyne bytter eysell egre wyne corrosynes fret perce depe narcotykes cause men slepe thus hir approche swete bytter broche hir reygne quene varyaunce whose ioye fyneth alway myschaunce trusteth hir wyll hym ouer caste hym deceyue playnly laste estate euer double lady mut abylyte se example kynge lamedon hath brought confusion lytell cause athynge nouthe hir cruelte hath dere bought wherfore rede euery man take hede gynne quarell nede lytell fyre vnder asshes reke may kyndled wyll breke suche flawme men may nat pea beste suffre shall haue ease therfore ye kynges lordes euerychone make myrour lamedone well ware vyolence vnto straungers whan none offence whan come fer regyon ne suffre nat none oppressyon boundes haue wronge owne though ye stronge myghty eke amonge lyeges alle nother daye perauenture may falle whan ye full lytell thynke sodayne case ye may quyt thanked nother place auenture ye happe pace therfore whan ye may suche espye doo good chere curtesye prudently consyder wyt lorde gentyllesse syt euery straunger goodly hym haue thyng may honour saue refresshe frely disporte may good hym reporte whose cotrarye hath moch wo wrought afore tyme well sought firste troy vtterly destroyed people sorowe wo cloyed lad exyle fer fro theyr cyte lyuynge thraldome captyuyte exyone ye haue herde telle lad grece thelamon dwelle guydo teche take great vengaunce wreche eyther parte trouthe moche routhe boke ye maye rede ceryously ye lyste take hede gladly aye reuolusion fatall thynge disposicion enuyous alway meynt wo worlde go truely may aduerte thought value thynge nought mortall cause werres firste begonne stryfe debate vnder sonne meued firste smale occasion caused great confusion noman harmes halfe endyte cause dere inough myte eche redy destroye man lytell wyll stryue brother blode vnkynde whiche greatly drede ala ne wyll take better hede olde troye newe thorugh small encheson trouthe knewe fynally brought distruccion olde bokes make mencion many worthy many noble knyght slayne felde dute e fyght kynges prynces sege dede whan attropos breke theyr lyues threde tell myscheif wo wante connynge fele also penne quake tremble honde lyste lorde dradde see londe whose worthynes thrugh ye world doth sprede makynge rude shall beholde rede whiche colour full naked bare grace spare disdayne lyste haue pyte fere tremble shulde se pbut onely mercy yt doth herte enbrace byd presume fully grace seynge hym moste vertuous gode mercy anexed vnto royall blode prynce longeth nyghe ferre aye tofore right pyte preferre thorugh supporte hye noblesse sowpowayled wyll style dresse wryte forth storye newe troye ordre ceryously myn auctour latyn guydo wryt prayeng reder worde myssyt causynge metre halte lame correcte saue fro blame lete hym wayte curyosyte syth ryme englysshe hath scarste dull certayne ne folowe guy clerke coryous man whiche latyn hath rethoryke set wordes nat lyke sewe style translacion worde worde lyke construccion maner gramaryens lyke style rethorycyens toke nat storye translate clyo came late suche crafte hath great experyence leue wordes folowe sentence trouthe metre sette also syde art hadde tho guyde reduce whan went wronge toke none hede nouther shorte longe trouthe lefte euryosyte bothe makynge metre nat purposynge moche varye dyuers contrarye vnto guydo discordaunce conforme fully substaunce oonly menynge conclude one ne way gone sewe floures eloquence peyntynge haue none excellence sondry hewes noble fresshe gay ryche colour byggen ne may muste procede sable blacke ennewynge ye fynde lacke axe mercy fro twynne fauour wyll anone begynne haste style forth dyrecte erre praye correcte tyme whan yt troye towne destroyed kyng lamedowne also slayne thorugh cruelte hercules vnder eyte sone storye telleth v whiche heyce called pryamus wonder manly discrete prudente whiche tyme troye absent whan fader loste lyfe tyme ecuba wyfe sone aboute castell lay knyghtes gete may hath myghtely werreyed fader haue falsly disobeyed vnto hym rebell wonder longe pryam wt saute huge stronge hadde assayled ofte many sythe strengthe lyke knyght kythe gete armes worshyp honour daunte lyke conquerour caste hym fully departe day day lyfe gan iuparte theyr walles preue myght many baron many worthy knyght yet hadde yonge lusty blode age flowrynge knyghthode assautes suche maner stryfe firste auntre lyfe herte men hym lyste nat behynde drede dethe sothly fynde afore castell hye thycke walled wyfe ecuba called pryam full worthy degree fyue sone yonge doughters three whiche eldest ector called whiche also fer phebus compas naturell daye goth cercle aboute fer hym without doute reported renowne name worthynesse noble fame lyke bokes hym specefye roote stocke chyualrye knyghthod soueraygne floure sour welle worshyp honoure manhod dare well expresse example myroure hye prowesse gynnynge grounde yfere wonder benygne lowely chere discrete also prudent vertuous dedes actes meruaylous remembred ben longe gone alone excelled euerychone olde auctours rede ye may fynde knyghthod yet make mynde nexte brother called parys nature gaue herdeuys shap fourme beaute semelynesse remembre excellent fayrenesse tyme without drede passed rede eke full manly knyght moost vsed whan shulde fyght hande bere abowe suche archer man coude knowe seke bothe fer nere shotynge myght pere founde whan hadde alysaundre called also thirde sone hyghte dephebus worthy knyght chyualrous hadde armes full great renowne man hye discreciowne wyse cousayle myn auctor telleth thus pthe fourth brother called helenus sad discrete hye prudence also man great scyente renomed therwith specyall artes called lyberall expert ryght fyfte sone worthy knyght fresshe lusty yongest sayth guydo troylus men hym call manly man founde barayle desyrous fomen assayle one beste tyme founde called ector secounde manhode thorugh troye boke within werre full ofte vpon hym toke knyghthod many hye empryse storye hereafter shall deuyse boke lyke wryte virgyle poete olde full soueraynestyle kynge pryam hadde also ecuba sone two recorde virgilius one called pollyodorus pryamus grene youthe whan comynge grekes kouthe troye warde haste anone golde treasour many ryche stone sent hym forth besyde vnto kynge full great truste haue hym kepynge tyll tyme sawe conclusiowne shulde falle towne eke fyne werre wolde take vpon grekes dyde make pbut thylke kynge false couetyse treasour ye haue herde deuyse whan sawe fortune varyaunce towward pryam vnhappy chaunce lyke tyraunt murdrer also childes throte made cutte two full cruelly made men burye hym pryuely man myght treson vnderstonde besyde see depe vnder stronde sone also irede virgyle called ganymede iubyter forest hente gpon daye huntynge wente bare hym vp aboue sterres clere made hym heuen botelere eternally hym wone stede hebe owne dere sone firste doughter kynge pryamus hyght creusa sayth virgilius eneydos sothly wedded vnto eneas sayth storye eke ylke enee wonderfull natyuyte fader fynde doutles tyme called anchyses hym begat venus goddesse hir hadde suche fayrenesse neuer wyght ne coude yet se man passynge beaute storye touchyng workynge shall declare many wonder thynge great los virgyle gaue eneydos boke worshyp enee compyled hath lyke ye may se knyghthod many stronge batayle hym acheued wan itayle full longe royall towne troye brought confusiowne conquest ye lyste take hede poete ye may ordre rede armes wrought age comynge also cartage fro troyewarde lytell whyle ye may beholde virgyle another doughter also founde kynge pryam hadde byrthe seconde called cassandra full great sadnesse maner dyuyneresse eche art hadde experyence thynges futur fully prescyence tell afore shall betyde fame sprange costes wyde whiche kepte hirchaste virgynyte aye prayer honeste ladde hir lyfe deuocion rytes relygyon paganysme vsed tho sayes obseruaunces kepynge theyrlayes thirde doughter hyght pollycene yongest euer maydeclene kepte hir selfe honest hir lawe vnto tyme pirrus hath hir slawe shap fortune neuer nature wrought shap fayrer creature eke fynde noble kynge also hadde thyrty sone boke sayth mo hardy armes noble founde called sone naturall excepte none worthy knyghtes manly men echone theyr name lyste knowe shall fynde wryte vpon arowe storye eueryche begynnynge firste eldest brother whyles pryam sege laye tofore castell gete maye theraboute hath many way sought wofull tydynges vnto hym brought grekes haue take troye towne slayne fader worthy lamedowne cyte olde foundaciowne full pytously tourned vp downe worthy lordes gentyll men echone taken slayne lefte nat one lyue thorugh grekes cruelte ruyne ala theyr cyte exion owne suster dere lad exyle hir eyen clere pwherfore kynge herte stoned sorowe ne wyste sodayne wo gan hym constrayne sobbeth wepeth mortall payne thought herte wolde sonder breste hye distresse myght haue reste teeres gan hymselfe dislylle deye fynally wylle pand fortune falsly varye drery herte gan warye hym deceyuable inly cruell vnmercyable dispytous sterne face vengeable deuoyde grace enuy rage thought hath hir wreste malys hy wrought felly shewed myght worlde neuer wyght wo suppose maner age reken hir harmes damage whiche anone euer maye faste chaungeth ryche araye tryste heuy deedly face pale astoned mortall tale desyre haue dede countenaunce enclyned hede lyfe ladde cladde hym blacke sodaynely sege bracke wolde tho lenger abyde folke anone gan ryde pyteously gan hym morne towarde troye attones retourne whan hath cyte founde playne soyle euen wt grounde hye walles whylom thycke longe vere downe made stronge toures paleys pryncypall byldynge excellent royall famous ryche great nobylnesse fonde tourned wyldernesse people slayne suster ladde awaye wo ne wyste saye constreynt aduersyte harmes wyll recured tyme fully sure vpon syde recure wherfore nat sobbe wepe brest wt syghes sought full depe broken deed vysage thus ala furyous rage full pyteously hooste without respyte contynewe dayes thre tyll laste derke skyes blacke gan theyr wo partye slacke tempest delegan withdrawe theyr wepynge bladysshe gan wawe whan floode wo ouer paste ebbe ioye folowe muste haste sorowe euer wolde theyr hertes shende terme euery wo muste ende though frendes men aye wepe wayle theyr deth may recure vayle wherfore kynge care hath sought waye cyte repare caste hym fully wolde make reuerture necessyte manfully tene whan eyre gan wexe clene mystes cloudy sorowe somedele adawe gan morowe heuynesse derke nyght chaced awaye sonne bryght newe ioye aye fyne wo muste gladnesse whan sorowe go pryam certayne space whan sorowe gan lyte aud lyte pace wysdome pytous smerte gan prudently plucke vp herte eyen wawes gan clere anone wrought right ye shall phow kynge pryamus sone vnto kynge la medone buylded troye newe agayne ca xi sorowe aswaged syghes olde longe processe lyke tolde worthy kynge called pryamus herte desyrous vpon playne waste wylde stronge towne newe bylde deuyse cyte edefye shall assautes vtterly defye enmyes mortall foone ryche toures walles harde stoone aboute countres enuyron made seke euery regyon suche workemen curyous wyt inuentyfe castynge meruaylous suche coude crafte gemetrye sotyll theyr fantasye eueryche good deuysous mason hewer crafty quarreour euery wryghte passynge carpenter may founde ferre nere suche coude graue groupe kerue suche able serue lyme stone reyse walle bataylynge crestes marcyalle suche hadde konnynge theyr hede alabastre outher whyte rede marbyll graye pullysshe playne make smothe vaynes grayne sente also euery ymagour bothe entayle euery portreyour coude drawe coloure peynte hewes fresshe yt werke nat feynte suche coude wt countenaunce glade make image wyll neuer fade countrefete metall tree stoon sotyll werke pygmaleon appollo whiche bokes telle ymagerye dyde excelle crafty workynge curyous tombe made kynge daryous whiche alysaundre dyde heyght reyse oonly men shulde fame preyse conquest perce whan went thus pryam euery mayster sent eche keruere passynge ioygnyour make knottes many curyous floure sette crestes within withoute vpon wall cyte rounde aboute excellynge practyke arte called mecanyke hadde name flowrynge famous sent come pryamus pfor purposeth noble worthy kynge make cyte moost royall byloynge brode large wyde lyst assayled werre proudely aboute enbatayled firste grounde made sought full depe lowe fayle nought make sure foundaciowne place olde towne firste ybylded walles sette lande many myle mette aboute compasse make large maystres toke charge deuysed haue settynge syte holsome eyre delyte whan soyle defouled ruyne walles olde made playne lyne workemen gan cyte founde full myghtely stone square rounde worlde none lyche workemanshyp byldynge ryche crafte curyous masonrye termes speke gemetrye wherfore muste sette asyde douteles radde neuer enclyde mayster foundour worke quare compas kepe theyr measure leuell lyne rude clerely diffyne discryue werke euery part lacke termes longynge arte dare well trouthe afferme world ne neuer pere vnto cyte wryte sothe boke mayster guydo dothe myght prosperyte hye honour felycyte assaute perpetuelly contune reysed worshyp neptune named troye forne lyke firste thorugh grekes lorne lengthe shortly conclude thre dayes iourne lyke latytude neuer herde make mencion suche nother foundacion huge compase suche largesse counte passynge fayrenesse edefyed iusty syghte rede walles hyghte two hondred cubytes marbyll graye magecolled without lautes assaye make pleasaunt delyte amonge marbyll alabastre whyte meynt walles rounde towne make shewe within without fresshe ryche delectable alone comparable cytes mortall man sawe euer yet sythe worlde began corner euery walle sette crowne golde ryche stone frette shone full bryght agayne sonne shene euery toure bretexed clene chose stone nat fer sondre beholde wondre therto cyte compassed enuyrowne hadde gate vi entre towne firste strengest eke largest also moste pryncypall myghty byldynge alone pereles kynge called dardanydes storye lyke founde tymbria named seconde thirde called helyas fourthe gate hyghte also cetheas fyfte troiana syxth anthonydes stronge myghty bothe werre pe square toures set euery syde whose corner pompe pryde workemen haue sterne fell vysages ryche entayle sette vp great ymages wrought stone yt neuer lyke fayle full curyously enarmed batayle thorugh walle theyr fomen lette euery toure great gonne sette assautes sodayne auentures tourette reysed vp fygures wylde beestes beres lyon tygres bore serpentes dragon hertes eke theyr brode horne olyfauntes large vnycornes bugle bulles many great gryf forged brasse coper laton cruelly sygnes theyr face vpon theyr foon made felle menace barbycans bul werkes huge afore towne made hye refuge nede erely eke late portekoles stronge euery gate nede nat none assaylynge charge locke thycke brode large gate bryght bra within myghty shyttynge stronge iren barres square rounde great barres pytched grounde huge cheynes forged diffence whiche ne wolde breke vyolence harde thorugh wynne euery hous bylded within euery paleys euery manstowne marbell thorughout towne crafty byldynge workynge moste royall hyghte euery walle sixty cubytes grounde accounted none yt hath surmounted cyte one heyghte alyche sothe bothe pore ryche harde hye estate lowe hous paleys sonder knowe egally tymbre stone theyr house reysed euerychone shulde reherse korue knottes craste masonry fresshe enbowyge wt verge right lynes housynge full bakewynes ryche koynynge lusty tablementes vynettes rennynge casementes though termes englysshe wolde ryme reken haue tyme ne langage pycked none sotyll ioynynge tell stone put stede mortere ioyntoures coper gylte full clere make ioyne leuell lyne amonge marbyll fresshely shyne agaynst sonne whan shene lyght smote golde burned bryght make werke glystre euery syde towne stretes large wyde crafte prudently prouyded werkmen sette deuyded holsome eyre amyddes myght enspyre erely morowe desyre zephyrus comfortable norysshe thynges vegetable tyme yere thorughe euery strete sugred flauour lusty swete moste plesauntly eyre gan smyte cytezeynes oonly delyte brethe recomforte whan lyste walke themselfe disporte thrugh ye towne wt crafty purueaunce great auyse discrete ordenaunce compase caste squared squyers polysshed marble vpon stronge pyllers deuysed longe large wyde frontell euery stretes syde fresshe alures lusty hye pynacles moustrynge outwarde ryche tabernacle vouted aboue lyke reclynatoryes called deambulatoryes men walke togyders twayne twayne kepe drye whan dyde rayne saue fro tempest wynde thundre lyst shroude themself ther vndre euery hous couered leede many gargoyle many hydous heede spoutes thorugh pypes aughte stone werke canell taughte voydynge fylthes lowe grounde thorugh grate perced yron perced tounde stretes paued bothe lengthe brede cheker wyse stone whyte rede euery crafte maner man lande deuyse reken kynge pryamus hye discreciowne ordeyned hath dwelle towne stretes seuered yonder eueryche set sonder myght comodyte eche hymselfe werke lyberte goldsmythes firste ryche iewelleres themfelfe crafty browdereres weuers also wollen lyn clothe golde damaske satyn veluet sendell dowble samyt eke eueryche clothe men lyste seke smythes also coude forge wele pollaxes swerdes speres sharpe stele dartes dagger mayme wounde quarethedes sharpe square ygrounde also crafty armerers bowyers faste fletcher suche coude make shaftes playne eke dyde theyr besy payne werre make also trappures bete baners royall cote armures deuyse standardes penounse felde fresshe gay getounse euery crafte may rekened tell shortly cyte thorughe towne soryche excellent myddes large ryuer went causynge full great comodyte whiche twayne hath parted cyte ofcours full swyfte wt fresshe stremes clere hyghte xamtus guydo doth v lere rede vpon flode eche syde many mylle stode wha nede theyr grayne corne grynde susteyne storye fynde ryuer eke fysshe full plenteous deuyded werkmen curyous craftely thorugh castynge souerayne cours stremes myght attayne areche guydo doth comecte archys stronge cours reflecte thorugh condyte pypes large wyde withall certayne meanes artyficiall made full purgacion ordure fylthes towne wasshynge stretes stode arowe gutter erthe lowe cyte fylthe sene canell scoured clene deuoyded secrete wyse man myght espye deuyse engyne sylthes fer nere borne awaye cours ryuere couertly euery thynge couered wherby towne vtterly assured engendrynge corrupcion wycked eyre infexion cause ofte theyr vyolence mortalyte great pestylence example flode made cybre rome wrought eneas whiche also departeth rome two myn auctour sayth note enhabyte royall chefe cyte kynge pryam hath aboute countre made serche hole entent prouynces adiacent borowes townes smale vyllages ygadred maner age thropes folkes full dyuers suche vacaunt dyspers aboute troye regiowne made hath entre towne great multitude yonge olde enhabyte ye haue herde tolde afore hym foreynes hath troye made cyteseynes full discretly lyke founde whan gan people abounde pkynge pryamus hye affecciowne buyldynge myghty towne hath herte caught fantasye newe cyte magnefye put remembraunce caste fully obseruaunce myghty mar sterne ferse hewe specially certayne playes newe hors foote many sondry wyse gyue men knyghthode excersyse eueryche put assay iustes boordes also tournay preue theyr force whan happe mete whiche playes fouded firste crete lande hye lowe estate martys honoure dedycate paleste wake nyght playes men assaye myght oonly foote many sotyll poynt naked enioynt wynne pryse dyde full entent founde clerkes full prudent chesse playe moste gloryous whiche sotyll meruaylous harde mater discryue though man studyed lyue shall aye fynde dyuerse fantasyes wardes makynge newe iupartyes great dyuersyte firste founde cyte durynge sege lyke sayth guydo iacobus de vitriaco coutrarye oppynyon lyke maketh mencyon affermeth fully aduyse philometer phylosopher wyse vnto kynge stynte crueltee fonde firste play made caldee grece then sent also troye great auysement playe founde firste dyce table castynge chaunces deceyuables haue cause ofte great debate one nowe founde fortunate wynne whyle fauoure chaunce ware sodayne varyaunce vnhappely put backe nother stode vpon wracke losse plonged distresse reysed haue vnto hye rychesse gladnesse one nother rage deuaunt hasarde passage one haue ioye another suffreth wo lyke bone ronne fro hondred sythe daye varye blandysshynge contrarye man assured ioye firste also rede troye songe red many fresshe comedyes dytees called tragedyes declare shortly sentence bothe two fynall difference pa comedye hath gynnynge pryme face maner complaynynge afterwarde endeth gladnesse dedes oonly doth expresse suche pouerte plonged lowe tragedye lyste knowe begynneth prosperyte endeth euer aduersyte also doth conqueste treate ryche kynges lordes greate myghty men olde conqueroures whiche fraude fortune shoures ouer caste whelmed theyr glorye whylom thus halowed memorye tragedyes bokes make mynde whan red songe fynde pin theatre smale auter amyddes sette halfe circuler whiche est custome directe vpon whiche pulpet erecte therin stode auncyent poete reherse rethorykes swete noble dedes hystoryall kynges prynces memoryall olde worthy emperours great empryse eke conquerours gate martes hye honoure lawrer grene fyne theyr laboure palme knighthod disserued olde date parchas made passe fate pand chere face pale style enclyned gan tourne tale synge theyr loo full mortally stroke antropos tell also theyr worthy hede sodayne brekynge theyr lyues threde pytously made theyr mortall ende thrugh false fortune yt world wyll shende fyne theyr worthynesse endede sorowe hye trystesse compassynge fraude false treason sodayne murdre vengeaunce poyson conspyrynge fretynge false enuye vnwarly dyde dye theyr renowne theyr hye fame hatrede sodaynly made lame theyr honour drough vnto declyne myschefe theyr vnhappy fyne fortune vnswete tolde red poete whyle pulpet stode dedely face deuoyde blode syngynge dytees mus rent amyd theatre shrowded tent cam men gastfull theyr cheres diffygured theyr face vyseres playeng sygnes people syght poete songe hath heyght maner discordaunce wene dytees theyr countenauce pfor lyke lofte dyde expresse wordes ioye heuynesse menynge benethe playeng poynt poynt alway answeryng triste glade heuy lyght face chaunged sodayne syght craftely coude transfygure conformynge chaunce plure synge sodaynly wepe well coude theyr obseruaunces kepe done apryll may whan blosmes newe bothe busshe hay floures fresshe gynne sprynge byrdes wood synge luste supprysed somer sonne whan playes troye begonne theatre halowed yholde thus ryte tragedyes olde pryamus worthy kynge began mater tell bvt wyll forth storye wryte mater boystously endyte pryamus passynge dylygent right desirous wardly feruent myght amonge werkes alle bylde paleys ryche halle whiche shulde chose chefe dungyon royall see souerayne mansyon whan gan werke approche made bylde hye vpon roche assure foundacion called noble ylion syght whiche iustly circuler compase cast rounde sper wold content ye grounde truely acounte place rounde theatre firste muste entre takynge ye lyne yt kerueth thorugh centre gemetrye longeth art trebled seuenthe part fynde myght experyence measure hole circumference lande also playnly eke conteyned within stronge wall creste whiche lowest hadde heyghte full syxe hondred pa bylded marbyll full royall full stronge many ryche stone amonge whose toures reysed vp hye raughte almoste lkye werke whiche man myght amende lyste greces vp assende myght se inspeccyon boundes many regyon prouynces stode rounde aboute walles within withoute endlonge knottes grauen clene depeynt asure golde cynopre grene veryly whan sonne shone vpon golde meynt amonge stone gaue lyght withouten phebus doth mydday spere worke wyndowe eke fenestrall wrought beryle clere crystall pand amyddes ylyon fresshe ryche foundacyon whiche clerkes yet theyr bokes prayse kynge pryam made halle rayse excellynge beaute strengthe latytude accordynge lengthe marbyll outwarde walle tymbre moste noble specialle halfe cedre reherse remenaunt ryche eban whiche moste able dare specefye stone ioyne crafte carpentrye tymber haue soueraynte tell eban tree lyke bokes sothely fynde cometh ethyope ynde blacke geete wyll wexe anone whan korue harde stone euermore laste endure nat corrupte water moysture halle diffyne stone square leuell lyne paued great dilygence masonrye passynge excellence aboue reysed see full curyously stone perre called chefe pryncipall reygne sete moste royall fore whiche sette great delyte borde eban yuery whyte egally yioyned clene werke ryfte sene sessyouns made euery syde oonly estate ordre deuyde eke halle couenable eche partye dormaunt table yuery eke eban tree euen agayne kynges royall se partye therto contrayre reysed many crafty stayre hye halle syte right lyne opposyte pured metall stone clere brede lengthe full ryche autere whiche stode fygure vysage massy fe golde wonderfull ymage honoured hye sete oonly honour iubyter grete pand statute huge heyghte fyftene cubytes complet heyghte crowne golde hye vpon heede heuenly saphyres many ruby rede fret enuyron stone ynde amonges medled fynde whyte perles massyfe large rounde chefe dirkenesse confounde carbuncle kynge stone alle recomforte glade halle enlumyne blacke nyght fresshenesse rody lyght value therof inestymable rychesse playnly comparable ymage dyuysion shap proporcion heed fote maysterly entayled apoynt workman hath nat fayled parfourme crafty excellence pryamus drede reuerence honoured hath aboue goddes alle myschefe hym clepe calle hym hole affeccion soueraygne truste deuocion hope also affyaunce helthe ioye assuraunce welfare prosperyte hath comytted deyte wenynge herte wonder sykerly assured myschefe therby diffended eche aduersyte holde reygne hye felycyte honour contynuelly shyne whyle iubyter thorugh power dyuyne hym hath proteccion truste full opynyon thus werke fynally achyeued wherof pryam ioye full releued cyte noble ylyon hath fully brought vnto perfeccyon lyke entent whan began thus pryam kyge worthy man full many day newe troye lyeges lad lyfe ioye hym leue royall sete soueraygnely reygnynge quyete procedynge forthe ye lyste vnto effect anone matere phow kyg pryamus sent anthenor ito grece haue suster exyone agayne ca xij hateful harme dred kyndled solonge osparke old hatred roote debate grounde enuy newe flawme hertes fyre grayne malys causer offence francour rusted impacience whiche hast newe made festred sore sinerte whan thou art one raked herte whiche disdayne mercy mayst lete man whyle lyue equyte deluest vp malys many folde debate newe buryed olde falsly quykest stryues restore enuyous serpent slayne yore whiche felly hath addre enuyous reste awaked pryamus venym persynge ylle made hym wery lyue tranquylle meued hym iniquyte vpon grekes auenged pea helde reygne lyeges ioy souereygne without anoye perturbaunce serpent hath newe remembraunce without aduyse discrete areste hoote flawme kyndled breste olde enuye fresshe rancour meynte lykly neuer queynte pryam nowe entenciowne caste compasseth reuoluynge vp downe howe stronge rychesse meyne howe noble myghty also cyte habundaunt shortly conclude bothe plente multytude men armes chyualrye whiche stered hym haue fantasye ala whyle vnhappy chaunce deed take wyll vengeaunce vpon foon fyre hoote enuye brent hym warde malencolye stondynge purpose yt man chauge may damage auenged day miuryes yt hym haue wrought whan tyme sought purpose moste conuenyent anone hath lordes sent knyghtes called euerychone come haste excused nat one namely hye degre obeyeng humylyte byddynge hooly made delay come echeone agayne certayne day sone also present ector except tyme absent stronge myghty regyon panomye whiche subieccyon kynge pryam helde thorugh worthynesse amende thynges redresse ector gone panomye certayne cause iustefye reason thought beste sette quyete reste aye iuste prudent well aduysed pacyent demened gouernaunce hym lothe vengeaunce myght easy wyse treate reforme thynges smale greate lothe noble worthy knyght haste execute ryght causeles rygour condempne whyle full worthy solempne kynge pryamus lordes great small within troye helde court royall lyste coste spare ceryously menynge declare see lordes enuyron gan thus shewe hertes mocyon worthy lordes present faythfull trewe herte entent nat vnknowen discrecyon great damage oppressyon whiche grekes haue vpon v wrought without cause thynge nought daye sayth late trowe newe yet date fresshe remebred mynde vnto blode ye kynde suppose foryetylnesse may put awaye mortall heuynesse harmes olde whiche aye renewe agayne memorye saye certayne trowe playnly thought euer grene ne dyeth nought haue slayne progenytours whylom noble werreours cyte brente brought vnto ruyne robbed falsly rauyne tourned wyldernesse grece caryed rychesse fader slayne hyghte lamedon without cause occasyon raught hym golde tresour whiche semeth foule errour myght right amendes well chalenge desyre v iustly reuenge afore goddes hye offence oonly reason conscyence passynge theyr mortall cruelte one thynge moste greueth vngoodly agaynst gentyllesse rewarde hauynge worthynesse byrthe ne royall blode hir fayre eke gode meane suster called exyon ala theyr confusyon difuse kepe nat lyke hir degre day day dishoneste thorugh hir honour hir name lorne consyderynge nat stok borne blynde take hede aduerte roote hir kynrede surquyde indu rate sythe hye estate ytreted lyke ye may se suppose lowe degre eouerned full dishonestly ye may thynke demetruely wyues maydens companye eke allye ynaunted vsed theyr luste grekes haue better truste ne spare nother blode age thus lyue turment seruage without touthe mercy pyte whiche toucheth well semeth equyte ryght ye oughte echone full myght wronges whiche ye offended seke awaye myght amended worke one assent procede lyke oure entent theyr malys cursed cruelte one auenged herte wyll thought one accorde ne vary nought force dowbled pouste right reason good equyte requyre vengeaunce hym doth wronge though abyde longe truste also goddes rightwysenesse shall helpe harmes redresse fauour v innocence chastyse wrought offence also ye knowe cyte stronge myghty great suerte toures hye walled werre also fer shyneth sonne sterre none lyke reken may force therto perygall ye knowe also shalbe founde chyualrye habounde expert armes olde assayed drede neuer dismayed haue plente also vytayle frendshyp eke ne wyll v nat fayle theyr myght v socour wherfore rede without soiour sette vpon sythe able tyme nowe semeth couenable manhode byd make delay venge wronge hap may differynge ofte great damage worke tyme double auauntage purpose lacketh neuer adele thorugh manhod assured wele lyste nat holde hasty rakell worke wylfully werre also stande auenture aye mart doutous eure rede firste grekes sende wyt harmes wyll amende without stryfe werre debate may sayne fortunate contrarye reason condyscende conclusion graunte askynge equyte ryght haue cause preue myght procede rygour shall offer measour fer right reason eke requere disdayne lyst nat quarell deuoyde wylfulnesse yrooted vpon sykernesse theyr great offence axe amendes firste pacyence god fortune hope wyll nat assente ende shall v nat repente better pea haue redresse gynne werre without auysenesse therfore lete v wofull auenture pacyently suffre endure porte humble playne vpon answere wyll sayn though myne entencion ymeued iuste occasion procede yre vengeaunce wyll put remembraunce lete slyde foryetfulnesse wronges voyde heuynesse towarde grekes axe wyll exyona restore v agayne whiche moste derre oonly stynte debate werre surplus mortall eure shall dissymule prudently endure harmes olde forth pacyence ye accorde vnto sentence saye vpon ye auysed sonde despysed lyste reason obeye may iustely seke nother weye haue redresse saue purpose sende anthenore whiche man discrete auysee specyally mater treate bothe wyse eloquente ye well knowe passyngly prudente whan kynge tolde tale anone counsayle consent euerychone anthenor iourney vndertake haste gan hym redy make without abode wyll nat denye take hym embassetrye well auysed discrecion toke wente informacion poynt poynt great charge hym caste stande large without errour coude gode effect full playnly vnderstode euery thynge prynted thought went forgate right nought worde caste hym nat fayle shyppe gothe began sayle short tyme companye aryued vp thesalye cyte called mynusyus fortune kynge pelleus tyme anthenor anone vnto kynge right waye gone guydo hath conceyued pryme face benyngnely receyued whan knewe cause comynge haste without taryenge authenor felle vysage shortly saye effecte message troya knyght astoned neuer adel full demure auysed wel nat hasty rakell sayne abydynge loke face playne pelleus manly chere sayde effecte right thus ye shall worthy kynge called pryamus wyse noble manly famous knyghthod passynge excellent hath firste goodly wyse sent torye royall chefe cyte full entent message shall saye wordes playne ye nat disdayne pacyently gyue audyence remembrynge firste aduertence harmes nat full longe ago wronges ye wroughte also full cruelly eke youres troye lande progenytoures iniuryes destruccion causeles without occasion ye shewed haue cruelte mercyles destroyed cyte slayne fader named lamedowne cyte brent bete downe nouther lefte paleys hous toure ladde awaye rychesse treasoure nouther spared reherse slaughter woman childe man myght none swerde asterte yet one thynge hath herte suster called exyon holde kept kynge thelamon dishonestly agayne gentrye great dishonour great vyllanye hir kynred lyke ye may se treated cherysshed lyke hir degre wherfore sythe ye wyse knyght ye oughte aduerte haue syght suche thynges iuste affeccyon consydre discrecyon gentyllesse equyte suche wronges myght amended wherfore pryam great auysenesse fully besynesse herte wyll desyreth pea reste sendeth besechynge beste ye wyll besy dylygence make hym lytell recompence may haue restytucyon thorugh knyghtly medyaryon suster without lenger space remenaunt wyll lete pace stryfe werre oonly eschewe desyreth fully sewe pea quyete hole affeccyon pursue measour reason fynally lyke ye may se occasyon werre fle consyder holde sage fyne fully message pwhan pelleus hym playnly vnderstode sodayne yre wexe herte wode loke fell furyous rancour right melancolyous ne myght attempre appease hasty fyre gan herte sease anone full despytous wyse gan pryamus threten despyse malys sette sonde nought meanes yt anthenor hath sought gan also troyan knyght menace bad haste shulde voyde place vpon peryll falle myght anone wente syght haste meynee without abode taken haue see began sayle thesalye theyr waye faste hye shorte tyme aryued vp salempne myghty stronge cyte fortune royall towne anthenor fonde kynge thelamowne paleys hath waye nome firste fynde whan come accepted vnto presence benynguely without offence exyone present tyde auenture stondynge syde reuerence hir woman hede anthenor toke better hede custome kynge thelamon hye despyte indignacyon euery troyan coude espye specially hadde enuye rancour oonly thorugh bytter rag whiche herte myght neuer aswage pacyence anthenor hath gyuen audyence whiche anone full sobre wyse tale gan shall deuyse syr quod support grace ye graunte opportune space declare cause comynge wyll reherse without taryenge mater hole breefly sentence make kouthe magnyfycence signefyeng without displeasaunce pryamus hath gouernaunce troye towne hath vnto sent faythfull menynge clene entent besechynge firste goodlyhede wronges forgete eke dede ye oonly hye noblesse equyte gentylnesse ye wyll restore exyona agayne whiche ye holde speke word playne sothe nat lyke hir estate wherfore prayeth stynte debate euery harme put memorye knyghtly honour owne glorye sende hir home make delyueraunce goodly hir without varyaunce ye haue holde many longe dayes ne taryeth natnor setteth delayes ne lete founde nowe slouthe sothfastlye great routhe recorde ye haue hir vsed may trouthe nat goodly excused shall lete lyghtly ouer slyde ye benyngnely prouyde sende hir home lyke haue sayde lo charge layde without abydynge certayne goodly answere ye wyll sende agayne pwhan thelamon herkened tale hasty yre gan wexe pale fyry coke hath hym made wode face aualed blode within herte gan frete byte loke askoye tourned vp whyte hye disdayne face despytous pale smylynge laughter furyous gan rake feble mortall fyre fretynge hate brent desyre shortly made conclusyon anthenor obieccyon sayde frende euer thou wonder greatly meruayle auenture sodayne newe thynge vnprudently meueth thy kynge vnto make suche sonde thou fole whan thou toke honde oather vnhappy infortunat brynge embassat hym haue thynge ado loke thou say hym ne aqueynted alyte thynge platly delyte shorte wordes thou lyst hym prayere ne haue ioye nouther feste right nought sothly requeste wote well whyle go troye myselfe mo reforme thynge amys thorugh offence shortly thus certayne thynge wrought lamedowne manhod wonne ye towne slewe kynge yt hym helde knyghtly wyse hym metynge felde eueryche myght se dyde entre firste cyte graunted memorye sygne oonly myne hye victorye without contradiccyon grekes haue possessyon hir moste entere exyona thou claymest well syker thyne askynge vayne truste well syker right well certayne thou getest hir nat one worde may shall firste made full great affray hir leue durynge lyue euer grutche agaynst stryue nat syttynge leue hir whylom great ado hir gat spendynge blode wrothe therwith wode wyll hir kepe shalbe founde hadde many mortall wounde troye towne hir wan good fayth ferforth shall nat lyghtly fro handes pace alone standeth grace hir beaute hir semelyhede hir bounte hir goodlyhede shall reason shortly fyne sothe moste femynyne euer sawe without drede porte connynge womanhede hath alone existence souereynte excellence pryamus ought thou canst sayne whyle lyue gete hir nat agayne hir bye many dedely wounde sharpe swerdes square speres grounde shall firste reysed suche stryfe shall coste many mannes lyfe agayne restored take forsothe thou gettest whan hym lyste may well begynne suppose shall lytell wynne none wyse tolde wotest great role holde put ferre iupartye execute embassetrye manly grekes boldly offende beware therfore sende vpon thy lyfe rancour pryde go thy way thou abyde lenger sothly syght thou wotest ye pryse yt haue hyght thou scapest nat lefe lothe anthenor anone shyp gothe sayle hym lyste nat delaye towarde yle called achaye whan taken hath londe ryuayle auenture fonde worthy kynges pollux castor right anone troyan anthenor without abode courte fare vnto message declare togydre whan present ryght thus sayde sentement noble kynge troye ryte hath vnto sent wyll besechynge full lowe maner ye lyste vnto prayer equyte condescende goodly helpe certayne wronge mende touchynge suster called exyon may haue restytucyon hir agayne discrete aduyse sythe ye manly wyse lykly oppynyon page duplicate page duplicate good medyacyon shelyghtly may agayne restored cherysshe pea vnyte wherfore prayeth wt herte entere goodly wyse deuere holde ben knyghtly sage wyll playnely surplusage wronges olde put suspence desyreth knyghtly hye prudence stynte werre noryll pe nouther rakell rekles auysed werkes caste afore shalbe fall thynges futur aduertynge ferre seeth perell werre wyll hym conforme vnto pea reste conceyueth beste euery man vnyte sewe prudently also eschewe debate eche occacyon lo fyne entencyon whiche comytte iugement castor yre inpacyent hastynesse ne myght nat abyde cruell herte swolle pryde brake anone despytous face sayde frende knowe trespace grekes dyde euer vnto thy kynge axe amendes wonder ynge v neuer dyde hym offence saue made maner recompence wronge wrought lamedon whiche firste sought occacyon agaynst grekes vngoodly wyse caused v vpon hym ryse one manly hym sette due right quyr dette lyke decrete haue hym playnly serued nothyg wrought hath disserued amendes gynneth late coueyte mortall hate vtter malys enmyte outher pea accorde vnyte effecte hereafter shall fele happe v dele bargeyn shall full dere ben abought frendshyp sothly sette nought ouer speke lykly semeth vnto pryamus loued alyte nat value suppose myte whan sent vpon message thou folye dydest great outrage take hye peryllous thynge vnto grekes brynge suche tydynge thorugh thy lyfe put iupartye counsayle fast thou hye syght lyst thou repente pand anthenor forthe shyp wente wynde gan sayle anon towarde yle called pyllyon haste whan dyde aryue shope hym forth court blyue duke nestor maner thynge housholde helde royall kynge anthenor full sad auysee tofore nestor syttynge see whan amytted sayne tale tolde full openly playne poynt poynt ye herde afore vayne reherse alway concluded hath one lyke ye herde touchynge exyone duke nestor face thynge rede hewe asshes dede fret coloure inwardly blode eche extremyte drawen downe vnto herte whiche yre sore made hym smerte gan quake euery ioynt vayne hande vnnethe may restrayne melancolye venged lyke lyon wood wrothe fer hymselfe alyenat inwardly rancour passyonat loke reuersed furyous syght tempre hymselfe vnnethes ne myght felte angre great aduersyte amyddes cruelte sodayne haste one brake euen thus anthenor spake thou quod thy wordes whyte suppose thou wyste full lyte vnto fore thou haste thy tale tolde meruayle thou arte bolde presume myne eres offende pryam proudely pretende maner tytle thy kynges name worthy grekes put blame vniustly foule hardynesse requere haue redresse iniuryes wrought amedon boldely affermynge false presumpcion vpon grekes wronges outragyous whiche myneres odyous fretynge eke bytynge sokene lyste may nat sustene herynge lo hatefull sowne ner honour hyerenowne refrayned shulde cruell wyse execute full hastely iustyce thorugh rygour mortall lawe bestes wylde firste drawe therupon thy fayned tale dismembre peces smale despyte pryamus kynge teche brynge tydynge presumptuously talys newe lorde better hym knewe shulde thy presumpcyon thy laste mede fynall guerdon without mercy lyke haue behyght haste bego syght vtterly dothe great offence vnto myn eye hauethe presence thorugh disdayne causeth myn vnreste anthenor thought beste nat holsom lenger abyde caste wysely rancour pryde beste bere hym fayre shyppe gan anone repayre haste possybylytee without abode taken hath see gan sayle homewarde faste drawe sodaynly boyle gan wawe see ryse cloudes blake appere wynde wake wonder gastfull also heuene dredfull fyre bryght leuene thonder smote tempest gan dryue maste gan soder ryue alofre poynt drowne felle weder gan frowne awayte nat vpon dethe euen poynt yeldynge vp brethe ne sawe none remedye euer amonge gan clepe crye theyr goddes auowes make deuoutly vndertake eche lyke age escape go pylgrymage lyke rytes theyr paynem wyse goddes theyr sacryfyse substaunce myght sodaynly weder derke nyght newe lyght grace gan adawe see waxe calme smothe gan wawe happe amonge euerychone tempest perysshed nat one tofore troye within sytell space aryued euerychone grace escaped safe euery ieopardye bothe anthenor companye temple toke right way prayer full longe lay many another also sake thakyng goddes yt made eskape euery peryll tempest see vnto kynge gothe lordes aboute hym full royall paleys dongyon pryncypall sat abode full solempnelye trewe reporte embassatrye knyght hath hym falle hath tolde kynge tofore lordes alle anthenor hath first made mecion tofore kynge iuste relacyon expleyt ordre wyse vncurteysly receyued kynge pelleus thretes wordes despytous suffred kynge thelamon beynge ferse wood lyon afterwarde gan also complayne despyte bretherne twayne rebuke great drede nestor dyde spede lyfe myght vnneth skape tolde gan ende make iourney eke repayre pryam fully despayre outher forte aduenture euer agayne suster recure conceyueth aduertence clere reporte experte euydence aye benygne vngoodly ayen hym malygne hym sheweth debonayre fonde agaynward cotrayre frowardly euer quyte shewynge sygnes sette lyte frenshyp ought coude aduerte wherof pure sorym herte constrayned right nede compelled iustly procede haue redresse oonly rygour profre pea myght haue fauour admytted tytle ryghtwysenesse thorugh hye despyte hasty wylfulnesse euery mene measour vayne saue oonly werre engendred disdayne begonne caused olde hatrede whiche gan anone suche bronde brede newe enuye kynges breste pryamus without areste iuly yre rancour fret disdayne sore grounde whet lese wynne vpon grekes wyll werre begynne iuparte manly knyght lyfe deth bycause hadde ryght caste hym firste nauee sende grece fomen fende lyke knyght force haunte knyghtly wyse caste hym daunte pompe grekes sturdynesse fynally theyr pryde oppresse pbut saye pryam infelycyte newe trouble hap destyne aboue hatefull influence descended vnware vyolence ue thou canste nat lyue pee sodayne sorte fortune gracelees chaunce vnhappy without auysenesse wylfull luste fonned hardynesse haue put thy soule tranquyllyte make werye thy prosperyte hast fauour bytter swete canste nat lyue pea quyete thou art trauayled wylfull mocyons ouer maystred thy passyons lacke reason hye prudence derked blynde prouydence full barayne cast afore se harmes folowynge thyne aduersyte thou slowe wysely consydere wante syght made slydere thorugh myste errour falsly forueye pathys wronge right weye voyde reason wylfull hastynesse wher thy guyde wher thy maistresse descrecyon prudent ladde vyselye shulde haue ladde trace sensualyte though full selde mannes power suffraunce hymselfe refrayne whan sodayne yre doth herte strayne thou shuldest afore better cast thy chaunce wrought counsayle nat put balaunce thy sykernesse ala dydest thou haue symuled dele thy wo caste thy chaunge well afore pryme haue forgoten wronges olde tyme thought afore thyn aduertence ofte falleth experyence whyles men moste besynesse vengeably theyr wronges redresse double harme ware falle agayne newe snare damage forgete clene false reporte rumoure fresshe grene renewed thorugh swyfte fame fleeth fer hyndre alordes name namely whan purpose wende oonly hede se nat ende pryde sodayne heete voyde themselfe quyete aduertynge nat worke auyselye prouerbe techeth comonlye stande sure enhaste hym nat meue shall hym greue walketh surely playne stumble vayne helyste folye neclygent put hym wylfullye auenture hymselfe reche eschewe peryll holde wreche sothly pryam thou rechelees comytte thy quyete pee dredefully durynge date cruell fortune fykell fate whose maner custome comonly whan man trusteth moste soueraynely goddesse blynde full vnstable hym moste deceyuable hym abate royall stalle sodaynly make hym downe falle tryp throwe hym bake gayne stryueth shall haue lytell take slyely hir gynne snare make man fro welfare hir pantre fraude englewed whan lest weneth remewed therfore man haue none affyaunce fortune hir vary aunce ne lete wyght ease iuparte lyst thou playe wyll afterwarde departe tourne chaunce outher well wo selde one doth game go ye may se example pryamus folye desyrous werke hede folowe owne wylle trouble ala calme tranquylle boke shalbe founde hym cyte platly confounde vtterly confusyon afterwarde longe successyon shalbe red storye fable remembred dytees delytable pleasaunce shall example may beware lere hasty luste volunte begyn thynge wherin suerte dependeth aye stryfe werre debate playe vnwarely cometh chek mate harme done late amende whose fyne ofte wende storye ye shall se lete pryam alwaye myrour hasty errour tymes correcte anone poyntell wyll directe maner trace rude storye remenaunt conclude worthy kyng euer one sentence aye fyred feruence hath breuettes letter sente lordes holde parlemente comaunded al hast may come anone theyr assygned day euery warde partye towne assemble noble ilyowne chefe reygne whan echone hym present noble kynge anone tofore shortly wyll declareth thus began syres quod bycause ye wyse nedeth nat longe processe deuyse reherse comynge cause tell shortly clause meane make delay ye wot day sent grece counsayle knyght myne anthenor men call haue recured exyona agayne whose message nat vayne grekes full vncurteysly receyued dispytously threte rebuked poynt haue dede vnneth myght escape hede put hym suche offence blame reboundeth aldershame day day must encrease ordayne remedye therfore mesour haue offred haue v werre stryfe yprof ed hye despyte rancour hete malys cruelly v threte wolde pea purchace wronges done fellyvs manace harmes haue v wrought nat purpose playnly theyr thought redresse amendes make vtterly werre v awake whose ioye fully encrease greuaunce wolde god repentaunce contryte herte stynte myschefe lykly falle grefe outher parte myght ouer slyde ala rancour pryde ar swolle newe threte god diffende halfe dele sore infortune euer shulde fall purpose v sythe haue shape thus v must resyste theyr wyll malycyous thorugh myght god necessyte diffence wyll none beste holde vnto oure entent worke one assent purpose sonest shall acheue discorde may quarell preue parte hertes nat one victorye may wyse gone chefe conquest pea vnyte right discorde aduersyte ouyde hertes maketh rewmes sure dyuysyon causeth discomfyture wherfore rede wyll herte lette v set grekes smerte sothfastly ye lyst se dare afferme strenger grekes vpon euery parte haue armes parfytely arte couted knyghthod crop roote plente haue men hors foote arrayed well eueryche degre therwith also stronge cyte withstonde fomen euerychone counsaylynge ordayne anone firste assemble hooly nauye stuffe strongly wt chyualrye grece hastely sende proude grekes manly offende iuste cause tytle ryght oa werre full myght theyr townes brenne theyr feldes waste herte vnfayned also v enhaste quyte deserued haue rede shall none saue cruelly take vengeaunce ne hath fere ne let greuaunce though afore fortune victoures lee auncetres progenytoures vnhap firste put downe remounteth ofte full hye renowne chaunge varyaunce werre stryfe euer balaunce day assured wele tomorowe caste downe whele victor ofte put aduenture vanquysshed discomfyture hym hadde afore victorye vp downe armes stande glorye martes chaunce man hym assure cometh let hym take eure gery mar influence gyue man whylom excellence wynne pryse lyke conqueroure sodaynly somer floure honour make fade whan aspectis glade man lysteth wrythe renowne olde goth awaye blythe floode ebbe foloweth aye men deserue prayse daye thoughe phebus day mery shyne tomorowe may bemes downe declyne thorugh thycknesse mystes trouble ryght mar chaunces double vp downe lowe alofte fortune whiche chaungeth ofte lyst hir whele make man assende vnwarely downe agayne descende stoundemele honoure auaunce asweygh throwe hym myschauce nowe fauour set hym vp full hye est auale hym twynclynge eye hir playe vnstable tourneth balle whyle one gothe vp nother hath falle reyseth one doth nother loute euery man whan cometh aboute must take tourne hir play requereth experte hir fraudes lereth shall hir sugre fynde galle meynt hir hony aye
