bytter spreynt pea werre honour fame dignytes renowne shame hi lykynge hir lyst graunte therfore man hap moche auaunte pfor though grekes whylom alofte may hereafter happe full vnsofte wherfore echone shewe worthynesse named strengthe hardynesse fortune playnely comytte let fer manly hertes f ytte stande hole menynge playne therupon let se ye wyll sayne atones theyr voyse gan reyse sentence hyghly preyse one herte manly gan expresse wyll dispende goodes rychesse theyr bodyes put iupardye nat one wolde tho denye graunte thanketh echone gaue leue lyst gone dissolued hath parlement euery man waye went repayred mansyowne kynge alone lefte ylyowne sole hymselfe inwardely musynge purpose myght aboute brynge soth thynge elles thought therupon euen thus wrought byng pryamus makyng thus mone tolde acceptable euery wyghtes grace nexte fader taken hathe place pand whan pryam leyser dyde espye syghes sore castynge vp eye echone syttynge enuyron gan declare hertes mocion pbut firste myght wyll expowne teres gan hymselfe drowne hertely wo outragyous wepynge sobbynge furyous vnneth myght worde breke vnto distresse speke openly inwarde menynge shewe tyll laste wordes fewe gan abrade pytous fare euen thus menynge declare pmy dere sone louynge kynde suppose ye haue mynde remembre discretly aduerte emprente full fresshely herte grekes agayne right lawe cruell swerde murdred haue slawe worthy auncetres full hye renowne destroyed brent bete downe firste troye walles olde vngoodly also holde myn owne suster called exyon full great shame confusyon hye reprefe worthynesse semeth kyndenesse nature ye oughte agreued inwardly herte sore meued suffre hyndrynge hir name treated alder shame ala nyl ye besynesse hye despyte knyghtly redresse auenge vpon theyr cruelte recure fynde iniquyte syth ye myghty stronge certes semeth ye byde longe fro day day ye differre knyghtly wyse gynne werre force myght manly assaye pure sorye ye lyste delaye comforte vnto desyre theyr hate brenne hote fyre vpon lyke ye may se fretynge yre auenged lyke theyr decrete quyte theyr mede ye ala take lyst hede whyle renowne doth fresshely shyne vnto luste hertes declyne consyderynge lyke kouthe haue grene youthe yfostred brought forth echone frothylke day ye coude gone tenderly coude myght whiche thynge inwarde syght ye shulde aduerte alway new newe nature sore rewe remedye myn aduersyte whiche toucheth also well syth ye wote sore doth greue ye shulde shape myn harmes releue sodaynly thus ganmourne towardes ector gan face tourne sayde ector truste ioye myn heyre also lyke reygne troye day ryght whiche euery thyng kynde doth constrayne bondes hir large chayne syttynge doth enspyre accordynge euery man desyre wronges done haue amendement hir lawe right conuenyent namely suche nobylte kynde hath endewed sette hye degre suche great reprefe shame whan wronge vnto theyr name echetrespasse must consydered iustly mesured qualyte hym offended also parsone wronge werre contek debate gretter grefe hye estate suffre harme case auenture wronge vniustly endure iniuryes compassed malys offence discrete aduyse famous manhode renomed borne gentyll blode suche one holde wretche wherfore must greatly charge retche oonly knyghthode worshyp eke wronges done amendes seke state consydered hye noblesse plyte stoude worthynesse whan bestes reason rude blynde desyre instuyt kynde pand parte truste certayne ye haue sone wolde halfe fayne vpon grekes auenged trouthe say faythfully yre brenne doth glede thurste theyr blode mede right eldest age amonge sone moste wt rage fret within iustly knyghthode right hande shede grekes blode shall fynde paraunter wene whan tyme cometh sothe shalbe sene pbut firste rede wysely mynde caste afore leue nat behynde ye begynne discretely aduerte prudently consydre herte oonly nat gynnynge ende myddes way wyll wende fyne fortune wyll lede ye thus amysse ye may spede counsayle myne opynyon worthy lytell discrecyon haue pryse cast nat course thynges ordre ceryously way trace wo delyte though gynnynge haue appetyte yet ende playnly fable ther may thyg folow nat comedable worthe agynnynge fortunate causeth stryfe great debate wherfor sothe pryncyples drede men well knowe fyne shall succede gynnynge grace well fortuned whan ende myddes lyke contuned whan wele ne may contene well better betymes abstene put doute standeth insuerte doth hath aduersyte humbly estate royall herte praye let nat offende bolde say mocion good fayth none entencion thynge meue offence oonly magnyfycence procede nat hede wylfully ne spyryte meue folylye begyn thyng wyll shende lacke ye se nat ende take hede aduertence consydre good prouydence grekes haue theyr subieccion europe aufryk many region ful large wyde knyghthod famous rychesse wonder plenteuous right renomed also worthynesse supporte dare well expresse full peryllous displese disturbe quyete parturbe whiche standeth pea greatly drede though asye helpe v nede loked euery parte aryght nat egall vnto grekes myght pand though also myn aunte exyon agayne right holde thelamon nat good hir redempcion put v destruccion rede nat beye hir halfe dere many v hap sytte mo myght hir sake deth vnder onge ende make whiche wysedome lyke semeth may happe also short tyme hir fatall cours shall fyne whan antropos threde two shall twyne wonne go enmyte thought sorowe wo slaughter men deth confusion wherfore rede without dissymylacion without wo endure nat put selfe auenture holde beste werke wyse douteles cowardyse saye nat hye presence forcause holde prudence fortune full doubylnesse syth sure put sykernesse thus effecte wylle worde ector helde hym stylle whan ector full hye prudence concluded hath fyne sentence full demurely kepte lyppes close therwithall parys vp arose gan tale thus afore kynge lorde quod lykynge hyghnesse take hede semeth shulde lytell drede knyghtly wyse vndertake vpon grekes werre make atones theyr pryde confounde syth passyngly habounde chyua rye within towne haue plente possessiowne eche thynge may werre auayle stuffe selfe royall apparayle longeth assautes marcyall specyal helpe socoure many regyon vsto werke theyr destruccyon pompe pryde manly abate grekes malys mate herte stoute semeth shortly nede nat doute parte dismayde wherfore rede let nat delayde shyppes firste redy make myselfe wyll fully vndertake lykynge pleasaunce empryse hooly gouernaunce assure put certayne exyona recure agayne fourme shalbe wrought haue awaye founde thought lykely done whiche vnto wyll declare anone firste haue cast wt stronge myghty hande rauysshe lady lande hye estate make taryenge myghtely troye hir brynge maugce hir myght conclusion ye may haue testytucion eschaunge hir ye desyre therupon shall nat longe behete grekes stronge shall nat prolonge wyll sayne excludynge euery doute aduyse shalbe brought firste shall purpose fyne goddes haue thorugh power dyuy e shewed reuelacion therupon hadde auysion late gone lay slepe vnto whiche ye take kepe ye may nat fayle dispayre haue recure hir fayre ye haue moche care pand maner hole wyll declare dreme magnyfycence ye gyue wyll credence tale shall nat dwelle ceryously ordre telle trouthe playne fable fayne lorde moste souerayne pfirste ye remembre mynde day whan last ynde aduyse comaundement mater whiche yourentent specyally hadde cherte knowen betwene whiche toke vpon charge bondes lande full large pthe tyme desyre spede whan tytan bemes rede gemyny droue chare golde towarde crabbe take holde whiche named paleys dyane bente moone wex wane whan halowed sonnes stacyon nygh myddes moneth iuyn whiche season erely morowe whan phebus voyde nyghtes sorowe doth pirrous wayne agayne vp drawe aurora estwarde doth adawe water hir teres rounde syluer dewe causeth habounde vpon herbes floures soote kyndely norysshynge crop roote vp rose bedde anone full desyrous huntynge gone prycked herte lusty fresshe pleasaunce loue dewe obseruaunce lucyna day magnefye whiche called lady venerye dewely rytes obserue cythera hir serue feres hertes releue cast v fully tyll drewe eue forest playe v disporte pleasauntly v recomforte longeth loue lustynesse thylke day venus goddesse sacred full great excellence great honour dewe reuerence unto hir bothe one fryday aduenture fall whan gan hast v wodes grene hope day game sene great labour rydynge fro tyll hadde full many bucke doo strengthe slayne myght fynde herte chaced wt houndes hynde thorugh downes dale lowe tyll phebus dayes bowe amyd arke meridyen whan bemes full hote shene moste besy vpon chaas befell wonder dyuerse caas fortune happed sodaynly whyle seuered fro companye sole selfe amonge holtes hore fynde game desyrous euermore ware thorow thycke thorow thyn full great harte sawe afore meryn downe lande vale grene sothe myght nat sustene swyfte nygh hym nere albe prycked coursere nyghe deth thorugh many sondry shawe syght fer gan withdrawe euer sewe myght anone loste hym syght woode yda bare name faynt gan wexe game myn hors whiche dyde ryde fomynge full whyte vpon euery syde flankes blode distayned pursute sore constrayned spore sharp dyed rede harte prycked stede vp downe full besy thought laboure auayled right nought tyll laste amonge bowes glade aduenture caughte plesaunt shade full smothe playne lusty sene softe veluet yonge grene fro hors dyd lyght faste bowe reyne caste faynte mate werynesse layde downe vpon gras vpon brynke shortly telle besyde aryuer cristalle welle water ireherse lyke quycke syluer stremes ran whiche grauell bryght stone golde agayne sonne shone pwhere right anone werynesse sondayne slepe gan oppresse fro tyme firste borne neuer asleped toforne lay wonder sweuen thought hye downe fro heuen wynged god wonderfull chere mercuryous dyde appere somedele firste aferde gyrde croked swerde hym brought also honde slepy yerde plyaunt wonde serpent goynge enuyrowne foot also lowe downe semeth also stode cocke syngynge houres trewe clocke mouthe god mercurye pypes sette longe wonder merye whiche swete sugred armonye made myn eres suche melodye semed tho myn aduyse rauysshed paradyse thus god dyuerse lyknesse wonderfull expresse shewed hymselfe apparence lyke discryued fulgence boke methologyes rehersed many poesyes many lyknesse lyke ye may se take moralyte longe yerde right lyne whiche syde wrongly may declyne signefyeth prudent gouernaunce discrete folke thorugh theyr purueyaunce cast peryll fall pypes loude shall thorugh musyke entuned trewe betokeneth eke many lusty hewe sugred dytees great excellence rethoryke eloquence whiche god soueraygne patrowne cocke swete lusty sowne iustly kepeth houres nyght vtterly aduyse warde syght suche voyde waker dylygence theyr court slouthe neclygence swerde whiche croketh agayne nat forged ymade vayne reuoke right weye suche wrongly trouthe forueye serpent whiche tolde whiche wryncled ye may beholde vpon yerde aboute gothe signefyeth falshode wode wrothe lyeth awayte many sleyghty weye gynne trouthe werreye god eloquence kynge brought hym eke comynge cythera louers serue iuno pallas called mynerue ven u hir lyeges delyte aboute hir hede hadde douues whyte loke benyngne eyen debonayre aye flykerynge snowy wynges fayre declare sothly sentence douues innocence loue trouthe mene theyr groude shulde honest clene ytokened clerely wytnesse without soylynge vnclennesse fresshenesse rose rede somer lusty sprede wynter theyr colour fade signefyeth hertely thoughtes glade yonge folkes amerous feruent hope inly desyrous whan loue gynneth theyr hertes floure tyll longe processe maketh loure wynter vnweldy age lust palled dulled rage febylnesse whan somer gone folkes knowe trowe mo one therfore venus fleteth see shewe trouble aduersytee loue hir stormy lawe whiche byset many sturdy wawe nowe calme rough taketh hede hope assayled aye sodayne drede next venus pallas behelde hir spere hir cristall shelde raynebowe rounde aboute hir hede colour grene blewe rede afore hir descryue growynge grene fresshe olyue therupon browes fowle braunches sawe sytte lyke nowle firste shylde pallas goddesse signefyed expresse vertue force manly hye diffence agayne vyces make resystence hir spere sharpe kene grounde iuste rygour forged confounde false put backe mercy shall medle wt wracke shafte sothe shauen full playne lest mercyles right ne wrought vayne werre make full releas olyue betokeneth pea owle also odyous songes syngeth festes funerall declareth playnly fyne euery glorye oonly deth hath memorye raynebowe grene rede perse sygnefyeth chaunges full dyuerse ofte falleth werre batayle wynne sodaynly fayle stable blewe chaugyng grene pallas playe alway meynt tene alder last haue mynde hir nynphes iuno came behynde whiche custome fulgence telles abyde floodes depe welles iuno poetes sayne amayden fruyte barayne pecok fresshe quene ysacred fethers shene splayed abrode large sayle argus eyen emprynted tayle pthe water rennynge ryuer flode labour men haue gode great trouble besynesse day nyght suffre rychesse euer flodes rowe lete hym beware aye flowe nature right dewe folowynge moone must ebbesewe moste drede aye vpon fulle lyste fortune fresshe fethers pulle ryche folke shyne golde shene sythe chaunge lady quene pand argus eyen set behynde nygardes hertes ofte sythes blynde whiche nat aduerte goodes ende lyke ebbe sodaynly wyll wende whiche nothyng consydre theyr syght fayre lusty fethers bryght pecok vnwarely fall away right rychesse shortly day wyll theyr mayster sodaynly forsake saynge dewe theyr leue take iuno barayne fruyte right naked bare distytuyte gredy hertes couetous whiche gadre desyrous thynge haue suffysaunce fret drede put suche myschauce ymagenynge worlde wyll fayle theyr fere agayne wynde sayle tyll atones must go fro thus good aye fyne wo namely pynche spare drede clarkes declare fruyte good spende large man full set lytell charge parte frely treasour comune whan discretly sethe tyme oportune hath ioye put good mewe herte fredome lyste sewe gentylnesse taketh hede therto pand wyse pallas iuno fresshe venus downe descended lyke haue shortly comprehended vnder guyynge mercurius whiche vnto gan tale thus parys quod lyfte vp thyne eyen se lo goddess nombre thre whiche fro heuen theyr eyen clere dyuersly vnto appere feste tell shall goddes aboue celestyall iubyter helde owne borde none absent oonly saue discorde despyte nat present auenged sette hir entent hir wyttes many wayes sought tyll laste euen thus wrought poetes lyke tolde toke appel rounde pure golde greke letter grauen vp downe whiche sayde thus conclusy owne without stryfe gyue anoon fayrest euerychone discorde lady goddesse debate maystresse hath appell passynge delyte brought feste malys despyte caste downe amonge borde deynous chere spekynge nat worde hir waye faste gan hir hye sodaynly preuy great enuye courte appell hath brought great werre suche contek wrought hertes ylke thre longe may nat staunchedbe amonge themselfe gan disdayne whiche beaute moste soueraygne whiche hath beste tytle ryght conquere burned appell bryght firste gan thus beaute stryue rancour theyr hertes almost ryue wyte right shulde firste possede yet enuye reygneth womanhede one fayrer holde eche woman hir kynde wolde haue parte pry aboue another eche estate sothe none eche hir owne aduys hath ioye beaute haue pry none foule doth myrour prye fayre hir owne eye lyke fole hymfelfe doth quyte aumber yelowe cheseth whyte goundy eye deceyued soone colour cheseth moone colour fyre made fyne encreased spyces wyne oyntementes confeccions nyght false illusion appere wonder fresshe fayre loke derke day lyght ayre prefe erely morowe suche nede beaute borowe nature hath hir selfe disposed therfore fastynge boystes vnclosed make thy choyse byd ouyde whan euery drugge pot set asyde lyst thou sentence deceyued lyghtly false apparence dayes suche crafte full ryue wyse thus began stryue betwyxe iuno venus pallas descended sodaynecas one assent touchynge theyr beaute dome therof comytted vnto speke called art parys holde art right prudent right wy auysed thy dome shall fyne ne may fro declyne obeye one assent without stryfe thy iugement herke firste thou procede eche shalbe thy mede consydre right take good hede therto thou appell graunt vnto iuno shall gyue plente rychesse hye renowne fame eke worthynesse haboundaunce golde tresour ryse hye honour thou alone shalt excelle thy guerdon lyke telle pallas goddesse prudence lyst fyne conclude thy sentence may lady appell thy mede shall assure wyt ofsapyence thou shalt hooly haue excellence wysdome discrecion dyscerne clerenesse reason also fer phebus caste lyght shall nat prudent knyght worlde sythe began iuste reporte manlyer man thy name none equypollent venus trewe clene entent lyste graunt conclusion appell haue possession fresshe goddesse syt hye aboue shall ensure haue vnto thy loue fayrest lady tofore worlde euer shalbe bore grece thou shalt hir knyghtly wynne aduysed thou begynne iustly deme thynge spare pand anone gan loke vp stare greatly astoned best tyll laste spake mercurye sayde certayne ne wolde gyue dome naked myghty haue fully lyberte eueryche vyselye se consydre euery circumstaunce fayrest vnto plesaunce goodlyest speke womanhede dome procede anone ye haue herde seye desyre mekely gan obeye haste theyr besy cure dispoyle clothynge vesture lyche statute dome bonde poynt ne wolde nat withstonde myght haue full inspexion fourme shap eche proporsion discerne remembre vysely ordre euery membre erst iuge ryght whan eche hadde syght gaue venus appell right anone bycause fayrest echone moste excellynge sothly beaute moste womanly goodly se deme playnly syght stremes hir eyen bryght ilyche glade egall euen lyght sterre sheweth towarde nyght whiche called esperus shene venus hir selfe fresshe lusty quene whiche anone heuenly emperesse dome hertely hye gladnesse appell hooly hath glorye wonne iustly victorye reioysed hir tell hir feres beaute dyde excell haste trewe affeccion concluded hath fully guerdon full demurely lowe nat lofte mercurye sobre wordes softe deuoyde bothe doubylnesse slouthe lyke beheste holde wyll hir trouthe sodaynly without iniurye disapered god mercurye streyghte heuen right way toke anone slepe woke pwherof lord loue drede ye aduerte wysely take hede beheste affermed certayne vnto assured nat vayne goodly venus lyke haue tolde wherfore rede ye herte bolde sende stronge myghty hande without abode grekes lande fourme haue sayde hope ye shalbe well apayde whan haue spede venus hath behyghte home retourne lady bryghte shall ye beste lyste nat speke vayne echaunge hir suster wyn agayne thelamon withholde hath yore lo say nomore touchynge effect hooly myn aduyse stylle sat parys fully hymselfe aquyte saye pryam ala thy wyte neclygence take kepe thy truste sette dremes slepe full thynne thy discrecyon take grounde false illusyon procede lyke fantasye vpon sweuen meynt flaterye ala reason thynge thy guyde pallas wrongly sette asyde nat receyued dewe reuerence iuuo eke hir sapyence hir good lokynge debonayre hir treasour hir hestes fayre refused ala wylfulnesse loue goddesse eke also vulcanus wyfe whose seruyce euer werre stryfe preferred appell procede agayne right parys toke none hede saue vnto luste sette syde trouthe thorugh ala yt full great routhe myghty ryche noble towne troye brought confusyowne oonly knyghthode hath forsake prudence golde choyse ytake oonly woman holde hym therto roote theyr woo storye ceryously shall telle dremes wyll lenger dwelle wryte forthe dephebus thyrde sone kynge pryamus tale gan open audyence kynge shortly sentence lyste trouthe nat spare euen thus conceyte declare lorde quod euery wyght aduerte shulde caste syght future thynge peryll doute cerche within withoute poynt poynt alwaye reason caste doutes tourne vp downe wyght shulde purpose wende matere make ende presume manhod thought caste perylles acheueth lytell nought plowman alway caste aforne many graynes felde corne shalbe deuoured foules rauynous doth sowe feldes plenteuous shulde neuer vale playne cowardshyp throwe abrode grayne lete suche drede nowe layde asyde holde folye lenger abyde parys brother make hym stronge shyppes venge wronge vpon grekes payne myght preue shortly knyght reason ye consydre may man iustly may say nay parys hath counsayled wele trouthe fer fele errour purpose contrarye wherfore let hym lenger tarye holde waye stronge nauye auenge great velanye grekes haue ye take hede done heretofore v kynrede fynall execucyon recure touchynge exyon treate dishonest wyse agaynst right tytle iustyse thynke gyueth herte wounde shame whiche newe doth rebounde vpon hir allye wherfore beste espye parys take vyage suche fresshe lusty age manly wende grekes lande force theyr myghty hande maugre grekes proude elate rauysshe lady estate ye may knyghthod brother ye lyste chaunge hir moste redy short conclusion se restytucion exyone parys wende counsayle shortly thus ende faste full discrete sage helenus fourth sone age rose sete great reuerence prayeng fader graunte hym audyence may say presence openly shalbe fall secrete thynges soberly thus tale began clene entent trewe affeccion lorde quod supportacion grace wherin truste let none offence vnto luste displease though say conceyte syth ye knowe mene deceyte neuer yet fayled sentence fyll experyence lyke tolde partye pryue treate generall without menynge doubylnesse folowed dyde expresse remembre ye shall fynde trewe god wyll shall nat newe spare say lyke conceyue dede fraude deceyue declarynge firste trewe entencion shall folowe conclusion parys grece wende truste well wyll v shende goddes haue reuelacion made vnto demonstracion eke knowe astronomye neuer yet prophecye ne deceyued shulde falle none lyste counsayle calle taught thynge yt shall betyde wherfore praye rancour pryde enuye none olde hatrede take vengaunce ye nat procede aduyse lyke ye purpose say playnly lyste nat glose ye shall repente ye parys sende grece whiche god defende wytte well conclusion shall fully tourne destruccion fynally ruyne lyke gan afore deuyne fyne folowe shall subuercion bothe towne wall paleys house cyte goth nought ye get semeth ought ynough suffyse haue sayde sythe ye wyse ye aduerte sawe doute nat ye wyll withdrawe hande tyme damage assayle constraynte rage better betymes abstene purpose whiche yet grene hede hastely assente thynge whiche shall echone repente plenerly shall thynge socoure shall folowe youre despytefull deth without excepciowne one abydynge towne firste selfe playnly endyte shall vengaunce grekes byte thorugh furye theyr mortall tene wyfe cuba quene shall lede hir lyfe thorugh grekes cruelte sorowe wo captyuyte lyeges swerde shall pace cruell de h without grace innocentes mercyles shall blede auyse ye procede wylfulnesse werre make folylye vndertake parturbe quyete reste whiche shall tourne thynge beste ruyne v myschefe fall counsayle afore prouyde wylfulnesse sette asyde specially whan deth tolde muste fyne ye purpose holde lo without wordes mo grece parys go pand wyse whan helenus playnly sayde guydo telleth v tryste heuy pale face agayne resorteth syttynge place whose sentence astoned euerychone sat sylence stylle stone powerles theyr hertes resume speke worde man dare presume prese kept theyr lyppes close laste troylous vp arose yonge fresshe lusty courageous also aye desyrous haue armes manly longeth knyght whan full glad lyght sawe fader bretherne euerychone inly troubled thus spake anone noble worthy syttynge enuyron hye prudence great discrecyon manfull also hye courage sodayn fere hath brought rage new trouble cropen breste sentence cowarde preste syth echone ye shall euer fynde desyre veryly kynde lyue luste voyde away trauayle dedely hate batayle theyr wyt fynally applye sewe theyr luste lyue glotonye fyll theyr stomacke restore theyr mawe reste ease euer drawe sewe theyr inwarde appetyte thus theyr ioye thus theyr delyte etynge drynkynge couetyse theyr studye fully deuyse may folow lust without right nought elles set store ala shame ye dismayde sytte mate astoned afrayde wordes helenus ferefull drede lytell mous quaketh speke fyght ouer agayne skylle ryght preiudyce goddes alle taketh hym say shall befalle thynge futur specefye spyryte prophecye graunted hym alone speciall though connynge perygall goddes hauynge prescience shewe afore thorugh sapyence shall betyde outher euyll gode let let wyght wode hath wyt gyue therto credence man crafte scyence mortall hath connynge deuyne fortune course fate termyne suche cause hyd conceled secree reserued goddes preuytee men may dyuyne folye take hede lye wherfore rede matere one lorde dere exclude drede may disturbe herte let thynge perturbe hye courage helenus hath tolde herte nat bolde manhode wold helpe venge wronge let hym go hyde hym temple stronge kepe hym close contemplacion wake praye deuocion without socour dayes nyghtes suffre suche lusty knyghtes haunte theyr youthe grene lustynesse manly armes preue theyr hardynesse may haue better acqueyntauce tyme comynge vengeaunce theyr enmyes theyr cruell oon comaunde parys may forth goon execute fyne entent afore purposed parlament vpon grekes theyr offencyon parfourme vp payne talyon wronges olde whiche yet fame rehersed vnto alder shame thorugh worlde ye wote le therwithall troylus helde pe sodaynly present began atones one assent troylus counsayle greatly preyse manhode heuen reyse fresshe courage hye prowesse feruent zele hardynesse one herte greatly hym comende right anone made ende pryamus whan done vpon tyme houre noone mete goth within ilyon sone syttynge enuyron mete called hath parys dephebus also full wy secretly bad shulde go day lordes mo panomye haste may make redy agayne certayne day aray worthy chyualrye may gete theyr companye towardes grece sayle hastely kynge sodaynely nexte day made counsayle calle euen thus sayde afore alle po noble lyeges beynge present purpose say myn entent without abode ye lyste suppose nat vnwyste grekes pryde tyrannye malys olde compassed enuye many wyse haue agayne v wrought whiche grene foryete nought day day encreasynge euer mo remembraunce renewed wo whan recorde caste vp downe greues exyowne seruytude amonge doth soiourne whiche ofte day causeth mourne herte almost asonder ryue consyder se lyue whose cruelte haue dere bought natwithstandynge yt haue meanes sought haue reste without whan grece sent anthenore peasybly suster recure surplus pacyently endure nought toke hede offred goodlyhede nat herde lacke gentyllesse recorde whiche doubleth distresse pwherfore muste techeth suxgerye sharpe yrons seke remedye cutte away roote rounde proude flesshe yt groweth grounde whiche wyll nat voyde wt oyntementes softe albe layde therto full ofte right example must duresse gette recure whan fayrenesse may none haue wherfore aduyse purpose sende forthe paryse grece lady wyn brynge hir home shall within kepe hir stronge maugre sayth nay tyll se agreable day fayne lyke myn oppynyon haue eschaunge hir exyon dere suster loue may nat fayle shall goddes v fauourable counsayle also acceptable echone whan kynge toucheth comonte wyse men affermed comon ought confermed thynge touchynge shulde apreued echone acheued wherfore caste aduyse echone playnly werke worde anone noble pryam sodaynly pea amonges prease whan whyste theyr aller syght knyght vp rose pentheus hyght sone euforbyus de transformatis sayth ouydius fayneth whylom soule pictagoras hooly transsumed wryte ouyde touchynge wyll lenger byde tell forth pentheus afore kynge whiche gan tale thus lyege lorde vnto hye noblesse displease nat worthynesse presence mageste shall say acquyte towardes fayth trouthe soth fastly may slouthe touchynge honour without drede zele faythe brenne doth glede harmes bydde beware doutelesse afferme well dare ye stande firste aduyse ye purpose sende forth paryse doute nat shall rewe god well wore olde nat newe fader called euforbyus discrete wyse right vertuous knowynge afore euery thynge prescyence byfore wyttynge tell playnly thorugh phylosophye heuenly sawe hertes eye e thynge secree hyd knowynge pryuetee knewe wyt sage laste whan age hondred yere wt lokkes gray hore remembre complayned sore wepte also pyte tenderly fully affermynge parys vtterly wente grece rauysshe hym wyfe shulde folowe suche mortall stryfe vpon v sothly cyte shulde asshes scyndres tourned shulde nothynge v socoure grekes swerde shall cruelly deuoure hye lowe playnly spare none wherfore praye amonge euerychone tell haue despyte wronge venge put respyte rancour olde rede ye lete tranquylle quyete hastynesse ye nat submytte fortune falsely flytte perturbe nat none olde enmyte newe sterynge felycyte ye iourney assente ye euerychone full sore shall repente ye wyll algates thether sende parys stede let wende lyst vyage spede counsayse full rede sayde vnder supporte oonly grace sodaynly gan echone chace pentheus loude agayne hym crye repreuynge hym prophecye fader theyr confucion pbut ala reuolucion ioye wo felycyte thynge ordeyned nedes must ordre thynges wt fate englewed shall falle may nat eschewed whiche caused assente one vndiscretly parys shulde gone vnhappely wt hap enuolued pand th cocludyg theyr cousayl dissolued casuelly befell right aduyse vnto eres ran cassandra great afray sodayne wo gan crye welaway palas quod ala wyll ye shall parys grece go worde braste wepe full pytously inwarde syghes depe gan wayle swowne payne furyously noyse complayne wofull rage many pytous sowne made mortall lamentaciowne dede myght hir nat withholde heer torne fystes folde sayde ala hondred sythe stormy fortune lyst thou kythe thy cruell force oure aduersyte vpon v vpon cyte mortall yre gery vyolence swerde vengeauce worse tha pestylence po troye troye thy gylte ala hast thou done thy trespas euersed tourned nought wylde fyre thy synne dere abought pryam kynge vncely thy chaunce hast thou gylte outher greuaunce thy goddes wyrched thorugh vnryght prouoke shewe theyr cruell myght vpon thy blode ala hast thou moder myn ecuba also maner cryme importable offence hast thou wrought haue suche recompence day abyde noble worthy quene thy sone suche vengeaunce sene wofull deth cruell horryble ala ye credyble counsayle suche harmes eschewe mortall purpose fully remewe go nat ordeyned thought whiche constrayned vnneth may wo endure hir fader wofull creature helde streyght hir way falleth plat groude hir wepynge water wounde hir chekes teres rayne myght constraynt hir payne vpon hym gan clyppe crye besechynge hym shape remedye pytous voyce knewe full wele matere playnly euery dele shall befaile full mynde sodayne harmes shall behynde hir clamour nat vayne shall falle clerkes sayne ne may nat well men eschewed eke fortune great aduersyte hasty ire furyous wode vnkynde troyan blode causelesse agaynst agreued rancour sodaynly ameued blynde awayte catche atrauce vyolence hir vnhappy chaunce hath wt sweyght tourned hir whele vnstable enuyous mutable haste troyens theyr confusion wylfulnesse vndiscrecion agaynst grekes quarell make therupon haue theyr counsayle take acheued ye haue herde deuyse without assent wyse diffynacion ector herde concluded reason matere helenus counsayle take pentheus aduerted wysely sentence without faynynge full credence cassandra neuer coude lye prudently herde prophecye fro poynt poynt caste aforne suche myschefe nat lorne floured yet theyr felycyte without damage aduersyte fortune wyll haue hir course alway whose purpose holdeth sayth ye nay made vyage forhede playne false vysage sugre shadde venym roote bytter taste shewynge soote wrynkled double lyke horned snayle faythe theyr face fraude aye ye tayle haste troyans accorde one parys shulde grece gone ye haue herde sayne vpon caste ordayne phow kyng pryamus sent parys grece wt dephebus men armes take vengeauce ye grekes toke ye fayre helayne quene vnto menelaus brought hir vnto troye capitulo xiij tyme approcheth wha ye sonne shene golden wayne whyrled vp wene clere sterres yades rede whiche haue theyr syght crabbes hede plyade seuenth sterre bryght whiche syxe appere syght seuenth draweth hir asyde couertly doth hir bemes hyde whylom dyde great offence vnto v causeth hir absence dare nat shewe hir stremes clere hir susterne openly appere whylom god mortall dyde synne crymynall whiche noysed kou thorugh heuen alone amonge susterne seuen shroudeth v shamefastly hir chere pand whan titan zoudyak spere atwene sterres take see bole syxtene degree vpon tyme ioly grene may whan flora hir hewes gay hath euery playne medowe hylle vale hir floures quycke thynge pale ouer spred cladde lyuere newe braunches blosme wt many lusty hewe byd v fully glad lyght assurauce haue fruyt behyght agayne autumpne lyst shake whan vynes rypeth euery grape thus season lusty disporte embraceth hertes newe recomforte oonly hope kynde dewe holsom fruyte shall blosmes sewe whan tyme cometh reuolucion thus may lusty fresshe season whan brydes synge theyr armonye tyme panomye repayred dephebus parys brought chosen deuys thre thousande knyghtes redy gone grece shyppes many one full vytayled may nede shyppes nombre rede two twenty lyke wryte guydo without ado kynge comaundeth vnto eneas anthenor polydamas haste redy make parys knyghtly vndertake ye haue herde iourney acheue tyme whan toke theyr leue pryamus short conclusion sheweth effect entencion specially theyr deuer done recure suster exyone ye haue herde tofore telle shulde mater dwelle whan redy without soiour parys firste lorde gouernour vyage made pryamus brother called dephebus theyr leue toke wepynge tenderly shyppe manfully whithout abode began dresse name venus goddesse myghty ioue toke theyr iournee hale vp anker large see gan sayle haue wynde wylle water calme blandysshynge stylle without trouble boystous wawe costes gan fast drawe grekes lande thynge lette fortune theyr cours mette grekysshe shyp myn auctour telleth thus whiche kyng menelaus towarde pryam famous stronge cyte vysyte duke hye degre nestor hyghte menelaus brother eke vnto kynge famous wyse worthy great agamenon name reputacion amonges grekes worthynesse menelay storye bereth wytnesse husbonde quene eleyne suster bretherne tweyne castor pollux whiche tolde theyr hande worthy knyght holde tyme lyke theyr degre strynestar theyr moste chefe cyte helde housholde solempne ryall loue speciall wyll herte accordynge dede atwyxe two bretherhede none coude lyue alone eke mayde hermyone yonge doughter quene eleyne fayrenesse moste inly souereyne moste passyngly excellynge beaute pand thus troyans saylynge see towarde grece amonge wawes wete auenture happed mete kynge menelaus saylynge theyr syde none lyste pryde enquere passe forthe full huge pa none coude knowe aye wynde pesybly gan blowe troyan flete causynge whyle approche noble yle called cithera day hauen hast may cast anker bonde shyppes stronge lyste nat tarye longe take lande full many lusty man arrayeng fresshely pnow yle passynge excellence temple great reuerence bylded olde foundacion honoured region thorughout lande bothe fer neere feste day aye yere yere lyke fylle reuolucion repeyrynge thyther great deuocion honour oonly venus goddesse grekes theyr besynesse honoured euery maner age gyftes bryngynge pylgrymage great offrynge sacryfyse vsed theyr paynem wyse pfor phane knele wake contryte herte theyr prayer make statute gaue euery question playne answere full solucion cerymonyes venus loute euery thynge doute hadde full declaracion thus grekes vpon citheron halowe feste wt ryche great aray rytes dewe ferforth may hope fully better thryue pand fortune whan dyde aryue vp lande aduenture ca tyme feste halowed many greke comynge fro euery coste temple go pylgrymage theyr vowes acquyte place relyques vysyte pand whan parys dyde espye gadred companye worthyest chese may temple toke right way full well besene knyghtly wyse dyde honour sacryfyce full humbly grekes lyche many ouche iewell ryche golde syluer stone perre spendeth lyke degre quyt hym manly oblacion deuoutely oryso hym demeneth ioye se pnow parys passynge great beaute amonges euer alyue none myght wt whym stryue troyan greke speke semelyhede wonder fresshe lusty rede porte full lyke gentyll knyght whose persone haue syght gan prease nyghe fere ryally hym gere coueyte hye estate lowe greatly knowe men aske besely fro whense came cause comynge enquerynge one one prudently kepte euerychone thynge openly espyde theyr answere haue gyde euery thynge kept secree eueryche auysee albe openly declare ne lyste nat spare tolde playnely cause comynge pryam stronge myghty kynge fader moste ryall renowne came also exyowne thus eche gan rowne pryme face whan came towne therupon ymagynatyfe sore musynge inquysityfe eche suspeccion demynge therof lyke theyr oppynyon rathest thynge ne knewe folkes done thynges newe whyles mater treate sondry wyse amonge theyr wordes greate saynge gan anone atteyne eres quene eleyne nygh besyde region whan herde reuelacion reporte came bytwene fayre eleyne fresshe lusty quene anone sothe vnderstode without taryenge abode hasteth hir solempnyte fresshe folke frygye se well god wote hir entencion se parys deuocion vnder colour holy pylgrymage temple taketh hir vyage great meyne ryall parayle parys se wyll nat fayle ala lusty new fyre hath hir herte en lawmed desyre go vigiles outher spectacle none holynesse myracles hath meued hir shall befall maner woman drawe thether platly conclude sure multytude gadred lyberte se fynde opportunyte theyr desyre full narowe awayte couertly theyr eyen bayte place sette theyr pleasaunce pryuely haue theyr dalyaunce sygne castynge eye token shewyng herte drye touche handes stole amonge prese arme fote catche vp theyr lese lyst fre bonde nature hym holde honde ayen whose sleyghte auayleth wyt myght lyste wronge ryght ay acheue saythe ye nay agayne whose lust defende hym man may thus guydo aye cursed false delyte speke harme hath caught appetite thorughout boke woman say yll translate agayne wyll hath aye ioye theyr honour transuerse sory muste reherce felle wordes boke founde woman moche bounde e echone goodly kynde dare nat say fynde guydoes wryte thorughout troye boke whan redde fere herte quoke veryly wyttes gan fayle whan therof made rehersayle lyke decrete guydo quyt ye shall anone chyt quene eleyne cause went deuoute herte hir offrynge presente temple venus goddesse thus worde worde saythe hir expresse mortall harme drede fraude aste sleyghte womanhede euery wo gynnynge crop rote agaynst whiche helpe may bote whan lust hath dryue theyr herte auayle aye dedely venyme seweth tayle whiche man hath power restreyne recorde take quene eleyne ho e brente ala hir desyres newe luste dele straungeres knewe nat ne neuer sawe aforne thorugh ala full many lorne cruell dethe embraced cheyne without pyte say thou quene eleyne goost spiryte ala hath meued sool fro thy lorde suche royalte thy hous go amonge prease thou wery lyue home pea wente straungers se takynge hede vnto thyn honeste thou shuldest haue kept thy closet secretly nat haue passed folyly absence thy lorde ala thou wylfull rakell se afore shulde sewe soone thou drawen mewe coude nat kepe home thy boundes thou wentest hare amonge ye houndes caughte wylfulnesse thy desyre coudest nat compesse though thy luste lyst nat refrayne many woman hath caught trayne theyr goynge suche halowes seke syt better selfe kepe close theyr chamber fle occasiowne neuer shyp shulde peryll drowne scatre rocke tempestrent carybbes deuoured shent go wrake weders ylle kept hauen stylle wyll nat occasion eschewe drede peryll sewe muste amonge necessyte ware endure aduersyte nat hir fote fro trappes spare let hir ware falle snare harme done late compleyne whylom worthy quene eleyne hir selfe kept home close hir ne wycke lose reported ye grene fre newe whose chauce vnhappy ethe man ought rewe cause suche destruccion many worthy confusion hir worthy husbonde many mo grekes syde troye also storye ye shall rede quene faste may spede temple hath way nome full ryally whan come full deuoutly within citheron made vnto venus hir oblacion presence syght many one many iewell many ryche stone whan parys espyed temple anone hath hym hyed full thryf tely haste myght whan firste syght goodly fayre fresshe quene cupides darte whet kene ware hath hym marked astoned ne wyste meruayleth hir great semelynesse hir womanhede hir porte hir fayrenesse neuer afore ne wende nature coude haue made fayre creature aungellyke hir beaute femynyne goodly se dempte lyklynesse hir beaute goddesse herte dyde hym aye assure mortall creature heuenly fayre celestyall thought party consydereth auysely hir future ordre ententyfly within reason euery thynge good inspeccion hir golden heer lyke sonne stremes fresshe phebus wt bryght bemes goodlyhede hir fresshely face replenysshed beaute grace euen ennewed quyckenesse colour rose lylye flour egally nouther wyte thorugh none excesse moche lyte within cerclynge hir eyen bryght paradys compassed hir syght thorugh abreste beaute wolde perce certaynly shall reherce hir shap hir fourme future guydo dothe ordre ceryously hede fo e clerely deuyse haue none englysshe therto may suffyse wyll nat tunge nat lyke wante floures also rethoryke sewe flourysshyng gay peynture descryue fayre creature coloures feble faynte nouther ennewe well paynte eke nat acqueynted use myn therfore excuse echone nat neclygence defaute oonly eloquence remytte guydo se descryueth ordre hir beaute take presumpciowne pbut wyll tell parys vp downe gothe temple eye caste towarde eleyne gan prese faste brente hoote loues fyre enflawmed greatly desyre ofte chaungeth countenaunce chere euer neygheth hir nere nere ydarted thorugh hir eyen tweyne agayne warde fresshe quene eleyne hoote brente herte pryuely albe man outwarde coude espy thought neuer afore men euer yet bore se none fayre lyke hir pleasaunce hym loke hir suffysaunce temple toke hede right nought compasse caste hir thought may catche opportunyte hym speke good lyberte hooly hir besynesse hym felte inly great distresse ofte chaungeth coutenaunce hewe venus hath marked newe hir brondes fyred feruence enflawmed sodayne influence egally brought rage saue eye atwe e message eche fyxe hath caste theyr syght conceyue wyste one ryght within themself theyr herte mente ne e hir euer parys wente seke fully gete occasion myght full relacion theyr hertes conceyt declare secretly vefell parys nygheth nye place quene eleyne stode hir see ther wene tweyne broke sume theyr herte gaue yssue theyr inwarde smerte done lyst espyed whan people moste occupyed temple stare gase mase kepte close worde asterte man treson myght aduerte twayne ne wolde mene laste parys quene concluded haue short auysement fully fyne theyr bothe entent sette purpose betwyxe certayne whan caste mete agayne lyste men hadde suspeccion made ende without sermon departe albe lothe soberly anone parys gothe temple herte euery parte wounded thorugh loues firy darte shyppes helde right way anone haste may whan assembled chyualrye one companye fewe wordes shortly tofore tale thus gan syres quod shortly expresse cause kouthe yor worthynesse fader grece v sente ye knowe chefe entent recure suster exyon handes kynge thelamon whiche thynge ought espye impossyble shortly myn eye waye fer se great stronge countre allyes aboute euery syde herte inly full pryde yelde hir vp hath nat disdayne therof treate nat vayne therfore beste deuyse syth power may nat suffyse werrey hym regyowne nat egall myght renowne lacke men hym holde felde may nat semble spere shelde encountre hym multytude wherfore beste conclude syth fortune hath v hyder brought goddes haue eke v wrought graciously make v londe venus temple faste stronde whiche haboundeth full great rychesse grekes offrynge vnto goddesse londe see fro many sondry porte men woman haue resorte place worshyp venus wyfe kynge menelaus present full ryche well beseyne manhode myght atteyne rauysshe hir temple spoyle theyr treasoure chesen coyle chefe iewelles charge somers golde syluer take prysoners maugre shyppes brynge nyght without taryenge may nat fayle euer say nay ye assente ryche pray wherfore haste ye redy make euery man anone harnes take arme hym well beste aray assente without delay theyr shyppes byde tyll nyght whan phebus chare wt drawen lyght vnder wawes sterres dyd appere heuen theyr stremes clere moone tyme dyde ryse shope forthe full thryfty wyse manly troyans stele armed bryght temple holdynge theyr way ryght caste lenger tarye proudely entre sentuarye chapell called citheron without reuerence deuocion done venus hir oratorye clene theyr memorye honour drede obseruaunce fynally theyr attendaunce myn auctor sothely diffyne right nought oonly rauyne toke came hande rychesse treasour lande golde syluer stone iewelles relyques sacred holy eke vesselles without abode sacrarye yfere theyr shyppes carye wonder thynke gode kylle e withstode pyte se blede many grekes shyp lede lyued captyuyte full many yere troye cyte pand whyles goth parys eleyne hir embraceth armes tweyne full humbly great reuerence fonde maner resystence sat hir nat womanly parys yolde hir vtterly hir herte hap yolde came therfore yelde hir hadde lesse fere nat stryue woman sholde anone gentyllesse wolde comforteth hir beste may ladde hir hym without delay shyppes full besyly sette wardes kepe hir honestly whyle retourneth temple agayne spoyle robbe make playne thorugh temple walles wyde pnow stode castell faste besyde ystuffed well grekysshe souldeours whiche awoke noyse pylours nyght gan make shoute therwithall anone yssue oute armed stele temple reskewe manfully sewe befylle whan togydre mette speres sharpe swerdes kene whette pthey ran togydre tygres vnmylde lyke wodelyons bore wylde faynynge founde fyght albe felde departed aryght troyans doubled noumbre vtterly grekes encoumbre myschefe made flee pursue cruelly slee without mercy castell gate rescuse came late skarmysshe fyne deth yolde vp breth myghtely troyans assayle withstande wolde nat auayle manhode felde haue wonne cruelly begonne haste spoyle castell shyppe brought euerydell treasour golde may wyn morowe sayle begyn stuffed good grekysshe see towarde costes troye cytee see calme fully theyr wylle bothe tempest stormes ylle clere also bryght heuen space almoste dayes seuen castell called tenedowne aryue sixe myle fro towne glad lyght lande wente fynde parys sente messager streyght vnto kynge hym enfourmeth home comynge theyr expleyt tolde hym euerydele pryamus lyketh wonder wele manly haue borne oute made puplysshe towne aboute tydynges great solempnyte hye lowe thorugh cyte ioye leste remembraunce halowe holde feste thanke theyr goddes full humble wyse obseruaunces sacryfyse theyr auters great deuocion whyle tenedon holdeth soiour quene eleyne whiche gan reufully compleyne hir vnkouthe lyfe dwelle straungers desolate amonges prysoners fer sequestred away hir countre solytarye captyuyte wepeth cryeth pytous chere burbly wawes hir eyen clere lyke welle stremes hir chekes rayne constraynt hir inwarde payne full ofte daye hir songe welaway sobbynge voyce fer away departed hir menelaus whose absence rage furyous hir lyfe hateth curseth eke fortune wo euer doth contune without soiour alway hir bretherne pollux castore loue hir doughter dere pale grene wexyth hir chere whylom fressher sene lyllye stalke gren ala chaunged hir rosen hewe euer hir wo encreaseth newe lyke woman beholde aye wepte water wolde tyll laste hir heuynesse parys hir came gentyllesse hir comforte appese hir rage besyeth hym hir sorowes aswage sayeng hir may mene ye ala goodly fresshe quene lyst thus selfe sorowynge diffygure wonder greatly ye may endure moche water causeles shede wepynge haue dewed wede lyke conduyte stremes ran downe lyke penytaunt contryciowne ye dis aye ala let fare let ouer go wepynge thought heuynesse lady distresse make ende greuaunce ease comforte pleasaunce men may truste well ye shall haue folye sorowe thus raue let passe ouer sharpe shoures trouthe ye youres lyst shall haue suffysaunce ferforth habundaunce ye hadde amonge grekes ensure thynge fere shall holde haue hyght trouthe trewe knyght worde dede herte entere anone dolefull chere myght sobbynge tho suffyse answered agayne full lowly wyse wo e quod lothe lese syth caught take myschefe vnto wyll may nat seye bounde must obeye vnder daunger may nat flee holde discryued captyuytee pye wot also nature drede ne longeth vnto womanhede straunge soyle stryue rebelle namely hir quarelle shall haue fauoure susteyned lyst haue pyte myne goodlyhede ye may god deserue thanke mede wyll rewarde iustely tho comforte care wo lady myne quod parys may lyke deuys shalbe truste right wele trouthe fer fele thynge may pleasaunce ye shall haue habundaunce ensure heste nat fallyble nat agaste fully credyble wordes hestes euerychone therwithall ladde hir right anone place royall apparayle comforte hir wolde auayle secretly betwene two parys firste without spake vnto hir sayde lady dere fayne nat speke herte entere hope ye shall dede fynde wherfore pray enprente mynde say remembraunce saye sythe ye purueaunce goddes brought thereto fortune eke wyll dare afferme playnly fyrste disposed haue nat wyrste good ye must take wherfore rede let ouer shake heuynesse loke ye glad lyght countre though ye owne lande faythfully vnderstande ye shall haue moche habundaunce euery parte full suffysaunce may plesaunt thynge dare make auaunt countre shalbe founde plente passe habounde rychely grekes yonder though ye fro sonder lande called achaye ye haue cause dismaye syth worshyp reuerence honour gretter excellence ye shalbe cherysshed ye afore ye playne ye haue forbore owne lorde left sole ye make wo dole ye shall haste sette better ease certaynely nat displease offende vnto womanhede stede hym purpose drede wedde trewe man loue serue euer without feynynge lyues ende lowly kynde dilygent laborous whylom menelaus euery thynge lustes obeye haue trouthe tyll tyme deye pand though word playne loue god haue disdayne request grutche nat leste stocke royall descended come hye blode menelay byrthe gode loue trewe euer chaunge newe pwherfore stynte thus playne wepe let comforte bosome crepe wo appese whiche nat worthe hawe myrthe let herte adawe beseche womanhede wordes take hede palas quod myght befalle haue left frendes one alle straunge lande alone shulde made mone haue cause god wote pleye chekes kepe dreye salte teres ala wyll nat none ende myn aduersyte good fayth agaynst kynde sodaynely put mynde thylke thynge ioye smerte worlde sytteth next herte ala sore destrayned sythe goddes haue ordayned better chaunce hope vnto must take gre humbly accepte also theyr sonde feble theyr power withstonde wherfore shall agayne wyll stryue albe wo herte fele ryue consente lowly admytte thylke thynge fro whiche may nat flytte maugre wyll necessyte fully obeye ye lyst wyll nat helpe though sayde nay thus payneth euer may lytell lytell hir sorowe aswage shulde aye lyue wo rage lese hir selfe tendre creature herte stele ne myght nat endure aye woman maner kynde nat sorowe make ende tyll leyser haue wept theyr fulle laste whan gynne dulle make sorowe happe faste grace soone ouer caste lyghtly catche comforte theyr smerte tendre yt men may conuerte wo ioye thought disseuer storme may laste euer clerkes wyse bokes lyst discerne thynge vyolente may nat eterne stormes phebus bryghter comforte counsayle paris dawed hir olde sorowe euen lyke glad morowe kynde seweth derke blacke nyght processe hir herte wexeth lyght hir wepynge dryed welle lyke storye shall anone v tell phow parys receyued troye home comynge howe wedded fayre eleyne capytulo xiiij whan quene called eleyne adawed hir drery peyne wawes hir heuy chere hir chekes gonne clere parys herte fresshe amerous haste hath sente kynge pryamus hors men apparayle clothes golde full noble entayle made eleyne wrought none ryche perle many sondry stone agayne hir comynge troye towne parys fro tenedowne shappeth hym lede hir troye pryamus mette weye full ryally faste may hye many lorde companye full many lady fresshe well beseyne many mayde ryde ageyne firste estate comuners hadde parys prysoners set ordre tweyne tweyne rode next quene eleyne dephebus vpon syde knyghtes enuyrondyde ryde next hym rode worthy eneas troyan called pollydamas meyne suynge eche degre gentylmanly ioye se eeche kepynge certayne space forthe rode softe pace tyll kynge mette sodaynly receyued solempnely beste coude goodly toke reyne hande quene eleyne hir conueyed forthe cyte great prease abode se sondry folke shoued faste croude shyrle trumpettes yreysed loude vp skye goth blysfull sowne whan people entreth towne many nother dyuerse instrument tofore gate went sondry wyse made melodye heuenly armonye musyke touched vpon strynge corde euen one iustly accorde wolde herte rauysshe ioye whan entred troye amydde palayse kynge pryamus alyghte anone faste euer myghte chambre ryche well besey quene eleyne haste doth conuey comaundynge herte wyll thought offycers hir fayle nought thynge bethynke spyces parted anone ye wyne drynke kynge toke leue tyll suppyre whyles chaungeth hir attyre pbut ioye towne euery place men went vp downe rude sothely wryte moche herte troyans delyte safe sounde retourned parys wende haue ioye paradys well sped iourne hath nat one loste meyne wherof herte glad lyght haste next nyght wryte guydo without taryeng longe erely morowe afore large songe pallas temple myn auctor sayth assured othe eke fayth bonde wedlocke hym eleyne euer laste atwene tweyne knotte knyt sacrament thus done fully assent firste kynge also aduyse cyte fauour paryse feste great solempnyte contynued moche ryalte weddynge myrthe solace thorugh towne eyghte dayes space shulde wryte reuell ye daunces fresshe aray countenaunces scole touch lokes amerous pryue grutchyng yt ialous great iustes bordes tornaye amydde palestre many sondry playe dyuerse course eke euery feste large plente done vnto leste straunge mete maner seruyse haue none englysshe deuyse passe ouer nat pbut whan weddynge came ere cassandra firste dyde espye thousande sythe ala gan crye pytous wo vntrussed heeres sayde thus speynte teeres wretched troye errynge case within thy selfe suffre trespase consente vnto suche folye susteynynge foule auoutrye parys shulde take vnto wyue quene eleyne whose husbande lyue wofull troye cruell thy fate beware almoste late tyme come thou shalte destroyed many fader shall sone se hole morowe shalbe slayne eue amyddes felde wyll hym sore greue many wyfe sore shall bewepe se husbande large woundes depe gryde thorugh body pale colde grene ala shall ye sorowe mowe sustene wretched moders shall ye endure se childerne cruell aduenture afore slayne without remedye wyll nat helpe though ye clepe crye moder myn eccuba quene shalt thou byde sharpe stoundes kene thy worthy sone seafore slawe felde cruelte idrawe blynde people deth thou takest hede ne wyl thou worke rede case prudent wyse take away eleyne fro parys right requereth without hir lorde iustely hir restore pwhat trowe ye thefte cruell dede shall passe thus nay nay without drede swerde vengeauce shall full sharpe byte offence shall bere wyte paleys hous se within throwe toures hye layde erthe lowe ala ala saye eleyne vnhappy woman causer peyne harde vnsely also graceles vnwelfull woman distourbler pe thou hast v brought myschefe kyndled bronde sette v afere ala thou arte grounde roote many drery feste fymerall shall beholde amonge v towne wyse cassandra vp downe aboute ran subarbe strete cryeth euer euer mete full ofte sythe ala welaway tyll pryamus bycause hir affray noyse dyde make without anone doth hir take bynde faste fetred pryson without mercy remyssyon toke hede hir sadde trouthe hir wordes routhe shet hir vp bondes great stronge without pyte abydde longe thus pryson whyle leue hir morne grekes wyll agayne retourne vnhappy tyme ye whyle fortune falsely gan smyle vpon troyans bad merye whiche hyely gan theyr goddes herye wenynge ioye haue assured wele thyng aduertynge turnynge ye whele hir lasteth stable throwe wha men truste hir make amowe tourne hir forhede hir face wrythe suche ioye hath hir doubylnesse kythe wrappe hir clerenesse vnder cloude agaynst whose myght may hy shroude wha flatereth tha l st tryste ioye troyans lytell wyste mente theyr confusiowne whyle aboute towne wende grekes haue goten full recure theyr damage euer haue sure thorugh thylke praye parys wonne wycked fame rumoure yronne swyfte wyng yt haue wrought menelay tydynges ybrought whyles abode nestor pyra firste temple cithera spoyled robberye golde treasoure tyrannye vpon men troyans execute assaylynge sute grekes made cruelly ne spared vtterly man woman came theyr waye ne toke ladde praye theyr shyppes also fyght afore castell nyght pand alder laste hereth wyfe loued moche lyfe tenderly god wote thousande folde astoned herte waxed colde stone pale hewe hertely wo inly gan renewe first whan herde hir name sowne without anone fell swowne ne myght endure stande tyll duke nestor toke hym hande hym awoke deedly swowgh ala quod haue lost howgh lyues luste hertely suffysaunce come deth make greuaunce fully ende thy cruell darte wounded thorugh euery parte herte also korue euery peyne wyfe myn owne eleyne deuorced frome welaway farewell ioye farewell myn olde play haue straungers possession whiche wyll full confusion ala noot cherysshe trete fayre eleyne mete ye gone pensyfenesse slethe may nat wayte dethe amyd wo menelay shope hym go reygne lytell besyde axeth hors sayde wolde ryde sool complayne yt felte hym greue whyle nestor wyll nat leue go hym consolacion frendely right hauynge compassion hym comforte full myght edynge hym many worthy knyght reygne menelaus firste storye telleth v sente agamenon castor come hym anon pollux myght whan come thre sawe brother myschef brought almoste murdred owne thought without abode wyse agamenon gyue hym comforte consolacion dyde labour dylygence entere sayenge hym right ye shall brother myn wo heuynesse deedly sorowe thus inly may oppresse knyghtly herte trouble manhede furyously iwys nede though right requered vtterly sorowe hadde cause yet semeth iuste prouydence ye shuld slyely dissymule offence syth eche wyse man aduersytee shulde fayne chere kepe secree inwarde wo bynde hym distresse manly force rathest compesse spirite ire melancolye people soonest myght espye doctryne prudent whan man furye rent fayne chere tyll tyme se leysere vengeaunce kyndele may fyere sorowe shewed shall nat fayne taketh hede doth thynges twayne causeth frendes syghe sore enemyes reioyse thy frende herte sorye nature thyne enemye glad thy mysaduenture wherfore herte wha wo doth haboude fayne gladnesse thyne enemye confounde shewe chere thou roughtest nought moste greuous thy thought wher thou hast mater complayne make good face glad porte ye fayne teres though thou distylle rende thy selfe thou woldest spylle helpeth nat legge thy greuaunce nouther honour pursute vengeauce sorowe makynge mowe execute though last ay ther cometh therof fruyte men lay dissymule wronge slyghe herte stronge pesyble smerte token hath manly herte nat wepe woman theyr rage whiche contrary hye courage worde wepyng auege payne meanes worshyp attayne let v swerde nat wordes fyght tunge appese mahod preue myght worde wynde water wepe though tempest floddes depe two encrease euer moo may nat augment woo soon therof prees gyue hym audyence anone full sobre wyse began tale shall deuyse syres quod praye take hede noble renowmede wysdome worthynesse manhode eke hye prowesse knyghthode reporte fame thorugh world reboudeth yo name douteles floure chyualrye men may fynde companye whosawe euer manly men yfere togyder met yonge fresshe couragyous also well besene haue orso lykely sythe worlde began without raskayle many knyghtly man kynges duke many another lorde wyll one accorde one herte assembled place fortune goddes theyr grace nat behynde iourney repreue may nat fayle purpose acheue pfor deme hym playnely arage wer e wood durste vyage wyse perturbe presume take agayne v outher assume myght hym malys excyte worthynesse neuer lyte v prouoke ire offence ne shulde mortall recompence aquyte mede lyeth myght haue amoge v many worthy knyght amonges whiche hondred yet mo coude chese able go manly force knyghtly suffysaunce take hym vengaunce vpon troyans hymselfe alone whiche gadred echone men suffycyent execute sume entent accomplysshe felycyte cause mene whiche assembled bothe hye lowe nat vnknowe shamefully troyans haue v greued prouoked v wylfully ymeued ryse agayne haue recure ryght wronges done force myght wherfore let v one assente wyll sette haue right skyll redresse fynde complayne one herte besy payne vpon troyans werre make suppose shall awake shall lerne thense wende remembre worldes ende hereafter shall dare take hande presume grece lande bolde whyle haue lyfe space agayne grekes trespace whose offence sayth late within herte brennynge hate feruent hete gredy yre fro day day setteth v fyre reneweth constreynt payne inwardely shall nat fayne must reason hye greuaunce selfe enforce vengaunce right requereth iuste sorowe compelleth v bothe eue morowe troyans harmes bewreke stoppe tunges speke reprefe vylenye must attones shape remedye foon hensforthe may drede worse v god forbede tyme comynge thorugh pacyence lykely suffre theyr importable offence passe forthe take nohede syth neuer yet grekes coude rede man dyde reprefe theyr name iustely myght rebounde theyr shame withouten quyte agayne thorugh theyr manhode openly playne man myght seyne wyse reporte amys new shall nat dissymule case chere oppressed dredefull face let slyde lyghtly ouer go great offence late whiche wolde tourne vnto v oures great reprefe successoures tyme comynge shamefully bespoke grekes vurste wroke vpon theyr foon whiche may nat ensure sythe one wyll refourme wronge therwithall myghty stronge coude brede lengthe right reherse power strenthe durste euer worthynesse assayle ne shulde without fayle repente herte ende rewe saue troyans day newe wylfulnesse foly rage lande made vyage vnware v theyr pray home wente whiche shall full hastely repente theyr trespas great offencyowne pfor worlde knoweth vp downe late gone grekes fewe vpon troyans theyr power dyde shewe slewe theyr kynge called lamedowne fader pryam kynge towne fordyde toures cyte slewe vp comynalte grekes swerde yt lyst spare amonge v seruytude care coplayne theyr harme yt may nat recured may stande full assured agayne v holde chaumpartye haue worthy companye lykely thousande acheue foure fyue lyghtly myght preue yet one thynge afferme well dare comynge troyans well ware theyr laboure theyr dilygence agaynst v make resystence theyr myght knowe doute gadre frendes countres aboute helpe theym strength theyrnede v withstande myght spede fynally one thynge counsayle hauen ferther sayle may fortunat one assent make ambassyat prudently wende delos haste sende whiche ile lytell besyde discretely iourney prouyde may haue better hap grace appollo patron place haue hym may spede fynall answere great nede expleyt shall fall ye wyll assent counsayle eke leste echone thought beste condescende conclusyon without contradiccyon attones without drede prayse counsayle wyse rede therupon discretely oughte sayth story euen thus wroughte phow grekes sente achylles pyrro de yle delos haue answere god appollo shulde spede iourney capitulo xvij tyme agamenon concluded hath fully reason ye haue herde sentence fyned grekes herte ful enclyned one voyce accorded playnely thus achylles also pirrodus comyn profyte sythe sage shall take charge message appollo answere gone shyppe haste anone sayle forthe large see towarde deluos prosperytee aryued ycome lande whiche yle vnderstande myn auctor sayth without le hath syght amonges cyclades men rockes haue moche ado amyd sec called helespontico whiche yle make descripcyon muste whyle make disgressyon fro mater myn auctor doth yle isydorus soth reherseth playnly latona quene appollo firste dyane shene childed hath iubyter hir lorde whan iuno discorde wryte ouyde alytell whyle befylle lytell yle temple whylom dedycate vnto appollo also consecrate worshyp olde foundacyon honoured great deuocyon bycause appollo bemes clere flood firste dyde appere shewed horne rather soone dyane eke called moone whiche shewynge yle bereth name day great fame oonly apperynge ylke twayne delos greke sayne shewynge apparence thus began great reuerence appollo firste honour eke hym idone many greke suster called dyane pale moone waxe wane called paynems goddesse whylom wod hunteresse lady sonne hir brother yle hath lordshyp none oonly theyr natyuyte shewed theyr lyght firste countre whiche yle grekes also calle ortygya theyr langage alle bycause curlewes firste iseyne otygyas seyne curlewe grewe vnderstande firste engendred lande pand appollo called eke titan tyme moche worshyp wan longe afore made sterre iubyter whan helde werre also ycalled phebus ynamed phycius pheton victorye whan hym stewe encrease glorye great serpent erthe lowe arowes myghty bowe whiche conqueste great god cupyde hadde enuye euen thorugh syde wounded hym depe herte arowe gold yt made hym sore smerte pheton phebus made fyne came phetonysses deuyne mene woman deuyneresses thorugh dede men false sorceress one whylom reysed samuel loue saule byble tell temple large longe olde stature pured golde full great hye huge weyghte therin thorugh deuylles sleyghte spirite vnclene false illusyon gaue answere euery questyon nat ydoll dombe stocke stone thus people deceyued euerychone fende brought great errour worshyppe suche false honour sacryfyce cursed mawmentrye wyse began ydolatrye place telle caste longe abode laste compendyously purpose descryue gynnynge ende ye shall blyue without ambygnyte byrthe natyuyte criste ihesu incarnacy owne ydolles braste fell downe vanysshed brought nought whan herodes blesfull childe sought thorugh malys cruelte horryble holy wrytte recordeth byble whiche pursuyte persecucion dyde apere auysion hooly aungell ioseph slepe bad hym ryse also take kepe vnto childe also marye go waye herode hym aspye egipt great regyon lyke gospell maketh mencyon right anone came lande none ydoll yt vpright myght stade shyuered vnto peces smale holy wrytte playnely tale recorded friste isaye lorde esy skaye ascende shulde holde forthe weye towarde egipt therwith shulde deye mawmetrye longer dwelle iewes recorde ysmaelle firste mawmetrye fonde made claye ydoll honde paynems wryte telle v alder firste promotheus founde ydolles shortly conclude symulacrum cometh symylitude thynge playnely lyknesse made man ymage expresse vnto whiche paynems theyr gyse false honour cursed sacryfyse begonne firste ryte drede man saye belus firste began suche false worshyp suche mawmettye theyr bokes clerkes specefye assirye lorde gouernour whose deth sone honour nynus hyghte ymage dyde make worshypped oonly sake brent golde false affeccion sette vp consolacion mynde memoryall vnto whiche herte wyll ignoraunce flesshely loue dyde honour god aboue temple moste excellence made people reuerence sayde heuen deyfyed man durste denyed tyll soone lytell whyle wycked spyryte folkes begyle ydoll entrede abyde gaue answere vpon euery syde people lyste demaunde agayne wyll comaunde obeye fully folke assyrye whiche vnto god dyde great iniurye makynge people suche errour falle belus bell hym calle balym belphegore felle errour alway belzebub named also whiche name made wordes two bel zebub thus signefye bel god zebub flye belzebub togydre specyfyes ioyned one great god flyes fayned false ydolatrye gan worlde worshyp mawmetrye pfor saturne god goddes gan theyr errour falsely call whylom myghtykyng crete gaue hym name planete heuen hath large spere poetes theyr fable lere thorugh sapyence sawe dyuyne prouydence sone shulde hym descende pand iuno goddes wende shulde hy playnely fro reigne expelle suffre hym lenger dwelle kyngdome whan came age wherof saturne fyll suche arage wyll shape remedye therfore byddynge wyfe whan childe bore hym shulde brynge anone stede wherof hym brought stone saue hir childe dyde hir besynesse saturne thorugh gredynesse stone deuoureth melancolye thus saturne bokes lye hadde sone thre doughter mo iubyter neptunus pluto iubyter grettest name moste renowmed worthyest fame amonge paynems veryfyed hye haue hym magnefyed hym calle god fyre eyre nert saturne borne heyre nert hym bokes rede god batayle myghty mar rede next appollo clere shene bryght dayes eye voyder nyght cheryssher fruyte herbe floure corne whiche god lyke sayde toforne delos worshypped honoured venus often hath socoured many louer fayre lusty quene aledge theyr woundes grene firste hurte hir firy bronde goddesse many londe worlde hath hir demeyne faste enbraced hir firy cheyne mene lady called venus next ordre mercurius speche hath moste excellence rethoryke sugred eloquence musyke songe armonye hath lordshyp hole regalye next moone wexe wane called lucyna also eke dyane delos hath hir mancyon lyke tofore maked mencyon full myght horned pale lady chaunge mutabylyte selde one halte hir tyme fare borne hir clyme aye delyte thynges newe whose herte cladde many sondry hewe dyuers theyr affeccyons wyse sondry regyons mawmetrye venym ronne lyke clerkes well deuyse konne fynde maurycyens worshyp iulam egipcyens honoure si theyr konnynge whylom doughter ynachus kynge taughte first theyr lode ere sowe also letter rede knowe lecture sette theyr besynesse whiche thynge calle hir goddesse iubyter honoured crete whylom helde souerayne sete leyde many dyuerse charge egles beten baner large lorde eyre londe see royall kyngdome deuydynge thre hyest hymselfe doth contune hole see gaue vnto neptune laste erthe holde see royall gaue pluto god infernall alder laste whan stellyfyed iubyter moste magnyfyed crete aboute ouer made memoryall large tombe statue lofte hym honoured theyr rytes ofte encens sacryfyse mater ferther deuyse larynes besy dylygence theyr rytes dyde reuerence goddes credyble called fawny muysyble haue hered wellynge wodes grene albe men theyr fygure may nat sene romayns deuyne moste honour haue theyr god quyryne whiche whylom bokes telle v amonges called romulus bylte firste walles towne herde came suche renowne thorugh manhode worthynesse spere bokes sayne expresse hede pytched grounde gan anone lyke founde florysshe floure budde myracle nature hadde none obstacle wexe grene fresshe blomes newe manhode men hym knewe knyghthode great fame pthe worthy knyght romebare ye name hym quyryte called hye heuen whan stalled amonge goddes ydeyfyed thus romeyns haue hym glorifyed theyr god golde great expense rede athenyenses hole herte chosen serue goddesse called mynerue pallas eke hir cristall shelde neptunus euen amyd felde helde champartye woman theyr syde men full surquedous pryde defendeth hym gyuynge name athene cyte moste fame sayne whether shulde right name cyte tyll befell gan stryue sodeynly sprange fayre olyue pallas part grene fayre blossomynge agayne welle gan sprynge hym pluto water large depe whiche thynge appollo toke good kepe whiche dome nat reckeles olyue tokeneth loue pe water trouble contek werre stry fe gaue sentence anone diffynytyfe pallas shulde called mynerue palme playnely stryue discerue anone gaue name towne called hye discrecyowne athene whiche speeyall sayne cyte inmortall wyldome firste began floure skyll cyte dyde honoure myghty pallas goddesse scyence hir aye moste hadde reuerence paue theyr regyon whorshyp moste quene cytheron mene venus full doubylnesse afore somwhat dyde expresse hir temple full solempnely sette hir hyest moste rychely gold asure hir statue paynte coloures may neuer faynte sette hir vp hyest see temple men may se stant naked wawy see aboute hir goddess thre assigned besy attendaunce awayte hir hir obseruaunce floures fresshe blewe rede whyte hir aboute delyte hir hede hath chapelet rose rede full pleasauntly yset hede downe vnto hir fote sondry gomes oyntemer sore ennoynte swetter smelle enuyron poetes telle dowues whyte flyenge eke sparowes besyde cupyde arowes hir blynde sone hurte dere loseth ofte smyte wote nat must nedes bycause blynde thus honoured mynde amonge people venus goddesse naxyens theyr besynesse serue bachus myghty god wyne whose lycour moste precyous fyne recomforte hertes glade refresshe hewes fade face pale maketh wyttes sharpe loseth tunges make loude carpe causeth walke lyberte discure thynge secree without aduyse discrecyon wyne hath domynacyon secretnesse may kept mewe bachus serue sewe amonge hym haue suche deuocion whyle voyde reason hasty wood without drede also toty theyr hede voyde power myght haue foot stande vp ryght yet iargaunt pye pale chered glasy eye full reason tyll wynde spent man woman vyolent veryly beest vnresonable dome holde eke vnable accepted companye whan theyr tunge wadeth lye ne may brynge forthe worde thus bachus stronge myghty lorde ofte causeth folkes erre debate make werre hastynesse nede wherfore wysdome men drede sleyghty werkynge falle snare feble braynes mesure spare vnwarely arested take bachus make shake feuer worse tercyen custome cotydyen alterat bachus myghty iou affered tournynge hous fordreynt drye lande whan hath loste bothe foot hande strawe playeth lyke ape deuoutely gynneth gape oddeth ofte iowsy hede hadde heuy cappe lede condycyon entre maye relygyon myghty bachus habylyte whiche lorde hath soueraynte hony mylke therto bawme ryche also lordshyp hath hye power deuyne bothe grape euery vyne gyue nourysshynge influence honour reuerence reysed moste vnderstande amonge vynters euery maner lande bycause gracyous lymme worshyp vulcanus god fyre iubyters smythe whiche forgeth blacke slythe great thonder hydous horryble leuenes whylom vysyble west oryent gasteth v dredefull dent smotry smythe swarte vulcanus whylom herte ialous towarde venus wedded wyfe wherof rose dedely mortall stryfe whan mar gan hir firste espye hye malys cruell false enuye thorugh shynyge phebus bemes bryght lyenge bedde mar hir owne knyght whiche herte brente glede makynge sclaundre brode sprede gan theron falsely muse god forbede man accuse lytell woman euer loue lette harde disseuer though suche thynge gentyllesse passe ouer lyghtly bere none heuynesse lest thou woman odyous yet smythe false vulcanus hadde thus espyed amonge paynems yet deyfyed falsely woke haue hym sette laste boke amonge goddesse false mawmetrye wyse gan ydolatrye ye haue herde thorugh oppynyons people errynge theyr affeccyons false trouthe cerche techynge holy chirche holy doctryne tradycyons shall despyse suche oppyons whiche fende founde nat oflate whan aungelles heuen create hadde prelacye prophete called ysaye wryteth right thus cedres grene paradyse nat fayre sene planys fyr heyghte sothe sayne hyghnesse myght nat attayne tree delycyous paradyse natso precyous nouther syght semelynesse egall hym fayrenesse thorugh pryde surquydrye whan sayde god sytte hys wyll lyke also set see hye northe passynge degree caste downe relygyons fayre heuenly mansyons sodaynely pytte helle perpetuelly dwelle sayde whan fylle ferre fylle thou thou morowe sterre myddes stone bryght persynge firy theyr lyght whylom thy great bryghtnesse called lucyfer criste sayth expresse gospell sawe fro heuene sathan descende lyke firy leuene olde serpent solowe falle heebre theyr tunge calle pbemoth doth latyn playne expresse beest rude full cursednesse vyle serpent leuyathan isydre well descryue whiche kynde neuer conuersaunte welles trouble hath moste haunte amonges watres large see sayth dauyd lyke ye may se sauter makynge mencyon snake monstruous dragon full venym harde grace whiche see large great space foule adder hath mansyon vnto mankynde illusyon whylom sawe ye holy monke bradan sayled occyan thorowe de ecte apytte horryble foule hydous credyble abyde tortuous serpent vnto daye playnely iugement malys enuyed mankynde whiche wt gynne sleyghtes fynde came faders firste paradyse deceyue bet deuyse couertly worme passage toke serpent lyknesse ymage chere loke countenaunce lyke mayde hath resemblaunce woman recordeth bede deceytes rather spede mene oonly nat elles behynde clerkes telles lyke serpent wombe backe tayle whan gan hym assayle towarde eue whan gan glyde firste enquereth hir roke lyde god forbade eten tree whiche ete sothly shulde lyke goddes knowynge good yll right forthwith gan sulfyll fendes heste theyr eyen vnclosed theyr gylte sodaynely deposed paradyse wretchydnesse lyue laboure sorowe distresse thus fende firste whan hetoke forme snake woman loke made tunge hir hede meue false engyne mankynde greue doth trauayled wycked spirites vaxed assayled meue tunges falsely breke blasphemye thynge speke serpent leuyathan contunynge aye falsely gan cursed yools dombe v fe blynde full ofte speketh spirites fynde whiche fendes dauid wryte certayne goddes folkes vayne honour rytes supersticious whylom appollo delphicus lyke tofore ye haue herde deuyse whiche ought inough suffyse trowe cause myn auctor reherseth grounde gynnynge idolatrye cause ought espye sawe mater nat knowe lyche well bothe hye lowe perauenture plesaunce hath grounde put remembraunce false goddes mawmetrye moste poysye storye resorteth soone agayne achilles ye haue herde saye pirrodus haue waye ynome temple thyder ycome haue answere theyr embassatrye great appollo whiche may nat lye prestes haue theyr counsayle take temple praye wake tyll may fynde vnto theyr entent haue answere houre conuenyent theyr purpose leyser opportune pand one herte longe contune prayenge fastynge oblacyons sacrifyse sondry orysons tofore god awaytynge alway faste tyll answered laste voyce sayde achilles twye home grekes faste thou hye thou hyder sente say sothely sume theyr entent shalbe fulfylled without wordes mo shall troye go abyde many stronge batayle laste without fayle ten yere daye wynne shall towne brynge playnely destrucciowne walle toures shall falle ruyne theyr purpose fyne kynge pryamus ecuba wyfe theyr sone mortall stryfe shall slayne brother brother fyne may none shall none escape place suche grekes lyketh vnto grace routhe mercy take thus ende make whiche answere achilles glad lyght herte myght thanketh appollo blesfull eure sodaynely sort aduenture selfe tyme befyll wonder thynge troye fro pryamus kynge sent bysshop ca haue answere whose name calcas came sool without pres houre whyle achilles present man great scyence mene calcas hadde experyence specyally calculacion sort also dyuynacion lerned astronomye whan tyme dyde espye haue answere conuenyent appollo lyke entent tofore maked memorye entred oratorye doynge rytes obseruaunces lyke custome circumstaunces besely gan knele praye thynges deuoutely saye god crye calle ful stronge appollo wolde nat prolonge sodaynely answere gan attame pand sayde calcas twyes name right well ware thou ne tourne agayne troye towne vayne fynally lerne shorte tyme shall destroyed sothe whiche may nat denyed wherfore wyll thou allyed grekes achilles go anone wyll beso shall haue haue disposed victorye honour may disposed fatall ne may nat varye thou shalt necessarye counseylynge yeuynge rede right helpynge theyr good spede worde rose hym vp calcas achilles went easy pa whan came presence great honour moche reuerence receyued lyke estate soone confederate swore togydre bonde assuraunce one without varyaunce haste togydre gone theyr shyppes shope forth anone pirrodus goynge theyr syde hale vp anker lenger byde sayle forthe calcas twayne towarde grece nedeth nat complayne wynde wawe tyll aryued athene stode vpon see large cyte olde foundacion achilles kynge agamenon hath calcas brought also pirrodus whan grekes story telleth v assembled togyder went tofore kynge calcas represent lordes lenger dwell right anone achilles gan tell without abode delos mette tofore appollo answere fette god hath playnely determyned grekes purpose shalbe fyned vpon troyans bad calcas also wyse troye go grekes abyde stylle tyll theyr purpose fynally fulfylle whiche thynge grekes glad chere calcas accepte herte full entere one confederat bonde one water londe without chaunge varyaunce othe made put remembraunce agayne fully hym assure cherysshe hym whyle theyr lyfe may dure wele wo
