made ende parte theyr lodgynge wende tyll morowe sterry nyght whan aurora gladded wt ye lyght phebus vemes grekes vp aryse theyr goddes many sacryfyse honour maye deuoutly holdynge feste daye theyr rytes meynt loue drede remembraunce good spede answere yt goddes haue sent agreable vnto theyr entent pirrodus achilles amonges pres calcas come tofore agamenon lordes syttynge enuyron lyke theyr estate eche place dewe humbly gan salewe vpon knee sobre coutenaunce prayed displesaunce stynte whyle gyue hym audyence right anone made sylence amonge calcas gan abrayde euen thus full soberly sayde osyres quod lordes dere kynges prynces duke sonoble echone worthy famous eke manly vertuous whiche place present nat fyne chefe entent cause also ye echone assembled troye togone power great strengthe purpose longe drawe lengthe differred forthe fro day daye damage platly naye longe ye soiourne yle trowe ye nat pryam whyle hath espyes amonge pryuelye wote wele saye faythfullye knowe fyne gouernaunce whyles may make purueaunce hym defende whyle ye ydell reste semeth sothly ye nat beste abydynge suche delayes great harme may fall certayne nay preue thus playnely whyle ye enmyes graunte lyberte puruey may myghty hade enforce power withstande theyr frendes theyr allyaunce leyser make theyr ordynaunce folye ye differre syth ye redy make werre ennemyes euery circustaunce thynge may quarell auaunce hasty suyte wyll sharper byte iren hoote tyme smyte nat abyde tyll colde nouther plye wyll folde go sette vpon one accorde shyppe anone within borde enhaste tyme remewe myght quarell pursewe agaynst haue trespassed many dayes somer passed many monthes ronne ouer slyde titan ofte chare hath ryde eest west wawes depe stremes bathed whyle ye haue leyne aslepe spent tyme place thus whyle wynde called zephyrus benyngnely enspyred hath lofte tempre eyer wether fayre softe calme see wawes stylle playne whyles ye waste dayes vayne whan foon therto take hede wyll suppose drede bolde sette lyte truste forsothe wyll quyte trewely lyke bounde thynke ye haue goddes founde towarde benyngne fortunat honour saued hye lowe estat shall forthe ingratytude prouoke nat purpose delude wylfully slouthe fortune wonder though nat contune towardes shewe theyr grace wherfore rede hense pace demynge grekes playnely see weryed faynted hadde longe saylynge parbraked forbroke wherfore caue haue wroke sodaynely sette hede put themselfe aduenture drede rakelnesse vn aduysely wherof selfe vnhappely befell whan grekes mette speres longe swerdes sharpe whette eche manhode shewe cause troyans fewe yssue dyde folylye felde nat parted egallye grekes innumerable mete troyans nat able tyme myght nat suffyse toke passynge hye empryse yet ne wold thyng wdrawe tyll wounded yslawe ouerlayne grekes vtterly bore downe cruelly mercyles guy dath reporte behoueth home agayne resorte nede necessytee attones gan flee mene suche lefte lyue castell ed full blyue ne myght lenger holde felde agaynst grekes spere shelde feble shortly conclude abyde great multytude flee grekes great pase ne cease nat sewe chase full hastely castell gate entre cruell fate kyll slee hye lowe spare none ne lyste wyghte knowe none estate felly hym oppresse fonde golde eke rychesse vnto shyppe caryed anone castell lefte nat stone aboue another turned vp downe walle toure chefe donge owne thynge stode vnder myne whan brought vnto ruyne grekes anone theyr shyppes haste one assent purpose faste without abode one wyll herte fro hauen playnely dyuerte sayle towarde tenedowne stronge castell whiche fro troye towne distaunce sixe myle stode full tresoure rychesse gode replenysshed habundaunce whan theyr ordynaunce ysayled haue bothe safe sounde fro see taken haue grounde theyr pleasaunce wonder agreable syght place delytable holsome eyre soyle right fayre grene lusty playnes goodly sene also habundaunt vytayle replenysshed may auayle osteynge sowgyoures firste lande full fresshe floures plenteuous bothe corne grayne wyne fruyt thyng lay barayne beste foules passyngly plente faste stode also see full habundaunt fysshe fynde season euery maner kynde whan within castell grekesse londed fere without abode arme went oute vpon make hydous shoute stuffyng castell wt meyne strong behynde toke theyr way guydo fynde towarde theyr foon knyghtly set vpon right forthe grekes eke anon mette vpon syde full surquydous right full pryde clenly armed harneys ofstele fresshe arayed besene wele felde thycke sworme eche syde men may beholde seen spradde playne downe vnto stronde tyll laste mette honde honde assemble square speres grounde hurtle yfere many blody wounde good day saluynge stroke felle men herde rynge bassenettes stroke rounde aboute cruelly fyre sprange oute amonge tuftes brode bryght shene foyle golde fethers whyte grene eke brestes perced many shelde besagues fleed brode felde many men ley mortall founde full dedely pale lawe grunde face gruf blody stremes wyde aldermost vpon grekes syde slaughter discomfyture myghtely troyans dyde endure tyll laste sewe multytude grek hewe mo forty agaynst one force abacke muste gone thyng lacke manhode dare sayne many haue ouer layne may lenger felde soiourne theyr castell home agayne retourne full great haste suche myght escape away lyue rape drede deth toke flyght horse backe troye towne full ryght wonder though haste faste gate chace grekes laste cruelly pursewe myght nat remewe troye syde forweryed fyght grekes slewe theyr full myght myght attayne may raunsome mercy gayne none estate without excepcyowne vnto tenedowne grekes went sette aboute troyan none myght escape whan hadde bulwerkes wonne skale walle begonne made saute manfully ofte troyans stode lofte put entre ne myght caste stone quarell bryght bowe turkey shote arbalasteres theyr gonners standynge corneres hym also caste wylde fyre yrous hate full hote theyr desyre lyke manly men selfe diffende aye grekes vp ascende cruelly put grounde tyll without ordynauce haue founde gynne deuysed none gonne great caste stone bent toures right lyne large sowes lowe myne vpon walle gone thycke made lyme stone entre many wayes seke sette theyr bastyles theyr hurdeys eke rounde aboute harde walle skalynge ladder saw e marcyalle gan vp caste hokes holde vp ascende sturdye grekes bolde tyll troyans crestes caste great stone whyle wolde laste callyowne eke grekes opresse wonder manly dyde theyr besynesse theyr diffence made plonge lowe caste quarell shote bowe thorugh olyettes necessyte put may none broke theyr neckes theyr shuldre boues felle square stone lye dede pyteous pale hewe grekes aye gan saute renewe multytude troyans assayle withstande gan fayle wexe feble rescuse came none force grekes gone thorugh ye walles whan haue broke troyans cruelly wroke fynally lefte none lyue slee kylle blyue walles theyr baners haue sette yonge olde myght bette goth wracke vpon troye syde ne wyll lenger byde treasoure golde may fynde caste hepe togyder bynde make spoyle within haste walles begyn pynacle toures also dungeowne brenne hewe bete downe soyle made euen playne great pray anone went agayne theyr shyppes glad lyght chere whan fyre flawmes clere castell consumed ybrent auyse prudent manly man worthy agamenon let make anone conuocacyon grekes bad shulde brynge golde treasour without tariynge praye wanne tenedowne presence conclusyowne may make distribucyon amonges without excepcyon lyke theyr desert vnto pore ryche departeth euery man lyche moste suche dyde beste disserue hymselfe hym lyste thynge conserue hath leuer theyr hertes gode suche hadde spente theyr owne blode manfully castell wynne largesse firste begynne ne fayleth nat well spede thorugh helpe men whan hath nede loue foloweth fredome comenly phow kynge agamenon assembled baron grece afore kepe counsayle sent vlixes kynge dyomede kynge pryamus message ca xix kynge let make cry kyng lordes oste duke erles come euery coste nexte morowe tofore hym appere nyght ypassed phebus gan clere hir emysperye larke songe whan kynge amonge grekes stronge vpon playne see royall faste moste chefe pryncypall lordes set theyr degre whan kynge sawe oportunyte made scylence euery lyeges standynge enuyron kynge chere sad eke iocounde speche full faucounde began tale sobre countenaunce effect whiche substaunce syres quod full worthy degre right necessyte compelled bothe hye lowe myght lyke ye well knowe redresse thynge amys thorugh worlde reported force power myght worthynesse euery wyghtes syght moste renowmed moste worshypable ydempt iuged moste able people lyklyest stonde parforme take honde euer grutcheth sayth nay yer semeth pay thylke power moste acceptable vnto goddes lengest stondeth stable deuoyde surquedry pryde kouth vpon euery syde eche lande bothe one many harmes greues haue befall thorugh rancoure oonly pryde wylfulnesse inportable coude expresse thorugh pryde done offence hye goddes make resistence tho surquydous whiche vyce contraryous may place abyde good fayth manhode pryde hath acqueyntaunce outher frendshyp alyaunce proude man confederate hym herte hye lowe estate nedes muste euer many necessyte lothsome firste enmy contrayre thynge may man moche appayre pryde sothe hye lowe degre wherfore rede playnly foule vyce herte arrace quarell may haue grace specyally dedes conueyed euer fall rightwysnesse volunte trouthe sothfaste guyde v directe rightfull lyne quarell shall aye honour shyne contune full felycyte ferthermore knowe ye come vengeaunce frendshyppe alyaunce vpon pryam wronges done olde hym haue ofte tolde vpon haue grounde ytake maked wake manfull hande castelles stronge ibete downe stonde haue longe take rychesse founde slewe men many blody wounde harmes mo done countre wote well theyr enmyte vnto v great moche afore dare saye double auenged myght v echone anone ye shulde se theyr great ire cruell huge execute without refuge yet sothe wote haue espyed beynge though nat askyred yet dare saye vtterly well ware faste ouer wote well also harmes haue whiche yet fresshe grene stronge myghty sustene werre v anone wolde gynne yet cyte whiche inne walled stronge toured rounde aboute wene fully doute meyne haue gadred theyr alyes shall nat wyn smale werre stryfe sothe hath prerogatyfe auauntage countre hym selfe diffendeth namely stuffed stronge frendes hym besyde alyes dothe abyde lyke rauen fethers blake within nest wyll ofte tyme make agayne faukon gentyll nature full harde diffence whyles may dure vaynquysshed outrayed yet whyle faukon delayed whyles rauen besyde nest doth flee within courte lyberte euery foule frowarde areste daunted owne neste yet wordes nat saye wyse put fraye knyghtly herte manly stable shulde doutabse troyans shall confounde theyr cyte whiche habounde playnely destroye albe stronge amonge shall fynally consumpt dethe thorowe grekes swerde yelde vp brethe pbut cause without drede saye thus ye take hede pryde presumpcyon aduerte discrecyon prudently reason nede haste may brydell lede ordayne hense wende laude prayse ende may reported haue deuysed many man hath nat aduysed pursuyte lacke prouydence se tofore aduertence shuld falle deth hath brought suche wylfull haste good thought v afore examynacyon well discussed reuolucyon pof thynkynge ofte nat repente firste remembre pryam sente v late oonly exyon yet holde kynge thelamon whiche v without aduysement vndiscretely denyed assent whiche hath v none aduauntage grounde rote full great damage thorugh wyse purueaunce hir hadde made delyueraunce harmes great eschewed parys pursewed temple cythera buylde besyde eirrea tresoure great also hadde iewelles hym ladde troye great rychesse slaughter men heuynesse yet made quene eleyne thorughoute grece great payne menelay hadde ben vnwrought hadde sene thought wysely afore exyon restored hadde nat harmes mourned v echone soth fastnesse spent laboure ydelnesse tresoure good wasted vayne come ferre fetche agayne quene eleyne costes inportable withouten harmes eschewable yet ne wote whether ioye aduersyte thynge shall tourne aboute syth ofte sythe dependent doute fatall thynge vnsyker vnstable fro gynnynge ofte varyable ende sene fortune transmewe hir gery cours therfore eschewe harmes lykly possyble fall counsayle amonge vpon trauayle trauayle eschewe mater sewe pryamus without sende firste agayne restore quene eleyne right reason harmes done eke parys trespas offency iustely make restytucyon may worshyp honour retourne home without labour assente requere axynge lyste nat folyly theyr wylfulnesse refuse worthynesse double assured asyker grounde iuste tytle troyans confounde thynges two shalbe vnder pyght firste power borne vp ryght shall v fyght quarell dareyne balaunce weye atwixe v weyne fyne shalbe excused tofore haue wylfully refused oure iuste profers made afore shalbe thorugh worlde therfore without spot trespas blame mysreport hyndrynge name folye shall ynoted wylfull wodenesse playnely shall stande free power vse euery man shall v well excuse though execucyon takynge vengeaunce offencyon man childe eche sect age shall deth holde passage swerde without mercy pace one better grace bvt yet tofore counsayle take hede ye mesoure bede holde beste moost sykernesse worke good auysenesse amonge selfe lenger tarye whiche counsayle contrarye varyaunt oppynyon saue moost discrecyon assented playnely ende chosen haue pryam sende amonges embassy spede wyse vlixes worthy dyomede whiche anone gan redy make shope forthe theyr way take towarde troye lyne ryght whan sonne shone full shene bryght holdynge course firy spere mydday arke wonder bryght clere gylte eche hylle vale playne roche bemes whan dyde approche walles gate towne go without noyse sowne full well esene porte hadde right manfully way ladde paleyes streyght lyne nedeth nat asyde declyne court large wyde square ful knightly wyght wold spare vnto effecte manly procede theyr charge without fere drede entre nat refused tho dayes paraunter nat vsed haue conduyte embassatrye custome man denye suppose entre passage come message court buylded ryally whan come meruayled full greatly royall syght huge strengthe well complete bothe brede lengthe nat hadde theyr lyfe fore sene none fayre yet wonder paleyes togyder gone paued iasper stone tree amyddes stode loke thought dyd gode musynge artifycyall erect sette magyk naturall engyne werkemen coryous thorugh subtyll craftes superiticyous werke nygromancye profounde castyuge phylosophye apparence illusyon outher crafte incantacyon vp downe caste theyr mynde reason coude fynde rote grounde wonder werke trouthe derke theyr wytte though longe trace pryuyte compace conceyue possyble eye vysyble sothe without fable mannes hande palpable whiche stocke guydo tolde soth fastnesse pured golde whiche shone bryght somer sonne enlumyne thynges donne body maste ryght proporcyoned moost goodly syght substancyall huge strengthe twelue cubytes body lengthe croppe rounde large brede compas gan flourysshe sprede playne aboute enuyrowne bowes shadowed vp downe ryche braunches leues fayre twayne twayne ioyned payre one golde nother syluer shene meynt amonge wt stone whyte grene rede sapher hewed euery daye blomes renewed blossomes many sondry fuyte stone ynde bare stede fruyte sayth guydo ferther telle grekes wyll lenger dwalle holde theyr way many sondry went parfourme fyne theyr entent tyll atteyne chambre pryncypall pryamus see royall lyke estate full kyngly wyse sat aboute full prudent full wyse lordes settes hym besyde whan grekes surquedous pryde sterne frowarde coutenaunce lytell remembraunce gentyllesse curtesye guydo doth playnely specyfye entrynge taken haue theyr place opposyte kynges face set downe without sermon obeyinge salutacyon worshyp honour reuerence done kynge excellence pretudyce gentyllesse anone vlixes gan expresse cause theyr comynge kynge pryamus without abode sayinge euen thus nat forberynge presence kynge oeruayle nat haue wondrynge though ne honour dewe comynge salewe syth ne longeth sothe thynketh rancour hertely enmyte dedely hate salutacyons fayned false affeccyons shewe hertes fyre naturally man shall desyre enmye helthe welfare platly lyste nat spare shortly shewe fyne entent lyke haue comaundement message agamenowne noble kynge moost worthy reuowne whiche v hath sent seyne vnto quene eleyne rauysshed grekes lande brought troy force myghty hade agaynst right vyolence wherfore shortly without offence iustely axe without demaunde thou anone rightfully comaunde menelay sent agayne axe nat vayne thou make restytucyon wronges done regyon pylfres great slaughter roberye parys done wylfull tyrannye whiche thy sone susteyned errour wrongefully meynteyned wherfore come fully condescende without grutchynge wronges amende thou mayste beste goddes queme lyke thou myght thy reason deme right requereth worke wyse thou despyse execute haue tolde truste right well lesson thou shalt lere whiche thou thyne shall sore rewe without feynynge thou shalt fynde trewe thou better ende make cruell vengeaunce shall take fynally shulde fayne force deth quarell shall darayne vpon vpon blode raunsomles golde gode questyonles reporte mercyles ryche stronge cyte shall downe bete ylayde full lowe walle toures also ouerthrowe well aduysed axynge nat despysed wysely werke haue sayde sodaynly kyng pryamus abrayde hasty ire myght nat abyde grekes whan sawe pryde great outrage presumpcyon without abode dely beracyon lixes anone gan breke vnto hym euen thus speke wonder greatly myn aduertence beunge astoned ye presence vngoodly dare make demaunde lyke ye hadde power comaunde constrayne byddynge obeye fere durste nat saye maner thynge ye axe contrarye ye requyre wherof sothly herte ameued thretes inwardly agreued astoned surely nat alyte ye bolde excyte vylaynously myn honour prouoke wordes worke truste right wele wyll nat passe boundes neuer adele rather shrotely ende axynge thynge condescende pfor consyder fyne entent nat syttynge conuenyent akynge graunte axynge thoughe stode myschefe captyuyte without recure vttraunce bought outrage playnely thought axe hym ye axe sothely yet suppose nat ye accomplysshynge may moche auayle ye haue sayde plately ye shall fayle purpose saye god toforne mauge myght though ye sworne request euery wyghtes syght wanteth grounde bothe trouthe ryght axe satisfaccyon selfe firste occasyon whan ye slewe fader lamedowne lyeges brent eke towne many harmes sought hym causeles ye wrought longe reherce whiche daye daye thorugh herte perce suster eke called exyon ye ladde awaye regyon whiche nat vnto hir worthynesse ytreted lyke gentylnesse pand ye wolde amendes haue wrongly whylom saue thynge pea stynte werre sente grece ferre oonly haue hadde exyona agayne whiche sonde ye hadde disdayne cruelly vngoodly wyse messager ye gan despyse vnneth myght eskape awaye grece ye knowe naye hadde vngoodly chere good fayth lyste nat request gyue audyence axynge great offence leuer hadde shortely deye condescende ought ye seye wyll fully conclusyon knowen agamenon haue leuer douteles fynally werre pee syth ye haue done great trespace trouthe selfe place cruelly anone ye shulde dye offyce embassatrye agaynst deth fully defence bolde without reuerence presence threte speke truste right shulde one bewreke wherfore haste without wordes mo counsayle ye go syght voyde cyte thus standeth whyles se herte may entre gladnesse fret ire put suche distresse good fayth may nat sustene portune rage tene inwardly byndeth whyle dyomedes tho began smyle sayde anone thus vnto kynge thou comynge thyne herte haste moche payne v beholde buttwayne art therwith inly sette fyre shalt thou neuer without yre thy lyfe deuoyde woo sythe thou hast many cruell foo grekes entred thy lande hondred thousande almoste thyn hande agayne whose myght thou mayst nat assure resyste playnely endure consyder well stronge thou shalt wyt paraunter aught longe somanly men well arayed expert armes olde assayed diffence many agayne vayle wyteeke well thou mayst nat fayle deth swerde theyr hande deye thyne seye though proudely thou speke thy tunge oonly wreke afermest thou mayst acheue better suche wordes leue wyse counsayle take better hede haste agayne dyomede surquydous moste full pryde rose vp kynges syde swerdes drawe hym haue fall hewe amonge hasty ire brennynge glede tyll pryamus gan take hede rose hym vp seynge disease manfully rage gan appease diffendynge vpon deth lyfe none hardy stryfe embassatoures harme greue though fole foly wyll nat leue presume speke vnconnyngly wyse man muste suffre pacyently thoughe happe offence thorugh foly speche lacke sapyence wyse man ne iongeth sothe sayne take hede speke agayne fole perteynent shewe foly right conuenyent wyse sothly suffraunce port haue tolleraunce foles longeth kyndely without aduyse speke folyly vndiscretely menynge fulfylle wyse man shall bestylle tyll se tyme haue pacyence dissymule aduertence rage foles last throwe tunge fole ofte knowe leuer hadde well assure persone damage endure suffre messagere court haue wronge outher great lyte swerde rancour may nat alway byte vengeaunce thynge nought ofte falleth wronge wrought lytell excesse foloweth great reprefe haste ayemedled myschefe wherfore bydde ye sytte downe wyse presumpcyowne attempteth nat maner wyse sygne worde despyse embassatoures grekes sent lette freely declare theyr entent ye whyles kepe lyppes close sodaynely eneas rose whiche next kyng haue tha see inwardely rancour fret ne myght hymselfe nat refrayne sayde syr ye nat disdayne shall saye semeth well accordynge whan one hath sayde amys reklesly spoken vnaduysed folye chastysed may example hym take well ware suche noyse crye make specyally open audyence offende toyall excellence sothely yet wote well myght gouerne playnely syght hastynesse without aduysement shulde comaundement deth deserue great offence trewely yet ne presence twayne haue yspoke without abode shulde anone wroke worthy right well syttynge whan fole presence kynge bolde hardy presumpcyon take hym indiscrecyon thynge reherce concludynge sentence preiudyce magnyfycence taught better gouerne large tunge konne bet diserne whan shall speke whan pese suffre hym renne lese doth spoke hath large wherfore hast counsayle hym charge without abode worde mo syght anone go beste hym rede anone ful proudly dyomede nat astoned sterne loke eneas yre quoke answered agayne wordes fewe sayde syr thy wordes doth well shewe thou thou art right wyse well kynge doth thyne aduyse hath nye counsayle ne may erre degre art rightfull thy iugement wylfulnesse without aduysement causea lorde bondes pace wolde god place myght fauoure fortune mete leyser oportune lyke desyre canst well endyte olde fable thy labour quyte thanke thy gentyll whiche knyghtly thou hast v shewed truste well therto haue therof drede tho vlixes dyomede gan interrupte word prudently hym sayde full aduysely beste stynte styll knowe fully wyll quod vlires full manly kynge wyll go hense without tariynge thy syght agamenon make hym playne relacyon thy answer ordre horse went sodaynly shorte tyme hast theyr waye come saye kynge satte tentorye worde worde came memorye reherce substraunce euery dele wherof grekes lyke thynge wele conceyuynge full remedye reporte embassatrye saue oonly vtterly procede shall gouerne nede agayne troyans necessyte well wot may none assented wyll bede purueye faste spede storye shall fynde bvt make therof mynde muste whyle eneas endyte myn auctor lyst hym wryte whiche sothly bokes saye manly troyan famous eneas anchisis sone great wortynesse whylom gete venus goddesse conqueroure many regyon whan troye brought destruccyon wente waye large see called tyrene saylynge forth goth many coste many narowe passage many daunger tyll cartage ryued segan sayle conquest great ytale rome hath way take whose ofsprynge auctours make came augustus cesar emperour whylom noble conquerour renowne daye doth shyne enee emperour iustyne boke called autentykes full playnely wryt therin rubrykes cesar cesares named yet right eneades enee name shulde bere whiche fro troye comen fere vnto ytayle eneas haue tolde cesar descended downe lyne right full manly royall firste rome sceptre imperyall mauge theyr myght gouernaunce wysoome sette gouernaunce comon thynges touchynge cytee procede ferther enee hooly lyfe knyghthode ye lyste rede ceryously ye maye se full autentyke style eneydos compyled virgyle albe noble clerke graue afore complete werke bokes olde make mencyon phow kynge agamenon sent achylles thelephus yle messa vitaylles slewe kynge made lephus kynge deth ca xx bvt nowe agayne agamenon without style wyl retourne whiche kynge wyll soiourne mater delayes make haste hath counsayle take lordes beynge present suche nat hath sent one erlys duke kynges sayde syres amonge thynges iourney necessarye counsayle lenger tarye firste make ordynaunce one assent prudent purueaunce alder firste shape vytayle without whiche none hoost may auayle parforme iourney thryftely wherfore rede faste lykynge plesaunce yle full habundaunce called messa sende anone one worde assented euerychone chosen haue worthy achylles geleffus sone hercules execute purpose fynally many worthy theyr company chosen thorugh hoost anone achylles messa gone whiche lande ryche plenteuous reygned kynge worthy famous tentran hyght whiche tranquyllyte without werre aduersyte hadde holde sceptre royall sete yle plesaunt mete albe saye lytell yle kyngdome longeth cecyle hath name gyuen plente messane huge great cyte full plenteuous see lande whiche kyngdome vnderstande sayde messana mess latyne thorugh habundaunce fruyt corne wyne aryuayle playnes large wonte stuffe charge marchaunt shyppes straunge fer countree thyder sayle large see fetche vytaylle aye fro yere yere fro many coste landes fer nere oonly eschaunge march aundyse eke also bokes deuyse guydo full playnely telleth v kynge called messanus countre firste messa toke name tyme great fame passynge ryche wonder plenteuous dare frygyus boke maketh mencyon shortly telleth concluycon howe achylles thelephus also messana togyder go thre thousande grekes chosen oute moste manly men amonges theyr route whiche faste gan londe kynge gan vnderstonde theyr comynge descended downe worthy regyowne ou hors fote stele armed bryght agaynst grekes manfully fyght deuoyde playnely ye sodaynely thus skarmysshe gan wyxe grekes theyr mortall fone outher parte many one slayne hurte deth ywounded euer vnlyckely therof sounded hor treate none atwene swerdes sharpe speres square kene go grounde euery man foo confounde laboure dyde besynesse though grek thrugh theyr worthynesse hadde theyr foo moche lande ywonne yet resorte begonne meruayle none bycause theyr fone hadde alway thre noumbre agaynst one tyme may none tyll achylles gan beholde se mortall slaughter vpon grekes syde tournynge backe wt woudes large wyde hasty rancour chaunge gan blode ire furyous wode whan behelde men lese theyr lande swerde whiche helde hande made waye kylled bare downe felde lyke fyers lyowne fared sothe whan men slawe makynge foon backwarde withdrawe grekes manly recomforte maugre made resorte euer way stode without mercy kylleth mode gayneth nat cruelte douteles ne manhode passynge renowne worthynesse knyghthode eke hye prowesse grekes hadde daye fynallye vaynquysshed without remedye thorugh helpe recure achylles sturdy wall gan serche sheltrouns theyr rangys brake fore whose face fomen go wrake alderlaste whan gan espye tentran kynge thorugh chyualrye diffende hymselfe lyke worthy knyght lyon bare hym fyght grekes oppresse achylles cruell hardynesse ne wolde cease putsewynge thorugh warde tyll came kynge manly force stoute full pryde makynge awaye rounde euery syde agayne whose myght thyng myght auayle tentran firste auentayle raced hath rente mayle sonder hewe wonder consydre day cruelte broke hath bassenet many cruell wounde myght smyt kynge grounde haste maked hath lette hede rende bassenette mercyles vengaunce harme gan heyghte auaunce fully purpose shall dede raunsomles gan hamyn hede blody swerde despytous herte castynge playnely shuld hym nat asserte ire furyous pbut fortune befell right thus thelephus yonge lusty knyght casuelly therof hadde syght achylles maner full behelde stroke anone bare vp shelde gan achylles mekely preye haue pyte hym deye syth lay wounded almoste deth brought poynt yelde vp breth besechynge hym benyngnyte manly routhe knyghtly eke pyte withdrawe hande hym grace graunte hym lyfe lytell space syth euery knyght shulde gentyllesse enmye spare whan distresse vttraunce brought specyally whan mercy requyreth humble volunte achylles feruent yre rancoure sette fyre answerde agayne lyst preye hym nolde pryde wyll obeye gan werre nede disdayne indignacyon hauynge truste presumpcyon manhode myght hy nat auayle agaynst grekes holde batayle preuyd playnely ende otherwyse shortly wende dyche iustely falle whiche made malys v alle pwhere wyll entencyon gaue vnto hym none occasyon vpon syde platly fer nere mynystred hym matere londe mente damage hymselfe grounde rage without offence done hym v efte agayne yonge thelephus humbly requyred achylle knyghtly routhe axynge fulfylle haue mercy hym ca fader kynge whylom quod thelephus bonde conferate whiche lyeth desconsolate expectant oonly dedely face vpon houre whan goste shall pace thorugh gyrte ala wt many mortall woude cause haue hym founde afore tyme full great kyndenesse manhode gentyllesse boundes regyowne vnto thorugh hye renowne whylom casuelly gan ryde shewed sothe vpon euery syde full ryall chere great humanyte bounde duyte remembre haue mynde douteles elles vnkynde whiche wolde name foule twyte parcell wolde hym quyte beseche respyte lyfe achylles without stryfe delyuered hath storye telleth thus tentran frely vnto thelephus whether hym lyste saue spylle whan hym wylle consydered woundes grene mortall sothely kene nede muste dye gayne remedye auayle may medecyne hour wha pheb westward gan declyne batayle brought ende whyle grekes theyr shyppes wende meane whyle tentran payne woundes gan complayne without staunche pyteously blede offycers faste gan spede lytter made full royall towarde paleys douge owne pryncypall cary hym softely easely pand prayer full benyngnely thelephus also achylles conueyed hym amonges prees tyll brought lyste receyued lyke theyr degre full royally kynge aye languysshynge drewe towarde endynge myght nat lenger drawe lengthe wofull lyfe weke strengthe spirite muste algates wende haste made sende achylles thelephus whan came sayde vnto thus syres quod full worthy degre helthe honour longe prosperyte vnto good aduenture whyle lyfe may dure specyally thelephus whiche haste gracyous gentyllesse paynes stronge oonly grace lyfe prolonge deth ala may nat eichewe swerde part remewe without recure knytte bytter bondes vpon brynke falle fatys hondes lyfe fully despeyre whiche body neuer myght haue heyre daye successyon gouerne lytell regyon whiche lyckely stande desolate gouernaunce disconsolate whiche wan wt full great trauayle day werre batayle haue kepte ye well knowe echoue defended maner fone without losse yeres toforne recurlees yore lorne ne helpe eke socour hercules great conquerour whylom fader thelepus stronge myghty chyualrous whose manhode whose hardynesse knyghthode great worthynesse whiche day day newe memorye foon hadde victorye daunted made ferde oonly rygoure sharpeswerde fynally thorugh manly hede made reygne possede maugre theyr myght pea quyete septre crowne royall sete none tyll dede hardy lyfte vp hede agaynst speke wordes fewe wherby may fully declare shewe euydence lytell yle perteynent longeth cecyle hercules memoryall tte pylers conquest royall whan hadde ryde go fere columpna yet name bere hym called herculea though saye hyght herracula name chaungynge corrupcyon whiche lande whylom mansyon people wylde barbarye whiche kyngdome magnefye frederyke sothly secounde golde good passyngly habounde chosen emperour rome towne myghty gouernour whylom eke kynge cecyle whiche made reyse large yle myghty toure hye thycke walle sayth guydo memoryall put name longe remembraunce soyle plesaunce floures fresshe many sondry hewe bokes londe named newe pealled vnderstonde fayrenesse lusty newe londe tentran aye lymge payne faste gan houre attayne cruell deth afore lordes made haste thelephus call presence mortall chere sayde openly myght sone quod nowe shall pace worlde gayne may grace lyfe saue thorugh mannes myght bycause equyte ryght compelled iustly sentence declare elerely conscyence fore deth herynge prees sage thy fader hercules wyse worthy knyghtly man whylom londe thorugh conquest wan whiche oonly goodly hede stocke manly hede toke vnto comyssyon gouernaunce regyon free wyll hole regallye nolde hymselfe cowne occupye sothely yet right nat lasse loue shall passe withall entent laste wylle graunt ryght skylle heyer iustely succede longe honour therin thy lyfe lede makynge prodestacyon full token confirmacyon wyll fynall myn herte fro whiche man may dyuerte vpon syde vtterly declyne hor firste wyll dissent lyne togyder combyne one whiche thynge mortall man may gone desyre laste langour thou playnely successour fynally thus conclude deme vnto septre dyademe delyuered euery circumstaunce wyll assuraunce made wryte testament fyne concludynge laste entent full pyteously thelephus besought hertely manly routhe knyghtly gentyllesse deuer besynesse deth lyke estate royall halowe holde feste funerall solempnely exequyes sodaynely without wordes mo kynge tentran yeldeth vp goste went way note coste nat deme suche mystyhede whan parcas broken haue thrde rokke forth waye thelephus marbyll graye curyously tombe madekerue dede corp therin conserue full rychely aboue graue epythaphe anone dyde graue honour playnely expresse knyghthode bothe worthynesse goste deuorced letter ryche golde aboue enboced rounde aboute wonder curyous tombe sayde playnely thus lyeth tentran kynge douteles whylom slayne cruell achylles sceptre regalye hoolly gaue whiche man may denye thelephus sone hercules whiche tombe resteth pee whan perfourmed euery thynge thelephus crowned kynge hye lowe one assent openly parlement made fayth hym ydone homage lyke theyr degree age hole herte theyr best entent othe assured sacrament trewe lyeges receyued hym kynge achylles without tariynge whan sette pea gouernaunce without grutchynge varyaunce theyr shyppes anone made carye euery thynge necessarye grekes corne fruyte vytayle flesshe fysshe myght auayle hosteynge helpe theyr nede downe see hedyde lede fully theyr vessell stuffe lade thelephus made stylle boundes regyon abyde conclusyon thorugh helpe dylygence besynes discrete prouydence agayne myschefe scarsyte whan nede myght theyr socour al lyke sayth guydo achilles full fayne wold haue go abode sothely beste bonde assured fully beheste euery thynge grekes releue haste achilles toke leue thelephus gan anone sayle shyppes stuffed vytayle towarde grekes made mencyowne shorte tyme thenedowne aryued taken bathe grounde knyghted rounde hemade firste full relacyon expleyt lyke falle presence lordes alle syttynge enuyron many worthy knyght pand firste messa telleth fyght whan entred theyr welcomynge ceryously tolde eke kynge tentran hyghte playnely also howe achilles amydde selde hym slowe dethe hole entent fully ordeyned testament thelephus also heyre tolde eke eyre vnto see eke vytayle thelephus wyll nat fayle sende may please whiche thynge grekes great ease brought herte lyke wonder well whan achilles hadde tolde euerydell greatly preysed hye prouydence manhode bothe sapyence beynge bare hym achilles go lodgynge lytell besyde knyghtes vpon hym abyde myrundones full glade comynge hym receyued longeth kynge abode rested hym whyle guydo declyneth style grekes troye towne muste also make dygressy owne myne auctor steppe shewe lyke conuenyent dewe matere syth guyde whyle grekes sette asyde reherce dare frygyus troye booke declareth vnto v ceryously maketh mency owne lordes came troye towne helpe manly theyr defence agaynst grekes make resystence ordynaunce many dyuerse thynges came erles duke kynges dare playnely made mynde rede boke ye may fynde alder firste rede specyally speketh kynges thre full manly also great e wryteth thus called panda u rede thabet secounde thu e andastrus lyke founde g ydo lyste specysye knyghtes theyr companye manly men euerychon called colloson lyke dare lyketh expresse came also excellent prowesse whiche firste ynamed carya seconde hyghte ymasyus thirde iiij amphymacus fyue thousande worthy knyghtes alle came manly falle vpon grekes helpynge towne yie full great renowne called ly ye came kynge glaucon ith hym brought sone spardon noble knyght armes full famous allyed kynge pryamus thre thousande shall nat fayne came knyght wt lordes twayne larys ryche lande also fynde came kynges two quyte manly ought thousande knyght troye brought kyngdome named lycaowne caphemus kynge great renowne brought hym dare bereth wytnesse thousande knyghtes great worthynesse fyue hondred dare telleth v came hupon epedus many knyghtes plate syluer bryght hym eke kynge remus hyght brought iij thousande troye many myle tabaria large myghty yle duke foure theyr chyualrye erie viij came companye hauyngem armes great experyence bare without difference theyrmen whan felde chief golde eueryche shelde wherby kynge booly nauye amonge knowen myght bore eke fro trace kynge pylex name fro thy ke trace moste excellent whiche plage oryent haueth syght fro myghty ky ge thousande knyght brought comynge myne auctor recordeth eke also hondred knyghtes troye go alchamus duke eke full famous came pylex guydo wryteth thus troyans helpe theyr great nede fro pauonye sothely rede came pretemessus noble werryour lorde lande kynge gouernour duke stupex hym eke hadde knyghtes thousande ladde towarde troye regyon storye maketh mencyon yle standeth moste wyldernesse woodes plenteuous thyckenesse growe therin many full dyuerse tree moste forest men may se buylde house fewe lande full dyuersely themshewe many lyknesse queynte monstruous bestes vnkouthe syghte meruaylous stoundemell apparence illusyon false existence wonder gastefull playnely sene dyuerse goodes woodes grene appere called satyrye cornys eke fawny incubye cause often men falle rage lande people full sauage hardy knyghtes furyous wode desyrous aye shede blode greatly experte specially shete darte spere peryllous mete caste euen lyne ile named botyne great arraye troye cyte lyke fynde came duke thre firste called auphymyus saume secounde thirde forcyus sayth dare whiche lyste natlye twelue hondred knyght theyr companye fro bytunye made remembrauce ryche lande hath suche habundauce spyces gomes fruytes corne wyne holsome rote ryndes ryche fyne wonder vnkouthe precious also whiche ile came knyghtes two full knyghtly men armes desyrous kynge boetes epysterus wt brought troye ferre thousande knyghtes arayed werre fro lande called paffogonye whiche seuered companye bokes saye hystoryall vnder plage oryentall sette ferre made rehersayle fewe none lande trauayle come almoste impossyble whiche lande called muysyble bycause oonly remocyon ryche regyon golde syluer also stone habundaunte plente none full treasoure gode hath syght ryche flode named tygre nat fer eufrates sayth myne auctour called dare fro whiche lande stele armed clene thousande knyght came phylymene worthy kynge whose sheldes orede querboyl guydo rede golde depaynte fret stone ryche worlde trowe none lyche floodes chosen deuyse whiche haue theyr course paradyse whiche kynge gyaunt stature makynge passynge measure stronge delyuer also fynde fro lande marcheth vpon ynde kynge porses came many knghtly man also honde hym wan moche honour noble meryon brother called sygamon whiche lande theyr subieccyowne duke erles knyghtes renowne thre thousande brought plate shene speres rounde whet full quare kene ethyope came noble route kyngdome also doute teremo dare called came kynge full prudent full wy manly man named theseus eke sone hyght archylogus thousande knyghtes theyr companye theseus full nye allye pryamus discent blode kynges twayne passynge ryche gode renowmed knyghthode fame guydo reherseth nat theyr name yet storye maketh mensyon agresta lytell regyon thousande knyght brought vnto troye grekes pryde daunte acoye chosen pycked ye none lande beyonde amazones lyssyny kynge epystrophus wyse worthy inly vertuous passynge counsayle discrecyowne full worthy renowne preuyd also specyall artys called lyberall lerned expert ryght natwithstandynge worthy knyght werre pea manfull ryght sage ron ferre age storye maketh rehersayle thousande knyght cladde plate mayle troye towne fynde ladde hym guydo sayth hadde wonder archer syght meruaylous fourme shap maner monstruous lyke myne auctour reherce fro nauell vp warde man lower downe lyke hors yshaped thylke parte man maked skynne blacke rough vere coueryd fro colde hym passynge foule horryble syght whose eyen sparkelynge bryght furneys rede leuene ye lyghtenynge yt cometh downe fro heuene dredefull loke reed fyre rede good archere bowe bothe euen morowe vpon grekes wrought moche sorowe gastyd many hydous loke sterne many quoke whan hym sawe ougly horrybly lothsome credyble many one hath wounded deth caused yelde vp breth grekes syde ye shall wyse assembled yfere kynges duke erles renowne sondry landes within troye towne gaderyd come fro ferre sayth dare helpe werre nombre maketh mynde two thurty thousande fynde worthy knyghtes lordes estate fythe worlde fourmed create ne sene trowe one cyte togydre assembled hye degre knyghtes great multytude yet dare sothly conclude boke maketh nomynde came troye smaler ynde nouther moste famous renowne wt pryam yborne troye towne fynally trewely sought syth houre world wrought dare afferme vnder phebus spere many worthy nat mette yfere manly men flourynge lustynesse fresshe yonge lyklynesse euery poynt shape arraye well sothely naye lyste consyder vpon outher sy e thorugh worlde men go ryde th floure knyghthode worthynesse chyualrye hye prowesse assembled withoute within fully assented werre begyn pwherfore ye lysters take good hede delyte boke rede firste lytell werre began lyght cause whiche many man hath loste lyfe myschefe pytuously yet man beware therby almoste nought stryfe begonne lyst loke haue thyng wonne oonly deth ala harde stounde many knyght caught dethes wounde withoute recure remedye woman shall nat lye gan stryfe pyte great myschefe aduersyte mortall slaughter euer shulde tyde better haue sette asyde suche quarelles dere ynough myte let passyd vengeaunce byte wysedome caste afore se suche sklaundres myght eschewed venym gonne rype though men horne blowe pype whan hous fyred hete sparcle late trete caused wherfore gynnynge remedy put euery thynge euery wyght may deme reason whyle grekes lay tenedon refresshe reste pe worthy kynge called pallamydes thurty shyppes grekes lande stuffed wt knyght ful worthy theyr hande beste choyse regyon aryued vp tenedon wherof grekes whan syght reioysynge right glade lyght hauynge rewarde vnto worthynesse afore hadde heuynesse absence longe grutched hym stronge nat kepte moustre athene shewe clene spotte conscyence full manfully open audyence lyke knyght hegan hymself excuse stoppynge tho theron lyste muse absence wynge cause sykenesse sodayne malady costrayned presence withdrawe sawe lykensse hath lawe helde excused fully absence moste reuerence amonge grekes wyght secounde also full wyse eke habounde golde good auyse prudent euer sette entent knyghtly wysely wolde aye well acheue gan ne wolde leue maugre foon maner wyse tyll sawe fyne empryse moste oppynyon amonge grekes reputacyon hym ought wolde theyr counsayle auysely tose euery maner thynge assenteth vnto theyr axynge benygnely gentylnesse grekes dyde theyr besynesse procede without delaye enhaste euer maye gynne sege differre nought sondry wayes serched haue sought theyr wyttes fro tenedowne maye remeue towarde troye towne hauen theyr shyppes thought moste comodyte moste expleyt nyght pryuely towarde troye stode faste proudely sayle theyr shyppes alle sayde great peryll myght falle towarde nyght take see lest derkenesse ennosed bee theyr passage knowynge nat waye wherof great harme falle maye thus dyuerse oppynyon procedynge nat conclusyon effect theyr purpose nat ne helde styll lye aye lodged felde lyke entryked drede tyll daye worthy dyomede grekes seynge cowardyse euen thus counsayle gan deuyse syres quod present ye lyste one assent goodly consydre aduertynge prudently shall saye tofore openly whiche knyghthode haue noble name sothly semeth ought haue gret shame whiche holde selfe myghty stronge lande soiourned haue longe nygh yere durste wyse remeue hense cowardyse haue nat ellys certaynely foon graunted folyly euen theyr luste space lyberte make stronge opportunyte v withstande playnely hande wyll ye may well vnderstande pfor day day confusyowne sought wayes full wysely vp downe gette helpe mene space enforced aboute euery place theyr large cyte barrerys palys theyr wall mascued agayne skalys trusteth theron made great ordynaunce gouernaunce haue aspyed seynge drede haue herte manly procede purpose holde werre aye se deferre wyll catche hardynesse v resyste theyr besynesse also se truste veryly hadde afore hande manfully began knyghtly forth contynued iourney hadde better fortuned sodaynely stronge myghty hande vnauysed hadde theyr lande without abode afore tyme aryued whiche whyle muste depryued delayed firste victorye honour palme glorye myght sothely ne slouthe wyl complysshed playnetrouthe maugre v lande aryue stroge defence wyl agayne v stryue put v stronde wynne aye tarye begynne sothe lyste nat lye put selfe echone ieopardye shulde fayne fage fro trouthe tariynge cowarde louthe lykely tourne v great sorowe wherfore erely tymes morowe counsayle ankers vp pulle mater lenger dulle enarme shyppes werre vp ryse morowe sterre lette v ordayne knyghtly apparayle hauen wynde sayle manfull herte lusty fresshe courage course holdynge right passage towarde troye lande oppedlye euer falle truste sykerlye without scarmousshe may nat aryue fro troye descende wyll blyue lyke manly men mete v berde lette v nat aferde voyde drede manhode sette afore cowardyse entre bore taste manhode herte worde grekes gan aduerte manly counsayle dyomede effect procede dede vnto poynt nothynge spare wyse anone shall declare phow grekes toke lande troye strongely fought ca xxi next morowe wonderly tyme phebus vp rose loge pme whan began full meryly dawe grekes hoste shypwarde gan drawe manly herte fully deuoyde drede thorugh comforte dyomede alder firste anone awoke lordes wysely theyr counsayle toke concluded amonge euerychone whiche theyr shyppes shulde mest gone see shulde guye aryue man aspye deuysed certayne marke nyght passed syngynge larke grekes shypped without tariynge bothe hye lowe dawnynge first tofore hondred shyppes toure stuffed many worthy warryoure gan proudely sayle charge baners brode bryght large splayed vpon euery syde departed fomy wawes wyde syghte whelmen vp grene next werre wel enarmed clene another hondred folowed faste whiche bare theyr sayles passyngly proudely ful many worthy knyght armed mayle plate bryght foloweth hoolly theyr nauye trowe suche companye worthy kynghtes lordes degree neuer afore sene vpon see olus fortunate eke neptune made none debate wt wynde trouble amoge sterne wawes atempre weder full mery dawes tyde sayled ryght troye towne caughte anone syght wherof herte full glade lyght whan troyans firste theyr shyppes se proudely sayle lytell fro stronde sawe caste londe bode arme hastely plate mayle iackes rychely irous herte done anone toke theyr hors forth haste gone gate made tariynge ne abyde prynce duke kynge lor e guyde gouerne haste forth many yerne torough felde great multytude amonges folkes rude manly men thryftely sayne clenly armed large playne whan grekes gan firste beholde nombre theyr hertes gan colde none manly amonge yonge fresshe hardy stronge hye estate lowe degre ne stonyed se hardy troyans proudly downe descede lette grekes nat assende wyste conceyue vtterly meane aryue oonly deth manly fyght cowardely take flyght conduyte playnely none sharpe sworde speres ca tyll sodaynely hardy fyerse kynge prothesylaus whiche gouernynge formest hondred shyppesladde gan haste hym ire hadde landed firste wolde haue haue mette wt great desyre suche wynde gan sayle dryue shyppes whan he hope aryue vnwarely smette vpon loude gettys drye sonde shyppes shyuered sonder dreynt broke yonder deuoured wawy see routhe pyte se harde myght none escape whyles bely take drye lande fylthe mudde ylade troyans full cruell slaughter made maugre theyr myght grekes constrayned wt theyr blode wawes ystayned mortally sothely beholde amonge sonde pale dede colde grekes lye woudes fresshe grene eyre shote arowes kene shadowed phebus bemes bryght vpon soyle derked lyght newe alway troyans assayle grekes playnely yuayle mortall infortunate vnwelfull disconsolate v sposed thorugh infelycytee trowe neuer see none hoost harde londe grekes ne wolde wonde lyfe deth manly aryue befelle aduenture blyue thre hondred shyppes next sewe auyfedly tyme dewe entrede haste nat faste stryke sayle theyr ankers caste werre strongly enbatayled theyr londynge leste assayled wysely firste sette theyr bala ters theyr gonners theyr beste archer pauysers go aforne knyghtly lade though troyans sworne contrarye proudely tolet e yet fyers vp sette grekysshe shote made withdrawe many lande lay slawe maugre stronde recure suche myght moste manfully endure sette afore tyll lande haue take attones suche assaute make vpon troyans tho began fyght whan prothesylaus ye noble worthy knyght wonder lyfely right passynge stronge grekes entrede amonge hardy troyans euery sought armes meruayles wrought thylke daye thorugh worthynesse many troyan brought distresse went felte full vnsofte thorugh whose manhode grekes lofte thy ke daye ne ha de knyght hode greekes hadde great aduersyte venquysshed fatall puru yaunce fynally brought vnto outtraunce put backe playnely lye uyleth chyualrye worthynesse fyerse courage myght helpe auauntage syth vij thousande grekes hadde hondred thousade troyans yet mo metuayle myght endure wyse stronde recure fewe holde felde themselfe one thynge behelde full prudently whiche gaue herte sawe myght nat erte escape lyue wolde flee theyr backe thynge see tofore hoost great huge waye refuge dye attones fyght manfully wherfore cast shope full knyghtly lyke rather maly men theyr lyues ieote cowardely theyr foon departe lese theyr grounde drenchen see thus longe wolde grekes defende ferre aboue myght many kylled fyght stremes theyr rede blode ran sonde large flode cruelly troyans hym set spere swerde ful sharpe groude whet routhe pyte thynke tyll almoost droue brynke grekes myschefe distresse great anguysshe passyngly wer nesse themselfe defende maat full ery shulde haue perysshed vtterly recurles sothe euermore ne hadde archelaus worthy p otenor theyr shyppes aryued vnto lande sodayne happe stande yet hadde full great aduersyte aryue thorugh cruelte troyans yet lande wynne grekes cruelly begynne agayne theyr foon stande defence manly force great vyolence th encreaseth blody werre newe oyle depaynt dewe firste gre e tourned rede eche syde many one laye dede vpon grounde lyfe depryued duke nestor sodaynely aryued knyghtes felle full irous herte right melancolyous speres archyers asyde entrede sterne full pryde swerde axe grounde sharpe kene ran fere mette vpon grene hoked rowes alway flewe amonge braste tourne wronge olys teled well whette longe daye haue togyder mette slaughter newe alway began euery halfe many worthy man wtih woundes large felle despytous prothenor kynge archelaus swerdes styffe amonge renges kerue many many troyan made sterue day passyngely irous auenge inly desyrous neuce seasynge theyr pursuynge releue alagus kynge londed eke kynge athalus whiche troyans full enuyous ire firy glede vpon olde hatrede theyr knyghtes sodaynely falle theyr ire bytterer galle cruelly theyr foon oppresse assent dyde theyr besynesse maugre bakwarde resorte amy de felde reporte choyse costrayned force manhode payned withdrawe theyr confusyowne haste downe troye towne worthy knyghtes fresshely armed newe deuyses many sondry hewe abode shortely conclude came downe great multytude armes depaynte vpon shelde theyr comynge glytereth felde theyr armure sonne bryght whan entrede fyght metynge felly enuye sette vpon foot melancolye suche wyll herte courage suche furye theyr mortall rage vnto accorde none mene slaughter dethe go betwene thorugh stroke axe dagger spere force coacte grekes retourne bakwarde stronde whose rescuse anone come londe kynge vlyxes hole nauye full knyghtly chyualrye towarde troyans enhasteth hym anone one herte grekes hym gone theyr courage holly resume gan theyr foon felly consume vnto deth theyr damage reuenge wyght may iustely chalenge manhode well haue bor e quyte agayne theyr harmes done whiche tyme lyke fyersly owne amonge troyans rengynge vp downe vltxes went swerde honde kylleth sleeth knyghtly gan sonde thylke daye lyke man founde many mortall wounde vpon troyans wrought wracke berynge downe fote horse backe ire stroke kene whiche tyme worthy phylomene lorde kynge paffogonye whan behelde companye many troyan vlixes slawe tawardes hym anone gan hym drawe horse backe spere rounde sadell bare hym grounde vlixes rose vp anone ryght takynge horse lyke manly knyght whiche anone phylomene hath sayne toke efte aspere rode hym agayne myghtely suche vyolence fynally gayneth diffence smote hym euen thorugh shelde whiche flewe sondre felde thorughe plate without fayle spere hede ran rested mayle forged stele full shene bryght whiche perce spere hede hath myght trewely made hawberiowne stroke vlixes bore downe yet efte agayne vp rose anone whiche stroke harme ne felte none raughte spere sharpe whet grounde phylomene gaue suche wounde myght armes twayne irous herte great payne thorugh shelde bothe place mayle smote hym vp thorugh auentayle gorge stocke gan glyde hors fell downe syde full perryllously pyght vpon hede knyghtes wenynge sothly dede whiche toke hym vp layde hym shelde bare hym home haste felde great dauger myght hym wyne thorugh grekes theyr lorde twyne troyans supposed sykerly phylomene without remedy hadde deed astoned case day ne fall physomene grekes stronde dde outrayed aryuynge vp londe thorughe knyghthode douteles phylomene vlixes v ho sed hath mortall wounde knyghtly wyse troyans confounde wherof astoned euerychon pbut tho agamenon greks ooste lorde emperour aryued vnto theyr socour knyghtes menelaus eke worthy thelamonyous called ayax lande come leyser haue theyr hors nome whyle grekes troyans occupye sor fyghtynge gan faste hye towardes makynge delay frusshe haste may ran yfere theyr speres bracke herte enuyous vpon hors backe myght men worthy knyghtes se theyr stedes eche flee styffe swerdes shaftes great rounde hedes square poyntes kene grounde myght men se theyr furyous tene many knyghtes dede vpon grene moste slaughter confusyowne fell thylke tyme towne grekes myghty stronge felde contynueth longe tyll prothesilaus stronge myghty kyng whiche daye skarmysshe fyghtyng full lyke knyght occupyed agayne troyans cruelte manhode oonly worthynesse aduenture werynesse hym refresshe take eyre brethe hym maked repeyre stronde dyde aryue pwhere thought herte gan toryue cruell yre alfo pyte caughte oonly se men lye slayne ende longe stronde comynge vp londe dreynt see amonge floodes depe whiche thynge gan anone wepe full pyteuosly nat espyed whose wofull eyen myght nat dryed constreynt whiche sat sonye herte tyll laste amonge paynes smerte cruell yre gan herte enbrace sodaynely despytous face without abode thought vpon theyr deth wolde auenged fynally attones deye stede toke ryght weye towarde foon full irous rage lyne right holdeth passage swyfte grayhounde renneth lee sawe grettest prees preceth thorugh amyddes felde wt swerde whiche hande helde grounde kerue byte full mortally aboute hym gan smyte troyans myght hym nat asterte ryueth euen herte woundeth sothely deth made yelde vp breth vnhorseth cruelly mette day vtterly hors made hym alyght rode fledde syght presence deth eschewe euer one gan sewe chase lyke wood lyon playe playeth towne tyll perseus ethyopye kynge ye cyte came sodaynely rydynge many knyght many lyfely man whose comynge newe began fresshe skarmysshe furyous woode many greke day loste blode felle assaute troyans make amonge ethyopyes blake manly bare fyghtynge troyans afore fere newe assured thorugh theyr helpe haue felde recured made lese also moche agayne tofore wonne playne hole myghtely kept togydre auysely gouerned pauys spere shelde grekes compelled felde maugre grutche necessyte sironde backewarde flee almoste dispayred mate comforteles whyle kynge pallamydes theyr rescous come arryuayle lusty fresshe entreth batayle knyghtes hole maynee takynge theyr hors faste see full proudely enbusshed attones spere swerde ygroude none conueyinge theyr worthy comynge haue oppressed theyr comynge manly troyans wonder se lye slayne yonder contynueth tyll amonge prees auenture pallamydes brennynge aye furyoushete amyd felde happeth mete worthy knyght called sygamon whiche brother kynge menon also guydo doth reherce manly man kynge perce whiche grekes daye sore opressed knyghthode expressed grekes worthynesse ofte brought full great distresse daye great encrees ut fortune ala pallamydes tolde hath felde hym mette aspere square sharpe whette whan knyghthode pryde rode hym smote hym thorugh syde laste dedely fatall wounde stede bare hym grounde playne blode rede amydes lefte hym pale dede amonges troye forth rode bare downe euer waye stode furyous wode maugre troyans tofore hym playne made resorte walle agayne manly knyghtes alway faste hym awaytynge full ententyfely redy honde euery great empryse tho began noyse aryse wofull clamour pyteous crye troye whiche vtterly agayne grekes myght nat sustene mortall swerde sherpe kene noble worthy famous knyght pallamydes great myght longe daye hath yborne hym agayne foon knyghtly persone thorugh hye renowne chaced hath almoste towne troyans echone manly made fle noyse entred cyte hydous crye mortall shoute pwherof ameued ector yssueth oute furyously haste sone mar knyght maly man worthy yet worthyest euer hardyest phebus bemysclere amonge sterres dyde appere excellynge stele armed bryght heuenly syght bothe nye ferre worthynesse lode sterre whiche whan entred felde lyke rede bare daye shelde shelde whiche pure golde thre lyon storye tolde whose coloure made mencyon fynde descripcyon passant reporte ryght borne breste troyan knyght grounde rote hye prowesse floure accompted worthynesse whiche manly without abode amonge knyghtes grekes rode lyke man comynge stoned gan thrynge amonges whiche kylleth downe slethe mette nat dethe afore swerde grekes go wrake theyr wardes knyghtly force brake maugre seuered sonder bare downe rydynge yonder casuelly meteth waye prothesylaus whiche longe daye hadde sore fought agaynst troye slewe tho come waye hardy knyght worthy fyers kynge whiche troyans euer pursuynge hadde hertely great enuye whiche thynge whan ector gan espye knyghthode gan take hede towardes hym gan reyne stede lyne ryght hasty ire rode swerde disteyned blode cloue hede thorugh basenet suche myght stroke ne let force mayle thycke plate fynally full mortall fate swerde ector thrugh nerf bone vayne worthy kynge parted hath twayne vtterly gayneth none armure agayne stroke ector endure kynge full worthynesse stronge myghty great hardynesse receyued hath laste fatall wounde lyeth dede parted grounde ector forth amonge grekes ryde euer stroke abyde refute none diffence deth many greke daye sleth whiche waye stode sharpe swerde batheth blode also ferre myght hym se deth swerde fle mortal vengeafice vpon wrought many greke felowe sought gan enquere myght theyr lyfe coude neuer se none knyghtly behaue hym batayle playnely dempte supposayle ector noble warryour knyghthode may bere away flour amonge euer yet borne greke yt hy may stade aforne daye gan enchace stronde euen afore face ne durste mortall stroke abyde whan hadde vpon euery syde grekes chaced wawy see wounded mate great aduersytee hy reste troyan knyght anone lyke mar hymselfe home troye gone whose partynge grekes e presume manly agayne theyr hertes resume newe theyr foomen assayle iuparte wolde auayle lyfe deth sette outraunce fortune wolde auaunce theyr parte agayne recure felde enforce myght spere shelde anone forthwith make delay wynne agayne troyans may viij tymes sythen begonne felde haue day loste wonne lyke fortune lyste theyr cure vp downe turne hyr eure hyr whele went aboute rounde right day wan lost groude specyally moste desmayde whan ector came hath outrayde thrugh knyghthod made theyr hert tyue resorte dyde aryue thus contynued maugre theyr myght whyle felde troyan knyght tyll phebus chare gan westre downe repeyred towne whiche hadde grekes wrought afore full ylle nowe hardy cruell fyers achylle aryued knyghtes alle myrondones men wonte calle whiche see taken hath playne whose comynge grekes haue agayne felde recured put themselfe prees thorugh helpe worthy achylles whiche felly troyans falle vpon hath slayne full many oon thre thousande stele armed bryght hym brought redy fyght knyghtes echone full worthy renowne whiche achylles grekes champyowne haue mercyles theyr cruelte slayne many troyan cyte feruent theyr mortall ire enuyous hate desyre newe newe shede theyrblode achylles thought dyde hym gode swerde troyans blode shede soyle se lye blede rowteles melancolye hath hote enuye without theyr deth may nat quenche swerde full depe made drenche longe daye troyans blode batheth werein flode whiche forged whette kene many ryuer hely grene ran hurtes sore knyghtes alway pursued afore hym flee walles troye cytee made full pyteous crye whyle fynde storye grekes hoost hoolly aryued lyke guydo descryued men armes suche multytude knyghtes shortly conclude theyr shyppes newe landed troyans astoned se abasshed gan wexe alle sodaynely gan falle euery halfe passyngly great prees euer one hardy achylles swerde made theyr sydes rede lay bodyes dede wounded entre gate knyghtly gan debate furyously felle cruell knyght child slewe theyr faders syght beholde full great pyte yet slaughter gretter without nombre towne perpetuelly theyr confusyowne lykely euer haue ouercome pif troylus ne vnto rescuse come yonge fresshe lusty inly desyrous come eke parys dephebus many worthy partye socoure grekes tho ne myght endure agaynst stande deffence theyr pryde make resystence worthy troylus well yt tyme hym quytte thus sothe greke hytte outher maymeth made deye wherfore deth fled weye achylles companye nyght homewarde gan hym hye towarde grekes glorye great honoure receyue hym lyke conqueroure whiche hadde well ymet troye haue theyr gate shet made stronge thorughout al towne tyme kynge agamenowne ycherched hath place couenable whiche hym thought moste greable lyklyed moste conuenyent euery lorde sette tente felde full large space moste competent lodgynge place dewe syght sette cyte eche lorde sygned shulde gan anone ordayne mansyons pytched theyr tentes pauyllyons suche myght centoryes haue storme rayne themselfe saue deuysed habytacles tugurryes smale receptacle shroude nyght also theyr shyppes moche myght haue theyr hors lande ordayne shulde stande also besy carye thynges necessarye nedefully vnto sege longe eke made tey shyppes stronge porte ankres caste assent besyed full faste conferme one entenciowne sette sege troye towne therupon bounde assured faste abyde whyle lyfe many laste fynally without repentaunce prudently made ordynaunce beste coude longe nyght bete fyres whiche bren woder lyght space deuyded fro fyres sette vp maner bares roude aboute lodgynge paled felde compas acheue fyne purpose felly wrought kept selfe aye close pand kynge treason falle let make watche without tentes alle hadde rested afore mynstrellys made ouermore sayth guydo longe nyght kepe tydes tofore fyres bryght meryly sowne instrumentes made reste tentes afore wery fyght see faynted theyr myght eke made theyr armure awayte wysely agayne aduenture disceyte founde syde thus kynge knyghtly prouyde aduyse nothynge hym escape nyght fynde dyde wake tyll morowe rowes rede phebus chare gonne sprede thus eche kynge desposed ought wyll procede tell wrought ceryously without within supporte thyrde boke begyn begynneth thyrde boke telleth howe troy an yssued morowe fought grekes valyauntly ector bare hymselfe daye capitulo xxij whan aurora hyr pale lyght vnder mantel myrke nyght curtyne hyr hewes fade yshroudyde ye derke shade abasshed rody desyre oonly hyr femynyne ashamed durste nat seyne bycause hadde longe bedde leyne fresshe phebus owne chosen knyght whiche hydde hyr sothely syght tyll stede called flegonte enhasted hym aboue oure oryzonte appollo bemys clere hath recomforted hyr oppressed chere saye dawnynge whan tytan eest rysynge hete atempre right softe hyr emysperye glade lofte houre troyan champyowne gouernour werres towne worthy ector whiche cyte next pryam hadde souereynte towne guyde knyghtly excellence manhode sapyence troyan knyghtes lorde eke cheuetayne whiche hath comaunded large playne hye lowe exceptynge none kynges pryces lordes euerychone morowe mete yfere theyr arraye mustre apere lyke name estate besyde temple whylom consecrate goodes called dyane moste honoured ryche faane array haste lyke deuyse knyghtly man playne passynge fayre se sette amydde troye cyte smothe right fayre full fresshe floures worthy noble werryoures troye towne togydre assembled many beholde se famous knyghtes arme place gan full streyte lace theyr doublettes made lynnen clothe certayne folde aboute hym gothe also dempte moste sureste batayle ar ste dyde firste theyr desyres sabatous greues cussues voydres payre breche alder firste mayle eke ne wolde fayle haue mayle payre bra therwithall custome payregussettes pety cote garnysshed golde vp vnto throte paunce plate whiche selfe behynde shet close theron fynde enuyron abordure smalle mayle chose newe entayle surmyd foos hole breste plate arere doos behynde shet elles syde armes rynged nat wyde voyders frettyd mayle cordes rounde fresshe entayle vambras wynges rerebras therto theron sette besaguys also vpon hede basenet stele within locked full wele crafty syght wrought vyser wolde haue plate bauer breste fastened aforne canell pece esy borne gloues plate stele forged bryght pand wolde armed lyght thykkes iackes couered satyne wolde haue mayle wrought ful fyne hawberion late wrought cassade weyghte nat ouer lade hymsefe welde lyke lyfly man wyll haue choce geseran doublet hawberion oonly sure gepon ouer poleyns rechynge thekne euys eke longe vambras may cured ner pryckynge palet plate cower wyll haue also vyser saue face oonly anaser wyll haue payre platy lyght welde hym well whan shall fyght wyll haue target spere pauys body targe made stronge laste wyll haue dartes caste pollax heded fyne stele pycked square laste wele swerde enemy mete wyll haue bowe shete arblast stande asyde pand foot tyde array themsesfe foomen sayle many one besy nayle felawes harneys make stronge dresse sytte nat wronge poyntes tresshes maner thynge suche case longeth armynge haue connynge euery thynge telle vnto longe dwelle fayle ye mot haue excused suche crafte lytell vsed ignoraunce doth penne lette theyr ordre termys sette ofte chaungeth suche harneys deuyse ye therin expert wyse dysdayne nat speke place theyr armynge grace right lyste correcte euery dell whan ector sawe well euery armed arrayed worthy knyght lenger hath delayed aduysely wardes make prudently badde shulde take theyr grounde haste put certayne stande ordre endelonge playne man founde recheles gate called dardanydes without abode ector made vnshette bad men shulde fette presence done haste cyncynabor brother borne baste vnto hym firste euerychon lorde named glaucon kynges sone lycye heyre many baner displayed eyre two ector gaue guarde gouernaunce firste warde hath thousande knyghtes sette speres rounde swerdes kene whette theyr breste full many ryche shelde werechosen felde amonge beste endure myght agayne grekes manly fyght vnto ector bad anone goddes name shulde gone gate sothely rede ie te fylle myschefe nede assygned selfe place manly chere kynge trace wysely hym awaytynge thousande knyghtes haue ledynge wenge knyghtly abyde wayte hym vpon euery syde hym sone archylogus age man right vertuous fulfylle longeth knyght bothe herte also myght next ector gan deuyse next warde kynge fryse tyme called zantipus vnto hym yonge stronge desyrous assygned wayte vanere thre thousande knyght armed bryght clere whiche warde kynge alchomus also ector comaunded go byddynge mekely dyde obeye full knyghtly haue take theyr weye gate passyngly arrayed towarde grek baners fresshe displayed theyr penons vnrolled euerychone ector assygned hath anone noble yonge lusty free brother troylus fresshe vpon se whiche knyghthode suffysaunce thirde warde haue gouernaunce iii thousande knyghtes yonge age flourynge force hardy courage suche custome wont lede ector bretherhede full goodly spake sayde departynge brother quod herte louynge towardes kyndenesse though haue partye great gladnesse thy manhode ferre kouthe knyghthode thy grene youthe yet douteles fantasye full ofte daye stonde iupardye pensyfehede warde besy drede whan remembre vpon thy manhede lest thy courage vyolent thy lyfe neclygent thy selfe put ferre aduenture surquydrye moche assure thy force kynghtly sterte euery peryll thy manfull herte hauynge rewarde suche mortall stryfe wylfulnesse nouther deth lyfe aduertence thy sauacyowne fortune turneth vp downe hyr whele meuable hye lowe martys ire wynde doth blowe whiche causeth full ofte syghe thynke wake whan shulde wynke reuoluynge aye thy hasty wylfulnesse gentyll brother hardynesse thus ylke day vpon euery syde praye wysely prouyde hate yre thy foos pursuynge nat excede syttynge let prudence kepe mene wysdome eke holde agayne reyne thy herte thy fyers courage fyred haue thy grene tendre age deuoyde drede eche peryll endure enemyes thy mysauenture reioysenat myn owne brother dere myghty mar praye herte entere thus euery day troyans grounde theyr handes kepe sounde lyke wolde dyde anone humylyte manly wyse yonge iusty knyght worthy troylus herte fresshe lyght answered agayne sayd glad chere myn owne lorde brother dere god fore fully shall obeye fulfylle lyste seye vnto gentyllesse nat declyne thorugh none reklesnesse poynt comaundement hole herte best entent shall take hede playnely none ye haue sayde myn owne lord brother lothe offende greue wyse lowly toke leue forth herode lyke manly knyght beholde noble syght amonge men behaueth hym wele thre thousande knyght armed bryght stele enuyron rode troylus felde day bare shelde passant golde iij lyon rychely chaumpe asure wrought full craftely gate yssued anone hym ladde knyghtes euerychone grekes holdynge next waye ector hasteth euer maye prudently wardes ordayne noble worthy bretherne twayne kynge hupon ardelaus assygned storye telleth thus fouthe warde guye wysse lande called larysse bretherne two hadde reygned longe kynge hupon passyngly stronge stature lyke chaumpyowne saue ector troye towne none hym egall myght delyuere better knyght foon passynge despytous whiche brother called ardelaus foure thousande knyghtes hadde lede seuen thousande sothly rede lyke wrytte guydo worthy ector assygned hath also one bretherne called brymarchus noble knyght armes right famous hadde manhode passynge excellence ector taken haue lycence rode theyr waye amonge prces thorughe gate dardanydes fyfte warde haue ledynge ector comytted kynge cesoyne lorde prynce brother called pollydamas cysones hye stature myghty armes passyngly endure vpon full many man behelde theyr kynge bare thynge shelde felde gowlys fynde sygne guydo maketh mynde forth rode full sterne pa noble kynge pollydamas whan hadde ector leue take whiche euer one full besy make sixte warde dylygence kynge called pretemense full worthy bothe werre pee duke hyght sterepes whiche also full worthy honde toke folke pauonye londe gouerne felde daye whiche people hath custome aye without plate hawberion mayle swyfte hors theyr foomen assayle myghty bowes arrowes sharpe groude thorugh harneys mortally wounde folke ector eke also deyphebus assygned go felde guyde lede theyr waye faste gan spede passe dardanydes full discrtely ector chees pauyseres cladde mayle plate comaundynge yssynge gate archer felde gone many worthy well armed euerychone awayte nat lore folke spake tofore pauonye hadde none armure prudent ector make sure agrest myghty regyowne hath chosen full worthy renowne beste knyghtes euerychon two kynges esdras phyon assygned take hede fotemen whan haue nede whiche phyon made full rychely rode chare yuory whiche wheles wrought full curyous tree ycalled ebenus whiche tree groweth ferre ynde blacke hewe also fynde whan korue tree wyll wexe anone nature harde stone whan graue eyther rounde square pure golde roued chare fret perle many ryche stonys nother trowe ther none worlde shall nat fayne ladde myghty knyght twayne men armes within withoute armed stele rydynge rounde aboute worthy kynges esoras phyon ector hath called hym anone one bretherne falle guyde leder alle name pyktagoras great troyan eneas tofore made mencyon ector goode delyberacyon vij warde assygned hath kepe vpon stedys lusty lepe suche vsed moche ryde full manly knyghtes houe syde whiche emphranye vnto troye towne come ferre theyr regyowne fostre ectors sake whan hadde hym leue take rode full proudely forthe eneas gate wonder knyghtly pa brode felde tyll haue atteyned whyle ector hath ordayned lyke myn auctour reherce eyght warde folke perce worthy knyghtes manly ryght wyse whiche comytted paryse hym day awayte besyly ector full benyngnely spake sayde departynge brother myn maner thynge whan thou art passed dardanydes daye ferre put nat prees amonge grekes iupardye leste thy foon myschefe espye haue olde newe date theyr hertes full fresshe mortall hate fyre breste hath enbraced harde arraced wherfore brother loke thou wyse nat ferre fro kepe nye mysauentoure falle vpon may socoure day myn owne brother dere parys full humble chere answered sayde euery thynge wolde obeye vnto byddynge rode waye anone meyne felde cyte ector aye dyde besynesse nynthe warde ordre dresse whiche thought hymselfe lede whiche put sothly rede fyue thousande knyght borne troye towne worthyest grettest renowne passyngly famous knyghthode borne descent troyans blode pand bretherne toke hym ten suche knewe moost manly men forayne fro stocke regallye lyne borne bastardye ector great chyerte knyghthode coude themse whan hadde knyghtly purueaunce wardes set gouernaunce lyke mar hymselfe faste gan hym spede without abode take stede whiche bokes called gallathe hors hauynge soueraygnete ferre men ryde coste dare maketh great boste shape hyghte also fayrenesse strengthe loke great swyftenesse lyke hors perfourmed oute wt wyer men myght hym turne aboute lyke dare maketh mencyowne ector rode thorugh troye towne armed came hym wonder well foot hede full rychely euerydell shone bryght sonne somers day pryam helde right way whan come kynge reherseth ordre euery thynge hath done ordynaunce lowly sayde pleasaunce noble royall excellence haue chosen besy dylygence thousande knyghtes full suffysaunce fyue houndred haue attendaunce persone alway ye footman cyte shall awayte euer one wherfore lorde faste gone lowly praye worthynesse sewe v good aduysenesse towne alwaye eke ye togydre kepe knyghtes meyne beseche full myght within boundes shall fyght ye suffre none passe kepe ye hole selfe place wyxe v stronge cyte haue nede ye may aye se v releue kepynge asyde specyally abyde moste lyckely partye sustene euer amonge shall men go betwene expleyt trouthe reporte whiche parte mar lyste felde sorte power ylke day fatalle ye shalbe castell walle refuge saue v smerte specyally one thynge ye aduerte disceyte fraude treasowne compassyd behynde towne foon thorugh reklesnesse whyles besynesse agaynste felde fyght wyse therto hath syght thynge tourne vnto damage thoughe engyne worke sage victorye may conclude grekes fraude v nat delude engyne vn ware vyolence hopynge alway none offence hyghnes haue sayde worde pryamus abrayde benyngnely chere countenaunce sayde ector sothfast suffysaunce fynall truste supportacion thy wyse disposycion hoolly putte thou lyste ordayne next god shall nat fayne fayth hope sykernesse welfare sothfastnesse comytted behole thy hande gouernaunce playnely lande thou ordaynest must nedes prayer make goddes aboue celestyall preserue partye eche myschefe aduersyte thou mayste home cyte repayre honour laude victorye prayse renowne memorye thy name put remembraunce perpetuelly thyne honour auaunce fare well myn owne sone dere ector tho full humble chere leue toke forthe rode anone amonge lordes knyghtes euerychone rote noblesse knyghthod groude strength hardynesse stocke therto inuyncyble asmoche possyble nature myght hym graunte kynde touchynge manhode bokes fynde hadde hym soueraygne excellence gouernaunce medlyd prudence nought sterte hy wyse ware shelde fynde bare vpon breste troyan champyon chief golde gowlys alyon depeynt therm baner bete selfe amydde strete toke waye dardanydes beholde huge prees noyse trumpettes claryons baners vnrolled longe fresshe penons rede whyte grene blewe blake wyse ector hath take felde without wt herte hole entent mar hymselfe hadde present guydo maketh mynde rode warde lafte behynde manhode wolde nat abyde smote stede sherpely syde fell courage hath hors payned firste warde hath attayned vale hylle fore frounteres nat astoned fell cheres grekes platly nat aferde lyke knyght euen afore theyr berde gan prease theyr foo mortall whyle vpon troye wall sondry place hye toures fresshe besene may floures ladyes ascended towne fayre yonge stondynge enuyrowne quene eleyne passynge fayre sene kynges doughtres goodly polycene many whiche womanhede herte full besy drede inly gaste fere frayde whan behelde felde displayde brode baners tendernesse loue kyndenesse pale dredefull theyr lordes theyr face hydde eke fere nat bolde lyfte vp theyr syght beholde armure clere bryght glyterynge agayne sonne shene theyr hertes tendre myght nat sustene theyr drede thus ette dwelle grekes forth shall telle ye lyste abyoe whyle must fordulled style agayne direct agamenon well may make exclamacyon ignoraunce standeth lyght whiche causeth full clowdy syght makynge speke werre lacke termes must nedes erre connyngely wardes sette cruell allector besy lette nyghtes doughter blynded derkenesse crafte armes trouthe expresse ordre dewe felde descryue chauncer ala nat alyue refourme rede lacke slower spede noble rethor dyde excelle makynge dranke welle vnder pernaso mus kepe whiche hylle myght neuer slepe vnneth slombre whiche ala playne sayne thoughe wede nat polymyte coloures forth wyll endyte cometh euen thought playnely wryte kynghath wrought manly knyght great agamenon lyke latyn maketh mencyou pwhat troweye entent founde slowe outher neclygent grekes halfe wardes make nay nay nat hym lyste wake tyme sothly slepe lyke kynge day felde kepe neclygence myght herte fade daye fynde made sixe twenty wardes well deuysed prudently man myght amende ordynaunce firste gaue gouernaunce manfull noble patroclus wt hym ladde myn auctour telleth thus myrundones myghty stronge folke achylles longe besyde thylke meyne whiche brought countre comynge sege troye rode forth waye felde made delay fyll day achylles kepte hym tente sykenesse daye ne wente lechesse made hym abstene woundes fresshe grene caught day tofore whiche hele theyr akynge sore counsayle kepte hymselfe close bed day nat ne rose hope oonly bettre endure whan restored vnto cure men toke patroclus whiche marmes passyngely famous descent come great kynrede also hym rede haboundaunt golde rychesse ferre comended gentyllesse hadde name hye discresyon aye suche affeccyon entyer loue trouthe faythfulnesse
