great desyre inwarde kyndenesse besy thenkynge great feruence moche frenshyp thoughtfull aduertence huge brennynge passynge amerous betwyxe achylles patroclus theyr hertes locked chayne euer shall nat fayne ton hath wrought broder vnto brother herte confermed tother wyll goodes bothe comune deth euer contune without chaunge theyr loue abode pand patroclus forth anone hym tode felde myrundones tente abyteth achylles seconde warde kynge meryon assygned agamenon worthy kynge ydumenee duke hyght menestee thre thousande knyghtes stele armed clene folke came athene assygned go thyrde warde kynge astalapho sone hyght phylymene knyghtes came cu ene fourthe warde without lettynge archelaus noble worthy kynge prothenor securydan whiche dayes stronge man assygned hoolly thre knyghtes boece great lande famous fyfte warde kynge menelaus folke regyowne called spertence full hye renowne iles adiacent thyse baner went menelay fresshe couragyous vi warde kynge epystrophus assygned kynge elyde many worthy rydynge syde prouynce famous yle called guydo fordesyle vii warde thelamonyus called ayax great kynge famous assygned ely termyne kes fro salamyne hym brought many another mo foure erles hym went also theseus eke amphymacus thyrde called daryus fourthe named polysarye viij warde shall nat tarye good aduyse daye assygned vnto kynge called thoas ayar cyleus ix warde ladde x kynge phylyk hadde kynge xi dyde assygne sothely bothe berthe lyne renowmed great encrease myghty kynge called pallamydes kynge nawlus sone hyest borne blode duke nestor full famous knyghthode xij warde ladde grekes syde melancolyke surquedous pryde kynge honux sone one mabente felde playnely whan wente ordre hadde wardes thyrtene proudely mustrynge endelonge grene agayne troyans redy fyght eke kynge vlyxes hyght ladde hym fourtene ede humerus kynge eke dyde lede fy eneth myne auctour wryteth thus duke called curybulus syxteneth ladde vpon daye whiche kynght kyng prothesylaye assygned great ordynaunce enforce vengaunce vpon deth theyr worthy kynge ector slayne grekes arryuynge kynge roydo ladde seuentene kynge occymene xviij warde hadde ledynge zantipus lyde kynge hadde kepe comytted garde grekes syde xix warde xx myn auctour lerneth v hadde kynge called amphymacus lyke knyght guyde wysse phylocetes kynge larysse one twenty ladde eke rede two twenty hadde dyomede heneus kynge cyparye whylom noble worthy thre twenty hadde gouernayle troyans proudely assayle xxiiij swerde spere shelde bynge prothaylus ladde felde carpenor carpedye kynge werre expert right wyse workynge fyue twenty ryche well besayne grekes syde brought playne sixe twenty sothely laste coudese afore caste euery thynge good inspeccyon wyse kynge great agamenon hadde hym prudent werryour ordayned emperour grekes hoost wysest echone wyse forthe grekes gone felde pompe full royall ensygnes token marcyall haue take theyr grounde passyngely arrayed theyr standardes rychely displayed brode banerys many fresshe penowne agayne wynde yt made hydous sowne right dredefull playnely theremen sawe many crestys clere many tufte golde syluer shene meynt fetheres redde whyte grene deuyse wonder incruaylous folkes amerous token borne shewe openly loue brente inwardly hye empryse day fulfylle herde loude noyses shrylle ferre felde dredefull souns bothe trumpettes claryouns kalendes shedynge blode noyse almoste rage wode fomy brydelles mouthes blede furyous neyhyng many bastarde stede praunsynge hors vpon eyther syde ensygnes myght pryde grekes partye troye also knyghtly wyse haue euery warde standynge place firste sonder lytell space began reproche full entent ector tho full vnpacyent formest syde torye ire whome man myght accoye lyke lyon hungry rage yssued furyous vysage towarde grekes myghty stede spore made sydes blede knyghtly herte inly torne mortall ire rode toforne brennynge full hote melancolye whiche thynge whan grekes gan espye patroclus without abode surquedye afore wardes rode toforne bothe hoostes syght encountre playnely myght worthy ector whan hym sawe ferre right lyne dyameterre rode vnto hym hatefull tene spere sherpe grounde kene thorughout shelde enuyous rage smote ector without damage excepte oonly hede stele afore forged whet full wele thorugh plate mayle myghtely gan glace skynne thyng myght trace albe came passynge vyolence yet ector dyde none offence sadell one hym flytte though sturdely hym hytte myght nat bakwarde bowe chyne partye make hym enclyne fatally confusyon myghty man troyan champyon ire aye brennynge vpon hym hate frat sore left spere myne auctor wryteth thus swerde rode patroclus auysed fully shalbe dede furyously gan ayme hede rofe hym downe theyr maner let breste thorugh basenet sayth guydo great payne stroke parted hym wayne mortall swerde whetted kene patroclus myght nat sustene vpon hors fyll downe grounde caught laste fatall wounde beynge present knyghtes euerychone delyuerly vpon hym anone worthy ector stede downe descendyd lyke wode lyowne hatefull ire brennynge fyre hauynge herte inly great desyre spoyle hym armure anone whiche full many ryche stone bothe rubyes saphyres ynde dayes playnely fynde kynges lordes knyghtes naye batayle went theyr beste araye sothly ector whan firste gan se multytude stone pe patro lu oryent sheyne vpon arme hynge hors reyne meane whyle whyle hole entent catche praye dylygent couetyse theyr alder syghtes tyll meryon thre thousade knyghtes armed stele rounde aboute hym alle sodaynely vpon ector falle dede corp patroclus saue purpose ector may nat haue lyberte ryche kynge spoyle whiche caused hym angre boyle kynge called meryon irous wode sayde amonge echon gredy lyon wolfe moste tauynous hatefull tygre passynge enuyous auaryce beste saturable desyre sothly vnstaunchable vpon praye thou shalt nat fede go elles sewe thy mede truste well conclusyon fyfty thousande thy destruccyon one entent playnely wyll nat fayle thyne hatefull pry e attones assayle sodaynely speres sharpe whette euery halfe gan hym besette maugre force myght manhode enforcynge refte hym stede soth fastely great vyolence constrayned stronge defence sayth guydo falle vpon kne thorugh myght magnanymyte manhode hath horse recured maugre grekes moche assured strengthe great myght recured lyke worthy knyght stede agayne amyddes foon right syne rode meryon full desyrous hym auenged furye hasty cruelte therupon sette delyte mortall lody appety e sothe hym slayne anoon saue kynge whiche called glacon came rescue hym kynge theseus sone hyght archylogus haue tolde meryon reskewe th e thousande knyghtes gan hym sewe full al ted attones batayle lyfe th ector assayle awayte vnware hym sette al whyle euer mette swerde kylled bare downe fynally gayneth raunsowne greke durste hym mete departynge felte full vnswete made waye aboute hym euery fledde hym deth fere rode made patthe ful playne rede patroclus agayne repeyred spoyle hym myght amyd felde grekes syght wolde praye nat lyghtly lete tyll dumee myghty kynge crete two thousande cladde plate mayle worthy kynghtes ector assayle whyles desyrous haue tolde spoyle patroclusi newe agayne confusyon lyke fynde came kynge meryon ector myght take hede force refte hym stede sothely none boote compelled fyght foote knyghode herte resumeth wt swerde aboute hym consumeth withstande bothe hors man furyously troyan knyght began armes legges shuldres boon hewe amydde mortall foon grekes myght afore hym nat sustene rede slewe fyftene besy hym take slaughter gan amoge make ne durste abyde afore face meryon selfe place meane whyle toke vp patroclus heuy chere face full pyruous tede layde hym beforne tente anone hath borne alwaye grekes theyr cruell mode aboute ector furyous wode felly ode fyghtynge vpon fote whiche felte vnlote presumed vpon hym presse manhode ne wolde cesse besette hym euery syde hauynge truste theyr great pryde fynally myschefe hym take dempte myght nat escape theyr handes shortly none aduenture stede lyklyhede recure force caste hym lette attones gan hym sette specyally amonge euerychone fynde sothe howe one grekysshe knyght right worthy fame caryon playnely name hym aforced ector oppresse whan moste myschefe distresse besette grekes hym enuyrownynge tyll fortune hym awaytynge longe daye felle fyght rescuse came atroyan knyght mydde grekes whan besette toke ij dartes sharpe kene whette furyously firste shoke toon thorugh herte smote caryon darte felde gan glyde plate mayle thorughout outher syde fatally dedely wounde caryon glode anone grounde amonge hondred knyghtes ferys afore conspyred theyr felle cherys slayne ector maner waye eft agayne yonge knyght troye full delyuerly raughte nother spere caste one sawe afere auaunce hymselfe ector felde thorugh platy playnely shelde lyne right ne shulde asterte myght roofe hym thorughe herte haste coude vpon troyans gan crye loude enhaste knyghtly socoure whorthy ector stode aduentoure amonge grekes hauynge refute sool hymselfe helpe destytute whiche crye grekes vnware firste came worthy cyncybare brother ector baste borne hymselfe rydynge toforne knyghtes whiche guyde wonder proudely pryckynge syde sodaynely bothe one alle frosshe grekes falle hadde ector rounde beset aboute thorugh manhode great route enbosshed backe threhondred knyghtes whiche yt spacke astoned gan withdrawe thurty firste cruelly slawe maugre ector manhede amyd felde taken hath stede entred amonge prees daye knyghthode pereles whyle helde blody swerde honde tho agayne hym stonde helpe playnely rede brake karfe two threde knotte cruell antropos onely let purpose good leyser spoyle patroclus therfore ire wode furyous full cruelly grekes quytte theyr mede whiche face faste gan spede whose sharpe swerde bathed theyr blode dyed rede dyde hym gode vpon auenged daye lyon played vpon grekes manhode haunte theyr pryde mortally gan daunte hym fledde rode makynge hote streyntes theyr blode endelonge renne vpon grene tyll tyme duke great athene called whylom menesteus thre thousande knyghtes full famous whiche bothe lorde guyde felde hath take vpon lefte syde deceyte full secrete wyse pwhere troylus folke fryse whiche hath daye lyste seke knyghthode kylled many greke lyke tygre gredy pray troylus bare hym longe day sleynge grekes many worthy knyght whyle besyest fyght agayne foon kynge antipus kynge hyght alchanus vpon grekes ylyche fresshe newe makynge theyr sydes blody hewe one assent thre thorugh theyr mahede specyally vpon bay stede euer troylus rode euery greke swerde abode sodaynely made sterue thorugh theyr plate depe gan kerue contynued tyll duke meneste troylus sawe great cruelte slaughtre grekes made hasty ire face pale fade hent spere threwe rest troylus smette euen amyd brest sternely maugre renowne erthe anone bare hym downe myddes mortall foon cruelly hym besette anoon hym treyne layde oke lase rounde aboute maner compase spere darte swerdes forged bryght hymselfe diffendeth lyke knyght great manhode honour auaunce albe lyfe hanged balaunce stode felte full vnswete poynt deth amonge horse fete great awayte duke meneste howe troylus myght haue take mortall hate castynge thought myschefe take escape nought euery halfe besette swerdes rounde kene grounde whette alone ala mortally bestadde seased hym forth haue hym ladde tyll myseres worthy knyght troye gan crye stode waye sore abasshed right furyous wyse ye noble worthy men fryse manly knyghtes aye preuyd felde moste renowmed bothe spere shelde consyder nowe vnto hye fame aduerte glorye name daye thorugh neclygence power myghty vyolence grekes troylus ytake sool felde ye haue hym forsake shall rebounde alder shame ye sothe greatly blame worthynesse floure take grekes lacke socoure ye take hasty wreche shamefull reporte honour shall apeche perpetuelly sayde therof amys defaute troylus taken whiche named worthy famous worde kynge alkamous melancolye felte herte ryue ire hente spere blyue pryckynge enhateth myght tyll playnely syght besy troylus ede full knyghtly syttynge stede ran one thorugh fell downe dede efte agayne pale thynge rede rancoure lenger wolde lette greke firste mette thorugh body smet spere men myght se poynt fere breste plate thorugh shulder bone grounde fell downe dede anone therwithall worthy fry alle came flokmele downe grekes falle myghtely maugre theyr diffence sette vpon great vyolence troylus daunger fre thorugh theyr knyghtly magnanymyte made hym recure stede specyally helpynge nede zantipus stronge manly kynge whiche disdayne comynge ou meneste gan spere grate thorugh shelde mayle thycke plate sore smote meneste hadde dede ne hadde armour whiche ire gan tremble shake troylus hondes take escaped prysoner despyte berde maugre power wherfore gan hasty hote enuye knyghtes furyously crye myghty renowmed stronge payne venge wronge vpon troyans mete face hast gan myghtely enbrace theyr sharpe speres grounde byte felly foyne togydre smyte tho began great mortall werre fyre brast shene sterre basenertes theyr plate bryght thorugh felde flaumeth ye fereful lyght lyfe deth toke tho hede downe playne lengthe brede wardes gan proudely auale lokes enuye pale aproche assemble yfere hate brennynge man may stere gan hurte spere swerde darte mortally vpon euery parte slaughter gan greatly rewe ylyche alwaye newe newe ector grekes thorugh worthynesse rode manly dyde oppresse mercylesse slowe bare downe without excepcyowne furyously routhe se newe duke meneste repayred enuyous herte hondes troylus sterte slaughter eke meynee rode besy ee troyan people whan myght mete auenge hym nothynge wolde lete tyll casuelly amonges prees knyght mette hyght miserees whiche despyte meneste hadde reskus worthy troylus maugre hym put hym pray befelle selfe day mete agayne aduenture meneste cote armure marked hym armes bare sodaynely ware myght take hede furyously sterne stede spere amyd renges alle bare hym ouer made hym falle maugre myght erthe downe fynde kynge hupowne descended storye lyste nat lye two thousande knyghtes companye whiche grekes felly gan sette berde kynge prothenor mette archelaus noble werryour boece lorde gouernour helpe oonly prothenor lyke tygre wood boor gan troyans assayle deth many one daye sleeth kynge hupon thorugh chyualrye tyme melancolye full many greke gaue dethes wounde thus gan eche confounde suche mortall hate amonges tyll fortune knyght pollydamas troye syde sone anthenor knyghtes hymselfe tofor grekes enuyous pryde myd theyr wardes falle syde gan breke knyghtly disseuer agayne whose swerde myght nat seuer inly furyous hym helpe came kynge remus wynge parte brekynge many spere darte agayne grekes thre thousande knyghtes beholde felly fyghtes sothe vnto troye luste heuenly ioye se grekes brake asondre noyse loude thondre felde stroke gan aryse whyle remus ye haue herde deuyse vpon grekes enuyous felde came menelaus worthy knyghtes spartense agayne remus make resystence full proudely makynge delaye worthy remus kynge menelaye hors backe sharpe speres whette myd felde enuye mette thorugh manly prowesse renowne hors backe eche bare downe none stroke myght shone whyle anthenor sone pollydamas lusty fresshe lyght delyuer myght desyrous honour atteyne mette felde neuewe eleyne myghty duke called mereus flourynge youthe right vertuous fresshe armed newe lusty courage sothe twenty yere age whiche yonge noble knyght right renowmed bothe herte myght fortune befell ala troyan knyght dauz pollydamas spere thorugh shelde mayle plate hytte hym cruell fate amonge grekes felle downe dede whiche thynge whan menelay toke hede sawe hym lye slayne grene herte remembrynge quene quene eleyne whose neuewe dole whiche full delyuer pa remus rode cruelte also ferre myght hym se full knyghtly mette hym berde smette hym sharpe swerde vpon hede hatefull tene stede myght nat sustene wounde passyngely mortall stroke pryllous fall knyghtes wende dede hadde hent hym vp began fle troye warde hym great paas befell pollydamas maner whan behelde made repayre knyghtly felde excepte byddynge hadde worthy remus home troye ladde pale dede woundes wyde tho came grekes syde celydys lusty fresshe kynge dare sayth wrytynge sothe boke lyste telle celydys dyde excelle bothe beaute semelyhede shape porte goodlyhede surmountynge dare lyste descryue fayrenesse tho alyue lymmes compact clene rede yonge fresshe quene fumynye whiche beaute floure kynge celydys loued paramoure vpon hym hooly hir pleasaunce prynted hir remembraunce chefe resorte sothely hir herte vpon hym euery houre aduerte fynally departed nought day nyght houre hir thought fully hir owne knyght fortune lusty fresshe lyght smote stede sharply syde surquedye proudely gan ryde mortall hate full furyous paas right lyne pollydamas spere made hym flytte sadell whiche dyde sytte marked hym great myght agaynewarde manly troyan knyght pollydamas despytous face celydys departed fro place aswerde smet hym hede stede fylle downe dede whiche grekes great confusyon tyme fyerser lyon ector grekes knyghtly gan enchace ofte made lese theyr place euer rode necessyte afore swerde made fle suche vengeaunce hath take felde fayne forsake pursewe wolde neuer fyne tyll amonge people salomyne ector mette worthy kynge famous theyr lorde hyght thesalus many troyan day hadde slawe ector towarde hym gan drawe kynge tenter grece also manly knyght prudent bothe two raught spere haste vnwarely vnto ector ran thorughe shelde plate mayle stele sperehede forged wele sharpe square kene grounde gaue ector full peryllous wounde ector reyne gan stede proude tenter aquyte mede full wysely haste myght right ferre seuered syght wherof ector melancolyous herte wood furyous akynge wounde grene haste auenge constreynte ten greke shortly mette bolde waye sette without mercy deth anone rede encountred one whiche pryde wolde hym dyuerte swerde rose herte thorugh harneys melancolye whiche stroke whan grekes gan espye astoned one entencyon peryllously besette hym enuyron suche assaute gan aboute hym make thorugh theyr mahode myght hy take accorde great multytude cruelly gan hym include lyklyhede mortall stryfe myght nat escape lyfe hym fell enuyous tyll kynge whiche hyght theseus grekes syde oonly gentyllesse suche routhe caughe vpon distresse se hym stande nye vpon wrake thus vnto hym manly pytespake flour knyghthode rote hardynes welle manhode stok worthynes lyst nat haue none aduertece thy lyf saue knyghtly prouydece wylfully moste drede thy lyfe iupardest take lyste hede mortall peryll thou arte besette amonge many closed yshette alone ala deuoyde socoure thy selfe wylt fauoure fortune lyketh ordayne euery wyght ought complayne beholde noble knyght whiche thorugh world cast clere lyght worthynesse wyll hym nat withdrawe reklesly day slawe pyteously thy persone lese withdrawe thy hande yet syth yu mayst chese thy hye prowesse compelleth preye suche myschefe thou nat ne deye whan ector hym gan take hede thanked hym goodlyhede maugre sothly power myght grekes lyke worthy knyght scapyd myd foon went waye thorugh euerychon blody swerde alway honde waye pollydamas fonde full lyke man besy payne diffende hymself agayne kynges twayne menelay thelamonyus whiche vpon hym full furyous wt spere greke thelamowne pollydamas smote erthe downe compellynge hym none vote agayne two fyghte fote assentyd fully hym wroke firste haue wen broke myghty charnelle basenet whan vyser smet face naked bare felle hym mortall snare toke hym storye deuyse sent hym forth full cruell wyse towarde grekes many worthy knyght whan ector therof syght sawethe myschefe pollydamas caste fully socoure caas prycked wooder lyon rode aboute hym enuyron swerde made large space tyll came place amonges greke furyous wode pollydamas selfe tyme stode socourles remedye tyll ector caste eye grekes made hastely withdrawe thurty firste hath slawe seuered maugre theyr pryde tofore swerde durste nat abyde agaynst hym make none obstacle knyghthode hye myracle pollydamas myschefe firste awhaped grekes honde frely escaped fresshely tho kynge epystrophns menelay thelamonyus theyr knyghtes togydre hole cloos agayne troyans gette aloos newe entred batayle great strengthe passynge apparayle myghtely troyans compelle theyr waye dare nat dwelle natwithstandynge theyr great worthynesse ector knyghtly hye prowesse fought manly tyme rede cowardely haue slayne stede constrayned fyght fote many greke felte full vnsote none aboute hym stode swerde ne shadde blode though thycke aboute layne voyded made aspace playne compasse rounde behynde eke afore fete well hath hym bore day greke none certayne harby hande hym layne stronge sturdy wall whan brother called naturall sawe hym fote amyd foon frusshe felle euerychon founde hym storye maketh mynde diffende hymselfe lyke tygre ynde hym helpe thorugh theyr hye renowne felle firste kynge thelamowne ector cruell founde gaue hym many blody wounde tyll one named dyndaron hath ferre amonge rengys gon bore hym oonly manhede hath wonne passynge myghty stede brought ector sothly stode amonge grekes bathed theyr blode whiche haste full knyghtly strode amoge lyke mar hymself rode full many greke makynge sterue swerde whetted kerue daunted hath theyr enuyous pryde tyll dephebus entrede syde felde knyghtly chere hym brought many good archere poeme whiche theyr arrowes kene fethers pecok fresshe shene vpon grekes haue felde recured shotte moche assured thorugh mayle thycke plate stele perced haue theyr harneys euerydele dephebus full lyke manly man kynge tentran hors backe tho ran furyously gan swerde enbrace wounded hym euen amyd face thorughe vyser felle tene hors backe myght nat sustene thus troyans grekes yronne agayne haue felde ywonne yrous wode theseus full knyghtly withstode knyghtes hym ladde rede ectora brother hadde storye sayth hyght quyntylene yonge fresshe lusty armed bryght shene whiche kynge called modernus proudely falle vpon theseus twayne togydre assent falle hym great aduysement fynally vnhappy chaunce wt theyr knyghthode brought hy outtrauce caste shortly shalbe dede whose purpose ector gan take hede vnto gentery myght loude gan crye besechynge thynge deye lowely byddynge dyde obeye withdrewe vengeaunce ector hadde fully remembraunce theseus daye tofore towarde hym goodly hadde hym bore whan hym sawe myschefe distresse knyghtly thought quyte gentylnesse lyke logeth euery gentylman theseus full lowely tho began thanke ector escaped kynge thoas tho hath faste raped felde knyghtes manye specyally calydonye came phyloteas myghty kynge also agayne troyans haue ado firste thoas spere ran furyously cassybelan one sone kynge pryamus gaue hym tho wounde greuous without recure fell downe dede whiche stroke whan ector gan take hede herte gan deth complayne haste dyde besy payne brother auenge hym myght many one made lyght thorugh knyghthode hors bake sothefastly went vnto wrake grekes syde came way worthely bare hym day tyll duke nestor entrede fyght fyue thousande stele armed bryght agayne troyans grekes socoure hym mette auenture kynge esdras myghty bolde kynge phyon chare golde worthy noble chyualrye argesta came ieconye kynges sone lande full renowmed worthy hande semble togydre ran tyme many worthy man hath loste lyfe vpon eyther syde slaughtre large woundes wyde soyle bodyes laye dede lyke ryuer ran stremys rede theyr cherys grysely pale fade blode men myght go wade ancle slaughtre huge kynge phyon socour refuge vnto troyans bare hym stryfe many greke made lese lyfe day well swerde whette vnwarely sore besette multytude grekes rounde aboute lyfe playnely stode doute lykely myght nat escape grekes shulde anone take ne hadde holpe worthy ieconye esdras loude gan crye ala quod routhe pyte pworthy phyon kynge shall take amonge grekes thorugh neclygence haste ye dylygence reskewe noble worthy kynge attones without tariynge maugre tho made resystence grekes swerde myghty vyolence haue reskewed noble kynge phyon large goon escape wonder gladde lyght ector many lusty knyght retourned dephebus also pollydamas many another troyan knyghtes desyre newe grekes make sore rewe assent fully purpose suche myschefe grekes enclose myght fewe shulde escape therupon knyghtly shape began fresshely assayle felde grekes gan fayle theyr power lese theyr lande fynally thorugh myghty hande force troianysshe knyghtes grekes hadde maugre theyr myghtes brought day confusyowne menelay kynge thelamowne whan sawe febly apeyre knyghthode made repeyre lyke men haue themself diffendyd tyll eneas troye discendyd ewfremus duke manly man theyr knyghtes newe began efte agayne grekes oppresse ector aye thorugh worthynesse lyke lyon sterne face euer one gan enchace compellyd necessyte echone afore swerde fle constrayned ryght nede whiche thynge whan ayax gan take hede hadde herte great compassyon se slaughter confusyon grekes syde guydo maketh mynde gan loke backe behynde sawe many warde stode abrode many baner penowne abode amyd felde hole nat broke redy attones wroke nede troye towne whiche wardes without excepcyowne hole floure grekes chyualtye anone ayax gan hym hye sore herte agreued crye hath comeued haste come reskuse amonges refuse faste gan assemble noyse hors erthe gan tremble furyously togydre flynge myght men strokys rynge sperys sharpe thorugh harneys borne thorugh sheldes wrought stele horne breste sturdy square brode fynde ayax rode eneas hym also great enuye atwyxe two nat deth myght theyr yre apese herte nouther myght haue ese tyll sperys sharpe grounde whette hors backe haue togydre mette coupynge sore haue hytte eueryche erth smytte beholde knyghtly syght bothe fote fyght lyklyhede theyr wode rage outher falle full great damage amonge horse stode vpon soyle louer sparde blode phyloteas ayar come hath hym vp amonge horse ynome knyghtly faught made memorye sothely ellys troyans victorye hadde felde playnely sayne tyll phyloteas wardes twayne euen face manly withstode spere firste ector rode vpon hym shafte fynde brake sothly vpon horse bake kept hym well felle stroke remeuynge nat sturdy oke sat sadell vpryght chyne spere right lyne body depe thorugh shelde phyloteas smote felde lyfe knyghtes doute tho came great route bynge humerus vlixes eke brought many worthy greke ten thousande knyghtes manly men echone gan troyans assoyle anone cruelly euery halfe certayne multytude haue layne dispayred disconsolate longe fyght awaped mate gan withdrawe faynted batayle eke theyr hors sothly gan fayle theyr syde went vp downe parys tho troye towne entrede full manly wyse firste mette kynge fryse vlixes nye allye parys smote great enuye hym slewe wherof grekes sore abasshed spere vlixes de auenge hym myght firste whan parys hadde syght reste gan spere throwe fynally bare lowe faylynge parys sothly rede vnder hym slewe myghty stede maugre hym grounde gone hym wolde haue falle anone troylus tho mette hym berde furyously sharpe swerde smote vlixes thorugh vyser lyke condyte small ryuer downe face blode stremys ran vlixes lyke manly man stroke astoned nat stede styffe wall swerde myghtely gan race thorughe vmbrer troylus face hym gaue large mortall wounde whiche stroke passyngly iocounde grekes supposyng theyr thought troyans fynally brought vnto traunce sothely hadde saue ector wt kynghtes whiche ladde hym eke parys dephebus brother knyghthod famous troylus also laste wounde alway noble knyght founde attones ioyned one vpon grekes sodaynely gone worthy ector alder firste began grekes enchace afore hym ran lyke bestes fledde fro deth euer one swerde sleth mette durste stroke abyde soon fresshe woundes wyde slaughter made alway renewe thylke daye blody rosen hewe hath theyr platy theyr harneyse steyned though hadde blode fro heuen reyned soyle redder myght nat ben aye ylyche swarme grekes flockmele fledde way guydo sayth ylke day actor hadde formest playne frounter grekes layne behynde knyghtes garde lacke hym warde wherfore whan hadde sought longe grekes sawe newe wexe stronge knyghtes agayne repayred whiche themselfe greatly dispayred absence tho whan hym se full inwardely recomforted glad herte haue lorde receyued theyr gladnesse whan hath parceyued spake vnto full affectuously prayed full benyngnely remembre knyghtly theyr herte consyder wysely aduerte firste wronges grekes haue yore agoo ouermore also grekes hadde day victorye farewell aye honour glorye troyan blode conclusiowne fynally eke towne shall mortally turne ruyne honour wont shyne thorugh worlde worthynesse eclypse shall turne derkenesse ye day lyke men quyte wherfore praye man atwyte hye renowne cowardyse sette vpon full manly wyse nat spare drede deth praye echone full lowely gan obaye desyre without lenger tale entrynge certayne vale vpon grekes worthy knyghtes folowynge ector sodaynely fall full mortally ware ector tho greke wolde spare euery theyr confusyon kylled slewe aboute hym enuyron knyghtes rydynge syde made theyr omen maugre theyr pryde lese theyr londe flewe theyr syght tyll kynge whiche toas hyght grekes syde warde gan hym dresse newe full knyghtly gan oppresse troye kynge manly man hadde afore slayne cassybelan one sone kynge pryamus rode fortune felle thus bretherne frusshe mette whiche assent enuyron hym sette sadell many greke behelde amonge hors smethym felde rente firste basenet cruelly hadde hede smet vnarmed myschefe stode saue duke furyous wode athenys rydynge great pace reskued hym mortall cace knyghtes aboute hym rode hym helpe without abode aspere sharpe whette kene firste felle quyntylene besy thoas haue slawe bretherne made also withdrawe whan quyntylene hors throwe parys tho drewe vp myghty bowe duke lette arowe glyde thorugh plate hyt hym syde vpon ryb made hym sore blede whiche stroke ne toke hede bycause oonly feruent amyd foon helpe kynge thoas amonge hors bore grounde poynt deth many mortall wounde oonly naked hede duke fully deuoyde drede knyghode pecyllous caas amyd foon hath holpe kynge thoas lyfe made hym scape free ector aye cruell enmytee ilyche fresshe thynge wolde leue vpon grekes manhode preue enforsynge hym theyr destruccy wone rode amonge vp downe kynge humerus hath bowe take shote gan hym redy make hatefully therin sette arowe ector marked hath narowe smote hym euen amyd face myght fertherpase ector smet hym great payne wt swerde rose hede wayne deth whan grekes knowe myn auctor sayth haue horne yblowe vnwarly dredefull sowne seuen thousade knyght came attones downe aboute ector without abode force thorugh rode maugre theyr myght hym tho sette slowe tho waye lette stynte nat playnely tyll cam fader worthy kynge pryam many worthy full famous renowne knyghtes faste towne lay daye men hors foote knyghode croppe roote kept hym close full hye prudence tyll ector came vnto presence hym besoughte great nede thre thousande wolde hym spede vpon grekes theyr felle rage falle moost auauntage hast worthy pryamus knyghtes fresshe desyrous towarde grekes hath waye take suche mordre gan vpon make many grekes lay dede playne pryamus sore hath layne euery halfe thorugh great myght full faste fledde syght sore newe vpon sette fynde togydre mette actor ayax auenture theyr stedes stronge wonder sure storye sayth haste konne lyke wood lyon togydre ronne great myght lefe lothe vpon playne vnhorsed bothe whyle menelay kynge sodaynely came rydynge slewe troye worthy amyrall thus slaughtre passyngly mortall benewed aye celydonas neue slewe kynge thoas madan met myn auctor wryteth thus grekysshe kynge called cedyus whiche wt swerde suche stroke hym sette thorughe vmbrer eye smette sardellus troye eke whyle slewe worthy greke lorde name hye prowesse though guydo name nat expresse also came margaryton troye syde agayne thelamon bothe two inly sette fyre hye disdayne hatefull yre mette hors backe yfere kynge thelamon sothly lere gaue vnto hym woundefull cruell tho came troyan phanuell prothenor smote downe stede thus sone playnely rede pryamus thynge disamayde grekes haue euery part outrayed knyghtly daye borne many greke fatally hath lorne lyfe sothe hate enmyte kynge duglas falle meneste athenys duke gouernoure aspere ire olde rancoure ran hym smet hym amyd shelde sadell yet helde duke spere hadde none swerde duglas rode anone thorugh owmbrer rofe nye nase astoned stode mase whan sawe condyte blode streme rode asyde fully deuoyde fere vnto tyme staunched deamor owne brother dere whan behelde mortall blody chere hye disdayne rode meneste hym vnhorseth vp anone sterte myght fully vp aryse another brother full cruell wyse falle hym thre attones vpon meneste fully purpose shall lese lyfe knyghtly bare hym stryfe agaynst wonder se vpon hym moste cruell thre one thoras eldest echone whiche hym slayne besy euer one broke haue basenet whan tenter sawe hym beset grekysshe kynge made mencyon hadde herte great compassyon thought playnly manhode hym releue myght foomen greue nought besy payne ector e le bothe twayne vpon tenter meneste hadde slayne ne hadde ayaxbe whiche vnto ector faste gan hym hye thousande knyghtes companye withstande hym meneste saue handes myght hym haue parys tho kynge perce fyue thousande reherce worthy knyghtes many troyan mo vnto ector attones go thryfty wyse rydynge rowe parys made trumpet blowe whiche came knyghtly enbataylled many troyan full well apparaylled whiche felde ector conueyed one herte fully haue obeyed vnto byddynge troyan knyght fresshe newe tobegynne fyght vpon grekes ferforth slayne many manly man aye slaughter pyteously reneweth many greke sore herte reweth theyr great losse destruccyowne wrought vpon troye towne specially ector fynde whiche day dare maketh mynde hande thousande knyghtes slowe neuer dawed theyr sowe greke dare none waye dwelle wt swerde coude compelle lese theyr grounde necessyte lyke shepe afore wolfe fle rede amyd victorye ector mette vnder tentorye amonge grekes meryon kynge spake without taryenge thou traytoure thy houre aprocheth faste thou arte come sothely thy laste thy fatall day hath course yronne truste well westrynge sonne caste platly quyte thy mede wt swerde haste thy blode shede thou bolde day lette ryche pray spoylynge kynge patroclus cause thou presumptuous disturbe thou shalt anone dede downe sterte smote first hede hym spoyle also gan hym haste meneste came hym faste whan behelde trauerse backe aspere whiche lacke smote hym great vyolence without syght aduertence worthy ector takynge hede wounde sore gan blede went made faste bynde meneste stale away behynde nat purpose sothly may mete ector ylke day whan ybounde sore wombe staunche blede furyous euer tofore repayred anger tore aye yre herte fret bare downe euer met sleeth kylleth mercyles tho put themselfe prees hardy hym mete boke lyke wryte darete sothe storye sayth men may gyue fayth credence possybylyte guydo clerely ye mayse caughte latter wounde fynally grekes confounde affermyd certayne thousande knyght wt hande slayne without tho spake rathe newe alway gan swerde bathe grekes blode sodaynely ouerlayne thorugh cruelte greke none hye lowe estate ne awhaped amate knyghthode manly excellence none make resystence vtterly durste take honde daye ector withstonde made also mensyon thylke daye kynge agamenon sayth guydo came nat felde cause great presence helde grekes syde goth vp downe ector playeth lyowne theyr tentes fledde socours troye proudely victours sewed trace theyr blode wan treasoure great gode spoyled full great distresse theyr armure theyr rychesse felle ware home troye good bare fynally day myschaunce grekes hadde brought vnto traunce without recure sothe euermore euery part layde sore thorugh manhode ector myght helpe many worthy knyght felly agayne grekes wrought myschefe playnly brought ne hadde theyr owne pyteous slouthe pryde oonly folye routhe hadde theyr volunte day euer hadde soueraygnete recured thorugh theyr hye renowne lordshyppe domynacy owne whiche shulde haue laste contynuell victoryously perpetuell haue endured saue cruell fate redy aye fortune debate agayne thynges gynne wylfulnesse make fyne aye wretchednesse thorughe theyr enuyous disposicyon sodayne chaunge reuolucyon vnware tournynge hir false whele wyll nat byde whan thynge wele ala frele deuoyde sykernesse cause dymmed derkenesse hath troyans thorugh false oppynyon yblynded theyr discrecyon specyally dyrked syght worthy ector prudent manly knyght se afore shulde sewe good aduyse myschefe eschewe folowed backe behynde ala wylfully made blynde day whan sete softe victorye hylle lofte nat coude neclygence se falle theyr felycyte put backe theyr aduertence lacke reason hye prudence theyr hap haue voyded theyr grace presently sette afore theyr face man nat comendable fortune hym fauourable blaundysshynge forhede clere smyle hym splesaunte chere oonly famour helpe hym oute whan myschefe beset aboute refuse hap wylfulnesse fortune auoydynge thorugh vnkyndenesse whan mynystreth hym hir grace another tyme shall hir nat enbrace whan hath nede hir helpe socoure hym catche fall rather ingratytude frowardly mowes hym delude whan beste weneth stonde sykernesse fortune aye full brotylnesse remouable redy flytte hyr welfull houre lyste nat amytte hir fauour allyed another tyme shalbe denyed whan leuest fynde hir sauourable houre sothly nofable vnto man graunteth desyres wyll nat thousande yeres parauenture one condescende vnto wyll luste hym sende hath falle daye vnhappely worthy ector wyllfully wrought hede grekes spare fatally whan snare lyke conquerour victorye tryumphe honour myght haue brought thurgh hye renowne palme conquest troye towne whiche hath day refused folylye rode ector cruellye amonge grekes slowe bare downe ca uelly mette thelamowne mene ayax nye allye hate cruell hote enuye ector rode lyke woode albe hym full nye bloode yet yonge lusty knyght dyde power full myght without faynynge haue borne hym downe whose fader hyght also thelamowne hym begat storye telleth thus exyon suster pryamus ayax flourynge yonge age fresshe delyuer great courage sette ector knyghtly hye prowesse mette bothe theyr woodnesse theyr stedes manly champyownes eueryche lyke tygres lyownes began falle proudely assayle furyously seuere plate mayle firste speres longe large rounde afterwarde swerdes kene grounde fyghtynge thus longe contune tyll befylle case fortune token sygne apparence nature kyndely influence whiche hertes doth full depe myne namely borne one lyne whiche cause paraunter twanye naturally theyr rancoure restrayne theyr yre modefye onely nye allye vnwyst outher therof vnsure tyll taught oonly nature naturally blode wyll aye kynde drawe vnto blode may fynde whiche made ector kyndely aduerte meuyd steryd herte bothe knyghthode gentyllesse whan ayax sawe worthynesse pspake vnto hym full benyngnely sayde cosyn saye trewely thou lyste grekes forsake come troye dare vndertake thyne allyes thy kynrede thou shalte without drede full well receyued partye blode royall sothely descended hyest degre right shall suffyse vnto kyndelye pleasaunce repayre thyne allyaunce gentyll herte sythe thynge gode confedryd owne blode conceyue worthynesse whiche nature dothe impresse troyan blode thou arte descended whiche grekes longe hath offended wherfore rede leue vtterly answered agayne full humbly sythen berthe greke youthe amonge fostryde eke tyme natyuyte taken hadde ordre degre knyghthode eke amonges aforne ouer bounde sworne trewe theyr nacyon makynge blode none excepcyon swore wolde conserue beheste ector made requeste manfull gentyllesse wolde knyghthode worthynesse shewe vnto hym great affeccyowne make troye towne oonly withdrawe grekes pursewe theyr tentes make remewe resorte agayne vnto towne knyghthode routhe compassy owne without assayllynge affraye made grekes ylke daye sythe vnto ought inoughe suffyse felde knyghtly wyse manhode fully possessours theyr foomen fynally victours lyke tofore fully diffyned whose requeste ector enclyned ala whyle hasty wylfulnesse made anone without auysenesse mydde felde trumpet blowe wherby troyans fully myght knowe wyll shulde withdrawe custome playnely lawe vsaunce bothe nye ferre amonges expert werre whan moste feruent fyght vpon grekes preue theyr myght hadde chacyd lowe stronde weyk power withstonde troye one desyre gan sette shotte wylde fyre brenne theyr shyppes hye myschaunce fynally put outtraunce hadde trouthe e hadde ector vpon routhe makynge troyans repayre towne vngracyously theyr confusyowne storye shall specyfye tho putte ala iupardye lyfe deth whiche myght haue sure whiche agayne neuer shall recure phow grekes sent kynge pryamus haue trewes eyght wekes theyr bataylles trewes faylled ca xxiij haue mater complayne sore fro daye farewell euermore victory laude fro towne denyed disposicyowne mortall fate whiche contrarye mater lyste lenger tarye troye entred theyr cyte shet theyr gate surete daye lyke made mynde thus ende euydo fynde wende haue done paraunter beste whan sonne ygo reste toke theyr ease ylke nyght tyll morowe tytan clere bryght shadde bemys theyr emysperye makynge day shewe merye whiche tyme troyans anone ryght hole lusty fyght gan arme purpose full day theyr foon mete platly may hole theyr wyll playne entent eke hadde comaundement tofore ector redy make theyr slepe morowe whan wake whiche thynge nat neclygent pryam grekes haue ysent messangeres day pryme take trewes oonly tyme eyghte wekes whiche pryamus assent ector story telleth thus hath graunted auctoryte wysest cyte whiche tyme whyle leyser haue grekes gan burye graue bodyes afore slawe lyke rytys theyr paynem lawe theyr myght theyr besy cure brent sepulture enclosed lyke theyr estate thus helde feste funerall fro day day durynge aye pee whiche space fynde achylles patroclus deth hath sore playned terys rayned inwardely loued hym herte anguysshe cruell smerte longe abode lamentacyon dyde make great affeccyon large toumbe remembraunce myd felde tho vsaunce amonge grekes great reuerence lyke honour excellence royall buryenge patroclus ygraue protheselaus theyr toumbes korue marbyll graye nye togydre playne laye werke aboute rychely ywrought erthe togydre brought solempnely lyke obseruaunces theyr rytys circumstaunces grekes vsed sothely tho dayes fro poynt poynt longeth theyr layes suche estate royall holden feste funerall two whyle trewes doth laste troye besyed full faste theyr myght theyr besy eure theyr grene hurtes woundes cure aduyse surgerye full well expert shape remedye sheyr swolle sore softe theyr payne space thyse monthes twayne restored helthe euery thynge whiche tyme pryamus kynge suche sorowe made cassybellan herte wyght ne hym recomforte heuynesse day day inwarde tendernesse full pyteously gan sobbe wepe bodye made kepe aboue erthe certayne space tyll hadde chosen place buryeng sepulture guydo v fully doth assure venus temple ryche shryne made workemen toumbe myne marbyll graye metall rychely whiche putte full solempnely dede corp cassybellan beynge present full many manly man phane cytherea whiche thynge whan cassandra within hir selfe consydered behelde sawe vp offred helme shelde swerde also vnto mar stede inwarde woo felte hir hette blede herynge noyse pyteous crye tendre wepynge sorowynge vtterly troye lamentacy owne whiche theyr frend thrugh al towne gan make slawe afore sodayne rage hir herte tore inwardely myght hir nat restrayne furyously crye complayne sayde ala full ofte wellawaye wofull wretch ye daye vnhappy eke graceles also infortunat inly woo bego howe ye may suffre great harmes kene whiche ye lykely hereafter sustene durynge sege towne beloke seynge foon redy wroke aboute beset euery syde venged great pryde wote ryght well ye maye nat eschewe ne shall vnto deth pursewe euerychone besegyd place without mercy pyte grace ala ala ne wyll ye besy ye wofull wretch shet cyte grekes seke pee swerde vengeaunce mercylees hye lowe execucy owne noble worthy royall towne euersyd ybrought nought lyste ye nat consydre thought modres theyr childresmale stretes shall face dede pale lye mordred thorugh grekes cruelte yonge maydens captyuyte wepe shall myserye theyr seruytute towne also famous ryche ala pyte grekes fyre shall destroyed shorte tyme sothly leyne v ala bought dere syth hyr sake shall euerychone pore ryche excepte none ende make wofull pyteous yre shalbe furyous vpon v none mene saue oonly deth v go bytwene noyse pyteous cry cassandra dredefully gan make aboute euery strete thorugh towne euer myght mete lyke hadde hir mynde tyll pryamus faste made hir bynde shytte vp routhe nat herde albe sayde trouthe neyther wysedome discrecyon counsayle wyt prudence reson trouthe rede without lye spirite trewe prophecye auayleth nat suche sapyence place audyence man inly neuer wyse counsaylynge hye deuyse werkynge outher eloquence eche thynge se aduertence falle afore reson amyd eye discrecyon yet dole without fauour holden fole vnfauoured wysedome vayleth nought neyther trouthe dere bought lyke cassandra hir wyse rede despysed taken hede troye theyr confusyon cruelly ythrowen inpryson whyle wyll leue hir dwelle grekes forth wyll telle firste pallamydes gan grutche agaynst ches beynge absent kynge agamenon haue lordshyp domynacyon namely syth nat worthy suche dignyte gouerne great myghty oost thorugh worlde come euery cost kynges prynces worthy renowne therof hadde indignacy owne sayde hymselfe poustee amonge grekes gretter degree concludynge maner weye power ne wolde obeye pea werre subieccyon syth ne eleccyon platly affermynge thre whan chose kynges degre thurty tyme absent whiche swore nat entent accordynge oppynyon wyse agamenon grekes shulde haue suche gouernaunce lo myschefe lyeth varyaunce amonge lordes whan nat accorde drawe fully one corde enuye cause suche dyuysyon couetyse domynacyon eueryche wolde surmounte felawe cursed vyse often hath withdrawe hap grace many regyon whan discorde false discencyon allyed ben hertes stryue amonge lordes kyndh may nat thryue tyll reformed agayne pee amonge themselfe playnely lee whiche thynge grekes toke hede thought nat ferther procede matere pallamydes ymeued hadde amonges prees thorugh theyr wyt set quyete made hym rancour lete accorde fully herte nowe muste style agayne dyuerte vnto werre telle manere trewes mette yfere lyke storye maketh mencyon worthy kynge great agamenon whan trewes passyd ygone haste gan ordayne anone myght waker dylygence deuoyde slouthe neclygence sette wardes full auysely achylle full prudently firste warde comytteth lede seconde vnto dyomede thyrde also kynge menelay fourthe day e hadde menestee duke athene ledynge stele armed clene wardes folowynge agamanon kynge full manfully ordayned hath shall procede werke dede full circumspect bothe werre pee worthy ector nat reckles sette wardes towne knyghtly wyse discrecy owne troylus yonge fresshe lyght firste warde many lusty knyght hath assigned wardes set prudently myght bet forth haste hym lyste lenger byde many worthy rydynge syde gate went towne towarde grekes troyan champyowne firste whan sawe fyerse achylle ne coude lenger kepe hym stylle sinot hors felly syde towarde hym cruelly gan ryde whiche thynge despytous eye whan achylles sothly gan espye agayne ector manfull hardynesse herte enuyous gan stede dresse felde togydre mette rounde speres poyntes kene whette encountrynge knyghtly excellence eueryche thorugh great vyolence force bare vnto grounde full ofte happeth founde whan stronge dothe mete perygall eueryche fall ector firste strengthe moste assured stede agayne hath anone recured lefte achylle tho gentyllesse great haste forth gan hym dresse amonge grekes rode kylled slewe hym withstode wt swerde made theyr woudes wyde thorugh brest thorugh syde percy hath waged foreuer brake sheltrous made disseuer herte hym thought dydehy gode bathe swerde grekes blode contynued tyll achylles caughte stede agayne amonge prees entrede amonges troye swerde made large weye sleeth bare downe euer mette none hardy hym lette tyll befell melancoly ctor mette rydynge sodaynely whan sawe eche come fere without abode eueryche caught spere ran togydre areste ector firste smette hym breste spere playnely tale shyuered peces smale achylles necessyte grounde goth wolde none vnhorsed erthe lay ector haste may enforced hym catche stede many greke great nede came reskues achylles loue put themselfe prees thrugh help hors doth atta e enhastynge hym myght payne auenged great miurye sodaynely woode furye swerde ful sharpe grounde whette smote ector vpon basenet sadell made hym remewe whiche stroke myght nat eschewe noble worthy knyght force thorugh great myght maugre foon sadell hath recured manhode moste assured sodaynely herte wexed wrothe arage achylles gothe swerde smet hym hede thorugh basenet blode rede face gan ronne downe lyke ryuer chekes enuyrowne hymselfe diffendeth knyght tho newe began cruell fyght wene two se wonder euery stroke great dent thonder range eyre none wolde spare sothe theyr fyght fare lyke woode tygres bore theyr rage sterne bulles whan sauage sempte sothfastnesse two full worthynesse contune longe fyghtynge endure tone bothe cruell aduenture muste haue dede necessyte whiche thynge hadde pyte bycause worthy knyghtes bothe whyle fyghtyng fell wrothe moste besy grekes begynne theyr wardes entre inne troye storye maketh mynde theyr party lefte nat behynde felde enhaste euerychone knyghtly wyse mete theyr fone prease also yonder knyghtes two seueryd sonder tho came sterne dyomede knyghtes whiche dyde lede full lustely selue place hath mette proudely face whorthy troylus hors backe neuer hadde yet manhode lacke countre storye dothe v lere eueryche vnhorsed knyghtly hath fere firste hors recureth dyomede haste gan hym spede assayle troylus stondynge vpon foote whan sawe none bote knyghtly yet euer dyde man agaynst hym diffende hym tho began dyomede hote fyre wonder enuyous hatefull desyre swerde rancour none ryche cercle full ynde stone tyme troylus basenet full cruelly hath racyd smet troylus ne wolde yt hym wtdrawe hym diffendynge hath stede slawe whiche sat tyme dyomede maugre hym muste alyght nede whan fote bothe twayne dyd theyr myght theyr cruell payne eueryche assayle swerdes sharpe plate mayle gan seuere sonder race woode lyon mortall chere face tyll grekes stronge stoute felle myn auctour boke telle haue thorugh theyr myght made dyomede sodaynely recure stede troyan knyghtes tother syde haue troylus brought stede ryde whan horsed bothe two without agayne togydre go stronge foynes yfere ran eche felly tyll laste cruell dyomede lyke ye may myn auctour rede case hap aduenture whiche man fully may assure fortune hir false vysage hadde tyme troylus vauntage hym falle myschese whiche thynge hym reprefe though hym toke amonge great aroute euery halfe grekes set aboute syth doutous euer fyne fyght vp downe derk bryght wyght may aye victoryous pea werre ylyche eurous let euery man syth hap sette doute take tourne cometh aboute though troylus take dyomede another tyme shall hym quyte mede storye telleth place dyomede lytell space troylus ladde forth prysonere reskewes stele armed clere many troyan came pryckynge nede maugre myght dyomede troylus haue handes take tho began slaughter sake euery halfe wonder telle troyans grekes felle felde entrede menelay whiche troyans ylke day full besy auenged hadde cruell enmyte whan parys sawe hym felde towardes hym right waye helde purpose theyr wardes sette eche tyll togydre mette tho skarmysshe slaughter gan outher parte many manly man whyle ector ne wolde cease amonge grekes cruelly prease new new hym rede lyke fresshe blode shede swerde trace ysene grekes myght nat sustene resyste stande afore face rode aye gaue hym place ptyll aknyght whiche boetes hyght yonge age whan hadde syght ector slewe grekes mortally euery syde hauynge mercy presyd encrease name perpetuelly purchace hym fame furyously herte nat afferde caste hym platly mete hym berde whiche thynge whan ector gan aduerte hye raucour enbracyd hath herte swerde indignacyowne rofe hym euen nauell downe fro crowne great payne felde partyd lay twayne ector tho assygned hath stede squyer bad shulde lede troye towne without abode whyle furyously rode amonge grekes euer mercylees slewe put selfe prees shadde theyr blode herte despytous whiche thynge whan kynge archylogus rydynge besyde sawe gan espye boetes cosyn allye cruelly ector slawe towardes hym haste gan hym drawe vpon deth auenged tode hym great cruelte fully purpose ector quyte sodaynely gan hym smyte ector vnwarely hyt hym hede myghtely felle downe dede partyd two cruell aduenture natwithstadyng myghty stronge armure agayne stroke diffence gyuen suche vyolence holpe hym maner thynge anone prochenor kynge hatefull yre foole hardynesse surquedye hastynesse melancolye indignacyon caught herte presumpcyon assayle ector inwarde foly pryde goth hym trauerse syde furyously despytous herte comynge myght nat aduerte oonly came backe behynde vnwarely guydo fynde ector smote hors grounde moch manhode foude anone knyghtly herte without abode sadell sterte right fyersly prothen purseweth fynally honde nat escheweth swerde marked hym wele thorugh basenet breste stele twayne withoute fayle roofe hym downe paunce mayle felle downe full pyteous wyse whiche stroke grekes sore agryse specyally hardy fyerse achylle whan behelde lyked full ylle phothenor nye cosyne descendyd lyne deth hath suche heuynesse inwarde thought great distresse worlde ne wyste hym moche payne wo deth archylogus auenge full desyrous herte many waye caste wardes gan seke faste many greke ector haue falle conspyred fully soth amonge alle one entent ector assayle nought wolde nat auayle day cruell rage myght hym haue none auauntage troyan knyghtes fauour fortune vpon grekes myghtely contune thorugh conueyinge ector myght anone haue put flyght theyr tentes maugre stryue pursuyte wouded dryue laye aswowe many greke mercyles slowe longe day tyll drewe nyght sothly lacke lyght troyan knyght full worthy renowne aboute ector repayre towne entre honour glorye day grekes hauynge victorye thus leue theyr towne within forth grekes telle wyll begyn whan esperus fayre bryght sterre agaynst eue caste stremys ferre west rathest gan appere whan twylyght pale chere maner morneth absence sonne nyght approcheth copy donne tyme whan tytan toke leue clerkes calle crepusculum eue whiche nat ellys meane lyght phebus absence derke nyght twylyght hatte mene daye nyght departynge betwene fully nouther bothe meynt heuen clustred depeynt bryght sterrys euenynge whiche tyme agamenon kynge lordes sodaynely hath sent come echone anone tent whan assembled yfere tryst heuy sorefull chere gan slaughter ector complayne affermyng playnly myght neuer attayne vnto victorye whyle lyue wherfore gan conspyre blyue deth hym many sondry weye echone concludynge whyle troye nat lykely grekes wynne alone withinne chefe diffence proteccy owne soueraynely vpholder towne theyr myghty castell theyr stronge wall vnto grekes dedely foo mortall ne myght great force endure neuer right agayne theyr foos sure standynge hole sayde degre whyle floureth felycyte wherfore echone one entencyon condescende conclusyon sleyghte awayte lymge whan moste besy fyghtynge amonge myschefe distresse achylles besynesse myght vnwarely hym assayle hym slee thynge fayle grekes gan theyr prayer make achylles vndertake empresse fynally sute thorugh manhode execute hasty deth theyr mortall foo achylles without wordes moo theyr request assenteth parfourme theyr luste gan hooly hym confourme tyme let hym beware rede hasty iourne spede vpon ector power kythe lyste fortune wronge hir face wrythe loke hym frowarde chere hym brynge vnto handes nere thorugh sorte hap ector folylye put lyfe deth ieopartye lyste vnto hym happe euen lyche falle hymsefe dyche ector compassed hath shape wonder escape syth ector hadde without drede brennynge yre great hatrede achylles deth puruey hym founde place sey conuenyent execucyon trowe shulde hym gayne raunson mede herte quyete onely deth whan mete ende fyne matere boke ye shall thus grekes made haue ende theyr counsayle one wende eueryche home theyr lodgynge toke theyr reste tyll morenynge phowe troyans toke kynge thoas prysoner ledde hym troye ca xxiiij whan aurora wt syluer droppes shene hitterys shadde vpon fresshe grene coplaynyge ay wepyng sorowe hir childrens deth euery somer morowe saye whan dewe soote enbawmed hath floure eke roote lusty lycoure apryll may whan larke messager day custome aye aurora doth salue sondry note hir sorowe transmue phebus ryse ioye gladnesse thorugh armonye leue hir heuynesse takynge hir leue seynt iohn borowe tyme grekes morowe lusty herte erely dyde aryse armed theyr beste wyse caste daye goon felde mete theyr foon ector hath morowe also caste hym fully grekes haue ado yssued knyghtly troye herte hath great desyre ioye day grekes fyght hym ladde many lusty knyght suche cyte borne forth rode hymselfe aforne eneas many worthy folowed wonder faste parys next hym dephebus sythe troylus couragyous wardes made troye towne wiche dare maketh mencyowne within boke troye syde fyghtynge men went dyde ryde hondred thousande armed go felde fyfty thousande mo whiche haue caste day eue one entent grekes greue mette strongly outher syde gan assemble togydre ryde full cruelly great hatrede tho parys dyde lede entrede full myghty stronge archeres perce londe many arbalasteres wt theyr arrowes fyled sharpe rounde quarelles square whette grounde full many greke hath reuyd lyfe amyddes mortall stryfe agamenon felde come towardes ector hath ynome right way threwe hym stede amonge knyghtes dyde lede spared nought great prees therwithall anone came achylles awayte ector hadde layne sodaynely myght payne pector smote hede sore wt ye stroke myn auctour sayth basenet bowed ycrased whiche stroke ector nat amased achylles shulde anone yfalle ne hadde eneas knynghtes alle worthy troylous come go betwene whiche twayne swerdes kene gan achylles felly assayle hewe plate perce mayle tho began slaughter euery syde men foote ryde lyke condyte woundes gan blede whyle cruell dyomede hap aduenture caas rode hath mette eneas right anone hadde hym founde smet hym gaue hym wounde lykely shulde nat recure therto better cure therupon full despyteously dyomede melancoly repreuyd hath troyan knyght enee sayd hym heyle thou art whylom gaue pryamus kynge felle counsayle hasty bytynge slayne sodayne vyolence whan laste troye presence truste well haue wel mynde amyd felde efte fynde thou shalt thy counsayle mortally repente fortune wyll assente brynge right vnto hande good leyser thyne owne lande full sette thy labour quyte trouth swerde shal kerue byte kenely thy troyan blode shede fynally deth shalbe thy mede bere atwene handes twayne wt worde myght hy nat restrayne dyomede rode sodaynely vpon enee furyously smote hym hardy cruell knyght suche payne great myght hors made hym falle maugre myght knyghtes alle whiche stroke lyked full ylle whyle ector hath achylle assayled thorugh basenet perced hath swerde hym smet narowe brought hym poynt hye myschefe disioynt constrayned hym necessyte hadde hym take ne oonly sodayne reskues chyualrous called sone tydeus meane felle fyerse dyomede whiche achylles hath holpen nede thorugh force armes twayne smote ector tho great payne hym gaue wounde full greuous thyge myn auctour wryteth thus astoned knyght manly man swerd haste smote dyomede furyous wrothe hors erth gothe pryde surquedrye whiche anone troylous dyde espye without abode downe stede lyght dyomede fote fyghte eche sothfastnesse aquyte hymselfe lyke manly man nouther moche lyte degree manhode wyte whyle faught ector achylles togydre mette agayne amonge prees ran yfere fyersly theyr rage woode lyon whan ramage right sothe fared theyr fyghtyng tyme menelay kyng full proudely shope hym troyans mete vlixes eke also polymete hym came neptolonyus pallamydes eke scelemus duke menestee nestor thoas currynulus phylotheas aud theseus made mynde knyghtes proudely came behynde partye towne came kynges without excepcyowne assembled theyr diffence agayne grekes make resystence except knyghtes whiche ector ladde wardes made hadde daye sayth latyn boke knyghtly wyse felde whan yt toke tho began felle mortall fyght whiche day ful many worthy knyght fatyshondes fynally falle fortune amonge wardes alle agamenon noble myghty kynge sodaynely came rydynge pantysylaus waye mette agaynst anone hors sette hym full knyghtly rode agayne mette sayne horsbacke whyles wrothe vyolence vnhorsed bothe menelay parys mette newe whiche two well togydre knewe full desyrous eche dere menelay caught firste spere hytte parys inwarde cure surenesse stronge armure myghty plat wounde small whiche effect greued nat stroke vnto grounde gothe whiche fall parys wexed right wrothe wonder confuse also rede shame lest reporte hyndrynge name came erys quene eleyne daye myght nat atteyne menely holde chaumpartye lykely sowne vylonye whiche herte greued hym full sore adrastus kynge without rode kynge vlixes fonde knyghtly foughte honde honde faughte downe erthe lowe hors vlixes hath hym throwe full proudely signe victorye sent hors home tentorye tyme amonges prees full sodaynely kynge pallamydes falle hupon locke hore ire wounded hym sore felle dede grouelyng ye groude mortall swerde kene grounde besyde neptolonyus assayled hath kynge archylogus whiche hymselfe manly gan diffende faught many stroke spende diffence wolde none eueryche hath vnhorsed tho came rydynge stede pollydamas gan take hede amonge renges lytell hym besyde kynge pallamydes doth ryde cruelly lyke manly man smote stede hym ran maugre myght worthynesse storye playnely bereth wytnesse oonly venge deth kynge hupowne stede proudely bare hym downe rancoure cruell hete despyte gan hym rehete tho besyde kynge scelenus dedely hate herte full irous kynge carras aduenture hath met furyously stede smet also kynge phylymene duke falle athene maugre manhod myght hath hors berafte hym fyght ladde hym proudely syde hym lyste shulde abyde phyloteas worthy kynge also selue tyme remus ado euery sothly rede felawe hath made voyde stede theseus kynge yt stronge amyd felde rode amonge great prese hath met curyalus worthy kyg knyghthod right famous bothe two armes wonder stronge themselfe faught leyser longe tyll eche woundes fresshe grene fro horsbak felawe threwe endlog ye grene afterwarde fynde two vpon foote knyghtly hadde ado armes somly desyrous manhode passyngly famous whyle sone naturell pryamus bare wonder well amonge grekes vp downe rydynge prudently togydre abydynge made slaughter grekes full pytous kynges duke lordes right famous rede worthy thelamowne tyme met kynge sapedowne theyr speres squared full sharpely eueryche hath wounded mortally thorugh shelde plate haberion mayle storye maketh rehersayle theyr harneys wexed blode rede fylle almoste bothe dede great myschefe amonge hors foot whose bledynge soyle gan wexe weet thorugh theyr harneys distylle whyles kynge thoas fyerse achylle kynne allyed amyd felde ector haue espyed faught beset amyd foon vpon hym one accorde goon mortally wolde auayle euery halfe gan hym newe assayle hate herte borne yore haue beset troyan knyght sore ala hede hath smet vyolence ryche basenet wounded hym felly hede ne toke hede worthy man floure chyualrye hym diffendynge tho myghtely kynge thoas smet hym face stroke rafte nose two shorted halfe dele whiche stroke brother naturele manly ector faste gan hye socoure hym whan firste espye great myschefe theyr comynge manly bare fyghtynge agayne grekes thoas haue take amon made awake newe assaute sharpe woundes kene take lefte vpon grene men borne home tent kynge thoas home troye went maugre grekes whiche helpe hy may dephebus also anthenore haue sente hym forth troye cyte menelay tho began se rode parys stonde syde shope hym shortly hate cruell pryde wolde falle chaunce sodaynely ymen hym myschaunce ware kept hymselfe narowe menelay marked arowe hede whiche wt venym enoynt intoxycate square poynt kynge dredefull wounde dispayred men founde whiche great haste bare hym tent anone surgyens hath sent whiche firste hede toke wounde albe yperced full profounde thorugh harneys full depe bone cunnyngely dyde theyr crafte echone drawe theyr instrumentes subtylly certayne oyntementes serched haue wounde enuyron make clene corrupcyon prudently firste toke hede venym nat procede rounde compasse clensyd aboute bounde sure withoute defensyues made euery syde menelay lenger wolde abyde bad haste brynge forth stede purpose full parys quyte mede hym fynde selfe daye hym lyste lenger put delaye euer falle grene wounde forth rode tyll hath hym founde aduenture vnarmed felde without swerde pollex spere shelde bowe honde reklesnesse refresshe hym werynesse menelay anone spere hath take yre elly gan shake towarde parys great auysenesse shulde haue slayne hym lyklynesse ne eneas whiche thynge behelde bore stocke stronge shelde diffende hym auenture destytute naked armure parys tyme suche peryll wherfore haste hath eneas ordayned knyghtes armed bryght stele aboute parys kepe hym wele myschefe confusyowne hym conuey vnto troye towne right despyte kynge menelay whiche awayte parys lay pwhom ector hadde ytaken sodaynely vnto troye ladde hym vtterly ne hadde grekes come diffence agaynst hym make resystence whiche ector came weye full many greke made deye remenaunt put vnto flyghte thorugh mahod day myghte troyans made grekes flee vnto theyr tentes necessytee sewe ne wolde neuer leue slee kyll tyll drewe eue phebus gan faste weste drawe home thought ye beste tytan goynge downe whan gan entre troye towne theyr gat shet theyr lodgynge wende day thus made ende tyll morowe rowes rede phebus carte gonne sprede afore vpryste oryent whiche tyme kynge pryamus hath sent suche hym moste pryue counsayle inwardely secre specially sent name worthy ector grettest fame parys eke dephebus troylus fresshe desyrous anthenor pollydamas troyan called eneas daye caste hym nat goon felde mete foon whan paleys come lordes haue right waye nome vnto kynge within closet whan hussher hath dore shet eueryche hadde lyke degree place take dewe see worthy kynge made mencyon gan declare hertes mocyon menynge afore specifye sayde syres moste affye knowen kynge thoas cyte taken prysonere yet belocked prysowne whiche euer hath vnto troye towne enemy great vnto power v offendyd bothe ferre ner many wyse lytell retche ferre force myght stretche grek came sege towne wyll destruccyowne therupon hath besynesse wherfore dome rightwysnesse reason equyte saye playnely semeth vnto acceptable ye thynke cousayle comendable lyke hath caste deth shape holde rightfull nat escape deth receyue guerdon right requereth also good reason deth deth skylfull guerdonnynge vnto wytte right well syttynge saye aduyse playnely caas firste tho spake eneas sayde lorde none offence hyghnesse gyue audyence thorugh supporte yt full wyse shall reherce playnely deuyse werke matere semeth firste lyege lorde dere noble royall excellence consydre shulde full hye prudence euery werke operasyon caste afore conclusyon caste afore conclusyon fynall ende may sewe wyse man oonly nat dewe se gynnynge ende nought bothe attones peyse thought weye iustly balaunce fyne folowe repentaunce say platly mene ye ought sene kynge thoas one pryncypall amonge grekes blode royall ye consydre descended lyne wherfore haue foule fyne slayne whyle pryson myght happen conclusyon ye youres therto assente afterwarde sore repente preue thus aduenture fortune man may assure lordes nother day grekes take happe may sone worthy renowne kynges towne truste well suche gentyllesse ye shewe theyr distresse wyl quyte whan case semblable fortune fynde fauourable whiche man costrayne may bynde wherfore lorde haue thyng mynde thoas shorte auysement shall deed thorugh hasty iugement another day grekes wyll v quyte rygour make theyr malys byte youres euer nouther spare hye lowe degre though paraunter blode whiche thynge worldes gode myght falle ye ne wolde se wherfore rede let kynge thoas honestely kepe prysowne lyke estate stylle towne lyste sayde another day lorde youres happe may casuelly take auenture eschaunge hym ye myght beste recure without stryfe youre owne man agayne mater sayne fynally full rede whiche counsayle ector toke good hede accordynge reason comendeth oppynyon pryam euer one entencyon stode alway fyx conclusyon playnely affermynge grekes may espye kynge spare gentrye wyll arrecte cowardyse anone dare nat venge v foone drede hauynge hardynesse herte nouther rightwysenesse yet neuerthelesse assent shall lyue wyll myn entent desyre fully condescende counsayle made ende without saue eneas go trylous eke anthenor also halle excellynge beaute quene eleyne purpose se eke eccuba quene ladyes goodly sene many mayde yonge lusty worthy troylus eneas dyde theyr laboure theyr besy payne comforte fayre quene eleyne stode werre drede womanhede thylke tyme hir herte entere well coude make good chere hauynge connynge inly suffysaunce bothe chere dalyaunce eccuba beynge halle example vnto woman alle bounte hauynge soueraygne excellencce wysedome eke eloquence besought tho wonder womanly counsayled eke full prudently haste bothe nye ferre auysely kepe werre nat iuparte theyr bodyes folylye aduerte caste prudently diffence knyghtly towne gouerne discrecyowne spake fayth coude thynge feyne hir eleyne toke leue lenger dwelle went theyr way forth wyll telle grekes morowe amonge selfe complayne make sorowe theyr harmes great murmur rage losse costes great damage haue enduryd folylye lastynge werre wyste neuer whye deth slaughtre many worthy man syth tyme werre began hunger thurste watche colde also full great vnreste sorowe thought wo togydre thynge nought sothfastnesse grounde sought noyse rumour eke ran thorugh hoost yt day fro man man moste amonge pore souldy oures whiche bare bronte euer suche shoures myschefe werre comenlye though playne haue remedy thynges whiche sytte full vnsofte thus grekes complayned haue full ofte many myschefe hath falle whiche myght haue eschewed alle ne hadde foly gonne werre grece nat come halfe ferre theyr myschefe confusyon daye lamentacyon pwhiche encrease next nyght derked without sterre lyght cloudy blacke thycke ayre dymmyd skyes foule thynge fayre wyndy eke tempest layne almoste fordrenchyd smoky rayne felde astoned yonder sodayne stroke dredefull thonder openynge hydous leuene sempte hye heuene cataractys hadde vndo cloudes skyes bothe two sodaynely wexen blake lyke goddes wolde haue taken wrake hadde newe assentyd oon lande drenche deucalyon worlde without refuge ouerflowe fresshe deluge wynde also sternely gan blowe theyr tentes stondynge rowe possyd ybete downe furyously theyr confusyowne flood raughte fro theyr stadyng place bare forth full large space wherof myschefe great distresse great laboure hertely heuynesse grekes bydde nyght tempest lacke lyght tyll floode gan agayne withdrawe wynde appese day gan dawe heuen gan agayne clere without cloudes fresshely appere phebus eke feruent hete hadde soyle dryed vp wete moysture enuyrowne playne grekes hadde theyr tentes set agayne adawed theyr nyghtes sorowe thorugh aperynge galde morowe arrayed nothynge pee felde firste went achylles ye shall entencyowne day fyght wt troye towne whan dryed lusty large playne wt pheb bemys ye haue herd saye troyan knyghtes full worthy renowne descendyd ycome downe felde toke theyr fyghtynge place achylles mete face tofore went lyke tolde lordes knyghtes bolde firste fynde without abode vnto hupon furyously rode mene hupon stature lyke geaunt bokes v assure achylles sharpe spere thorugh body percyd hym fere fylle dede wounde kene kynge octamene fyersly ector wolde haue gone without abode ector hym siewe anone cruelly quytte hym fatall mede sodaynely agaynst dyomede zantipus worthy kynge gan drawe full pyteously hym slawe right anone kynge epyscrophus eke kynge hyght cedyus one assent proudely batayle begonne ector mortally assayle spere firste epyscrophus ran hym herte despytous guydo also doth deuyse rebukyd hym vngoodly wyse hym sore herte meued wherof ector furyously agreued hath mortally wounde made large hym ne geyneth plate shelde targe fyll dede amonge men echone ector bad shulde gone furyes depe downe helle suche wordes amonges telle quod men take hede thus whan waged mede anone brother called cedyus suche sorowe made epyscrophus hertely dole wofull chere pyte se inwardly deth thought thousande knyght yt brought auenged manhode alle despyteously ertor falle hym founde fyghtynge wt foon thorugh force euerychoon sore enuyrowne haue hym beset stede downe haue hy smet pwhom cedyus aye cruell rage whan sawe auauntage ector vnhorsed stede swerde lefte inwardely hatrede markynge hym great payne force armes twayne fully purpose without delay slee ector playnely may stroke descende myght downe ector hate indignacyowne swerde full sharpe whet shuldre hath arme smet reuyd hym lyfe eneas amyddes stryfe came rydynge woode furyous mette kynge amphymacus fell hym slewe hym rage grekes holdynge theyr passage came downe firste menelaus hym kynge thelamonyus great duke also athene moche manhode sene vlixes eke cruell dyomede eke also helpe theyr nede came kynge machaon alderlaste great agamenon theyr wardes fyll sodaynly vpon troyans full manfully diffende selfe agayne grekes proude put full knyghtly coude eche sothly mette spere swerde enuyously sette mortall hate betwene whan sonne merydyen myd day angell passynge hote shene grekes gan felly theyr tene myghtely falle troye made gyue weye force necessyte achylles full cruelte amonge renges gan hym drawe kynge phylem enuyously hath slawe amyd grekes tyme ector maugre slewe kynge alphenor eke kynge called dorous cruell yrous thorugh vertue knyghtly honde troyans haue wonne agayne theyr londe vpon grekes made flee thylke houre torye cytee epyscrophus full manlynesse felde hath take thorugh worthynesse grekes proudely none knyghtes falleth attones seuered made twynne gan felde faste vpon wynne hauynge tyme companye amonges dyde guye acertayne archer whiche fynde monstruous wonderfull kynde myddell vp vnto crowne man remenaunt downe bare horse lyknesse fygure horse heer monstre nature hadde skyn growynge enuyrowne full rough thycke voyce ye sowne lyke neyhynge horse rede though face lengthe brede shape mannysshe yet suthfastnesse coloure semblable lyknesse vnto fery hoote breynnynge glede whose eyen eke flawmynge also rede blase ouen mouthe syghte vnkouthe euer met berde bothe man hors sore ferde face hatefull odyble loke hydous horryble aye hadde custome vsaunce bokes made remembraunce go vnarmed felde without swerde spere axe shelde thynge coude myster fynde good archer bare bowe styffe wonder stronge also tyller longe arrowes lyke tyller busshement trussed wonder ner syde aye redy hande outher see lande fynde none armure agayne shot playnely myght endure hors stede courser durste abyde nouther fer ner fledde anone theyr full myght faste hym hadde syght passynge odyous lyke deuyll monstruous foude none hardy knyght hors backe hadde force myght holde hors whan myght hym se anone backe wolde fle archer fynde wryten eke day slewe full many greke wounded arrowes kene thorugh ye plate forged bryght shene none afore hym abode theyr tentes faste awaye rode myght nat hydous loke endure tyll befell wonder aduerture whyle troye helpe archer sewe chase theyr lodgynge ner slewe myschefe drede besyde tent mette dyomede archer necessyte stode ne myght hym fle maner way backe remewe lyfe deth myght hym nat eschewe many troyan tho backe flyinge hadde go wracke pwherfore anone worthy dyomede cruell herte faste gan hym spede towarde hym proudely dresse archer great aduysenesse firste arrowe smette dyomede thorugh harneys made hym blede whiche stroke wexed wood wrothe monstre hydous lothe went pase hym vnarmed fonde ye swerde helde honde gaue hym laste fatall wounde fylle dede grouelynge vnto ye grounde deth grekes reioysynge haste theyr hertes resumynge began selfe recomforte felde proudely resorte conueyinge polixenare worthy duke well hym bare vpon troyans day felde whan ector slaughtre hym behelde vpon duke anone gan sette theyr stedes fyersly mette ector hym slewe full great hatrede gallathe stede rode forth amonge prees ware mette achylles theyr speres longe large rounde purpose fully eche confounde ran yfere irous right wrothe ye stroke vnhorsed bothe achylles wth despytous herte firste rede sadell sterte besy inwarde peyne gallathe take reyne therof euer ector depryue bad men lede home blyue ector none bote full lyke man faught stondynge fote amonge grekes fomen alle knyghtes loude gan calle stede shulde sewe haste hors reskewe ben attones fallen achylle maugre hym force agayne wylle haue hym berafte playne ector restored agayne knyghthode somoche hy self assureth despyte sadell recureth whiche afterwarde full dere aboughte lyke lyon day wroughte amonges rydynge deth fled swerde fere thorugh whose manhode troyans eft begyn vpon grekes felde agayne wyn befell amyd theyr great fyght anthenor certayne troyan knyght amonge prese fer gone grekes take anone theyr tentes sent haste albe sone called pollydamas reskue hym dyde dylygence manfully neclygence founde hym lyste seke full dere boughte many greke day thorugh worthynesse cause oonly derkenesse gan drawe towarde nyght made ende oonly lacke lyght grekes went home theyr lodgynge eke troyans tyll mornynge phebus gan bryght bemys shewe aurora newe gan dewe erbys sote grene leuys hayes fresshe greuys syluer bryght rounde perlys fyne clerely agayne sonne shyne shewe selfe oryent shene hylle vale euery grene rody morowe tyll hote bemys bryght phebus fyrye stemys vapoureth vp theyr moysture ayre weder clere agreable fayre attempre also heete whan troyans caste mete theyr fomen platly may went theyr beste array theyr wardes felde rowe agaynst grekes nat slowe shope forth without lenger lette tyll togydre manfully haue mette theyr speres theyr swerdes clere ran togydre despytous chere tyll shyuered sondre many spere sheldes stronge selfe ryuen pecys many targe hexys rounde brode large basenettes smyte shrede full many knyght mortally gan blede sothfastnesse tell day slayne many man outher parte troye towne albe guydo maketh mencyowne persone specyall nouther syde generall saue concludeth playnely fyght laste fro morowe tyll nyght whiche troyans haue full dere bought day fortune holpe nought tourned hole theyr confusyowne repeyred towne theyr tentes grekes faste spede tyll morowe sent dyomede pwhith vlixes troye cyte trewes oonly monthes thre kynge pryam therto wolde assente two message wente certayne knyght borne troye towne hyght dolon great discrecyowne also ryght famous rychesse curtely gentyllesse deuer dyde dylygence conueye vnto presence pryamus paleys royall see chefe pryncypall sat lordes enuyrowne many knyght full worthy renowne gan hym firste specefye hoolly substaunce theyr embassatrye trewes theyr entent tolde assente wolde kynge benyngnely herde auyse prudently answerde therupon honour saue good leyser wolde counsayle haue lordes fully hym gouerne mater lyke discerne conclude shortly euerychone assentyd except ector alone vnto trewes ne wolde nat denye ector sayde trecherye oonly slaughter false treson theyr axynge vnder occason firste berye grekes dede vnder coloure therof drede afterwarde selfe vytayle well knewe theyr stuf gan fayle enfamyned leste shulde dye soughte space selfe purueye outwarde sygnes dyde espye wherfore quod lyketh nat lye apparence dare presume whyles waste consume oure stuf within drede wyll prouyde yt haue nede auauntage myght v hyndrynge damage whyles encrease amende shall store discrease dispende yet neuertheles euer touchynge trewes monthes thre sythen ye assente accorde fro sentence wyll nat discorde wyse varyaunt thus trewes confermyd graut outher syde thought beste bycause shulde quyete reste mene whyle ease releue felte theyr woundes sore greue myght haue leyser selfe recure whyle trewes dyde thus endure fylle tretee comunynge athenor thoas kynge anthenor delyuered shulde kynge thoas troye cyte thoas shuld grekes home agayne oonly eschaunge ye haue herde sayne one nother accorded whyle ye bysshop hight calchas remembred hym vpon doughter dere called cryseyde hir eyen clere troye lefte behynde whan wente boke maketh mynde felte passyngly great smerte
