tenderly set herte enprented eue morowe chefe cause grounde sorowe lefte behynde hym towne without comforte consolacyowne caste sothly absence specyally great offence hath wrought agaynst troye hym thought shuld neuer haue ioye tyll doughter recured hath agayne pwherfore calchas storye sayth certayne wyttes many wayes caste myght whyle trewes doth laste recure doughter maner way fynde vpon certayne day porte wonder humbly wepynge eye wente pyteously complaynynge terys albe reyned whose inwarde wo sothly nat feyned knee anone falleth downe tofore great kynge agamenowne besechynge hym humylyte mercy hye pyte kynges syttynge place haue routhe hym grace woo haue compassyon may haue restytucyon doughter loued prayinge theyr deuer thorugh theyr prudent medyacyon anthenor theyr pryson pwith kyng thoas myght eschauged lyst theyr benygnyte requeste goodly assente hym graut forth anone sente kynge pryamus haue cryseyde calchas sake therwith leyde charge hir wonder specyally went embassatry troye towne kynge pryamus calchas odyus hatefull eke thorugh towne reporte hym vp downe traytour also false worthy enhonged halfe treson doubylnesse ouer sayde eke expresse disserued hath right lawe shamefully firste drawe afterwarde horryble deth may haue yelde vp breth lyke traytour despytous wyse herte thynke deuyse eueryche affermynge iugement deth none fully equypollent deserte falsnesse yonge olde playnely bare wytnesse concludynge eke iniquyte wolde assent degre vnto thynge myght herte please cryseyde hym ease caste nat make delyueraunce leuer hadde gyue hym myschaunce hym myght haue good large fynally effect charge ferforth dryuen ende pryamus hath grauted shall wende kynge thoas shortly vnto hir fader dauz anthenore euer grutche kynge parlement hath therupon gyuen iugement vtterly may nat repelyd worde sentence asselyd must parte hir eyen glade sorowe playnely made hir partynge hereafter ye shall whan agayne cometh matere phowe durynge trewes thre monthes ector walked grekes hooste ye comunycacyon achylles hym ca xxv trewes affermyd ye haue herd deuyse outher syde yt full wyse full assentyd euerychone tyll thre monthes come gone lyke rede certayne daye whan agreable morowe graye blandysshynge pleasaunt delyte ector herte caught appetyte lyke guydo lyketh wryte day grekes vysyte full well besene wonder rychely many worthy company suche none ches tent firste achylles fynde sothe troyan knyght vpon stede toke waye ryght full lyke man made mencyon nowe hadde achylles great affeccyon herte bothe day nyght worthy ector haue syght neuer lyfe none occasyon myght hym haue none inspeccyon hym beholde good lyberte vnarmed myght hym neuer se wonder knyghtly well porte chere mette fere right manly theyr countenaunce laste felle dalyaunce achylles firste began abreyde vnto hym euen thus seyde ector quod full pleasynge leyser naked may syth neuer myght haue syght whan thou armed knyght shalbe full greuous whiche inly enuyous thou sayne slayne anone handes twayne sothe hoolly pleasaunce cruell deth take vengeaunce full ofte werre eke fyght haue felte vertue great myght thy force thorugh many woundes kene vpon full fresshe grene many place byshedynge blode thou wre furyous wode aye com assynge destruccyowne many mayle myn haber owne thy shar e swerde racyd hath sonder cruell seuered yonder mortally sygnes shewe plate stronge percyd yhewe ha eys forged bryght stele myght neu r assured wele thyne yr whan thou lyste smyte thy sw rde wolde kerue byte flesshe full depe full profounde sheweth ye many mortall wounde body large longe wyde yet appere vpon euery syde day day full sore ake smerte whiche thynge semeth herte enbolleth newe nowe whan hye despyte auenged fret enuyous rage may neuer breste aswage tyll vengeaunce fatall sute cruell deth execute one thynge moost greuaunce whan haue fully remembraunce mynde consyderyd vp downe howe thou madest dyuysyowne ala patroclus yonge manly vertuous loued skylle ryght ryght selfe full myght hole herte inly kyndenesse tunge may telle expresse haste thou made departysyon v hole affeccyon yknet one hertely allyaunce without partynge disseueraunce entyerly faythfull hertes twayne ylaced locked chayne whiche myght nat none aduersyte lyfe deth sonder twynned tyll cruelly thou madest v departe thurgh herte iwardly doth darte wyll neuer soth thoughte truste well full dere shalbe boughte deth hym thynge parauenture endyd yere vpon oonly sake cruell deth vengeaunce shalbe take ensure without bonde may lyue myn owne honde shall deth execucyon without abode longe delacyon right requyreth without drede deth deth fynall mede selfe theron shalbe wroke thorugh ye worlde hereafter shalbe spoke achylles venged foo patroclus loued soo though enuyous thy deth inly desyrous ne wyte nat put blame well wotte thou arte hast dethe many day desyred therupon inwardely conspyred thus shortely atwene v two deth without wordes mo whan fortune hath tyme shape hope fully thou shalt nat escape truste none say vtterly ector nat hastely answerde agayne sobre countenaunce auysed well dalyaunce nothynge rekles euen thus spake achylles syr achylles without fayle thou oughtest nat herte meruayle though power full myght herte wyll dewe ryght day day thy deth conspyre euer one compasse desyre laboure erely eke late pursue full cruell hate thou oughtest nat wonder wyse fully knowe sentence wyse maner taketh hede rightwysnesse may nat procede outher wyght shulde hym loue myght deth pursueth destruccyon ouer confusyon hath layde sege aboute cyte kynred also vpon therupon felly doth presume mortall hate werre consume v euerychone wysse nat fynde herte lawe kynde suche one loue right equyte haue hym chere sothly degre werre may frendlyhede debate loue right procede sothly loue moste specyall faythfulnesse hath orygenall hertes ioyned conuenyence one accorde difference doubylnesse may degre nouther ioye aduersyte lyfe deth sondre disseuer loue contynueth euer hate contrarye whiche sothly hertes whan varye procedeth rancour eye men may se debate enuye stryfe enmyte mortall slaunghtre bothe nye ferre moder whiche sothfastnesse werre fyn wherof longe seuereth hertes frendeshyp kut two causeth loue layde full lowe wyll well thou knowe thy proude wordes herte thought sothe agaste right nought shall ferther breke without auaunt trouthe speke say playnely hense two yere may lyue werres swerde knyghthode forth acheue hope sothe mortally grene grekes whan mete thou shall fele full vnswete ye contynue werres haunte shall pryde surquedye adaunte suche wyse handes two werre fully full many greke sore shall rewe well wote olde nat newe grekes gaderyd one surquedye founde euerychone oonly lacke discrecyon vndertake presumpcyon hye thynge sege layne selfe ouer charge vayne empryses withoute fable weyght importable peys great heuynesse fynally wyll oppresse pryde auale enclyne berthone eke enbowe backe chyne vnwarely cause falle ye haue done say one alle ouer full suerte thou achylles speke vnto fatall deth firste shall assay tofore thy swerde thynge auiyle agaynst thy worthynesse great hardynese courage wyll vygour force ght meue thy herte manhode kiyght take derrynge darreyne betwene v two thylke quarell befalle whiche stryue wyll assente playnely iupa te tyll deth one v departe lordes kynges prynces wyll accorde yfere fully one assent holde stable herte entent whiche felde oonly tweyne haue sayde quarell may darreyne fynysshe condycyowne happe thorugh thy hye renowne venquysshe put outtraunce wyll make fully assuraunce firste lorde pryamus kynge shall vnto grekes maner thynge sceptre crowne hoolly hym submytte poynt varye nouther flytte fully yelde subieccyowne lordshyp within troye towne lyges captyuyte shall go theyr way cyte leue quyte gouernaunce without stryfe varyaunce therupon make suerte deuoyde ambygnyte tofore goddes othe sacrament shall swore full good entent ouer fayth also saue assure pledge ye shall haue mene whyle kepe syde choyse hostage abyde troye towne worthyeste ye lyste chese also beste ye shall thynge euer saye achylles without wordes mo thou lyste accorde full therto haue sayde thy honour encrease make werre sodaynely cease lykly laste longe betwene troyans grekes stronge thou shalt nat oonly wt honour fame thorugh worlde gette name therwith nat lyte thorugh thy knyghthod many man fyte fro deth shall escape lyue countre hole sounde aryue lykly cruell aduenture dede werre endure come therfore let nat prolongued let day wene v two ioyned haue sayde condycyowne diffence oonly towne haue victorye fortune axe nat anone ye breke vp sege werre lete suffre v lyue quyete grece home whan ye gone whiche thynge achylles anone hote ire furyous also brennynge full hote anger wo assentydis despytous chere gan anone ector dresse hym nere sayde wolde delyuer hym vtterly fro poynt poynt axynge made none excepcyon hole herte entencyon requeste accepted euerydell semed lyked right well parte caste gloue downe sygne token confirmacyowne lyfe deth wyll holde day agayne ector happe happe may vnto whiche ector lyfly sterte toke vp glad herte euer yet dyde man knyght quarell toke foo fyght man sothe ryght deuyse gald hye empryse whiche noyse great sowne ran erys agamenowne anone came downe theyr tent lordes parlyament pwhere achylles ector yfere wytte theyr wyll matere wolde assente fynally put quarell full iupardy outher part atwene knyghtes tweyne ye haue herde fully dareyne one voyce grekes denye sayde ne wolde suche companye kynges duke lordes eke also lyfe deth iuparte atwene two course fortune submytte hir face day chaunge flytte troye conclusyowne iuparte ne wold theyr lyues theyr towne handes oonly knyght put auenture fyght pryam except whiche sothly caas within hym selfe fully assentyd playnely put set iupardye hoolly honour regallye supposynge aye made memorye ector shulde haue hadde victorye empryse toke honde pryam myght natwithstonde agayne many one entencyon contrarye oppynyon bothe grekes troye syde helde pea let ouer slyde grekes parted echone ector achylles gone home troye hym leue whyle whyles directe shall style telle troylus lamentable wo whiche made parte lady fro ala fortune gery vnstable redy aye chaungeable wha folk trust thy stormy face lyke theyr desyre ye fully embrace thy ioye away tourne wrythe vpon wretch thy power kythe recorde troylus yt fro whele lowe false enuye thou hast ouer throwe ioye whiche inne lady make hym twynne whan best wende haue suryd woo hath enduryd must nowe helpe hym complayne whiche herte felte great payne inwarde wo great distresse haue cunnynge expresse whan knewe partynge cryseyde almost woo payne deyde fully wyste departe shall sentence iugement fynall fader gyuen parlyament whiche wo tourment rent poynt haue fallen rage man myght pea swage hyd paynes whiche breste gan dare lyke man furye gan fare suche sorowe day nyght make complaynynge oonly hir sake whan sawe shulde aweye leuer hadde playnely deye lyue behynde hir absence hym thought without hir presence dede sayne intoterys began rayne whiche eyen gan bolie breste syghes vp swolle sobbynge sorowes depe ne rore wepe sore loue herte gan constrayne ne felte nat lytell payne wepte also pyteously gan crye desyrynge aye myght dye rather parte fro hym troye hir owne knyght hir lust hir lyues ioye hir chekes terys downe distylle fro hir eyen rounde droppes trylle dewed haue hir blacke wede eke vntrussed hir heer brodegan sprede lyke golde wyre rent torne yplucked nat sherys shorne ouer hir fresshe rosen hewe whylom ymeynt whyte lylyes newe wofull wepynge pyteously disteyned lyke erbys apryll reyned floures fresshe dewes swete right hir chekes moyste wete crystall water vp ascendynge hye hir breste hir heuenly eye aye amonge hir lamentaeyowne ofte sythe fyll swowne downe dedely pale dymmed hir syght ofte sayde ala myn owne knyght myn owne troylous ala shall te rather let deth spere darte thorugh herte vaynes kerue rage stryue rather ala fro knyght twynne wo deth inne ne wylt thou come helpe make ende shulde troye wende abyde grekes goon dwelle amonge cruell foon ala ala wofull creature shulde werre endure wretched woman selfe alone amonge men armes euerychone thus gan crye longe day hir complaynte wt full great afray hir pyteous noyse tyll drewe nyght vnto hir hir owne trewe knyght full tryste heuy came agaynes eue myght hir comforte leue sothe hath cryseyde founde swowne lyinge grounde pyteously vnto hir went wofull chere hir armes hent toke hir vp atwene two began newe suche dedely wo routhe pyte sene chere pale grene coloure lyke asshes dede fro hir face gone rede chekes deuoyded blode wofully atwene two stode ne myght nat worde yspeke redy deth wreke vpon hym selfe naked swerde besyde full ofte gan grounde glyde armes fylle swowne hym selfe gan terys drowne stylle dumbe stone mouthe wordes none wery spyryte flyckered hir breste deth stode vnder reste withoute menprys sothely lyfe thus semed stryfe whiche two shulde firste ypasse deth portrayed herte outher face suche coloure men go theyr graue thus wo gan togydre raue disconsolate longe nyght good fayth shulde ryght processe hole theyr bothe sorowe made tyll next morowe fro poynt poynt specefye wolde full longe occupye euery thynge make mencyon tarye translacyon shulde hir wo procede semeth nede syth mayster chaucer afore mater hath well hym bore boke troylus cryseyde whiche made longe deyde rehersynge first troylus contrayre ascende vp loues stayre surquedye became one companye loues folke olde game whan cupyde made hym full tame brought hym lowe subieccyowne temple walked vp downe whan gynne hooke leyde amyd eyen cerclyd cryseyde whiche day myght nat asterte thorugh breste percyd herte wente hym home pale syke wan wyse troylus firste began seruaunt mayster telleth thus tyll holpe pandarus thorugh whose comforte medyacyon boke made mencyon great laboure firste came grace contynueth certayne yeres space tyll fortune gan vpon hym frowne fro hym must go towne sodaynely neuer hym se lo ende false felycyte lo ende wordely brotylnesse flesshely luste lo vnstablenesse lo double varyacyon worldly blysse transmutacyon daye myrthe wo morowe aye fyne ala ioye sorowe cryseyde kynge thoas anthenor shall go forth ala vnto grekes euer dwelle hole storye chaucer telle ye lyste man better lyue processe halfe well descryue englysshe gylte sayes rude boystous firste olde dayes full fer parfeccyon lytell reputacyon tyll came thorugh poetrye gan tunge firste magnefye adourne eloquence honoure laude reuerence thorugh lande gyuen songe laurer englysshe tonge hym gyuen excellence right whylom full hye sentence perpetuelly memoryall columpna cardynall petrark fraunceyse gyuen ytayle reporte neuer fayle honour dyrked name regystred hous fame amonge hyest sete mayster galfryde chefe poete euer yet langage name shall pallen none age euer ylyche without eclypsynge shyne parte wyll neuer fyne hym magnefye wrytynge playnely tyll dye god praye soule brynge ioye lefte wyll agayne troye storye telle firste guydo within boke speketh troylus rebukynge hym full vncurteysly sette herte folyly vpon cryseyde full doubylnesse boke guydolyste expresse hir terys hir complaynynge hir wordes whyte softe blandysshynge meynt faynynge flaterye outwarde farsed many false lye vnderhyd varyaunce curyd aboue fayned countenaunce woman falsely terys borowe theyr herte though sorowe lyke wolde trouthe deye thynke nother seye serpent vnder floures fayre venym hydeth doth repayre sugre afore galle hydde behynde appropryd vnto theyr kynde dyuerse double nature rathest deceyuynge whan men moste assure vnder coloure euery thynge werke fayre aboue foule derke hydde man may espye though wofull eye outwarde wepe pyteously tother eye laffe couertly whose sorowes tempryd allyes theyr coloure euer meynt rayes vpon chaunge mutabylyte stande hole theyr truste theyr suerte sure doubylnesse alway double theyr sykernesse semynge one whan beste varye lykest corde whan contrarye thus varyaunt accorde holest seme whan discorde guydo sayth fewe none hir herte apayed one yet one twayne thre foure theyr speche fayne lyke one mo hole theyr loue well eke wo eueryche shall hym selfe deme next lyke doth seme thus hope standeth eche alle trewest aye redyest falle serueth beste next apayred thus chaunge theyr loue fayred let man truste catche whan may farewell morowe though sure day fayre chaunge lasteth ouer yere folye bye dere thylke treasoure whiche harde possede flyeth away whan men therof mostenede happe chapman sayth guydo yet day men may se sheweth large fenestralles chaumbres hye lowe downe halle wyndowes eke euery strete also eke men may mete pylgrymages oblacyownes spectacle cytes townes sayth guydo selle hym ferther telle eke sayth sentement fraude fully equypolent fraude sleyghty compassynge woman lyke workynge set faythfulnesse wenynge fynde stabylnesse shall fynde stedfast mone poynt chaunge soone yonge caste hym rage olde falleth dotage wherfore counsayle bothe two caste brydell lyghtly let go techeth guydo god wot nat hath delyte speke cursedly alway woman thorugh boke men may se lyste loke hadde enuye specyall good fayth right wroth wt lyste debate yre whiche latyn translate inwardely herte felte blede hye despyte clause rede resowned conclusyon oonly malys accusacyowne woman full euyll mote thryue generally secte descryue whiche made nat thorugh discrecyon good badde none excepcyon blame foule mote falle cause one hynder alle dare well afferme rode agayne one badde hondred gode though one bouble newe hyndreth nat trewe example also though shewe one whylom shrewe good take shall hede hyndrynge womanhede though twayne thre double fayne agayne lothely colayne virgyns inly full grace leuen thousande holy place man may fynde kalender full many mayde parfyte enter whiche deth stable trewe rosen hewe marterdome blysse heuen wonne also bokes tell konne lylye virgynyte vyolettes parfyte chastyte ascended aboue sterrys clere sercle nynthe spere wherfore ioye euer gladnesse eterne wherfore sothe discerne though clerk shrewes haue myssayde let good woman therof myspayde lacke one nat blame eke men may sayde trewe reprefe though nother thefe worse degree though tother hanged tree vnto woman hyndrynge none amonge hondred though one gouernaunce vycyous agayne thousande vertuous ye lyste lyghtely ye may fynde though guydo wryte haue kyde double men shulde goodly take agayne maner grutchyng make nature werkynge hath full great powere harde course hir holde restreyne wyll nat gyded reyne coarted hir dewe ryght therfore eche man full myght shulde thanke god take pacyently woman double naturelly shulde men ley blame though myn auctor hyndre name wrytynge oonly cryseyde vpon hir suche blame leyde counsayle lyghtly ouer passe myssayth hir place hyndre woman outher eue morowe take hede let sorowe skyppe ouer ye lyste nat rede tyll ye come dyomede hir sent troye towne ceryously made mencyowne firste hym delyuered anthenor kynge thoas troylus gan hir conueye many brynge hir weye dyomede waye gan hir brydell lede tyll hir broughte hir faders tent calchas fall good entent receyued hir lodgyd lay hir speche durynge day maner hole euerydele rehersed ceryously wele troylus boke ye haue herde sayne wryte ofte holde vayne guydo sayth longe nyght cryseyde forsoke hir owne knyght gaue hir herte vnto dyomede tendernesse womanhede troylus wexe hir herte colde without fyre ben asshys olde none excusacyon oonly kyndes transmutacyon appropryd vnto hir nature selde neuer stable endure experyence men may ofte lere nowe agayne matere must resorte though ferre began wryte werre phow whan ye trewes endyd wente batayle agayne many man slayne partyes ye discrypcyon ye palays ylyon also dyed many grekes pestylence demaunded trewes xxx dayes whiche obteyned capitulo xxvi tyme passed trewes ytake next morowe wha tyta hath forsake vnder partye emysperye nyght full merye aurora lyinge syde bed hym lyste lenger byde shope hym vp caste stremes shene troye walle whan ector armed clene felde faste gan hym hye fyftene thousande companye worthy knyghtes manly men fynde troylus hadde ten knyghtes eke baner sewe hast parys gan remewe towne perce longe eche bowe honde arrowes sharpe trussed theyr syde knyghtes aboute hym ryde hadde also thre thousande fynde dephebus next hym came behynde thre thousande knyghtes armed clene whose plate sonne shone full shene next hym came troyan eneas rede sothly thesame day troye towne hondred thousande knyghtes renowne lyke recordeth dare frygius boke guydo wryteth thus grekes tofore day seuen thousande went menelay knyghtes echone whiche dyde lede many went dyomede next foloweth hardy achylles mayne called myrundynes zanptipu worthy kynge eke hadde thre thousande knyght whiche ladde felde agayne towne alderlaste came agamenowne suche nombre grekes felle wonder telle whan wardes felde abrode hadde theyr place without abode agrekysshe kynge whiche yt phyllys hyghte anone ector hadde syghte towardes hym syttynge stede spere gan hym faste spede whan ector comynge sayne hente spere rode hym agayne thorugh shelde plate rounde gaue hym laste fat wounde vpon whose deth auenged full many greke gan ector flee firste worthy kynge famous grekes called zantipus hye disdayne oonly phyllys sake towarde ector hath course ytake spere ran hym full ryght ector firste hyt hym suche myght thorugh harneys speres hede zantipus fylle grounde dede deth greke sore playne dyde theyr myght theyr besy payne euery halfe furyous wode auenge troyans blode thorugh passynge cruell hardynesse began troyans oppresse many one day ne myght asterte thoruh breste yperced herte dede slayne amonge prees amonges whiche cruell achylles slewe lychaon eufrobyus noble knyghtes right worthy famous ycome theyr countre agayne grekes helpe cyte whyle troyans costrayned narowe spere quarell darte arowe ector wounded thorugh vyser face lyke ryuer reed blode downe began rayle harneys thorugh auentayle wherof astoned whan hadde syght full many troyan toke hym flyght cyte faste gan drawe chase full many one slawe myght felde remewe euer one grekes sewe vnto walles almost towne tyll ector troyan champyowne knyght hode gan take hede albe wounde sore gan blede yet manhode gan recomforte maugre felde resorte namely whan hadde inspeccyowne walles toures towne eleyne eccuba quene suster fayre polycene many lady gan beholde hym thought anone herte gan colde shame knyghtes shulde fle lyke lyon cruelte made tourne manly euerychone waye mette meryon agrekysshe kynge nye allye achylles bokes specefye swerde ector smote hym hym rofe pecys two whan achylles sawe hym dede parted two euen fro hede hent spere thought ne wolde fayle tohyt ector thorugh shelde plate mayle rode hym full enuyously amyd shelde smet hym cruelly stroke ector neuer adell remeueth nat sat faste well swerde anone taryeth nought ran achylles enuyous thought knyghtly ran vpon coursere creste shone bryght clere suche myght ector hath hym smet percyd thorughe basenet racede eke auentayle stroke many pece mayle achylles constrayned nede maugre myght stagre stede enclyne bowe backe whiche tyme ector hym spake sayde achylles well aduerte great enuye thy cruell herte specyally thou haste yet beware counsayle thy selfe put aduenture one thynge playnely ensure desyre laste day felde mete may truste right well gayneth socour shall acquyte thy labour mortally vnderstande swerde holde honde thy lyfe thou shalt nat escape cruelly vengeaunce shalbe take efte whan met euen vpon thy hede whiche thynge whan achylles toke hede aduertynge herde hym sayne right wolde haue answere agayne pworthy troylus knyghtly entrede inne made sondre twynne thorugh manhode companye worthy knyghtes dyde guye hye prowesse owne myght hath grekes put agayne flyght slayne day drede sixe hondred knyghtes sothely rede losse whiche grekes faste fle theyr tentes necessyte tyll menelay dyde besy cure make felde agayne recure thorugh whose manhode yt day doute worthy knyghtes hym aboute felde grekes recured anone tho fro troye came kynge odemon haste possyble may came enbusshed vpon menelay hym vnhorseth selfe place suche wounde gaue hym face fro deth wende nat escape doutles anone hadde hym take helpe troylus lad vnto ye towne grekes suche prese came downe reskewe hym great nede odemon ferther myght lede kynge menelay towarde cyte whan dyomede came meyne many worthy rydynge hym aboute troylus mette amonges route sodaynely hap aduenture hym vnhorseth eure anone hent stede bad squyer shulde lede vnto cryseyde oonly sake besechynge hir wolde take gyfte hir owne man syth day hir loue wan amyd felde thorugh great myght hym whylom hir owne knyght haste waye went therof made vnto hir present prayinge hir full humble wyse lytell gyfte nat despyse receyue remembraunce pleasaunce pyte womanhede hir seruaunt called dyomede remembre come hir knyght anone herte glad lyght full womanly bad hym repayre agayne vnto lorde playnely hym sayne shene myght kyndenesse womanhede gentyllesse refuse hym platly hir grace hir straunge place kynde founde comfortable euery thynge seruyable may nat lyghtly mynde thynke hym trewe kynde pwith whiche answere messager gone vnto lorde tolde hym anone worde worde lyke hath sayde therof full well apayde hym thought playnely herte recured paynes smerte forth hym armes knyght day durynge stronge fyght troye manly haue borne grekes myght nat stonde aforne theyr tent haue chased downe ne hadde kynge agamenowne grekes hadde dryuen felde whiche thynge anone behelde came vpon many worthy man tho newe slaughtre agayne began euery halfe vpon large playne grekes haue troyans layne efte agayne haue felde ywonne troyans constrayned tho begonne lese theyr londe tyll pollydamas whiche knyghtes besyde gan falle vpon endelonge grene troye full manly sustene grekes gan enchace whan came loste theyr place stronde euen vpon see thurgh knyghthod made fle theyr lyfe drede whiche myschefe whan dyomede behelde sawe pollydamas mortally pursued chas hors backe felde fere cruell herte hent anone spere spryngynge rode hym full ryght agayne acquyte hym lyke knyght lyste partye feyne stede helde agayne reyne raughte spere threwe reste dyomede smote breste mortally lyke founde vnhorsed hym greuous wounde ryght anone knyghtly herte pollydamas attones sterte vnto hors dyomede reyne proudely gan lede vnto troylus foot stode bathed grekes blode euery halfe whiche shadde amonges knyghtly hym hadde ne myght endure sustene sharpe swerde grounde kene delyuerly maugre foon sadell vp sterte anoon force armed vnwarely aduenture ca sharpe swerdes none whette achylles togydre mette worthy troylus rancour pryde achylles smote felle asyde downe hors lowe grounde natwtstandynge grene mortal woude rose agayne faste gan hym spede myght recure stede nought wolde nat auayle sodaynely fresshe batayle troye made mencyon compasse wyse beset hym enuyron eueryche armed bryght clene ector tho furyous tene dare telleth maner howe day thousande knyghtes slowe whiche withstode oonly diffence achylles make resystence tyme deth stondynge iupardye certaynely bokes lye lyklyhede myght nat escape myschefe dede take ector hym furyous rede thelamonyus reskued hym great nede caused hym recure stede natwithstandynge great prees duke lorde athene case herte hole entent helpe achylles wonder dylygent hym ladde many noble knyght bycause drewe nyght storye maketh rehersayle made ende batayle troye entred towne made mencyowne hauynge delayes mortally foughte thurty dayes withoute interrupcyon outher parte great destruccyon aldermost theyr great pryde lost moste grekes syde saue pryamus loste specyall sixe sone called naturall hadde full great heuynesse storye lyketh expresse mene whyle ector certayne face wounded agayne thus haue cruell rage euery parte receyued great damage tyll kynge pryam troye sent downe trewes vnto agamenowne sixe monthes assente wolde therupon hath counsayle holde lordes beste echone accorded therto graunte axynge conclusyon whyle within ylyon durynge pea outher parte assured woundes fully cured lay worthy ector protector towne ryche royall chefe doungeowne ylyon troye bare name whiche byldynge hadde suche fame shulde comende vp downe dare doth descripcyowne wante cunnynge termys aplye boke doth specefye wrolde none ryche hye deuyse byldynge lyche whiche stode delyte recordeth twelue stone whyte alabastre shortly conclude twenty pase latytude grounde ypaued thorugh wt crystall vp hyghte parformed euery wall stone man fynde dyamountes saphyres ynde royall rubye oryent lyght derkenesse dymme nyght enchaced bemes shene euer amonge emeraudes grene stone maner man worlde deuyse reken pryse value rychesse ther wrought large gret roudenesse sayth dare yuory pyllers therupon set corner pured golde aboue hyghte ymages wonder huge weyghte many perle many ryche stone euery pyller halle hadde one massyfe golde borned clere bryght wonderfull mannes syght werke meruaylous fasyon lyke estymacyon thynge ymade founded fayrye werke wrought fantasye thorugh wytte man lyklynesse boke dare bereth wytnesse lyke reken syght apparaunce thynge celestyall syth boke ye get wrytynge myght neuer se albe dyde excelle therof thynke nowe telle retourne agayne pryamus whiche whyle inly coryous myght besy cure ordayne sepulture sone afore dede tyme syke lay dyomede loues darte wounded herte felte inwardly smerte wofull syghes whiche breste abreyde full ofte daye loue cryseyde shake feuer newe caused hym full pale hewe wexe bothe megre lene pyteously gan hym abstene fro mete drynke solace sene dedely face ofte day hir wolde playne dissease mortall payne prayinge grace wolde se vpon woo haue pyte mercy take hede hir seruaunt oonly womanhede planely ellys seye hir sake sayde wolde deye cunnyngly full sleyghty wyse kepe hym lowe vnder hir seruyse delayes helde hym forth honde made hym weer stonde full vnsure betwene hope dispayre whan grace shulde haue repayre put hym heuynesse daunger newe brought hym distresse disdayne encrease payne double weer brought hy trayne woman holde man full narowe whan hurte cupydes arowe sette hym many felle assayes day day put hym delayes stonde vnsure betwyxe hope drede right cryseyde left dyomede entent sette hym fyre woman kyndely desyre whan man haue brought traunce vneuenly hange hym balaunce hope drede lynke hym chayne fyne vnsure twayne dryue hym forth yeres serue force lyue sterue fyne loues fyry rage wolde haue hym inseruage locked hym vnder suche keye wote nat lyue deye doute thus lette hym dwelle forth wyll storye telle matere eke resorte agayne myn auctour recordeth certayne trewes wered gone twelue dayes suynge one grekes faught wt towne great damage confusyowne outher partye aduersyte whyle great mortalyte bothe swerde pestylence amonge grekes fatall influence noyous hete corrupt eyre engendryd great dispeyre theyr lyfe felde leye day day sodaynely deye theyr nombre faste gan discrece whan sawe ne wolde sece theyr aduyse kynge agamenowne trewes sent towne thurty dayes pryamus kynge without graunted axynge phowe andronomecha ectors wyfe hadde vysyon hir slepe hir housbonde fought morowe shuld slayne whiche wold byleue hir nouther fader moder achylles slewe hym ca xxvij whan moreyne wofull rage pestylence began aswage trewes wered goon grekes caste mete theyr foon vpon day plate armed clene whan phebus rose bemys shene full plesauntly gan shede lyght fynde tofore selfe nyght andronomecha faythfull trewe wyfe worthy ector hym louynge hir lyfe hadde gete child two wonder semely inly fayre also lamedoute called tone yonge tother ne myght gone astronanta rede hyghte fetured well passynge fayre syghte guydo lysteth endyte moder pappes whyte yonge tyme soukynge arme hir brestys embrasynge nyght made mencyon hadde hir slepe wonder vysyon note sothe may neuene outher dreme veryly sweuene fro aboue reuelacyon whylom hadde kynge scipyon shewynge outher oracle goddes warnynge myracle sothenesse slepynge lay hir thoughte playnely next day ector went fomen assayle wonte armed batayle hene shulde escape vtterly fatys hondes falle fynally ouer antropos shall fyne euermore lyues threde twyne shewe force hir fell myght whan parodye worthy knyght proche shall without wordes mo felde playnely go whiche astonyd streyght short breth lay abrayde vp deth syghe stynte slepe pyteously braste wepe constraynte hir hertely sorowe specyally wofull morowe whan sawe stocke worthynesse wonte manfully hym dresse arme hym stele borned bryght troyan wall ector worthy knyght fete felle downe lowly declarynge hir vysyowne quakynge herte womanhede wherof god wote toke lytell hede therof hadde indygnacyon platly affermynge discrecyon truste suche fantasyes dremes shewed gladly meynt lye full iapes illusyons whiche playnely conclusyons benat ellys folkes delude albe people rude therin whyle haue affeccyon iuge deme theyr oppynyon dyuersly may pretende ofte falle happen wende foloweth lyke conclusyon drede whiche lamentacyon encrease gan andronomecha hir swowne firste cryed sayeng ala myn owne lorde dere trewe wyfe ala ne wyll ye whiche faythfull hoole affeccyon desyreth aye sauacyon vp rose dedely vysage lyke woman caught sodayne rage kynge pryam eccuba quene haste wente hir selfe mene hir wyfely herte trewe stele ceryously declared euery dele hir pyteous dreme whiche thorugh myracle hir oonly deuyne oracle shewed thorugh goddes purueaunce tolde eke fynall ordynaunce fortune false disposycyon fully purueyed destruccyon hir lorde without delay felde go day pwherfore prayeth dedely hewe vnto kynge meccy rewe vpon hir wo haue compassyon ordayne discrecyon lordshyp soueraynte hir lorde nat destroyed reckeleshede wylfulnesse worde kyndenesse aye somoche loue founde tofore quene swowne fell grounde sayde ala full pale chere helpe case myn owne moder dere womanhede routhe grace lorde felde ne pace deuer moderly pyte benyngnely goodly se knyghthode hye prowesse restrayne renowmed noblesse thylke day handle spere shelde go armed felde bothe twayne assent beste condescende vnto hir requeste fynally accordynge one whan wardes redy euerychone yssuynge troylus firste alle parys next grekes falle hym troyan eneas kynge sarpedon pollydamas kynge eroys kynge epystrophus eke kynge ycalled forcyus plate mayle eueryche armed clene alderlaste came kyng phylymene kynges lordes renowne diffence come towne grekes knyghtly debate pryamus sothly gate conueyed goynge set wardes noble worthy kynge full prudently thoruhe sapyence gaue congee lycence vpon greke proue myght agaynst full redy fyght fomen royall apparayle amyd felde abydynge batayle pryamus mene whyle lyke guydo remembreth style thylke fyne ye haue herde sayne worthy ector repayred agayne hym contermaudynge ne shuld gone thylke day fyght agayne theyr foon whiche thynge hye despyte brent whan sawe lordes went gate alone abode whiche wexed furyous wode hoolly cause arettynge wyfe cherte tender lyfe puttynge fully occasyowne abydynge day towne preiudyce hir worthynesse disencrease hye prowesse lyfte thorugh tunges hye estate thorugh false reporte derogate caste anone full knyghtly herte lyfe deth shulde hym nat asterte within felde day founde though wt many mortall wounde shulde pecys wen sondre vpon playne dismembryd yondre hole manhode herte sette anone without lenger lette agayne arme hym full dylygent agayne precept comaundement fader rode forth weye fere whiche wolde deye wyfe newe crye gan shoute hir pappes also hangynge oute hir lytell childe hir armes twayne afore hir lorde gan wepe playne besechynge hym routhe pyte wolde vnto hir sorowese leste hir wyfely trouthe manhode haue herte routhe vpon hir childe hir also whiche bare hir armes two nat myght hym cryinge kepe whan sawe wofull moder wepe knelynge downe vnto hym sayde hir sobbynge myght abrayde myne owne lorde haue mercy nowe lytell childe whiche ye se pyteously afore wepe crye haue mercy lorde v dye haue mercy eke vpon cyte myn owne lorde haue mercy cruell deth passe shall echone lacke helpe ala whan ye gone crye andromecha eke hir suster cassandra eccuba fayre polycene eleyne lusty fresshe quene whiche attones felle hym beforne heer vntressyd wepynge torne loude gan crye place besechynge hym mercy grace thylke day abyde towne herte haue compassyowne hir complaynte hir wofull mone syth truste twone alone hym abode resystence agayne deth chefe diffence hym hoolly theyr affyaunce theyr suerte theyr suffysaunce eche thynge myght greue yet ne myght herte meue abyde yet goodlyhede hym besought theyr womanhede wolde enclyne herded herte stele myght lytell droppe fele oonly pyte theyr woto rewe lykly morne renewe fynally theyr distruccyowne cyte sothly towne vnhap endelesse ruyne yet myght hym nat enclyne ne wolde conclusyon indurate herted lyon alway contynuynge rage whose herte myght softe swage nouther prayer waymentacyon hym restrayne oppynyon euery perell layde syde way gan anone ryde thorugh wyfe none bote hir rage kynge ran mased hir mortall wo vnneth myght speke hym diffacyd rewefull hir syght hir hewe knoweth hir wyght loste hadde bothe myght strengthe plat fyll grounde lengthe tofore kynge routhe sene besechynge hym entent full clene grace consydre hir wo helpe ector go seynge hir faythfull womanhede hir request raughte anone stede prycked oonly hir sake great haste hath ouer take worthy ector within cyte hent reyne great diffyculte maugre hym made hym tourne agayne suche wyse durste nat sayne albe full lothe therto force prayer also stede made hym lyghte reste eschewe ne myghte ne wolde agayne fader stryue albe felte herte ryue melancolye hertely ire disdayne newe set fyre inwardely steryd blode lyke tygre lyon wode depryued newly hir pray right fared ylke day lyke bore tuskes whette whyle grekes troye mette furyously walkynge vp downe diffence sothly towne troylus firste bay stede aduenture mette dyomede eche surquedous pryde sharpe speres gan togydre ryde guydo sayth without drede one bothe hadde anone dede ne menelay knyghtly go bytwene furyous tene smette hors full k yghtly wyse meryem myghty kynge fryse menelaus marked hath full wele swerde full sharpe groude stele vnhorsed hym threwe hym grene stroke myght nat sustene menelay hym wode lykly euen stode lyfe shuld nat escape grekes full hastely shape meryem ye haue herde sayne sette rounde vpon playne sesse hym auentayle euery part cruelly assayle destytute dredefull caas hym helpe came pollydamas knyghtes gan nyghe nere whan hym sawe taken prysonere maugre vpon hym sette theyr handes pollydamas hym fette whose reskues great stryfe many one therfore loste lyfe grekes rather shulde escape theyr handes hasty rape caste playnely shalbe dede fully purpose haue hadde hede stode myschefe great disioynt hym helpe euen vpon poynt came troylus moste knyghtly array manhode made suche affray amonges reskues kynge maugre comynge delyuered myghty lorde fryse cruell deth ye haue herde deuyse therupon came thelamonyus proude armes euer surquedous thre thousande full worthy euerychone vnhorseth pollydamas anone amonge knyght proudly bare hy downe troylus hath thorugh hye renowne myd foon gete hym hors agayne troye sore layne euery halfe thorughe grekes pryde myght afore nat abyde newe newe hardy achylles assayled myrundones compelled necessyte myschefe made flee home walles gate towne great damage confusyowne theyr partye backe gon whiche thynge whan margaryton behelde sawe game goth herte gan wexe wroth passyngly haue disdayne storye recordeth certayne bothe hardy famous sone also kynge pryamus noble knyght great worthynesse whan sawe myschefe distresse troye gan fle caste anone auenged vpon achylles great myght ran hym full lyke manly knyght hors backe townes sake hym enforseth achylles take amyd felde amonge knyghtes alle achylles ala shulde falle day hym slewe cruell aduenture thorugh troyans myght nat endure felde holde homewarde gan hye mortally make noyse crye firste deth margaryton pursuyte kynge thelamon made chase thorugh cruelte home gate troye cyte slewe kylled alway rode albe parys manly hym withstode brethre baste borne theyr grounde haue lorne lefte forsake vtterly felde home went broughte shelde dede corp margaryron theyr gate shette anone whiche myschefe ector gan beholde ire herte gan colde sayde platly without delay wolde auenge deth day made haste stede fet vp sterte basenet vn wyste kynge lefe lothe gayne forth anone goth tyll passyd gate towne furyous tygre lyowne whose comynge thycke swarme tofore swerde grekes gan fleen thought tyme withdrawe firste fynde hath slawe two worthy duke mette besy waye lette tone ycalled eurypalus tother hyghte hascydyus troyans felde agayne haue wonne newe manfully begonne grekes sewe folowe tras yet myschefe dauz pollydamas tyme grekes take ector hath borne hym sake sorest layne thorugh knyghthod reskued hy agaye put grekes great distresse thorugh manhode worthynesse euer thylke day rode sharpe swerde bathed theyr blode cruell mercyles knyght callyd leothydes shope hym anone ector mete whyle moste irous hete sette hym full presumptuously ector tho deuoyde mercy anone hym slewe threwe hym felde whiche thynge whan achylles behelde great slaughtre woundes wyde ector made vpon euery syde gan anone compasse herte vp downe caste aduerte grekes neuer may sure agayne theyr foon fyght endure kepe felde stryue whyle ector lyue wherfore caste shope many weye engyne ector myght deye auauntage myght hym fynde therto eke polycenes ynde worthy duke also assent oonly herte hole entent hope stode suster wyue loue felte herte ryue hir grace better stonde caste fully take honde hye empryse haue tolde whyle hym moste bolde ector hym slewe none geyne whiche anone achylles hath seyne ire wexed herte wode bore tygre theyr cruell mode vpon ector auenged furyously hym gan fle ector caughte quarell sharpe ygroude threwe hym gaue hy suche wounde thorugh thyghe vpon outher syde felde myght nat abyde hym withdrewe anone wente men home vnto tente made anone surgyen bynde mortall wounde fynde whan staunche ceaseth blede haste agayne toke stede lest wounde dede afterwarde great drede thought firste auenged vpon ector myght hym se hap sorte wolde falle hym thought paynes alle hym beste remedye honde myght dye lyfe roughte nat amyte ector myghte quyte deth deth conclusyon hoolly entencyon desyre fully suffysaunce deth vnwarely gyue hym myschaunce tyme ector vp downe wont playeth lyowne amonge grekes many sondry place swerde gan enchace deth myght hym seen fledde afore hym lyke swarme none hardy hym sette whyle grekysshe kynge mette hap aduenture whiche sothe cote armure enbrouded hadde full many ryche stone gaue lyght whan sonne shone full bryght clere ioye sene perlys whyte emerawdys grene full many one sette cercle basenette rounde enuyrowne auentayle veluet fret aboue mayle saffres ynde stone rede arraye whan ector taketh hede towardes hym faste gan hym drawe firste fynde howe hath hym slawe force manhede hent hym vp afore hym stede faste gan hym ryde wardes lytell syde good leyser playnely may spoyle hym ryche array full glad lyght newe empryse ala false couetyse whose gredy fret whiche great pyte hertes may nat lyghtly staunched etyk gnaweth great distresse defaceth hye worthynesse full ofte sythe conqueroures theyr fame rent away floures desyre hauynge gredy thought hye noblesse sothely longeth nought suche pylfre spoylynge roborye apparteyne wrothy chyualrye couetyse knyghthode lere one chayne may nat knet yfere kouthe ofte suche rauyne hath cause rote ruyne many worthy lyste take hede lyke ye may ector rede sodaynely brought endynge oonly spoylynge ryche kynge desyre hym hadde hors backe whan hym ladde reklesly storye maketh mynde caste shelde backe behynde welde hym selfe lyberte haue opportunyte spoyle hym wyght spare breste disarmed bare except plate diffence aagayne stroke make resystence ala tho rekles floure knyghthode mahode pereles whan foo ylke day hym alone awayte lay myschefe hate enuye felde myght hym ought espye achylles cruell venymous hertely hate moste melancolyous whiche couertely houynge hym besyde whan sawe ector disarmed ryde hente spere sharpe grounde kene ire hatefull tene vnwarely ector myght aduerte ala whyle smote hym herte thorugh ye breste dede fylle downe vnto erthe troyan champyowne thorugh neclygence oonly shelde deth whan odemon behelde worthy kynge myght hym nat refrayne achylles rode payne hyt hym amyd prees maugre myght myrundones dede guydo sayth certayne wounde fyll gro felyng ye playne knyghtes shelde lofte layde hym caryed hym full softe vnto tent haste leue dedely wounded man full sore syke tyll may releue whan drewe eue troye great reuerence dyde theyr laboure theyr dylygence dede corp carye towne worthy ector whan tytan went downe temple dolefully wende day wofull ende thus longe nyght heuynesse skylle ryght wyll leue agayne retourne mater helpe mourne pof complaynt lydgate maketh deth worthy ector cap xxviij ala shall procede storye wo drede fele hande tremble quake worthy ector oonly thy sake thy deth lothe wryte shall helpe endyte vnto shall clepe calle certys none musys alle accorde synge euer oon vpon pernaso besyde elycon aungelyke theyr armonye tunge none may specefye great swetnesse theyr goodly songe discorde founde amonge theyr musyke entunyd sytte noughte helpe wo mater wt mournyng shent tragedyes tore rent complaynynge pyteously rage theatre dede vysage ala clepe dare crye troublyd penne grace guye nouther clyo callyope allecto thesyphone megera euer doth complayne lyue euer wo payne eternally tourment dwelle cerberus depe downe helle must praye gracyous mater whiche furyous wyghte complaynynge drery fere right well syttynge matere meynt heuynesse acordeth well chere drerynesse allyed vnyte pwherfore helpe thou wofull nyobe drery tere thy peteous payne penne dolefully rayne helpe also thou cruelly yxione belydes doth boget gone thy stone helpe thou zepherus thy ryuer helpe eke tantalus hungre haste huge pyne wofull playnte helpe fyne besynesse stocke roote worthynesse knyghthod groude mahod shours well tofore bare awaye bell derrynge floure hye prowesse example also gentyllesse neuer coude amys seye ala ector ala shuldest thou deye cruell parchas toke ye hede cruelly twyne fatall threde ye hasty ala ye namely threde breke two thou antropos thorugh thy great enuye troye ala well mayst thou wepe crye make wofull lamentacyon whiche haste newe thy confusyon loste thy diffence thy stronge wall thy beret vp thy suerte royall thy honour chefely begonne ala ala thy bryght sonne eclypsed thou standest desolate comforte disconsolate thy lyght loste thou derkenesse plounged arte soth fastnesse worthy thou haste worthyest day yloste knyghtlyest shall ensure euer borne whyle worlde may dure wonder though thou wepe sore day day complayne hym euermore thy shelde ioye wo thou wont loue tenderly thy hole herte may nat lyghtly sterte haue hym euer thy remembraunce whiche soth thy full suffysaunce guydo maketh mencyon man dwellynge towne ne hadde kyndenesse loue hym wryte expresse childe lefe dyed caas outher eyer well belouyd goddes fate destyne disposyd hadde myght haue woman also euery maner age deth falle suche rage thorugh cyte aboute euery strete sobbynge salte terys wete heer rent dedely wo furyously ronne fro mortall theyr aduersyte beholde ala pyte yonge maydens matrones olde sobbe syghe theyr fystes folde loude crye sayde fynally ala nowe shall faders cruelly syght slayne day day ala whyle man shall saye nay farewell helpe ector gone surnesse v euerychone wont reste nowe dede ala body whan caryed presence pryamus kynge anone loste offyce spekynge gan hym selfe salte terys drowne pyteously therwith fylle swowne vpon corp colde stone inly desyrous deye anone without tariynge hym lay force rent away bretherne eke whan toke hede tryste pale sorowe nye dede haue selfe rage torne neuer trowe seen aforne bretherne yet suche another care eche hym selfe gan fare wolde haue dyed cors theyr lyfe platly gaue fors grounde many sorowes sore lyke wylde bulles gan crye rore routhe theyr dedely wo sene herte stele myght nat sustene pwhat shall saye eccuba quene suster yonge polycene cassandra prudent wyse wyfe sorowe deuyse whiche rent self tourment wo fynally wolde selfe cruell deth wepe wayle shulde make rehersayle wryte theyr sorowes theyr complaynges theyr pyteous sobbynge throwes wepyges wofull cryes pyteous sowns theyr drery playntes lamentacyowns theyr woo specefye large boke wolde occupye eche thynge shulde ordre telle trowe longe dwelle man tedyous many day lere woman wepte afore corp lyinge selfe defacynge theyr complaynynge wonder myght endure haue sothely nature kynde wepe playne syghe sore terys rayne tyll tempest theyr wofull rage may processe lytell lytell aswage thus leue syghe sorowe make cely woman theyr clothes blake shroude theyr face wympled vayne whyle tourne mater agayne telle playnely kynge pryamus herte inly desyrous caste awaye entencyon corp kepe corrupcyon whiche naturelly men take hede corrupte must right nede kyndely disposycyon may made none opposycyon aboue grounde body lye reason must putrefye crafte aboue nature vncorrupt myght nat endure pwherfore kynge shope hym ordayne preserue hole fro thynges twayne odoure abhomynacyon therwith eke crafty operacyon slyght nat founde horryble lyfly vysyble eye apparence lyke quycke existence coste kynge wyll spare nought made anone afore hym brought craftyest maysters towne suche hadde moste discrecyowne parfourme axynge curyously obeye byddynge faythfully theyr wyll entyer dylygence temple moste reuerence cowne whylom dedycate full yore also consecrate appollo olde foundacyowne besyde gate standynge towne callyd tymbr theyr troyan tonge storye botheradde songe phane speke made firste hye autere great deuyse lytell oratorye perpetuelly memorye sette ryche receptacle made maner tabernacle egall syght large ymage reysed ryche stage borne vp eche corner puryd golde vpon foure pyllers eueryche full craftely ydyght aungell stode golde borned bryght ceryously werke sustene crafty archys reysed wonder clene enbowed ouer werke cure meruaylous celature rofe closure enuyrowne fyne golde platyd vp downe knottes graue wonder curyous fret full stone ryche precyous euery kynde man deuyse ryally thryfty wyse derkenesse blacke nyght bemys theyr clere lyght enchacyd dyde shyne fro grounde vpright lyne degree men ascende made well man coude amende workemanshyp euerychone parformed vp cristall stone atteynynge vp fro table ba standynge restynge ryche crafty tabernacle hauynge aboue vpon eche pynacle ryche rubye reysed hye hyghte stode ymage huge large weyghte massyfe golde hauynge lykenesse worthy ector gan face dresse towarde grekes dyde stonde aye thretynge swerde honde amyddes great rychesse haue yset good aduysenesse dede corp worthy knyght syght man standynge vp ryght sotyll crafte lyuynge face chere quycke lokynge colour sothly hewe beynge fresshe rose newe lyke supposayle lyued apparayle stede lyke tolde thrugh smale pypes wrought made gold mesure enbowed downe entre made crowne great aduyse subtylyte eche partye extremyte body lyuealy porrect thorugh nerfe synewe dryuen direct secrete porys craftely extende wherby lycour myght downe descende kepe hym hole fro corrupcyon without transmutasyon hyde hewe part tourne hede golde ourne fylde bawme naturall ran thorugh pypes artyfycyall thorugh necke hede many place penetrable vaynes face thorugh vertue force lycoure conserued lyfely coloure fresshe hewe quycke thynge pale myghtely bawme dyde auale comparysownyd semblable soule vegetable whiche without sensybylyte mynystreth lyfe herbe floure tree semblably euery vayne corp vertue dyde attayne breste arme spredynge enuyron moysture discencyon hande fote sothly rede thorugh bone ioynte gan vertue shede distyllynge myghtely flete fete full gommys swete vyoll stode tempred bawme ymeynt processe may nat wexe feynt day day encrease amende whiche vapoure vpwarde gan ascende causynge eyer enuyron delyse resemble paradyse flauour holsome soote odour spyce gome roote pure golde foure laumpes lyght tofore corp brennynge day nyght oyle sothe credyble crafte made extynguyble ne myght myn auctor sayth certayne nouther queynt wt tepest wynde rayne processe wasten yeres whiche eyre bryght borned wyres full craftely reysed lofte whose swetnesse men reioysed ofte theyr courage lyked well whan werke complete euerydell rounde enuyrowne full ryche fresshe se made parclose eban tree longe laste may dure whiche tree oonly nature whan cut smelleth wonder swete may nat waste brenne hete though layde amonge colys rede mydde flawme many fyrye glede nat consumeth though men assaye ofte water houeth eke lofte kyndely grounde goth toswymme heyght sothe loth lyke also techeth pluuyus tree whylom passyngly famous hye pryse reputacyon large myghty regyon worthy londe ethyopye ynde yore agon folkes fynde hadde tree great honour gaue trybute emperour remembred antiquyte golde yuor ryche tree gyftes famous royall quyte theyr dette hym specyall whan pryam full thryfty wyse parformed hath ye haue herde deuyse ryche werke noble excellent hertely loue beste entent ordayned eke guydo telle certayne noumbre prestes dwelle temple theyr deuocyons contynuelly deuoute orysons soule ector preye goddes spyryte lyste conueye eternally dwelle yfere ioye blysse aboue sterres clere whiche prestes kyng gaue mansyons abyde possessyons whiche hath mortysed perpetuelly ye haue herde deuysed whyles knele praye wake caste fully ende make fynally thyrde boke rude maner vnder toke whyles troye wepe morne vnto grekes wyll agayne retourne dulle style storye trace oonly borne vp supporte grace pexplicit liber tercius incipit liber quartus hereafter foloweth fourth boke whiche speketh grekes made kynge pallamydes chefe captayne theyr hoost deposed kynge agamenon capitulo xxix ector thus dede ye haue herde sayde achylles tente ylayde wt woundes mortall fresshe grene vpon morenyng whan sonne shene enchased hadde away derke nyght agamenon wyse worthy knyght werkes passyngly prudent hath haste lordes sent whan assembled euerychone within tente sayde anone syrs quod lordes kynges prynces duke eke yfere ye aduerte clere inspeccyon ye ought echone hye deuocyon hoolly herte goddes herye wardely right merye ye consydre wysely take hede ennemye ector dede whylom berer vp troye theyr full truste theyr honour theyr ioye theyr hole diffence proteccyon vnto v deth confusyon vnlykly euer v haue hadde victorye whyles floured glorye agayne whose swerde myght nat auayle slewe nat aryuayle ye remembre firste day noble kynge callyd protheselay next shall nat fayne patroclus parted euen twayne felde amonge v euerychon slewe nat eke worthy kynge menon archylogus also prothenor eke kynge hyght alphynor phyllys also epistrophus ende brought zantipus meryon myghty stronge kynge waye came rydynge slayne hath kynges two cedyus drodyus also polycenes stronge polybete letabonia kynge phylete manly knyght kynge isydyus eke kynge hyght humerus ire cruell tene worthy kynges slayne hath eyghtene whiche hyder came grekes londe power myghty honde laude honour goddes alle whiche caused haue falle dede encrease ioye discrese foon troye shall fynde experyence laude also pryse reuerence fortune v hath holpe wele tournynge hir double whele hye comforte consolacyowne v echone syttynge enuyrowne stoude nowe parfyte sykernesse thorugh deth hym dyde v oppresse may wayte towne deth destruccyowne hastely ende woo theyr truste ector goo without may nat longe endure wherfore may fully v assure purpose hole shall acheue fynally daunte greue vnto shalbe importable one assent stande stable theyr party tourneth wrake theyr hope fully put bake dispeyred nonsuerte vtterly theyr cyte shall weer deth depende soth shall day day amende helpe god bothe see londe victorye redy honde voyde platly ambygnyte excluded eye ye may se bothe wantrust foreyne drede counsayle procede ferther vpon foon ryde prudently whyle abyde kepe v close passe boundes tyll achylles helyd woundes echone myghty vyolence oppresse whan haue diffence haue sayde thorugh helpe achylles let v nowe sende pee two monethes kynge pryamus lyste graunt v lykely playnely shall whyle flawme funerall consume may dede bodyes pale lye abrode euery hyll vale whiche reporte haue repeyre fro day day infecte eyre thorugh felde engendrynge pestylence stynke great vyolence whyle may ease reste woundes cure semeth beste assente therto euerychone vnto troye messageres gone haue trewes graunted kynge repeyred without tariynge therof made full relacyon grekes afore agamenon whan ende home tent euery lorde doth wende whyle trewes endureth pee amonge grekes kynge pallamydes complayneth sore agamenon hadde domynacyon aboue hauynge enuye day melancolye hye despyte indygnacyon full inly fret yrous passyon gan breke rancour shewe certayne sygnes though spake fewe tyll day wyse agamenon conceyued hath hye discrecyon hoolly thynge though ne wold spare fro poynt poynt hym selfe declare whan lordes togydre present tofore owne tent noble worthy kynge full circumspect euery maner thynge nought rakell melancolyous attempraunce inly vertuous well auysed wonder prudent whan knewe menyng entent conceyte pallamydes nat hasty rekles longe abydyng thorugh prudence reson within boundes discrecyon whose tunge oonly sapyence restreyned neclygence hasty speche sothly rape myght make worde lyppes escape vnauysed thynge hym asterte firste examyned herte aye speche thryfty wyse conueyed doctryne wyse vnder reyne wyt hye prudence fourme eloquence alway sayde reason went aforne worde tale lorne wyse shewynge sentence tofore open audyence sayde euen thus whan pee vnto kynge called pallamydes sothly quod ye take hede semeth playnely nede auysely lyste aduerte muse grutchynge herte hoost haue gouenaunce wysely consydered euery circumstaunce estate whiche man may denye wolde maner neuer occupye tytle fre eleccyon nat interrupt medyacyon brocage roted vpon mede aye vnder meynt fauour falshede depycte coloure trewe entencyon supporte suche false ambycyon whiche thynge wyll quyte tofore nat wyte wyse hye offence stonde clere conscyence without spot suche vayne glorye touchynge estate whiche transytorye pyet neuerchelesse haue cure wyt helpe procure euery thynge touchynge comonte perseuer myght prosperyte hauynge eye inwarde syghte vnto estate euery maner wyghte comytted gouernaunce great laboure besy attendaunce indifferent vnto hye lowe helpe fostre coude knowe stode myschefe nede day nyght take hede beste coude aduysenesse aye dylygent nat felle distresse sothfastely loke ryght dayes thynkynge watche nyght herte inly aduertence without fraude slouthe neclygence faythfully full myght aquyte euery maner wyghte lyke estate without excepcyon man iustly reson greke nowe lyue vnto gylte may duely ascryue falsehede engyne trecherye loue hate fauour flaterye cause named specyall haue lyke egall one besy payne man hath mater complayne party hye lowe estate deuoyde rancoure debate amonges haue deuer generall thynge partyculer hyder towarde thyg hath myscheued god wote well shulde nat agreued herte set pryse chose discrete aduyse domynacyon haue subieccyon ease herte tranquyllyte lyke lordes degre wyll fully haue obeyed lyke one vtterly haue deyed quarell haue vndertake destyne hadde shape saye sothe full loth fayne ouer also ye playne chosen without assent meruayle nat syth ye ne present longe ye remembre ryght towarde troye waye nat dyght ye consydre nere ye came passyd full two yere longe abyde comynge hadde grekes great hyndrynge passynge harme full great damage huge lettynge vnto vyage hadde without wene comynge taryed athene lykely ye nat well say nay haue yet vnto day ye thought nat credyble afferme eke impossyble grekes shulde maner wyse dare take great empryse absence manly acheue wynde thynge leue none offence grekes haue without presence thorugh force water londe full many thynge parformed wt theyr honde acheued thorugh theyr worthynesse one thynge ye gesse say degree shulde herte reioyse lordshyp great estate pompos elate porte occupye aquyte trewely nat lye deuoyde suspeccyon wyll make resygnacyon tofore excuse auysed discretly se ye lyste haue agayne morowe pryme without settynge lenger tyme prolongynge forth delay thus made ende day went theyr way oonly nyght tyll morowe tytan shad lyght whiche tyme counsayle generall grekes helde specyall lordes congregacyon haue tolde eleccyon whan mette yfere agamenon anone ye shall sayde euen thus sadde countenaunce lo syres quod touchynge gouernaunce haue hadde domynacyon haue hereto hole affeccyon clene entent besynesse euery thynge myght wylfulnesse encrease parseuer contune recorde take god fortune whiche haue conserued cause floure felycyte honour hye noblesse stande hole sounde yet syketnesse whyle fame moste flourynge semeth ryght well syttynge myn estate fully resygne specyally whyle fortune benygne many present alone suffycyent without helpe bere charge men moche may ouer lade barge namely tempest rage syth ye discrete sage burthen let releued man therwith agreued let v one entencyon without stryfe discencyon chose suche one moste acceptable echone moste couenable gouerne discrecyon echone hole affeccyon assentyd speke generall men may se naturall men delyte thyng newe truste people faynt vntrewe aye vndiscrete full doublenesse varyable theyr sykernesse aye awaytynge theyr oppynyon chaunge transmutacyon selde neuer standynge hole one day loue morowe gone full selde sykernesse oonly nowe newfangelnesse hath embracyd theyr affeccyon haue stede agamenon newe chose oonly fauour pallamydes theyr gouernour grece lyke desyre haue sceptre hole empyre called aboute euery coste emperour grekes hooste right tofore agamenon fyne conclusyon daye theyr parlement euery man went lodgynge home right way tent wounded lay hardy knyght hardy achylles whan herde pallamydes fro poynt poynt leccyon displeased oppynyon playnely thought aduyse agamenon passyngly wyse discrete vnto gouernaunce tother plesaunce sayde none eleccyon maner subrogacyon bycause hym selfe parlement chesynge nat present arettynge passynge great offence choyse made absence wherwith herte inly wrothe lefe lothe conclusyon strengthe stode eleccyon phow kynge pryamus went vnto batayle auenge deth ector dyde meruaylous dedes armes ca xxx trewes passyd yweryd oute wounded eke recured aboute next morowe pryamus herte inly desyrous grekes manly fyght ectors deth auenge myght olde pryam knyghtly felde whan troyans selfe behelde great wyll hye courage hym ferre ronne age gan reioyse plucke vp theyr herte specyally whan gan aduerte great manhode worthynesse lyflyed hye prowesse sake euery maner man gan arme hym haste pryamus day lyue deye felde proudely hym conueye hondred thousande fyfty towne lyke dare maketh mencyowne worthy knyghtes euerychone without pryam gone afore wente dephebus parys nexte pryamus menon kynge worthy eneas alderlaste came pollydamas fynde sterne full pryde pallamydes came tothersyde felde many stronge batayle firste whan eche gan assayle kynge pryamus knyghtly wayches thorugh wardes pallamydes hym vnhorseth thurgh hye renowne lyke knyght kylleth bereth downe proude grekes rode none hardy swerde abode narowe gan coharte theyr wardes made sonder parte felle furyous day dedes meruaylous armes wrought wonder sene meruayle may sustene great age felde endure credyble ensure se thorugh great myghte grekes put proudely flyghte dephebus also nat behynde agayne foon knyghtly fynde acquyte hym self make go backe sarpedowne eke lacke yfallen neptolonyus proudest greke moste surquedous famous strengthe myght whiche agaynwarde rode full lyne ryght sarped owne spere rounde delyuerly smote hym grounde sarpedowne full yrous herte without abode foot vpsterte neptolonye ire hote ye thyghe wt swerde smote anone kynge perce londe worthy famous honde sarpedowne whan toke hede knyghtly hym restored hath stede natwithstandynge menelaus vpon hym passynge despytous hym eke duke athene enclosyd haue amonge great prees kynge perce ala shulde falle slewe hym amonge alle full knyghtly faught lyke champyowne multytude enclosyd enuyrowne hym selfe alone ala destytute mortall ca thorugh whose myschefe troye towne gan withdrawe tyll sarpedowne hath holpen recure theyr londe full many greke kyllynge honde kynge pryam manly founde sone called naturall whiche vpon hym rode longe day manfully abode partynge nat playnely fro syde kynge togydre ryde full mortally grekes confounde pryamus many cruell wounde hath slayne many worthy man horse backe amonge ran none day yonge olde troye towne hardy bolde none estate hath well hym quyt amonge grekes ryt fro poynt poynt reken euery thynge hath pryam noble worthy kynge alone confusyon grekes destruccyon theyr outter myschefe discomfyture afore whose face myght nat endure thynges two mortall yre inwardly sette hym fyre hertely hate bare olde vnto grekes doubled many folde deth hadde remembraunce worthy ector countenaunce whiche platly thorugh worthynesse swerde shope hym redresse fret hate constreynt payne veryly thylke thynges twayne whiche day loke ryght force doubled myght thorugh toke cruelly vengeaunce grekes brought outtraunce thurgh knyghthod put ye flyght grekes attones dyde theyr myght assent assemble one sleyghte syde gone playne large fayre se betwene pryam troye cyte fyne oonly theyr entencyowne hym debarre entre towne euery way grekes haue set troye hadde tho belet theyr repeyre storye telleth thus manhode pryamus whiche anone lyon stronge swerde gan ryde amonge seuered large woundes wyde slewe tho wolde swerde abyde euery endelonge playne parys eke hath belayne myghty shote stronge archery pursuyte arbalasterys ne myght shote kene mortall harme abyde sustene gan anone fle place kyng pryam narowe gan chace nede necessyte thorugh slaughtre cruelte swerde sharpe whette grounde greke felde yfounde fled away eueryche tent troye theyr cyte went bycause drewe faste towarde nyght phebus hadde reued lyght honour hye victorye worshyp eke laude memorye perpetuelly palme also pryam kynge hath wonne mo day release sorowe rede next morowe hath ysent troye towne atrewes agamenowne whiche graunted selfe day pryme albe therof rehersyd tyme longe laste boke expresse durynge whiche dyd besynesse hertely laboure inwarde dylygence ordayne great reuerence corp worthy kynge perce londe without tariynge kyngly honour troye towne shall caryed regyowne buryed predecessours outher kynges progenytours whiche thynge complete ye aduys alysaunder called parys firste corp enbawmed rychely conueyed full solempnely wryte guydo huge route knyghtes rydynge hym aboute tryste heuy cladde blacke echone chare right way gone towardes perce ledynge kynge dede corp towarde buriynge whiche halowed lyke estate royall whyle feste funerall holde also great deuocyowne worthy ector within troye towne lyke custome vsed tho dayes rytes theyr paynem layes whichefeste made mencyon fro yere yere reuolucyon yhalowed space fourtenyght many flawme many hydous lyght brent enuyrowne seyntuarye called anyuersarye came aboute yere yere certayne day theyr kalendere whiche custome remembraunce people shulde contynuaunce playne wepe also praye rede theyr frendes afore dede full pyteously theyr heer torne mornynge blacke knelynge aye aforne dede corp worthy knyght whiche tyme passynge myght done whyle trewes dure grekes trustely myght assure whan lyste good lyberte without daunger entre cyte day day troyans myght also vnto grekes frely come go whiche tyme full great delyte hath achylles caught apetyte entre se maner towne without wysdome discrecyowne beholde playnely se hooly maner solempnyte forth went certayne day towarde troye haste may vnarmed sothly myn auctour sayth without assuraunce fayth except trewes lefe loth firste temple goth appollo halowed feste thorugh towne downe vnto leste cleped anyuersarye ye haue herde shulde lenger tarye many worthy present amyd temple hye lowe estat lordes ladyes affeccyowne euery parte gaderyd towne corp worthy knyght fresshe coloure kept vnto syght lyfely eke quycke hewe beholde rosenewe thorugh vertue oonly gommys swete bawme gan aboute flete euery ioynt eche extremyte feste solempnyte eccuba yonge polycene womanly goodly sene many hye estate lowe tofore corp syttynge rowe heer vntrussyd cladde wedes blake euer one suche sorowe make routh pyte sene playne deth mene worthy ector knyghthod groud welle trowe ye guydo lyste telle polycene hir wofull rage ychaunged hath vpon hir vysage hyr natyfe colour fresshe syght rose lylyes whyte outher fresshenesse hir lyppes rede terys gan shede hir chekes crystall clere hyr heer also resemblynge golde wyere whiche lay abrode lyke vnto syght phebus bemys spere bryght whan v doth lyght auale aye rent hir fyngers smale hyr golden heer hir blacke wede whiche thynge achylles toke good hede gan meruayle greatly thought god kynde euer myght haue wrought theyr werkes fayre creature hym thought myght nat endure beholde bryghtnesse hir face felte thorugh herte pace persynge stremys hir eyen two cupydes bronde hath hym marked loue hyr desyre brente hote fyre soone sodayne colde quoke alway fyxe hir loke arrowe god cupyde perced hym euen thorugh syde herte gaue hym suche wounde neuer lykely sownde aye one loke hir caste durste gan prese faste towarde hir namely eye hym thought must nedes deye founde hir grace geyne playnely place newe caughte loues snare helth welfare dispeyred herte ne knewe beste eche thynge well assure set nought toke cure thought hole hir mo longe day thus went fro tyll phebus chare lowe gan declyne golden axtre clere doth shyne saye sonne went downe pwhan eccuba quene troye towne hir doughter polycene also temple paleys go aye achylles hir syght whyle myght tyll lacke lyght maye haue leyser opportune loke hir cursed fortune whiche haste maked hath went knyghtes home tent anone withoute taryinge bedde goth full tryste complaynynge aye hym selfe castynge vp downe mynde eke reasowne hede fote hir beaute euerydell herte felte knewe full well fynall cause languysshynge polycene beaute moste passynge loue moche payne felte hete thought herte melte aye bedde walowynge fro constreynt hydde wo whiche almoste hym thought yt deyde hym selfe euen thus heseyde allas quod wo begone sorowe knowe ende none suppose syth worlde began ne neuer wofuller man whylom great myght renowmed euery maner wyght thorugh worlde bothe hye lowe none sothe coude knowe man armes famous yholde victoryous tofore tyme remembred style vnto day ala harde whyle nouther ector playnely none polycene worthy brother power hadde whan mette theyr myght ouer sette felde force daunte pryuely dare auaunte ala mayde tendre age hath sodaynely brought suche arge stremys hir eyen twayne perced hath clouen euery vayne herte may nat sterte dede thorugh constreynt smerte shall wysshe teche ala shall leche shall helpe men saue deth graue hope playnely none saue hir mercy ala gone nouther prayer tresour rychesse force myght nouther hye prowesse hyghnesse blode byrthe kynrede may auayle helpe nede meue hir sadde trouthe vpon wo euer haue routhe pwhat newe furye inportune rage hath brought herte suche outrage agaynst whiche nat debate loue hir beste dedely doth hate good fayth wysely lyste adueret lytell wonder though hate herte syth come hyder fro ferre hir kynred make werre whiche confusyowne hir knyghtly brother worthy renowne haue fatally myn hondes slowe whiche worlde hadde felowe worthynesse manlyhede ala ala nowe may quake drede lyfe falle dispeyre shulde bolde haue repeyre dare ala come theyr syghte wofull wretche vnhappy wyghte shall hardy appere presence hir eyen clere certys se none mene weye fynally muste deye dispeyred stonde euery syde helpe nat prouyde right anone profounde syghes depe achylles braste wepe dedely chere pale funerall face tourned wall routhe pyte sene hertely furye paynes kene oppressyd thought lyfe deth rought nought contynued tyll drewe nyght tytan hath withdrawe clere lyght euer one lyke wofull man ilyche syke coloure pale wan without slepe fretynge sorowe tyll lucyfer next morowe tofore sonne bemys clere full lustely gan appere oryent whan achylles vnpacyent without reste pee quakynge aye feuer newe sene playnely hewe tyll abrayde anguysshe sodaynely called one hym preuy counsayle trusteth well vnto hym telleth euerydell fro poynt poynt hym stode sent hym forth bycause coude gode message streyght troye towne full aduyse informacyowne mater eccuba quene thorughe wysedome amene myght discrecyon fynde way sauacyon vnto lorde louyd quene anone go mater wysely gan conueye tofore grace wolde preye enioyeth gyue hym audyence tale none offence foole newe lere wherfore quene goodly gan hym euer hym lyketh sayne worde ylost spoke vayne tale man coude amende craftely gan discende substaunce tolde clerely oute premysses full well brought aboute fynally conclusyon chefe sayde entencyon effectuelly wolde make pea vnyte atwene grekes folke troye whiche thynge knewe better weye werre theyr alder ease wytte prudently appease mortall stryfe bytter rage allyaunce oonly maryage hir lyste wyse worthy quene hir doughter fayre polycene may wedded vnto achylles thorugh theyr myght fynall pee eccuba hir discrecyon thorugh hir wytte medyacyon hir prudence myght aboute brynge pryamus fully assentynge achylles myght doughter wyue myght parformed blyue lyke haue made mencyon couenaunt oonly condycyon grekes shall theyr werre lete suffre hym lyue quyete maryage ylke twayne parformed knyt vp chayne whan ye quene hath knowen entent full soberly good auysement tofore worde asterte full pyteously syghed hir herte laste sobre chere sayde thus messagere frende quod touchynge thy requeste make beheste leste wyll condescende lyeth brynge ende thy lordes wyll herte entere vpon muste firste requere kynges wyll wyll gyue assent purpose whiche thou arte sent ouer muste wytte also pif parys wyllynge eke therto whiche thynge euery circumstaunce wyll selfe make enqueraunce full faythfully pryam parys mene whyle theyr aduyse without within dayes thre whiche tyme come agayne achylles wyll sende fynally thou shalte knowe ende matere answere playne home goth achylles agayne pwith full glad chere lord ye plese sette herte better ese auysely hye discrecyon hath made relacyon tolde tale thryfty wyse coude wordes deuyse brynge hope lordes herte full relesse paynes smerte pwherby made sorowe withdrawe thus whyle hope gan adawe amyd breste eccuba quene pryam spake polycene touchynge sonde achylles profre make pee tolde hym forgate thynge wherof astoned pryamus kynge spake nat worde halfe houres space hym selfe gan compace full prudently myght mene achylles wolde haue polycene vnto wyfe aye wondrynge laste syghynge wonder sore discloseth conceyt herte sayde ala howe sore doth smerte remembre may haue pee great offence achylles towardes playnely whan slewe worthy ector thorugh cruelte hoolly vpon euery syde assuraunce gouernour guyde myne platly sayne therwithall myn eyen twayne alone sothfast lyght shelde protectour thorugh great myght manhode agayne mortall rage grekes werre croked age ala confusyowne slayne worthy renowne achylles whiche may nat mynde herte neuer fynde allyed mortall foo rote grounde sorowe woo full harde herte appese loue hym causeth myn vnese euery halfe thorugh cruell foon proude grekes herted echon agaynst fortune contrayre tourned newe quarell apayre causeth grekes wode furyous ala presumptuous ector berafte way sythen none choyse may agaynst herte though anger ryue mater assaye shall stryue though loth sytteth full sore yet eschewe harmes whiche lykely hereafter falle saue myn sone alle wyll consente achylles make trewe fynall pee atwene grekes also cyte without playnely haue vnto wyfe doughter polycene leste treson mene wyll firste wende beheste make ende without fraude myn aduyse whiche counsayle assenteth eke parys rather conclusyon made none excepcyon trete quene eleyne menelay neuer shulde atteyne hir recure agayne vnto wyfe whiche parys without noyse stryfe grutchynge outher vnto entent within hym selfe fully assent therby hopynge without fere drede perpetuelly eleyne possede right luste man shall say nay vpon thyrde day achylles hath wytte matere eccuba sent messagere tolde hym answere kynge ceryously gynnynge endynge assenteth well therto parys eke hir selfe also playnely hym tolde touchynge pea purpose holde firste heste brynge aboute sure therof hym nede nat doute shall haue purpose euerydele werke prudently wele hereupon informacyowne messager troye towne without abode haste may achylles helde right way tolde hym hole effecte matere alway feruent entere herte brent hote glede sawe way spede oonly pea ye haue herde telle aye breste syghes gan swelle loue polycene caste alway amonge paynes kene purpose awaye fynde whyles besy mynde shulde purpose brynge aboute hym selfe caste many doute anone dispeyre rage vp sterte cruelly caught hym herte whiche hath hym throwe suche weer hym thoughe power behe e fulfylle dede except hadde well lesse drede euery thynge putte certayne wenynge greke wolde luste sayne desyre varyable hym selfe thus fauourable parforme thynge denye lusty fantasye maner louers euerychone suppose cheue anone thynge take honde disioynt mater stonde though impossyble theyr foly aye credyble achylles trusteth fynally fulfylle hestys vtterly supposynge aye worthynesse mainhode hye prowesse whiche dyde hym selfe gloryfye pryde surquedye grekes shulde dispeyred theyr trust myght appeyred vpon troyans wynne londe withdrewe honde helpe therwithall also home grece wolde go sege oonly sake theyr quarell vtterly forsake day fyerse achylle abode cyte spylle whiche thynge lordes assent assembled entent amonge achylles byddynge pallamydes whan gaderyd yfere tofore lyke ye shall achylles hath tale ygonne sayd syres somoche konne wysdome hye prudence renowmed eke sapyence thorugh worlde discrecyowne worthy also renowne kynges duke royall name eest west floureth yet fame bothe knyghthode manlyhede say praye take hede saye ye consydre playne entent comynge hydre good auyse destruccyon hadde grounde founded reson cause roted tytle ryght ye lyfte vp syght aduerte clerely mynde full ferre backe wytte sette behynde prudent lokynge auysenesse firste whan foly hastynesse toke vpon v come fro ferre agayne troyans gynne werre iuparte lyues euerychone loue one man alone ye wote trowe mene kynge menelay defaurded quene telle trouth lyste nat feyne ye well wote oonly eleyne groude gynnynge debate many worthy estate recurlesse remedye lyfe good haue put iupardye londes lefte regyownes cytes eke ryche townes whiche absence stonde desolate wyues child eke disconsolate woo abyde mournynge distresse whyles sothe expresse fro day day beset euery syde lye flede deth abyde sorowe care laboure woo wot ye wyte well also sythe tyme werre began grekes many worthy man hath lost lyfe thorugh dethes fatal woude myght hytherto haue lyued sounde home grece assured well ioye ne hadde come vnto troye remembre full great pyte ouer saye also amonge troyans theyr cruell mode haue loste moche blode hath full ofte made pale hewe day also grene newe hadde ector suche mortall wounde quarell sharpe whet grounde aboue theygh kene hede daye afore dede happe shape fro deth vnneth myght escape whiche yet fresshe vpon sene large wyde yet grene smerte whiche sore yet pleyne good fayth semeth eleyne ye aduerte wysely thought suche pryse shulde nat bought thorugh lyfe good yfere honour yput dredfully hange ballaunce ye remembraunce conceyue right caste vp downe sodayne chaunge reuolucyowne fallen hath sythe werre began slaughter deth many worthy man hir sake hath loste lyfe yet worste mortall stryfe doth moste rebounde damage disencrease eke disauauntage lykely encrease ordenaunce nat made therfore remedye shape outher syde fyne oonly eleyne abyde troye styll towne lette v caste good inspeccyowne ease meane way kynge called menelay hym wyfe londe lyke estate suraunce bonde vnder
