wedlocke confermed vp newe vnto hym wyll founde trewe sythe without gylte synne may lawe eleyne twynne dyuerse cause ynowe thorugh ye world euery wyght yknowe auoutry foule vyce lawe preiudyce though menelay iustly hir forsake whan hym lyste another take shall hym better queme please v shalbe full great ease whan werre brought ende whiche lykely many man shende forth contune great laboure importune ne shall whyle mowe sustene sothe without wene troyans yet floutynge theyr myght wt haue full many worthy knyght helpe hye lowe degre therwithall stronge theyr cyte euery part without withinne nat lykely wynne purpose though euer abyde wherfore wysdome let v voyde pryde wylfulnesse oonly prudence haue eye aduertence profyte vayne glorye whyle honour shyneth victorye wysdome withdrawe honde syth may nat constrayne bonde fortune whele abyde stable wherfore rede mutable gery goddesse hir double chere let v gyue vp suche thynge lyeth whyles may worshyp saue werre laude yet haue consyder well manhede moste foo ector dede whyle honour floure counsayle fortune loure saydeere chaunge hir bryght face whyle beste stonde hir grace one assent one oppynyon without contradiccyon herte wyll bothe one alle honoure party palle grece home retourne lenger soiourne quarell haue longe sewed douteles may bee schewed full great damage without fayle haue done shall folowe tayle wherfore beste folye vp resygne whyle hap welfull benygne blandysshynge face fayre tyme beste make repayre whyle stande party enmyes honour perygall fer aboue playnely coude haue eye felycyte whyle ascencyon lest man wyll make obieccyon may nat honour saue repayre playnely haue eleyne agayne cause whiche thynge anone answere shall man fantasye dishonour vyllanye arrette wolde maner kynde go home leue hir behynde shortely saye holde shame sythe haue one great name eleyne berthe gode amonges v ycome kynges blode suster pryam lorde troye towne exyona thelamowne kepynge hath shall nat feyne troye towne parys hath eleyne sythe nowe may none let tone set agayne tother surplus olde enmyte bet wixe v troye cyte counsayle bothe ease one assent wysely apease hen wende tale ende anone kynge menelaus yre wode furyous kynge thoas duke eke athene myght lenger hym sustene suffre hym reckeles spake attones vnto achylles nat oonly thorugh inpacyence court perturbyd without prouydence tumulte gonne repreue achylles proudely comeue agaynst hym oppynyon sayde shortly conclusyon vnto reed ne wolde neuer assente condescende thynge mente gouernyd hym caas whiche thynge anone achylles full yre rancoure herte sodaynely see sterte went way rage tryste pale wode vysage shortly sayde hym lyst nat fayne ne wolde lenger payne helpe spede agayne troynas maner nede bad anone hardy achilles knyghtes callyd myrundones spere shelde helpe grekes entre felde kepe close home within theyr tent thus yre gaue comaundement men ye haue herde deuyse withdrawe euery hye empryse whan euer go batayle whyle scarsenesse vytayle fyll hoost flesshe brede wynne many greke brought vnto fyne ne myght endure distresse constreynt hunger dyde oppresse tyll laste kynge pallamydes thynge reckeles hath therupon made purueaunce remedye redy ordynaunce assent counsayle echon hath sent wyse agamenon worthy kynge messa besyde ell ile oonly prouyde grekes myght spede releue great nede telephus kynge londe gentyllesse hath put honde large wonder free renowmed humanyte socoure comaundynge anone purueours haste gone euery party aboute enuyron thorugh landes regyon faythfully serche euery coost take vp vytayle grekes hoost full hastely made stuffe theyr shyppes playnely lade euery thynge necessarye grekes water carye requeste agamenon without tariynge delacyon kynge plente vytayle fraute ylade gan anone sayle towarde sege meynee aye costynge grekysshe see wynde good kynge blyue nauye troye dyde aryue fewe dayes grekes anone ryght repeyre full glad lyght expleyt good spede well hath borne hym nede pallamydes anone sayth guydo shyppes gone consydre loke aboute nede within withoute amende repare lyst coste spare euery thynge without neclygence touchynge charge dylygence tyll trewes fully ronne werres newe agayne begonne whiche many man sothly dere aboughte ceryously wryte howe wroughte purpose playnely sentence vnder supporte pacyence dvrynge one dedely cruell hate stynte maye cesse date atwyxe grekes towne great damage destruccyowne outher parte felynge full vnswete tyll daye caste mete wonte proudely wt spere shelde theyr wardes entrynge felde armyd full bryght vpon outher syde enbatayled stoute full pryde full knyghtly haue chose theyr groude take theyr large baners wynde yshake tyll togydre sodaynely haue mette alderfirste dephebus hath sette fresshe lusty herte yrous vpon kynge called creseous enuye storye telleth hors backe togydre ran dephebus firste spere blyue thorughout breste euen dyde hym ryue vnto herte spake deth grekes playne sore loue suche woo make astoned haue felde forsake gan anone vnto theyr tentes flee whiche sothe whan troye se vpon chase faste gan spede vnto tyme worthy dyomede hym eke kynge pallamydes hye despyte cruell mercyles twenty thousande worthy knyghtes alle vpon troyans sodaynely falle mortally made lese theyr weye resorte home agayne troye eke grekes felle furyous tyme came thelamonyus hyght ayax stronge knyghtly man lyke lyon amonge ran vpon troyans ouer sette casuelly waye mette cecylyen lusty fresshe lyght tyme wonder manly knyght sone pryam rede thelamon pryckynge stede slowe cruelly swerde anone rasynge arme shuldre bone heallas fyll dede felde deth whan dephebus behelde wodder anone tygre lyon spere ran thelamon smette hym thorugh plate bryght force made hym lyght lese sadell sete amonge prees whiche stroke whan pallamydes behelde sawe clerely gan aduerte irous wood furyous herte caste hym anone auenge thelamowne dephebus full worthy renowne mortally guerdon hym quyte spere grounde byte sharpe kene large rounde square full cruelly ware thorugh harneys without areste dephebus smote breste stroke brake shafte two tronchone hede also lefte breste weye fynally muste deye none helpe remedye wounde cruell mortall lyfe myght nat abyde whyle parys came besyde auenture whyle dephebus wounde inly anguysshous gan haste aproche nere face pale right heuy chere distresse wepte pyteously knyghtes comaunded hastely wounded brother asyde fere haste shulde bere wardes fro great prees vnto payne relees brethe hym leyser auente open eyre vnto hym wente maugre grekes wounded bare hym full easy pa towarde walle faste towne great dole lamentacyowne full softely grounde hym layde tyll laste dedely man abrayde mortall loke face funerall chere pyteous eche ball gan tourne vp deedly eye euen thus parys gan seye brother myn loued haue pyte rewe vpon wo kyndenesse brotherhede wordes routhe take hede syth deth muste sondre twynne antropose shall lenger spynne lyues threde knotte breke wherfore brother praye wreke vpon deth hense pace thou lyste suche grace kyndenesse yet dede breste sperys hede rent away thou auengyd vpon foo truste may wyt deed spirite passe fynally firste descende depe downe helle eternally pluto dwelle myd boundes dyrke ben lowe fynally may knowe deed seye gyue forse soone deye whose requeste parys toke good hede felde faste gan hym spede thought woo pyteously wepynge whyle brother lay languysshynge nat awaytynge oonly deth vpon poynt yelde vp breth knyghtes parys vp downe wardes soughte aboute enuyrowne tyll laste pallamydes fonde sarpedon fyghtynge honde honde kyng worthy sarpedowne come diffence troye towne whiche hande noble knyght whyle full myght moste besy pallamydes presse lyke lyon whettyd woodnesse pallamydes herte nat ferde let flye hym sharpe swerde myghtely wonder theygh parted hath sonder smote harde bone sarpedon fyll downe dede anone troyans whan slawe compellyd force withdrawe thorugh pursuyt kynge pallamydes whiche vpon mercyles cruell wood lyon deth sarpedon whiche ala whan parys dyde espye marked hym cruell eye hente bowe passyngly stronge arowe tyller longe entoxycat venym hede smote therwith dede hytte hym auentayle thorugh stuffe thykke mayle throte gan thorugh pace fell dede selfe place pallamydes manfull worthy knyght thorugh grek toke flyght made noyse wofull crye deth complaynynge wonder pyteouslye theyr lorde myghty gouernour late chose emperour theyr chefe socour souerayne refu ala stonde destytut gouernaunce broke disarayed without guyde right shepe dismayed disconsolat comfortles yshent eche flyeth vnto tent troye sued chace hors backe wonder huge pace mercyles slewe fle euery syde routhe se without pyte grace lyke lyon gan enchace tyll compellyd necessyte constrayned thorugh theyr cruelte tourne agayne selfe diffende troye downe anone discende hors backe euen vpon playne attones none gayne gan grekes proudely outtraye cruelly disamaye fynally gayneth diffence mortall myghty vyolence troyans grekes diffoyle alderfirste leyser dispoyle grekes tentes golde rychesse whiche tyme troylus gan hym dresse parys eke downe theyr nauye thurty thousande theyr companye kyllynge tho playnely mette theyr shyppes wylde fyre sette walle troye cyte men myght well hydous flawmese gone destruccyon ne ayax ycalled thelamon thorugh manhode knyghtly excellence come anone made resistence grekes many worthy knyght tho new began mortall fyght atwene troyans grekes stoute rede blode rayllynge aboute vpon playne hydously blede bothe lengthe brede deed maymed full pale syght vpon soyle full many noble knyght atwexe cruell hate theyr fyght togydre debate wylde borys euen fare none lyste spare felde worthy thelamowne thorugh knyghthode hye renowne manly bare hym grekes diffende man myght manhode hy amende thorugh ye world though men sought daye sone hath wrought meruayle army thorugh great myght sothenesse grekes anone ryght withoute hym hadde fynally shent theyr shyppes attones loste brent thorugh pursuyt parys daye worthy troylus made affraye amonges thorugh hye prowesse fyfty shyppes guydo doth expresse loste brent thelamowne reskus came knyghtes downe vnto see remenaunt saue troyans daye haue hyer hande mortall fyght thorugh force great myght troylus oonly whiche hath many slayne grekes sothe fayne withdrawe felde lete abydynge fonde full vnswete wherfore gan lese theyr place amonge whiche kynges sone trace heber hyght wounded deth myght vnneth drawe breth aspere breste styckynge achylles came complaynynge vnto tent euen laye whiche felde nat daye sake oonly polycene loue sharpe kene aye herte ylyke grene newe heber mortall hewe complayneth sore arrettynge cowardyse manhode trewandyse daye myght shame withdrawe hym hyndrynge name felde hym full great reprefe grekes seynge myschefe confusyon vpon brynke theyr destruccyon abrode felde se lye dede lyste nat one take hede knyghthode grekes releue whyle heber gan hym thus repreue spere whiche body sodaynely drawen ala eye vp caste rancour yre full pyteously heber dyde expyre presence achylles therwith came sodayne re tent certayne knyght achylles axeth amonge grekes clerely stode answeryd full yrous mode certys quod full vnhappely troye haue cruelly grekes daye theyr fyght full shamefully put vnto flyght many slayne ala wela waye vnneth none ne went awaye vnhurte maymed withouten wounde felle v troyans yfounde eke suche multytude suppose shortly conclude daye oppynyowne nat lefte man within troye towne able stonde batayle spere swerde enmye assayle wene sothe come oute v fyght huge route ne myght force take honde felde agaynst stonde nowe lorde draweth vnto nyght faynte fyght pleasynge worthynesse manhode hye noblesse take encrase fame euermore gete name owne glorye perpetuelly memorye ryse vp arme anone sodaynely vpon gone feble weke make resystence agaynst manly famous excellence victours euer conquerours durynge worlde remembraunce euer brought vnto outtraunce soth fastnesse haue drede achylles toke hym hede heber lay afore hym dede full colde strake coloure lyke lede one lyste yeue hym audyence vnto hym haue aduertence may worde herte myne sayde make hym enclyne vtterly euen lyke ferde though maner worde ne herde thorugh eres passyd sowne lo maner condycyowne custome playne vsaunce louers hangynge traunce honour worshyp manhode prowesse strengthe myght fame hardynesse encrease name vertue victorye knyghthode noblesse armes glorye loue ley asyde suche myght god cupyde whiche hertes hye hoke sease lothe playnely displease outher chere countenaunce wyll dede disobeysaunce hir theyr souereyne lady dere loke hir eyen clere full well daunte theyr pryde venus soone felly prouyde arowes kene perce nerfe vayne enlace firy chayne oonly thorugh importable charge restrayned go large whiche cause day douteles noble hardy achylles wolde nat withouten wene come felde drede polycene lyste offended hir herte thynge escaped asterte achylles thorugh mysgouernaunce whyles hynge thus balaunce grekes faught towne tyll bryght phebus goynge downe troyans necessyte lacke lyght entre cyte whyle homewarde repreyred lay dephebus lyfe dispeyred complaynynge aye dedely wounde whan parys troylus haue hym foude myschefe gan wepe crye wolde routhe dye wofull noyse pytous sowne alte terys gan renne downe theyr chekes vpon outher syde whyles vpon hym abyde wounded man gan drawe ende whose spyryte redy wende brest wery goste full hastely another coste dedely eyen tournyd vp downe whan knewe relacyowne parys hath pallamydes yslawe anone bad shulde drawe large tronchone stelen hede anone fyll downe dede corp gan faste spede towarde towne nede dole wryte lamenciowne made sarpedowne thorugh cyte namely kynge quene euer one wepynge brother susters dere vayne reherse pryam hath great dylygence two towmbes made royall excellence dephebus kynge sarpedowne many ymage grauen enuyron many knotte koruen yonder buryed lytell sonder lyke custome theyr rytes olde whyles feste halowe holde called feste funerall grekes haue made specyall ryche toumbe worthy kynge pallamydes buriynge sosempnely made ordynaunce amonges vsaunce great dole pyteous heuynesse haue kynge great worthynesse royally brought sepulture myght longe nat endure without hede gouernour chosen haue theyr emperour one assent affeccyon worthy kynge wyse agamenon made lettynge troye next day suynge theyr wardes felde goon fully purposyd fyght theyr foon grekes manly face mette worthy troylus ouersette greke none shortly telle thylke day afore hym myght dwelle cruelly gan chace came rode place fledde swerde theyr lyfe doute yonge kynghtes rydynge hym aboute suche vsaunt lede euer one grekes blode shede whiche lyke streme disteyned playne whyle huge rayne day huge myste euery man hath felowe myste specyally vpon grekes syde storme theyr woundes wyde manhode troyan knyght pworthy troylus fresshe yonge lyght coact thorugh cruelte maugre theyr myght drede deth fle theyr tentys socoure fynde troyans aye pursuynge behynde full mortally sterne paas storme cease caas home repeyre theyr cyte stronge tyll morowe larke songe troylus eft manly batayle grekes newe caste hym assayle guydo wryt yonge champywne thylke daye rode vp downe amonge foon thorugh hye renowne therne kyge duke erlenor barowne swerde wende theyr lyfe made mortall ende whyle phebus gaue lyght tyll laste drewe nyght troye repayreth manfully seuen dayes suynge lyfe ladde knyghtes felle vpon grekes guydo telle aye newe newe gan confounde cruell swerde kene grounde ne myght mortall tene afore syght abyde sustene vengeaunce toke rode waye forsoke trase renges rede sothe felde lay dede whiche slaughter confusyowne grekes newe sent towne trewes pryamus kynge anone graunted theyr axynge two monethes fully assent lordes parlement wherof made full relacyon enbassatours agamenon theyr lodgynge forth wente vnto achylles sente meane whyle messagers wyse shall anone deuyse agamenon guydo lyste endyte lordes sent achylles vysyte certaye cause lyk ye shal whiche storye rehersed vlixes worthy dyomede duke nestor went playnely rede fyne oonly theyr counsayllynge herte myght brynge induce hym haue fantasye wyllynge thorugh chyualrye stonde hath toforne haue many theyr men ylorne lacke oonly hye presence achylles dygne reuerence receyued right knyghtly chere whan set yfere lyke theyr degre anone audyence pwhyle vlixes full eloquence gan tale prudently deuyse achylles sayeng wyse syr achylles moste renowmed glorye thorugh worlde memorye knyghthode shoures welle displaese nat shall telle youre noble famous excellence erys let none offence shall say goodlyhede pacyently ye wyll take hede wordes sayde herte thought ensure fayne nought saye ye remembre well firste cause purpose euerydell grekes ye haue mencyon fully sette one entencyon well v parde whan come firste cyte kynges prynces except none whiche sothe reken euerychone selfe speke specyall one firste pryncypall assentyd full troye cyte thorugh manhode destroyed shulde perpetuelly brought vnto ruyne newe note doth enclyne worthynesse sodaynely varye purpose contrarye consyder firste sage wronges done great damage grekes londe towne conspyrynge aye destruccyowne ye aduerte wysely thought slayne haue ende brought full many worthy sythe gone full yore treasoure man may restore despoyled v brought great distresse goodes raughte golde rychesse shyppes brent thorugh theyr cruelte ala ye lyste nat se whiche may nat delayed thorugh manhode fynally outrayed syth ye haue slaye theyr hope suffysauce actor theyr affyaunce fully theyr truste diffence also dephebus also go lykely apeyred fro day day fynally dispeyred frowardly fortune loureth honour fame floureth worshyp hye renowne atteyned hath exaltacyowne hyest prycke fortune whele great wronge ye loke wele wylfulnesse vnkynde hir ye frendely fynde frowarde whyle benygne influence gracyously assygne hir spokys meue vnto plesaunce hap tourne wt plente chaunce whose helpe nedeth nat calle pwherfore ala wyll ye suffre palle noble fame wylfulnesse whyle hyest worthynesse knyghtly prudence shulde nat rte whiche thynge euery gentyll herte shulde haue routhe compassyon wherfore praye discrecyon ye shape purpose amende ye wolde herte condiscende v stonde knyghtly werre manhode spoke ferre renowne worldes ende reported men wende perpetuelly fresshenesse hewe day day encrease newe tryumphe hye victorye put storye eke memorye enprentyd foryetylnesse power haue malys oppresse fame knyghthode dyrke difface shyneth yet clere many place without eclypsynge sothly lesse whiche conserne ye reckelesse wylfulnesse cloude lyght renowne yt whylom shone bryght myghty hande manhode wt drawe consyder firste grekes yslawe tofore tent wt mortall woundes wyde thorugh felde vpon euery syde haue disdayne oonly lacke routhe ala whyle lytell slouthe ley hande theyr myschefe whylom theyr stroge myghty wall theyr chefe diffence theyr champyowne soueuerayne helpe proteccyowne ye haue ofte shadde blode agayne theyr foon whan stode full myghtely theyr enmyes assayle without lytell may auayle sothe ne none v echone ye knyghthode lyste v gone agayne troyans ye wont truste fynall hope also ye shall helpe socour vpon praye ye saye auyse full wylle anone hardy fyerse achylle whan vlixes concludyd hadde tale face anger dede pale sayde euen thus openly playne syr vlixes right ye sayne haue declaryd conclusyon purpose entencyon fynally brenne destroye royall cyte called troye holde sothe lyketh nat lye entent grounded folye put v thorugh discrecyon reckeleshede hasty mocyon lyfe deth suche iupardye specyally chyualrye grekes londe smale thynge many prynce many worthy kynge haue iuparted theyr body theyr gode yloste theyr lyfe yspent theyr blode myght haue full well home pee nat nowe kynge pallamydes yslawe also sayth newe wyse manly trewe lyfe pryse alone cause whiche echone gaderyd loke ryght grekes many noble knyght haue slayne bothe worthyest worlde seke manlyest euery lande regyowne grekes party towne chyualry knyghthod ye sourayne floure wynne armes worshyp honoure assembled come fro ferre whiche sothe duresse werre full many one felde dede veryly without drede shall well mo werre laste euery day nombre lasseth faste worthy knyghtes dede without routhe dare saye conclude trouthe rage furyous wode full lykely gentyll blode thorugh worlde shall destroyed rurall folke great pyte shall haue lordshyp hooly gouernaunce churles eke sorowe myschaunce euery londe shall lordes alone whan gentyll men slayne echone nat ector noble knyght worldes sonne lyght manhode floure slayne pyteously werre soth myghte parauenture whiche may nat attayne noblesse shall nat fayne waye shall deth eschewe myght pursewe fro day day whyle lye therfore shortely requere touchynge werre outher praye vayne herken saye nat purpose werre stryfe iuparte lyfe leuer haue pallyd name slayne haue ydell fame worthynesse deth yblowe wynde lasteth throwe though renowne pryse blowe wyde foryetylnesse leyth ofte asyde lengthe yeres oblyuyon thorugh enuye false conclusyon laude knyghthode worthynesse wysedome eke gentyllesse fredam bounte vertue suche grace foryetylnesse derke difface therwithall malys enuye yseryd hath palme chyualrye false reporte wherfore saye wyll wysedome suche folye let quyete forth lyfe nowelede ouer thre rede seke pea troyans ye may hasty wyse without delay counsayle platly alle myschefe deth vpon falle well done ye toke hede bothe vlixes thou dyomede nestor eke sythen ye wyse werke playnely lyke deuyse sume fyne myn entent reporteth hym hath sent anone shorte conclusyon bepeyred agamenon suche answere ye haue herde sayne nedeth nat wryte newe agayne vpon kynge agamenon let make anone conuocacyon lordes theyr presence fro poynt poynt sothly sentence hath rehersyd achylles desyrous haue pee troye platly prayer wyll degre agayne troyans spere shelde helpe grekes armed felde wherfore kynge full wyse vpon axed theyr aduyse thought beste mater sythe stode firste speketh menelay angry chere sayde platly nay haue pea nat entent ne wolde therto assent sythen cytee conclusyon stode prycke destruccyon ector dephebus dede yt whylom trust euery nede theyr diffence ago farewell truste hope also without hole pryde may nat deth abyde truste well without le though achylles ne helpe v nat towarde empryse therof nat drede maner wyse withoute hym haue victorye manhode owne glorye full sure therof certayne vlixes gan replye agayne qestor also sodayne mocyon contrayre oppynyon affermynge playnely wonder though menelay sothly ca vnto pea wolde nat assente openly wyste mente grounde roote werre cause also come ferre theyr londe quene eleyne sake oonly tweyne grekes whiche man may denye theyr lyues put suche iupardye hym hir grounde sought well wyste rought nought menelay wo endure wyfe myght agayne recure sayth ector dede hath heyre speke manlyhede knyghthode wyll founde called ector secounde pworthy troylus whiche yt brother worlde nat suche nother worthynesse reken alle troye myghty walle diffence ector agone ye knowe well selfe euerychone ye lyste take hede whose sharpe swerde sore doth v blede euery day furyous hete amyd felde whan hym mete stede worthy dephebus whiche tyme wonderly famous brother parys nowe founde worthynesse knyghthode perygall haue none auauntage vnto houre rather great damage reken sythe gonne sothe haue lytell wonne lykely alway lese contynue sythe may chese holsome lyue quyete haue pea werre lete one assent sythe ye wyse ye worde calchas gan ryse troyan traytour wt pale chere ire sayde ye shall worthy prynces thynke ye done chaunge lyke doth moone olde purpose firste entent agayne wyll comaundement goddes euery thynge gouerne purueaunce discerne ala ala ne wyll ye leste credence fayth gyue theyr heste whiche wyse may nat fallyble sothe impossyble vtterly troye cyte ordynaunce necessyte myght destroyed hen alyte slouthe nat wyte victorye worshyp honour fynall palme eke labour reported water londe reserued hoolly honde purpose ye forth contune hyndre nat folye fortune sothe dare well conclude peryllous goddes yllude neclygence slouthe wylfully wherfore rede manfully herte thought full vnyte platly deuoydynge ambygnyte sette vpon knyghtly resume force agayne fully consume cruell foon let shet withoute wan hope drede dispeyre euery doute castynge parryll slouthe cowardyse let manhode vtterly despyse drede deth causeth hertes feynt cowardyse atteynt fynally goddes haue hyght thorugh prescyence theyr eternall myght victorye ye shall attayne lyke desyre sayne whan calchas conclusyowne false traytour vnto troye towne grekes hadde thorugh wordes fayre touchynge werre put dispayre herte one caste fulfylle hoolly counsayle though achylle frowarde aye helpe theyr nede gaue force toke hede euerychone redy make ye shall felde haste take trewes passed ye monthes wayne ye felde grekes ordayne troye agayne yssue oute worthy troylus huge route grekes gan alderfirste assayle swerde made firste rayle rede blode thorugh theyr harneyse bryght deth theyr fledde fro syght daye thorugh cruelte caste hym fully auenged vpon deth ector vtterly dare reherseth specyally knyghtes troyan champyowne day hath slayne rydynge vp downe myn auctour guydo lyst endyte saue hym ferther wryte boke yeueth hym suche name manhode knyghtly fame grekes put vnto flyght day tyll drewe nyght morowe dawenynge grekes haue phebus vprysynge yarmed great dylygence agayne troyans stande diffence amonges day rede well hym bare worthy dyomede many troyan thorugh cruelte hath loste lyfe tyll troylus gan se dyomede felde rydynge anone without lettynge spere threwe reste troylus rode smote hym ye breste myghtely nede downe horse smote dyomede albe wounde hadde damage furyously troylus rage ofenuye gan hym abreyde whan downe loue creseyde deceyte trecherye grekes faste gan hye amonge hors myschefe lay drawe hym haste may shelde brosyd affrayde bare hym home dismayde stroke home vnto tent menelay whyle hath hent myghty spere auenge dyomede troylus faste gan hym spede fully auysed vnhorse hym anone troylus firste made stede gone swyfte course towarde menelay anone erthe lay myghtely hyt hym spere shelde plate myght hym nat saue hym mortall wounde kynghtes anone hym founde prese whan hym rent bare hym home owne tent grekes aye stondynge distresse thorugh knyghthode ye hye prowesse troylus whiche hath belayne euery part rode playne tyll vnto tyme agamenowne felde valyd downe many worthy aboute banere shone full shene agayne sonne clere wt knyght hym rydynge enuyrowne sore enchased troye towne woundeth sleeth put flyght hym selfe acquytynge lyke manly knyght without abode amonge troyans fyersly rode worthy kynge great agamenowne spere troylus smette hym downe maugre grekes gayneth socour whan sawe theyr lorde gouernour suche myschefe grounde lyende hente hym vp made hym ascende thorugh theyr manhode stronge stede wyt gan take hede consyderyd wysely thought disioynt troylus brought grekes theyr great pryde tofore swerde myght nat abyde prudently hye discrecyon noble knyght kynge agamenon hadde aye aduertence gouernaunce thorugh prouydence whan sawe grekes gan fayle wexe feble stande batayle lacke stuffe shulde recomforte full prudently made resorte eueryche owne tent hath pryam sent atrewes troye cyte sixe monethes myght counsayle pryamus kynge without abode graunted axynge albe guydo lyste endyte euyll apayde longe respyte theyr mortall foon maner wyse yet graunt ye haue herde deuyse stode strengthe fully rede whiche tyme womanhede creseyde lyst lenger tarye though hir fader therto contrarye vysyte haue syght dyomede come hir kynght pwhich troylus late caught woude tent whan hath hym founde benygnely vpon beddes syde set hir downe selfe tyde platly caste hir owne thought touchynge troylus yt nought lyue hope recure thought wold thynge vnsure purueaunce without store gaue anone without hooly hir herte vpon dyomede lo pyte womanhede mercy eke benygne routhe newly hir olde trouthe nauture lette slyppe asyde rather shulde se abyde man myschefe theyr sake chaunge nat redy make lombarde strete crowne doket poyse good prent set theyr lettre chaunge doth man abyde wynde redy tyde passage aye lyste pace man loste lyste seke grace daunger none counterfete disdayne see calme rockes playne mercyles neuer man ne deyde soughte grace recorde creseyde whiche fynally hath gyuen hir herte dyomede relese smerte prayed hym right glad lyght calleth hym hir owne man hir knyght hym behyghte rather deye euery thynge howe wolde obeye honest hym pleasaunce leuer chaunge varyaunce founde hir lacke pyte syctynge femynynyte nature nat vengeable fayth othe rather mercyable mannes lyfe standynge distresse wyll dresse tell forth translacyon ceryously agamenon durynge trewes tyme pee hym selfe wente vnto achylles besechynge hym rewarde haue knyghthode grekes saue presence nomore withdrawe suffre mortally slawe theyr enmyes pompous elate achylles alway indurate ilyche newe bothe herte thought purpose platly chaungeth nought fully enclyned haue pee asmoche achylles entyernesse affeccyon louynge agamenon vnto hym graunted leste great parcell touchynge requeste saye achylles graunteth hym myrundones full knyghtly men oonly absence grekes make resystence felde agayne towne whiche graunte kynge agamenowne duke nestor thanked hym herte alwaye contynuynge smerte loue fayre polycene ne knewe gayne woundes grene dispeyred languyssheth euer one whan trewes passyd gone vpon adaye morowe full benygne achylles knyghtes dyde assygne felde take agamenon storye maketh mencyon gaue bendes fresshe rede men may knowe theyr manlyhede withholde specyall lyke man deedly mortall tent achylles abode felde hym whan rode oonly dole shulde hym twynne absence werre begynne maugre wyll agayne towne forthe went agamenowne vpon troyans sterne full pryde mette syde manly knyghtes troyanysshe blode whiche furyous wode cruelly grekes oppresse backe fere gan dresse inly felle kene tyll duke athene entrede grekes diffende vpon hym vnwarely wende came myghty troylus lyke wood lyowne stede anone bare hym downe put hym prees tyll mette myrundones slewe daye full many one fet troylus ygone grekes put vtterly flyght thorugh knyghthod tyl drewe nyght fro swerde raunsou myght borowe guydo wryte next morowe full mortall slaughter outher syde amyd felde togydre ryde manly knyghtes wonder sene faughte kynge phylymene helpe oonly pollydamas taken hath worthy kynge thoas gan hym lede towarde troye towne myrundones hym come downe wonder proudely gan sewe thurgh myght thoas reskewe hym delyuer stronge troylus hurtled amonge furyously lyke champyowne caste threwe downe slewe made blede tyll cruelly slewe myghty stede whiche sat yet neuertherles faught fote agayne myrundones hadde caste troylus haue take parys tho gan wake brother aboute hym rode place troylus stode vpon fete hym selfe alone myrundones slewe many one knighthod thorugh theyr manlyhede vnto hym brought another stede amyd foon made hym ascende full knyghtly gan hym selfe diffende set grekes selfe stounde neuer yet better knyght founde felte well foon brother callyd emargaron faught puttynge hym selfe prees slayne ala amonge myrundones deth cruell yre troylus angre newe sette fyre playnely purposeth auenge may swerde began make way parys aye faste rydynge brother vpon hym awaytynge whiche yfere mercyles fynde vpon myrundones force necessyte compelled playnely fle troylus furyous vengeable eke despytous gaue many mortall wounde yet sothe day founde noble knyghtes quyt wonder wele crafte knewe euerydele longynge army rede made theyr sydes blede thorughe mayle theyr plate shene ne myght playnely nat sustene swerde troylus chasyng ouerall albe kepte close wall hole togydre wente nat sonder troylus aye chaseth yonder seuered maugre theyr myght tyll felde many worthy knyght came menelay kynge agamenon vlixes eke cruell thelamon dyomede whiche woundes grene recuryd sayth myn auctor clene troyans sodaynely fall theyr wardes theyr knyghtes tho began fyght renewe euery halfe blody hewe plate bryght newe steyned troye manly haue peyned agayne theyr foon myghty stryfe many greke berafte lyfe moste myghty batayle troylus came gan assayle euery parte many blody wounde knyghthode gan comfoude aye fledde aferde mortall stroke sharpe swerde theyr deedly foo destruccyon contynueth tyll kynge thelamon manhode whan behelde grekes made recure agayne felde gan troyans assayle wonder sore tho began slaughter eche syde tyll troylus newe agayne grekes hathe fyersly ouerlayne myrundones euerychone afore swerde made gone theyr tentes felde sake honde day hath take hondred knyghtes came weye thorugh prowesse sent troye euer one gan enchace myrundones loste theyr place achylles lyenge tent repeyre forwounde rent theyr harneys broke bothe plate mayle nombre fynde fayle hondred knyghtes slayne deed ala founde taas amyd felde thorugh gyrt wt many woude troylus swerde ector secounde wherof achylles whan hadde syght heuy nexte nyght bedde walo wynge fro deuoyde slepe constreynt wo herte wounde kene men fayre polycene wyttynge well dyde payne venged shulde nat attayne wyse vnto desyre thus brent double fyre loue ire made hym shyghe sore cause loue aferde agayne towne sone offencyowne lyste pryamus eccubathe quene offended namely polycene thus stode double weer herte satte hym wonder neer many wonder dyuers fantasye haue louers poynt dye ryght euen fareth wofull man woo rede ne entryked wende deye recure knewe better weye whyle lay throwes whyte lyke guydo playnely lyste endyte storye maketh mencyowne dayes seuen troye towne encrease augment theyr sorowe grekes mette euery morowe thorugh force bothe theyr myght outher parte slayne many knyght whyle lay achylles grekes deth ylyke reckeles loue oonly toke maner hede hole mortally dothe blede playneth wound large hym thought parcell charge moche hath thynge thynke ofte waketh whan shulde wynke thoughtfull aye ymagynatyfe wery owne lyfe tyll daye kynge agamenon seynge deth destruccyon grekes halfe without remedye troye sent enbassatrye trewes certayne dayes space myght therof haue grace lenger tyme platly endure leyser sepulture worthy knyghtes deed aforne felde outher party lorne whiche taas full besely soughte playnely wroughte durynge sege great vyolence shall descryue pacyence phow achylles slewe worthy troylus ectors brother vnknyghtly trayled hym aboute felde hors tayle ca xxxi cruell force mortall yre martys myght alway set fyre wt newe enuye gonne olde hatrede brenynge hert hote glede atwyxe grekes troye cyte whiche lykely nat staunched tyll deth consume mortall darte full many worthy vpon outher parte execute ala fynall fate eche enuyous deedly hate whiche ne myght destyne remewe parchas lyberte eschewe antropos wyll suffre none maystresse guyder therother dethes shyp tyll goth vnto wrake fortune gan tourne hir face bake hye disdayne fro troye cyte storye right soone ye shall se whan trewes hadde take wered gan redy make proude grekes felde gone vpon morowe whan phebus bryght shone armed full shene eueryche deuyse menelay firste mette parys daye storye rede eche smet stede whiche tyme dauz pollydamas vlixes rode sterne paas eche cruell enmyte styffe swerdes gan togydre flee nouther manhode wyte aspere squared byte myghty duke called meneste rode lyne ryght myght se anthenor troyan full pryde sadell caste hym downe asyde furye hatefull tene tho haste came kyng phylemene oonly helpe towne gan assayle kynge agamenowne thorugh knyghthode hardynesse hym hadde brought great distresse outter myschefe confusyon ne hadde oonly kynge thelamon full proudely came hym reskewe sore gan pursewe spere vpon phylemene hors layde hym grene maugre force storye telleth thus hym mortally irous yonge archylogus mortall couts ran vnto brumus one sone pryamus kynge yonge delyuer beste lykynge hym smette great myght fell deed fresshe lusty knyght deth whan troye espye made shoute pyteously gan crye wofull routhe deth complayne tyll noyse gan vtterly attayne troylus erys platly rode lenger abode place felly gan approche swerde sette broche without routhe grekes hatefull blode mercyles hym withstode slewe daye cruell auenture greke none whiche myght endure tofore swerde gan oppresse knyghthode hye prowesse hadde put vtterly flyght ne hadde ben manhode myght myrundones whiche day one assent vpon troylus lay wherof full melancolyus courage manhode famous ne lyste lenger lette attones vpon sette furyously gan amonge ryde smote euen thorugh syde thorugh body thorugh herte swerde thorugh doublet sherte thorugh shelde plate thorugh haberion percyd hath lyke wood lyon slewe day many one maugre fledde euerychone grekes eueryche tent troye went swyftly hors tyll haue take suche murdre grekes make fynally better reskuse oonly deth passyngly confuse grekes myschefe desolate troylus narowe brought chekmate coude better remedye hydously wayle crye deth forwounded grysely chere achylles whan gan firste dredefull noyse wofull sowne caused refleccyowne eyre agayne coude knowe rochys harde kauernys lowe lyke one worde spoke two men wont called ecco confuse lamentacyowne grekes syde whiche deedly sowne pyteously achylles ronne lay agayne hote sonne mortall woundes yeldynge vp breth roumble swowhe resownyng deth suche noyse grekes made ment achylles dyde enquere cause theyr clamour tolde hym lacke socour grekes eche centorye troylus slayne victorye goth fynally troye towne euermore conclusyowne many greke lay slayne tent gapynge vpwarde blode yspent thorugh constreynt woudes smerte whyle achylles gan aduerte full sodaynely came hym man whiche tale euen thus began ala quod may ye sustene se men hereupon grene afore youre face slayne lye dede lyste nat one take hede stonde stylle pensyfe tent vpon poynt selfe shent hasty houre ye abyde fyfty thousande knyghtes besyde redy armed plate mayle caste playnely attones sayle doute vnarmed ye stonde ye knyghthode manly take honde resyste selfe place lyke man mete face whiche anone cruell mode achylles lyke wode armed hym fomynge bore farewell loue sette store hasty hete yre kene forgat fayre polycene hir beaute yt whylom made hym smert rage vp anone sterte toke stede lyon wroth agayne troyans felde goth lyke wolfe hunger gnawe right gan agayne foon drawe rode without excepcyowne woundeth sleeth kylleth bereth downe lytell throwe troye gan swerde knowe whiche infecte newe theyr blode none yet yt hym withstode mortally gan aboute hym layne deed bodyes enlonge playne tyll casuelly troylus gan espye achylles caste eye gan hors spore constrayne rode hym myght payne achylles hym ware also smette stede made hym go towarde troylus selfe tyde full course togydre ryde full lyne ryght theyr speres sharpe whette suche myght haue togydre mette hye disdayne sayne grounde felle bothe twayne achylles caught suche wounde body depe profounde longe lay myn auctor sayth certayne helthe restored agayne troylus eke thorugh plate mayle wryte guydo hadde wounde small whiche vnto hym dyde greuaunce thus daye contynuaunce dayes sixe suynge proude grekes mette cruelly amyd felde troye towne great damage confusyowne outher party playnely nay many worthy slayne day day theyr rancour hertely hoote enuye albe guydo doth nat specefye none theyr name playnely boke ye shall fynde ye lyste loke al whyle sodeyn thyge pensyfe tryste pryam ye kynge achylles tourned hath clene herte away fro yonge polycene chaunge sodayne newe thought behestes nat trewe deceyte doubylnesse fraude falsly newe fangylnesse sleyghty treason vncouert gyle rage loue lasteth whyle vtterly founde beheste lyke wynde man may areste fareth worde discordaunt fro dede whiche wyse man take shall hede lette passe reckeles albe achylles whylom caught within loues snare hym lyste nat nowe one tospare hye rancour lady offende nat lyke troye wende eccuba nouther polycene pwherfore pryam spake vnto quene angre gan hir abreyde hir truste entyerly leyde achylles falsly mene wherfore full tryste polycene enclyned hir eyen clere counsayle hir moder dere haue weddyd achylles fyne oonly shulde haue pee wene grekes troye towne false conclusyowne fyne trouthe ysene whan achylles woundes grene fully curyd certayne day gan compasse euer may ymagyne enuyous herte vengyd woundes smerte vpon troylus stacke aye mynde auauntage myght hym fynde hym bare passyngly hatrede herte brennynge glede whiche day nyght may degre fully queynt tyll auengyd hoote rancour gan hym gnawe auysed platly shalbe slawe hondes whan falle day hym gan calle myrundones knyghtes euerychone vpon morowe whan grekes gone tofore towne stele armed bryght agayne troyans purpose fyght come proudely felde opposyt many ryche shelde newely depeynt coloures fresshe fyne vpon whiche full bryght gan shyne firy tytan golde tressyd spere vpryste bemysclere whan felle enuyous achylles knyghtes called myrundones vpon troylus gan hym complayne besechynge theyr payne agayne troylus felde day catche hym myschefe may besely theyr dyllygence hym haue theyr full aduertence one assent ryde thynge sette asyde nought ellys take hede saufe fynally agayne hym procede myght catche hym trappe within selfe troylous clappe enclose sette hym rounde aboute wyse go nat oute whan beset amonge alle nat slee hym euer falle thorugh theyr myght maly hym coserue tyll hym selfe come make hym sterue swerde none wyght loo manhode preyse ryght vengeaunce deth rancoure pryde compassyd treason knyghthode layde asyde worthynesse enuye slawe falshede lofte trauthe backe ydrawe ala armes shulde falle trecherye bytter galle shulde worlde many knyght befoude trauthe ordre bounde ala ala achylles conspyred hath myrundones dethe one worthyest wyght euer beste knyght ala wo herte fele dede sake storye whan rede whan fortune hath thynge ordeyned though euer wayled compleyned gayne remedye though men galen aye crye touchynge matere wryte forth lyke ye shall myrundones haue theyr lorde behyght theyr power theyr full myght fulfyll comaundement felde grekes went troylus firste opposyte knyghthode hathe great delyte without abode manly mete ybrent feruent hete hardynesse hye courage worthynesse vasselage hym ne lyste lenger abyde folke began ryde amonge grekes folke hye renowne wt swerde woudeth bereth downe sleeth kylleth vpon euery halue mortally may salue theyr sorys sounde deth rode yeldynge vp breth furyously gan enchace made lese lytell space theyr londe echone afore hym flee troylus swerde suche crueltee maugre felde hath wonne tyme whan bryght sonne hye southe mydday marke shoone euen houre whan drewe noone whan myrundones gadred one compasse wyse rounde aboute hym gone furyously one entencyowne made cercle aboute hym enuyrowne whan sawe hym helpe desolate herte nat disconsolate vpon syde thorugh manlyhede lyke lyon toke hede thorugh famous knyghtly excellence tygre stondeth diffence manfully gan encoumbre gan lesse discrease theyr noumbre maymeth woundeth dethe made yelde vp brethe layde erth lowe made ouerthrowe swerde theyr blode wete great myschefe vnder hors fete vpon stede sturdy wall worthy knyght man marcyall playeth pley amonge myrundones hym selfe god wot alone helpeles tho ala myght force auayle whan thre thousande knyghtes hym assayle euery parte bothe lengthe brede cowardly firste slewe stede theyr sperys sharpe quare grounde whiche ala stante grounde without reskus refute socoure day chyualrye floure welawaye haue hym beset hede smote basenet brake harneys hym assayle seuere stele myghty stronge mayle disarmed bothe necke hede ala whyle wyght toke none hede knyghtes longynge towne yet alway troyan champyowne knyghtly wyse naked hym selfe diffendeth tyll achylles ala came rydynge furyous wode whan sawe troylus stode longe fyghtynge awaped amate folke alone desolate sole hym selfe myschefe pyteously achylles wonder cruelly behynde vnwarely toke hede swerde smyteth hede caste forthe cruell cursyd herte thought platly shulde hym nat asterte shewe malys wolfe vnmercyable full vnknyghtly vengeable vpon body lay deed colde ala euer shulde knyght tolde wryte rehersyd foule dede boke ala men shall rede knyght storye horryble vnto erys passyngly odyble achylles cruelte ala deed corp toke taas vengeably bonde fynde tayle hors behynde hatefully euery wyght behelde drewe hym selfe endelonge felde thorugh renges wardes alle ala euer shulde falle knyght herte cruell hatrede despytous fell drawe man dede thou omer shame rede astoned holdest thy self wyse achylles sette suche pryse thy bokes chyualrye aboue echone doest hym magnefye sleyghty full fraude gyuest thou hym hye pryse laude certys omer thyne excellence rethoryke eloquence thy lusty songes thy dytees smerte thy hony mouthe doth sugre flete yet one thynge thou greatly arte blame causeles gyue hym suche name tytle tryumphe glorye passyngly put hym memorye thy bokes saye wryte thurgh knyghthod slewe ectorys two firste hym lyke vnto none troylus yt owne brother thou arte meued affeccyon whiche thou haste grekes nacyon preyse hym thou canste endyte thou shuldest aye fauour wryte trouthe playnely indifferent saye sothe clerely entent whan slewe ector felde afore disarmed shelde besy eke spoylynge kynge hadde beware comynge hadde hym quyt thorugh chyualrye false deseyt trecherye ne hadde lyghtly hym gone troylus also naked alone amyd thre thousande closyd beshet pwhan achylles hath hede smet backe full cruell herte whan nothynge treason dyde aduerte pwas dede manly knyght slee man forweryed fyght faynt trauayle longe daye amonge many stondynge bay kynges sone hye borne naked hede armure torne euen deth selfe poynt disauauntage playnely ioynt lyfe standynge wrake pwhan achylles came falsely bake assaylynge hym whan halfe dede lyke cowarde smote hede tofore hurte wounded sore pwherfore omer preyse hym late nat pryse thy ryall boke difface page duplicate page duplicate haste renowne arrace name whan neuen veryly vp vnto heuen semeth infecte eyre sowne therof foule vufayre hadde aduertence outher eye prouydence vnto knyghthode worthynesse outher manhode gentyllesse renowne owne name reporte knyghtly fame wyse haue taken hede hadde neuer done foule dede vengeably haue ydrawe kynges sone slawe namely hym gode knyght whiche tyme loke ryght passed achylles dare well expresse bothe manhode gentyllesse dede ala deth whan pollydamas parys eke dyde firste espye fared sothe wolde dye specyally face dede fade parys ala suche sorowe made constreynt dedely wo whan sawe troylus ago shall neuer alyue hym se suche sorowe also troyan dauz enee hym hath made many another mo attones togydre go deed corp recure may grekes werre felle day theyr laboure vtterly vayne wyse corp gette agayne tyll menon noble worthy kynge whiche loued troylus ouer thynge caughte suche routhe affeccyon haste fearser lyon deth caste hym wreke firste ire thus gan speke achylles hye treasowne thou traytoure thou scorpyowne thou serpent full trecherye whiche dishonour chyualrye thorugh false engyne haste day yslawe one beste hadde felawe whan worlde lyue ala ala may right descryue thy venym hydde thy malyce vntrouthe without pyte vnknyghtly routhe drawe knyght gentyll gode kynges sone worthy blode thorugh felde thy hros tayle behynde euer shalbe mynde cruell dede vngentyllesse yt worde menon gan hym dresse towarde achylles without areste spere smet hym breste enuyously great hatrede vnneth kepte hym stede menon pulled aswerde caste hym manly mete hym berde rode hym fully deuoyde drede suche wounde gaue hym hede maugre hym many mannes syghte erthe made hym lyghte pryde mortall traunce wounde felte suche greuaunce dethe lay huge whyle swowne space halfe myle tyll myrundones assembled one great labour hente hym vp anone full deedly pale gan blede sette hym stede laste herte caught agayne smet hors hate hye disdayne towarde menon fast gan hym hye whan comynge gan espye full lyke knyght lyste nat abyde hyt hors sharpely syde mette achylles proudely playne theyr swerdes togydre layne gan hurtle horsbacke yfere herte enuyous despytous chere kynge menon auauntage achylles wode rage poynt abrought hym confusyowne tyll wardes newe come downe outher parte bothe yonder whiche sodaynely seuered sonder storye telleth playnely began slaughter many manly man nouther party felde ne wolde leue pryde tyll drewe eue phebus gan asswage hete gan bathe wawes wete bryght bemys occyan fro felde home goth euery man theyr lodgynge seuen dayes faughte yfere made delayes full mortall cruell aduenture whyle achylles besy cure woundes grene sore sounde hath newe treson founde vengyd vpon kynge menon wytte set therupon cruell enuyous achylles charged hath myrundones worthy menon amonge enbrace hym founde opportune place theyr myght theyr besy thought theyr hondes escape nought tyll hym selfe auengyd hym befell menon se nexte morowe lyke manly knyght agayne grekes armed fyght troye syde wonte auenture day fylle achylles menon mette eche gan sette horse backe full great enuye longe theyr melancolye myn auctor wryt togydre fyght eche made force lyght whan menon stode vpon grounde myrundones wente abounte hym rounde charged fyerse achylle whan allas without goddes wylle dysseuered knyghtes alle myschefe vpon hym falle destytute alone helples suche poynt slewe hym achylles storye lyke founde menon firste gaue hym suche woude tofore deth felle stryfe dispeyred playnely lyfe achylles false treson take hede omer deme thy reson false fraude sleyghty gyle treson caste afore many wyle achylles iuge ryght euer slewe worthy knyght prodycyon recorde take kynge menon tytyle laude ala entryked fraude falla thou omer mayste coloure though thou paynte gold asoure thy wrytynge venym nat enclose thorne hyd vnder rose whose malys aye dareth rote though floure aboue fayre sote men fraude vnder may nat se treson ye gette wyll tell grekes day meneste kynge menelay dyomede thelamonyus troyans passynge despytous cruelly theyr wardes alle theyr myschefe vpon falle made flee home vnto towne whylom troylus chapyowne dede ala hath forsake haue dede body take day great diffyculte dolefully cyte haue brought cryeng oft ala deth suche woo trowe man lyue whiche coude right halfdele descryue theyr pyteous wo lamentacyowne certeyse nat boy suche renowne drery wordes wepe crye complaynynge phylosophye thorugh boke accusynge aye fortune selde nought one contune full transmutacyowne stace thebe make boste sowne drerynesse wryte nouther deth festes funerall makynge sorowe aduersyte let thy wepynge thou nyobe py e suster also mellenger custome haue fle fer fro yere yere brother complayne thou weptest thyn eyen twayne edippus kynge thebe cyte thou wofull myrre calixtone well rage bemene dydo eke cartage quene lette dole contrycyon phyllys eke thy demophon ecto eke newe dost begynne crye wayle also thou corynne whylom great affray deth oonly thy popyngay boke telleth v duyde let woo layde asyde make comparysowne vnto woo troye towne deth oonly worthy knyght loue euery maner wyght hye lowe olde yonge age falle newe suche rage coude theyr wo none ende whose salte terys wyll theyr eyen shende pyteous lamentacyowne euery strete thorugh towne ala coude theyr sorowes telle trowe certeys pluto depe helle tourment paynes kene nouther proserpyna quene nouther wery woode tycyus ixyon hungry tantalus ne coude nat theyr bytter payne furyously wepe complayne troyans troylus thy sake suche sorowe make wepe kynge pryamus wepeth nowe face full pyteous maketh sorowe eccuba quene pwho wepeth nowe fayre polycene wepeth nowe parys eleyne nowe wepe vnto terys reyne troyans dedely swolle chere neded wepers hadde ynough theyr owne store ala nowe euermore helpe sole comforte destytute shall nowe refute nowe ector also dephebus troylus eke vertuous dede ala shall theyr socoure sustene werre theyr cyte conclusyon deth fully destruccyon theyr toures theyr walles stronge mater shulde playne longe vayleth nat alway morne wherfore wyll agayne retorne mater telle kynge grekes hath without tariynge trewes pea ysent certayne tyme great auysement whiche graunted agamenowne wha anone repeyred towne phowe parys slewe achylles temple appollo anthylogus duke nestor ygraue day day haue lyke custome festes funerall rytis cerymonyall bothe dewe obseruaunce seruyse done contynuaunce theyr temple lyke guyse whiche longe deuyse tedyus eke dwelle purpose ceryously telle howe eccuba endyte hir caste fully achylles quyte tyrannye sothely may vnto hir calleth day alysaunder full secrete wyse vnto hym shall deuyse wepynge eyen full heuy chere sayde euen thus lyke ye shall parys quod ala saufe goddes wylle thou knowest well fyerse achylle sone hath slayne nye echone none lefte thy selfe alone hath made ala gayne full cowardly child barayne bothe ector troylus eke therto whiche euery trouble wo fully comforte plesaunce solace wherfore caste playnely compace engyne deth ordayne lyke treason dyde payne trayterously swerde smyte right thynke treason hym quyte sytrynge right equyte sythe thou wotest platly hath sette herte loue clene oonly doughter yonge polycene fyne oonly haue hir wyue whiche caste hym sende blyue come treate matere temple appollo temple moste chefe cyte whiche tyme wyll thou thy selfe armed full pryuelye certayne knyghtes thy companye armed also agayne daye wyse scape nat away handes dede haue sayde therfore take good hede vnto thynge herte preye fro poynt poynt byddynge obeye assenteth hole herte behotynge hir shulde nat asterte hym toke twenty mo manly men well durste temple full good aduys yhyd byddynge parys whyle eccuba couert hir entent hir messager achylles hath sent ye haue herde conclusyowne come haste vnto troye towne effect hir message oonly treate maryage haste cometh hir sonde coude thynge vnders onde hir treason hyd playnely aduerte hote marked herte oues bronde firy glede oflyfe deth toke hede sette asyde wytte reason caste afore good discrecyon lokynge full prudent sothe loue blent troye whan shulde gone lyke fareth louers euerychone whan haue caught herte fantasye peryll though shulde dye haue myght power warre tyll vnwarely trapped snare theyr maladye furyous thus achylles anthylogus nestor sone haue way nome towarde towne togydre come temple ye haue herde telle parys tho lyste lenger dwelle vnwarely knyghtes alle achylles myschefe falle eueryche swerde full bryght bokes say nyght whan deth longe afore desyred eccuba parys conspyred achylles mortall caas amonge naked hent swerde selfe steuen lyke knyght slewe seuen force maugre theyr myght whan parys therof hadde syght thre dartes raughte kene square sodaynely ware full secretely hyd vnder shade markynge hym noyse made caste hym euen euer hede shafte thorugh body ran therwith knyghtes nat fewe sharpe swerdes gan vpon hym hewe lefte hym nat tyll lay grounde full pale deed many mortall wounde rightfully reason syt thus fraude falshed quyt achylles hye treason deth deth skylfully guerdon egall mede without fable mercyles vengeable thylke day guydo wryteth thus achylles anthylogus parys temple yslawe afterwarde body drawe achylle fro holy boundes cruelly throwen vnto houndes deuoured brode strete canell rennynge wawes wete without pyte maner routhe lo ende falshede vntrouthe lo fyne suche trecherye false deceyt compassyd enuye lo knotte conclusyon god quyt aye slaughtre treason lo guerdon fynall mede delyte falshede euery thynge platly sayne lyke guerdon doth attayne ye may se achylles whiche nyght temple le lyfe aye customable fraude treason vengeable befell requeste eleyne bodyes ylke tweyne conserued hungry rage beste foule gredy ramage yet lay amyddes cyte full openly men myght se great gladnesse towne tyme agamenowne kynge pryam sent massagerys haue lysence fette home berys graunt haue corsys take grekes suche sorowe make pyte routhe eueryche spake thus vnto fere farewell truste achylles dede farewell hope hoolly spede farewell ioye chefe diffence hadde manhode great excellence farewell ala soueraygne assuraunce farewell knyghthod suffisaunce nowe ala vnlykely shall euer wynne gette cyte v ala frowarde fortune myght nat contune alway wo payne endure made haue ryche sepulture achylles stone precyous another anthylogus shulde lenger dwelle ceryously rytes telle theyr buriynge wo make theyr wepynge theyr clothes blake loure theyr hode go mylke blode dolefull herte fyre shete caste gomys swete amyd great flaumbe funerall playes called pallestrall wrastlynge wake vayne vndertake telle wherfore lette fully purpose lyke ye shall se resorte conclusyon telle great agamenon lordes haste hath sent whan assembled tent full prudently kynge manly man great aduyse thus tale began syres quod fortune varyaunce hir chere frowarde double coutenauce sodayne tourne hir false vysage hertes hath put suche arage murdre god man odyble achylles cruell deth horryble compassynge eccuba quene semeth shalbe sene manhode hertes knyghtly force aduersyte endure vertue suffraunce tyll deth ye take may vengaunce manly quyte outragyous offence whan tyme cometh make recompence syth ye manly prudent wolde firste se playne entent mater wyse hereupon aduyse one assente voyce comune ye wyll werre forth contune sege ygonne vpon towne tyll brought destruccyowne grece resorte agayne cause oonly achylles slayne whylom stronge chapyowne diffence proteccyowne fynally dede hereupon lette se rede saye openly lenger tarye anone gonne varye grutche castynge fro stondynge doute beste sayde tother syde lyfe deth wolde ende abyde wytte rude theyr partye gonne conclude wolde home agayne retourne sayde wyll soiourne styll sege happe happe may thus treate longe day euery man lyke oppynyon tyll laste conclusyon accorded fully one fro sege neuer gone vnto tyme haue towne thorugh theyr knyghthode full possessyon theyr fce wyll spylle saue achylles buryed ygraue truste euery worthy knyght fynally goddes haue behyght haste shall towne possede hope fully deuoyde drede vndispeyred theyr oppynyon anone ayax thelamon worthy knyght famous hande amonge tho grekes lande sayde euen thus playnely sentence syres quod presence counsayle platly rede standeth achylles dede sone haste sende hyder come se ende sege helpe v nede pwhiche nowe abyt kynge lycomede bysayel named pirrus hym call neptolonyus right lusty fresshe lyklynesse able attayne great worthynesse reporte fame kouthe drawe hym armes youthe sothfastly bokes lye haue redde herde prophecye fynally troye cyte without hym shall neuer wonne thus bokes saye olde memorye grekes shall haue victorye tyll come sone achylles wherfore haste nat reckeles sende hym done anone comende counsayle euerychone rede fully assente aduyse full prudently sente haste embassyat wyse kynge full famous estat mene prudent noble menelay forth goth selfe day iourney gan hym faste spede tyll came vnto lycomede olde kynge ye haue herde telle wherfore tyme wyll leue hym dwelle grekes mene whyle directe agayne style phowe parys thelamon ayax slewe eche felde capitulo xxxiij tyme yere whan shene sonne crabbe course yronne hyest ascencyon whiche called somer stacyon whan vertue euery roote drawen vp bawme soote crop fresshe floure lusty hewe coloure tyll phebus chare descencyon crabbe towarde lyon holdeth course firmament mene whan retrogradyent dryeth vp moysture wete herbe floure feruent hete veer afore hym made grene whyte tourneth bemys shene bothe sede grayne decoccyon naturelly digestyon firste rawe fruytes floures watery eke plente humoures dryeth vp rypeth fulle feruence men may pulle eche kynde season fro yere yere reuolucyon theyr braunches fresshely sprede whan cheryes powbly rede firste iune seweth may whan hoote mery somers day dwery lyke geaunt longe tyme grekes stoute stronge rancour brent theyr enuyous hete haue shapen theyr foon mete bryght armed felde go troye towne also theyr wardes ordeyned euerychone felde haue take mete theyr foon gan assemble vpon outher syde thelamon foly pryde day hym rede hadde deth drede disarmed batayle arest mayle plate bare vpon brest foly surquedous outrage bare hede bare eke vysage bare also without basenet naked eke vyser palet herode day thynge aferde hauynge wepen naked swerde wylfully lefte home shelde spere whan toke felde full lyke knyght syttynge stede hym foloweth dyomede lyke mar hym selfe aboute hym meyne faste came duke meneste kynge vlyxes agamenon pryamus wt troye towne toke eke felde wt full heuy chere bothe ferefull great dispeyre inly full drede yssue ector dede pworthy troylus also dephebus hym selfe demyd playnely thus feblyd greatly myght theyr deth grekes fyght goth hap happe may parys eke full knyghtly array kynge phylymene pollydamas pworthy esdre eneas one assent seye day knyghtly lyue deye theyr diffence vtterly iuparte goddes lyste felde departe proudely firste grek gan perce parys tho perce fyll asyde sonne shene archery arrowes square kene grekes gan ondre disseuere felde myght nat perseuer oonly shot stronge archery perce londe arbalasterys whiche made fle right nede tyme proude dyomede whan grekes sawe sodayne flyght releue lyke manly knyght come vpon felly tene firste sette phylyment worthy kynge came troye syde whiche agayne gan hym ryde dyomede hath lytell wonne swerdes styffe togydre ronne beholde noble syght eche quyte hym lyke knyght togydre ran horse backe man coude nouther se lacke euer one troyans felle vpon grekes ne myght dwelle kepe theyr londe made blede maugre force dyomede slaughter hydous stronge thorugh felde wofull noyse ronge mortall crye wounded folke lay slayne soyel endelonge way tyll meneste syttynge stede worthy duke gan take hede myschefe grekes beset hent anone spere sharpe whet smytynge hors felly syde thorugh renges knyghtly gan ryde stynt nat furyous tyll mette pollydamas troyan knyght manly man vnwarely hym ran hytte hym many mannes syght erthe made hym lyght swerde grounde whan lay hadde hym slayne sylfe day rage cruell tene ne hadde oonly kynge phylymene hym reskewed auenture whiche frendely hym dyde cure maugre myght menestee handes went free bathyd spreynt blode whyle ayax proudely rode surquedy wylfulnesse foly rage foule hardynesse nakyd body hede euerydele amyd foon armed bryght stele troyans suche slanghter made lay dede bothe sonne shade thorugh felde thelamon amonge rode woodder lyon troyan none myght hym tho wtstonde whyle helde blody swerde honde wonder nakyd rode without wounde longe abode guydo maketh rehersayle wryteth eke great meruayle vnslayne myght contune whan thynge shapen fortune myght befalle euer thynge wele wo ioye aduersyte whan one shall dye whan shall escape ala alder firste iape brynge aman vnwarely myschaunce whan beste weneth haue assuraunce lady transmutacyon lyke fyll worthy thelamon day whiche foly pryde amonge foon gan fer ryde ylyche fresshe right began slewe perce many manly man hym selfe toke maner hede knyghtly herte voyde drede tyll parys sawe great hardynesse howe knyghtes dyde oppresse enchasynge mortally narowe without abode anone toke arowe entoxycat sharpe venymous ire fell despytous shot hym selfe tyde sayth guydo smet hym thorugh syde hurte eye felte well muste deye whan sawe none remedye forth rode supprysed enuye thorugh prees swerde ay honde tyme parys fonde vnto hym pale chere sayde thus anone ye shall parys quod mortall wounde thyne arrowe sharpe square ygrounde hath fynally lyfe put dispeyre neuer grece haue repeyre right shall short conclusyowne awaye shape troye towne thy lyfe thou entre shalt herte venym byt sore gayne none deth pbut yet tofore yelde vp breth truste right well may socoure thou shalt firste predecessoure go afore depe downe helle pluto eternally dwelle right necessarye tyme set whiche may nat tarye trouthe morgage depose haste shall make deuose atwyxe quene eleyne twynne asondre eke false theyne whiche lynked coloure wedlocke hath longe shet vnder locke oonly fraude false engyne also pbut nowe knotte shalbe broke two right hande trouthe darayne thorugh cause oonly twayne werre many worthy knyght lyfe hath loste many another wyght outher syde bothe sake shall ende make loue foule auoutrye fynally parys thou shalt dye handes thy chaunce yt worde swerde gan enhauce aboue hede smote hym face fyll deed selfe place hede partyd hath twayne right forth sayne ayax ala mortall wounde fyll deed also gruflynge vnto grounde full pyteously troye haue parys take vp weye bore hym home theyr cytee dyomede duke menestee many greke rydynge enuyrowne sewed chase euen towne cause tytan gan lowe downe arke dayes bowe west vnder rowes rede esperus gan lyght shede say drewe nyght grekes repeyred anone ryght eueryche lodgynge place take theyr reste nyghtes space saue rede agamenowne grekes made faste towne sette theyr tentes papyllyons habytacles newe mansyons pryde faste wall troye dispeyred ouerall refute coude grekes lette assent faste theyr gate shette nyght walles wake ouer suche wo make thorugh cyte parys dede fynally rede wepe crye sorowe euer one sone pryam gone fortune ala hath appeyred theyr lyfe dispeyred hope good welfare perpetuelly lyue care vnto deth fast bye maner remedye vpon syde refute none kepe close within wall se pyteous thynge suche wo maketh kynge parys deth deedly smerte hym thought platly sorowfull herte recurles wolde ryue tweyne terys gan styll reyne wolde sorowe deye quene ala shall seye eccuba owne moder dere cryeth wepeth wofull chere polycene wo begon susterne also euerychone haue theyr heer theyr clothes torne hadde theyr owne deth ysworne drery woo pyteous peyne forby fayre quene eleyne wayleth cryeth deedly hir eyen whiche whylom clere dyrked dolefull terys smerte corp sodaynely sterte clyppyd hir armes twayne pyteously enbrace restrayne lyke wolde hym dye anone styll lay dombe stone marbyll colde hir lymes craumpysshynge redy towarde hir buriynge tyll men force corp hir hent hir heer chekes rent fallen rage chaunged ala hir vysage hir natyfe coloure hir rody hewe whylom fresshe rose newe lyke vnto asshes colde hir handes aye togydre folde hir selfe smote hir pale face euer amonge corp dyde embrace hir swownes fyll grounde twenty tymes wept full wounde wo wapyd amate comforte ala disconsolate herte beynge inly desirous thorugh hir rage passynge furyous dye attones hir owne knyght towarde deth enclosyd hir syght lyst lyue trowe neuer man woman sawe falle suche distresse suche disioynt deedly heuynesse wo pyteously yraue nat cleopatre goynge hir graue wofull tesbe fro kaue sterte whan hir selfe smote vnto herte faythfull trewe orestylle whan sawe hir lorde agayne hir wylle marcus prolancus vnto shyppe gone loue fyll downe deed anone sorowe trewe iulia feruence faythfull porcia whiche one fyll deed sodaynely sawe blode speynt cruelly hir lordes dredefull grauement porcia trewe hir entent whan hir lorde brutus loste lyfe bycause myght haue knyfe colys rede slewe hir selfe ala nat also selfe caas arthemysya quene tarse londe mansalus graue whan fonde hir owne knyght whose bone smale full wofully chere right pale poudre made dranke euery morowe wo furyous sorowe echone yet may nat atteyne vnto sorowe quene eleyne fynally wyll hir selfe parys sake loued hym wyll nat lyue day wreke playnely may vpon hir lyfe rather disseuere thus wo aye doth perseuere hir herte parys sat depe ala sayth woman nat douteles haue nature though wo endure yet feyne salte terys fynde plente ynough theyr owne kynde sorowles morne compleyne saye nat quene eleyne wo wounded herte fro deth wende nat asterte dethes darte hir herte made ryue yet rose agayne fro deth lyue oonly grace hir felle rage euery wo processe muste aswage ouer gone wasted myracle eche venym made tryacle euery wo hath remedye though eleyne fayne wolde dye hir kynde ne wolde assent yet therto sodaynely slee hir selfe wo woman man shulde hir wyte lyste hir wo endyte lyste vnto tedyous hir paynes furyous hir cruell wo lamentacyon whiche wolde meue compassyon sothe wryte euerydele herte though made stele kynge pryam quene also hadde suche couthe hir pyteous wo se hir wepe complayne hir felte asmoche payne dyde almost parys hereof pryam deuys rage mortall wo amyd temple sacryd iuno ordayned hath full besy cure corp ryche sepulture haste therin made shette sothnesse shulde lette totelle rytes gyse made theyr paynym wyse costes buriynge shulde longe tariynge ceryously thereon abyde wherfore nowe lette ouerslyde theyr paynym rytys supersticyous phow pantasyllya quene amazone came socoure kynge pryamus troye howe pirrus achylles sone slewe hir capitulo xxxiiij tell wyll kynge pryamus comauded hath myschefe nede thorugh troye towne oonly drede shytte theyr gate strongly may therupon bothe nyght day kepe watche shortly troye disconsolate theyr olde ioye refute wepe sorowe make ne durste vndertake agayne grekes felde gon tyll day kynge agamenon messager good auysement pryamus troye hath sent requerynge hym manhode lyke knyght yssue grekes fyght wonte chyual ye kynge pryam axynge gan denye shortly sayde hym sent ne wolde assignemenet nat one passe gate towne owne fre eleccyowne whan euer hym lyste without compellynge yet sothe cause tariynge pwas hardy quene femynye towarde torye faste gan hir hye hir lande lytell regyon whiche bokes make mencyon syght firmament plage oryent called reygne amazonys whiche custome vse oonly woman therin shall abyde wonte armed ryde haue armes great experyence theyr laboure theyr dylygence fynally haue excercyse fro day day martes hye seruyse ouer theyr custome vsaunce day made remembraunce man shall nyghe nere thre monethes yere say iune apryll may woman haue custome aye vnto ile lytell besyde men selfe abyde fro yere yere togydre euerychone vnto men theyr lande gone abyde regyon tyll tyme cometh concepcyon without tariynge lenger whyle anone home vnto theyr yle repeyre countre vnto tyme delyuered faste childe borne lacke kepynge nat lorne fostryd tyll thre yere agone amonge woman right anone ile besyde adiacent vnto men childe haste sent kynde masculyne falle femynyne woman abyde stylle shall tyll actes mercyall full well experte eke knowe handle spere drawe bowe lyke statute regyon whiche bokes make mencyon sette bytwene ewrope asya lande pantasyllya whylom lady gouernesse full renowmed strengthe hardynesse thorugh world length brede yet sothe speke womanhede hir myght hadde huge pryse bothe vertuous wyse wonder discrete hadde honest name nat withstondynge excellence fame hir renowne armes glorye conquest hye victorye moste surmuntynge drede woman rede sothely yet bokes bere wytnesse womanhede gentyllesse kepte hir nothynge hir asterte whiche loued hir hole herte pworthy ector hir myght oonly noble knyght hir ioye worldly plesaunce hir hertely ease soueraygne suffysaunce sothe wake wynke euer one vpon hym thynke fayth without slouthe vnto hym bonde trouthe confederat olde affeccyowne whan herde troye towne besegyd grekes felle hardy quene lyste lenger dwelle hasteth hir faste euer may towarde troye full good array wrothy woman hir lande full well experte preuyd theyr honde well horsyd eke armed rychely fynde hir company thousande maydens rydynge hir syde worthy quene durste well abyde hir brought stele armed bryght loue ector hir owne trewe knyght hir way faste gan hir spede helpe hym se nede thynge coude hir delyte towarde hym faythfully hir quyte hir luste hertes ioye whan come troye herde telle relacyowne dede worthy renowne louynge trewe anone gan chaunge chere hewe pyteously wepe crye fared sothe wolde dye wo hertely heuynesse thought wold thurgh hir worthynesse auenge deth platly may grekes vpon day prayeth pryam wt great affeccyowne open gate towne go grekes fyght may knowe experte ryght woman great worthynesse quene famous hardynesse kynge hopynge beste without abode graunted hir requeste next morowe wha pheb shone ful shene tofore goth phylymene noble kynge paffagonye hym knyghtes manye folowed worthy eneas troyan eke dauz pollydamas quene pantasyllya gate called dardanyca towarde grekes proudely yssued oute hir woman rydynge hir aboute whiche anone whan grekes dyde espye felde gan faste hye firste worthy meneste pantasyllya whan dyde se spore made stede gone spere rode hir anone quene astoned neuer adele kaught spere squaryd wele rounde shafte hede well grounde coupe smet hy downe groude maugre hym reuyd hym stede haste came dyomede cruelly quene ryde faste tother syde rode eke hym plate bryght shene mette theyr sperys kene hytte felle dyomede myght manlyhede hym made adell lese myght tho nat chese despyte men echone hath shelde hym berafte anone delyuereth proudely rode mayde vpon hir abode lyke tygre gredynesse lyke soth lyonesse dayeshe fared rydynge vp downe amonge grekes tyll thelamowne gan beholde slaughter made hye despyte rancourouer lade myght ire nat sustene gan reyne hors fall vpon quene whan comynge dyd espye fyll hym hir melancolye mortally maugre knyghtes grounde made hym fall grekes put great disray euer rode ylke day myght afore hir nat sustene thorugh helpe kyng phylymene myn auctor recordeth boke amyd felde thelamon toke sent hym forth thorugh hir hye renowne prysoner towarde troye towne tyll vnto reskus came cruell dyomede cruelly gan hym lede fyll vn warely huge route knyghtes rydynge hym aboute theyr hand maugre al theyr myght hym delyuereth lyke manly knyght whiche tyme hardy quene anone hir woman aboute hir euerychone grekes hath afore hir playne wryt guydo mortally belayne made necessyte felde hir swerde fle veryly incredyble leue maner impossyble se woman grekes enchace whiche myght nat abyde afore theyr face felde wyse stonde dryue selfe stronde downe clyffe salte see slewe huge great plente fynally hadde destroyed euer vtterly accloyed ne hadde dyomede stonde diffence knyghthode made resystence day party grekes stode sturdy wall alone theyr helpe chefe socoure worshyp honoure pantasyllya made memorye repeyred conquest victorye hir woman troye towne vpon houre phebus goynge downe syde hardy quene armed stele rode kynge phylymene pryam hath great reuerence knyghtly receyued dyde dylygence refresshe euery maner thynge myght vnto theyr lykynge theyr hertes coude best deuyse full goodly wyse thanked hath noble hardy quene hir goodnesse hir lyst sene helpe hym great nede offrede hir guydo rede hath treasour rychesse hopynge fully thorugh hir worthynesse vpon grekes auenged kepe hym cyte maugre grekes whiche say nay rede day day stynte nat proudely assayle agayne whose swerde myght nat auayle mortally made theyr sydes blede tyll menelay frokynge lycomede repeyred neptolonyus whiche bokes called eke pirrus whylom sone cruell achylles se full huge prees grekes goynge enuyron successyon borne heyre achylles receyued myrundones great honour great solempnyte glad theyr yonge lorde se echone made affyaunce eke sworne bonde assuraunce lyfe deth hym trewe lyeges chaunge newe obeye lust maner thynge agamenon kynge made hym knyght thelamonyus pwith swerde gyrte anone pirrus sayenge hym selfe place bawdryke whan hym dyd embrace take hede quod myn owne cosyn dere resemble manhode chere knyghthode eke worthynesse thy fader whiche sothfastnesse tyme noble knyght ouer thy full myght auenge deth thou thy payne grekes worthy duke twayne full humbly began downe toknele sette spore vpon eyther hele maner golde bornyd bryght wyse pirrus made knyght ye haue herde full hye presence great honoure due reuerence lyke custome grekes layes ryghtes vsed tho dayes anone hath agamenon full glad great affeccyon delyuered hym fully sentence armes hole without difference whiche achylles lyfe bare worthy fader shuldres square next heyre lyne discent tresour also tent armure delyueryd anone vnto pirrus grekes euerychone eyght dayes suynge thorugh hoost full solempnely halowe honour yonge knyght tyl morowe wha pheb shone ful bryght lyght shyneth fro ferre diffaced hath stremys sterre lucyfer dayes messagere whan grekes gan plate bryght clere enarmed day soure swete fully purpose theyr foon mete manfully theyr tentes wyde agaynst troyans began ryde warde warde proudely felde pirrus bare day vpon shelde faders armes lyke sayth guydo hadde vpon also cote armure became hym wele forth rode armed bryght stele casuelly formest mette firste pollydamas knyght troye full manly man furyously pirrus hym ran hors backe myghty swerde gan hurtle hym berde myghtely hatefull stryfe pollydamas hadde loste lyfe ne hadde reskus ben without tariynge phylymene noble worthy kynge oonly knyghthode worthynesse pirrus gan hym dresse swerde smet hym syghte hors made hym lyghte stroke myght nat sustene sothfastly worthy phylymene pirrus hadde ytake anone saue knyghtes assembled one paffagonye came hym rekewe pirrus aye fyersly gan pursewe vpon kynge myrundones beset myschefe amonge great prees many knyght noble kynge yslayne reske wynge stode deth streyt caas tyll fortune came pollydamas reskus dyde full myght hym delyuere quyte hym lyke knyght sothenesse suche resystence pirrus knyghtes stondynge diffence aye myschefe stode kyge phylymene tyll pantasyllya femynye quene hir woman great companye gan thynge auenture espye whiche echone delyte theyr armure day clade whyte veryly lylye floure snowe flaketh fro iupyters toure whytnesse fressher sene felde hardy quene whiche firste amonge grekes chees proudely falle myrundones amonges rydynge vp downe horseth thorugh hir hyerenowne slewe vp euery syde makynge theyr renges seu r wyde tyll thelamon furyous hete spere vn warely dyde hir mete arage smote hir playne anone full lyfely rose agayne wt hir swerde marketh thelamowne hors made hy lyght dow ne plat grounde handes twayne hir woman dyde theyr besy payne make theyr quene hir stede recure whyle stode auenture lyfe worthy phylymene pirrus knyghtes hym kene maugre men haue hym take geyneth nat diffence make grekes haue strongly hym beset forth lad hym myght bet towarde theyr tent thorugh felde whiche thynge whan quene behelde hir woman aboute hir rode pursued without abode fynally haue sewed thorugh theyr force reskewed maugre manhode myrundones pantasyllya mercyles vpon grekes necessyte thorugh hir force hir cruelte afore hir swerde durst nat abyde whan pirrus sawe hir great pryde knyghtes loude gan crye sayde shame vyllanye woman lese theyr londe slayne felly hir honde wherfore echone hertes doth resume assent let v nowe consume ryde none away escape remedye shape ylke day theyr force confounde shamefull reporte v shall rebounde perpetuelly slepe wake pirrus gan swerde take furyously knyghtly hardy quene happed pirrus knyghtes spake hirlyste nat one tourne bake thret take hede platly hadde hym drede right proudely gan drawe nere hym sayde anone ye shall thou pirre sone achylles slewe ector knyghthode pereles thorugh treynys trecherye malys oonly false enuye vnware whan thynge dyde aduerte whiche neuer may herte grene stycketh remembraunce vpon deth vengeaunce syt well semeth vnto deth venged vpon firste thy faders blode loue hym gentyll gode deth shuld world coplayne nat oonly men theyr besy payne quyte deth woman eke also theyr myght helpe eke therto right requyreth without excepcyon full execucyon stonde plyte thou haste v woman despyte power shortly sentence thou shalt haste haue experyence knowe force sothely euerydele right shorte tyme truste right wele felde shedynge blode pwherfore pirrus wexed gan wode tygre bore wood lyon frat coloure complexyon ire fell despytous toke spere pale furyous ran hir myght payne agayne warde lyste nat fayne encountrede hym deuoyde fere pirrus firste bracke hir spere myght hir nat remeue hir sadell lytell greue agayne sore gan hym hytte stede may nat sytte descendeth endelonge playne vp rose full great disdayne toke swerde honde anone made stede lyne ryght gone vpon quene passynge wortynesse inwardely hate woodnesse herte yfret smet hir many stroke euer sat styll oke force hir yre pale efte agayne made hym auale erthe maugre payne thus fyghte lasteth twayne large whyle tyll myrundones haue take theyr lorde force prees made hym hors recure agayne tyme selfe playne baner descendyd downe worthy kynge great agamenowne kynges duke endelonge grene theyr wardes wonder sene prudently felde batayled haue troyans mortally assayled pbut tho haste kynge phylymene ye haue herde reskewed quene whan hath thanked hir worthynesse knyghtes gan hym dresse pantasyllya assembled bothe one vpon grekes gan gone men may se speres sharpe grounde eueryche bere vnto grounde men may se proudely without lacke manly
