knyghtes renne horse backe woman mortally oppresse fell grekes thorugh theyr hardynesse oonly thorugh force myghty quene deed lay couerynge grene pwherwith came dauz pollydamas fro deth reskewed hym eneas kynge esdras eke troye cyte tho wardes gan togydre fle eyther partye fell furyous pbut moste neptolonyus pirrus hyghte grekes champyowne irous wood troye towne made swerde theyr flesshe byte pantasyllya proudely hir quyte ne spareth nat mortall woundes wyde grekes slee vpon euery syde theyr confusyon pirrus falle glawcon halfe brother pollydamas anthenor eke fader pirrus cruell yre melancolye newe sette fyre smot glawcon toke hede amonge prees fylle downe dede pantasyllya hir woman tyde pirrus falle hir whan hadde syght rode vnto hir lyke manly knyght hurtle hors backe yfere auenture swerdes styffe clere eueryche made alyghte hatefully fote syghte longe outher myght wynne tyll made force twynne wardes went atwene mene pirrus hardy quene tyme dauz pollydamas wood ire herte amyd grekes brother deth mette loue sleth without mercy hatefull tene alone worthy quene suche slaughter grekes make felde vtterly forsake gan toflee theyr tentes downe tyll dyomede ayax thelamowne pirrus eke made tourne agayne sothe ouerlayne ne myght day releue thus faughte tyll drewe eue moste damage grekes syde tyll phebus gan bryght chare hyde lowe west shroude lyght vnder courteyne blacke nyght eyther parte thought beste departe drawe theyr reste toke theyr ease nyght may moneth suynge day day without interrupcyon faught yfere albe mencyon made therof wryte specyall persone generall euer dyde euell well troye boke fynde neuer adele saue quene lyke wryt guydo hir woman hondred hath forgo slayne thylke moneth day deth playnely may shall well quyt fortune fauourable frendely contune hir face chaunge nat contrarye euery day varye ala whyle selde one soiourne gan fro quene hir loke away tourne enhaste thorugh hir vngoodlyhede antropose breke hir lyues threde storye playnely shall lere benyngnely ye lyste fatall houre harde remewe cruel deth noma may eschewe lyfe fynally escape specyally whan parchas haue shape approche gan may none bene ala whyle hardy quene pwhiche day furyous wroth felde troye goth gan grekes proudely sette alder firste pirrus hir mette mortall hate indignacyowne haste renges downe rode vnto hym swyftly hir stede whose sporys sharpe made sydes blede mette theyr speres reste bare euen markynge breste theyr shaftes sothly tale gan shyuer peces smale without bowynge outher backe chyne neyther made enclyne saue hede forged harde stele pantasyllya grounde wele pirrus breste percyd hath depe plate soth mayle myght hym kepe sharpnesse speres hede blode party rede whiche stroke whan grekes gan espye astoned loude gan crye attones noyse sowne vpon quene felde came downe compasse wyse goynge enuyrowne thorugh hir prowesse hir hye renowne hir diffendeth meruayle ala sore hir gan assayle hewe haue hir basenet amyd grekes thycke beset ax swerdes square hir hede sothe made bare hir shuldres naked eke ala mayle hewen rere bra pirrus lyke founde anguysshe oonly grene wounde doute playnely shulde escape towarde quene faste gan hym rape auenged euer falle amyd felde amonge grekes alle whan sawe came faste force oonly mete hym yet caste hir swerde firste gan hym assayle hir stroke happed hir fayle amonge prees narowe beset pirrus swerde sharpe whet sodaynely hir arme smette ala none armoure hym lette raceth thorugh shuldre bone quene fyll downe deed anone malys venge hym herte yre fret sore chere anger pale hath hir hewen pecys smale whiche foule cruell dede euer one pirrus gan blede nyghe deth mortall wounde lacke blode fyll grounde traunce full longe gruflynge lay tyll knyghtes haste may haue take hym vp layde hym shelde dolefully home felde haue hym borne wounded woman quene ala sorowe inwarde deedly wo whan sawe theyr lady ago deed desyrous haste wood furyous rage without gouernayle grekes gan newe assayle auege theyr quene hertly kyde slewe sothely fynde two thousade grek wode ala great dis oynt stode oonly lacke haue gouernour gone theyr chefe socour whiche also speke hardynesse woman lady maystresse hir honde rede oye troyans ye stande great drede amyd felde gouernaunce day come vnhappy chaunce haue ye leder none gyde farewell truste euery syde grekes vpon stronge ye felde may nat kepe longe caste felly quyte day dare lyste endyte wryt homewarde drawe ten thousande troyans grek yslawe theyr wardes came attones downe mortally without excepcyowne kylle slee withstode moste vpon woman wode auenged playnely rede euery halfe theyr blode shede without mercy remyssyowne chasynge troyans home towne felde none abode pyteously tho stode ne none otherrecur caste kepe theyr towne shytte theyr gat faste theyr hope clene agone fyght theyr fone theyr trust knyghthode away theyr worthy men slayne weylaway refute none theyr cyte kepe close may none thought myght kepe longe theyr walles myghty stronge hadde plente vytayle though worlde attones assay may sure whyle kepe euermore man shall wyn pyet neuertheles erely eke late grekes made tofore euery gate full myghty watche awayte full stronge preuy spyes goynge amonge theyr foon none escape away none engyne ferforth may whyle within troye towne make descripcyowne quene great sorowe euery wyght bothe eue morowe ala slayne hir mede whiche came fer helpe nede aldermoste ne myght haue deed corp burye graue reuerence honour dewe whiche gan grekes sewe great prayer great besynesse vayne ydelnesse theyr requeste grekes wrothe fynally many sondry othe oonly malys hote enuye deed corp denye shortly sayde mortall enmyte houndes shall deuouryd gayne theyr rancour copesse pirrus gentyllesse ne wolde assent foule dede wood wroth cruell dyomede sayde openly syttynge fayle hir buriynge slayne hadde many worthy man thus stryfe amonge grekes gan great rumoure altercacyowne tyll laste vnder troye towne hir haue dede corp ytake cruelly profounde lake haue hir caste lete hir lye vnto troye agayne wyll hye tell forth lyue pyne cruell mar hast made fyne thorugh thyne yre worthy blode troye ala hast thou wode agaynst slee theyr knyghtes hast thou lette thy bytter venym fall ala thou sterre infortunate worlde make debate hatefull sterre hote combust drye firy irous grounde enuye hasty euer full discencyon coleryk thy complexyon murdre deth aye thy delyte takynge vengeaunce moste thyne appetyte firste meuer anger hate rote contek causynge debate stryfe murmur moste thy desyre feerfull loke wylde fyre gastfulleuer thy wode syght leuen flamynge thy lyght lyke twynklynge spakes rede great fyres abrode sprede consumynge aye melancolye hertes enbraced enuye thy wrathe aye fretynge kene causest men longe lene consumpt sklendre browne cytrenhewed vnmercyable right euell thewed wonder sleyghty engenyous compassynge suspecyous tryste solen full heuynesse assentynge cursydnesse awaytynge deth roberye murdre also trecherye without remors conscyence venymous thyne influence helper arte vnto false treason house scorpyon crowned arte caprycorne bole thy kyngome lorne therin thy deieccyon thy power loste domynacyon haste also thy subieccyon exyle werre chaynes pryson proscripcyon captyuyte thy malys troye cyte wolde god coude chyde ryght haste kydde thy felle myght thy rancour hoolly outtraunce firste vengaunce speres sharpe swerdes kene whette pryson enclose shette vengeably dare nat oute grekes felle aye lyinge aboute nat holde maner wyse thy temple sacryfyse neyther bulles borys wylde bestes euer vnmylde tygres berys wode lyon whiche thou art souerayne patron nat holde brymstone smoke thyne auterys whiche art felly wroke ala nowe worste alle thou haste shad chefe thy galle amonge selfe brynge treason fayned trouthe symulacyon make hertes amonge selfe deuyde lo serpent discordecan glyde full slyly tyll haue caughte place voyde away happe grace venym discencyon whan sprad regyon comon borugh towne cyte amonges men hye lowe degre whan hertes loue nat one farewell fortune theyr grace clene agone discorde holdeth resydence well worse swerde pestylence worse outher fer nere foo famylyere may harme hym luste enmye vpon men truste descryue shortly clause rote trewe cause myschefe confucyon euery lande discencyon peryllous pryue recorde take troye cyte founde fortune frendly aye nede tyll longe byd hate gan brode sprede prudence sothly hath prouyded regne selfe deuyded shall recules tourne wylde waste dweller desolate haste mar enuye lorde amonge selfe sowen hath discorde agayne whiche may socoure worse werre sothly semeth treason cured vnder fayned pee roote olde anchyses pwith sone called eneas dauz anthenor pollydamas haue contryued amonge vtterly vnder veyl concelyd secretly falle grekes troye haue first may theyr owne lyues saue engyne sleyghtes treate may nat caste maner weye wolde rather traytours troye pryuely nat espyed couertly grekes ben allyed stonde hole towne trouthe wylfully neclygence slouthe surauce othe olde made towne refuse playnely conclusyowne allyaunce lette slake slyde theyr lygaunce sette also asyde theyr auyse thought beste caste lyue reste meryer eke ernest game saue theyr lyfe wandre forthe shame wylfully dye myschefe traysshe towne helde reprefe myght escape selfe lyue lyste thynge towne stryue sought sothe soure swete mene waye lyue quyete therupon haue theyr way nome vnto kynge whan come presence full couert wyse vndercoloure began deuyse telle theyr tale fynally teyr counsayle pryam vtterly maner nat reckeles pursewe grekes pee gette may yelde agayne kynge menelay without stryfe fresshe quene eleyne ouer nat disdeyne harmes done parys gon full yore cytheron iustly restore bvt ala false iniquyte counsayle rose vnder secrete venym sugre vnder galle well wyste grekes alle ne wolde accorde conclusyowne haue pea troye towne whyles suche myschefe brought treate therof sothe nought pryamus eccuba quene sone polycene yet left hym towne myght haue reygned longe successyowne grekes full nat repentyd vnto pea holly hadde assentyd counsayle gyuen late sythen grekes well elder date proferyd firste tenedowne aduyse kynge agamenowne fynall pea shortly seyne wolde restore agayne eleyne amendes requyred reason damage wrought cytheron messenger firste whan sente pryamus wolde nat assente requeste iustly brought pea meanes sought pryde denyed wylfulnesse ala guyed lacke oonly wyt prudence haue wt cost great dispence slaughter men many great damage sharpe shoures cruell rage abyde fully mortall werre full sure wyll nat differre tyme forth treate pee lyste thynge reckeles vnauysed ought trowe ye wyll lyghtly go home grece without recompense wolde seme neclygence speke nat therof wyll nat tpecyally troye cyte myschefe stande vpon fynall fate remedy shape late grekes thought right truste troye stode theyr luste holdynge selfe veryly victours theyr foon fully conquerours without doute ambygnytee counsayle ylke enee anthenor anchyses ye haue herde treate pee ne roos sothe doublenesse oonly treason hye falsnesse pryamus conceyueth theyr chere lyke boke ye shall day whan pryamus sone called amphymacus counsayle helde towne thre haue made suggestyowne vnto kynge touchynge treate anone discrete auyse prudently wolde assente gan vndergrope playnely mente oonly wytte discrecyon put execucyon makynge therof maner delay proudely stondynge bay anthenor without reuerence spake kynge open audyence shortly sayde sterne chere thou lyste counsayle platly thou mayst chese thou wylte thou wynne lese fyne thou gettest worke thy counsayle kynge wonder soberly answered agayne full benyngnely syre anthenor ye ought nat greue myne entent nat repreue wyse counsayle prudent rede conclude comon spede people sauacyon wyte right well iustly reason vnder sugre curyd galle preiudyce lyeges causynge myschefe fyne wyll vtterly declyne right requyreth alder ease semeth shulde nat displease thy conceyte none offence euery man holden prudence worst leue better take wysedome sewe folye forsake remedye seke sore worde troyan anthenor sodayne ire gan chaunge blode abreydynge foot stode full felly sayde vnto kynge sekerly wonder thynge wysedome auysenesse blynded wylfulnesse ye may nat nosyde se great myschefe aduersyte vpon euery syde may nat dissymule hyde disioynt playnely stande nat foon also hande haue sette walle rounde aboute fere dare nat yssue oute bolde vndo gate fyghte v deedly hate feble stronge sothly yet haue amonge fyfty kynges worthy renowne confederat destruccyowne therupon platly wyll abyde whiche vowed haue theyr great pryde neuer parte hense fro towne tyll walles tourned vp downe pyour worthy sone also dede wonte helpe nede manly knyghtes slayne euerychone v saue remedye none vayne treaty diffence wherfore rede reason prudence slayne cyte lese two harmes leest chese saye entent syttynge expedyent treate p lenger feyne restore agayne eleyne loue many worthy man hath loste lyfe sythen werre began parys vnderstone ygraue beste rede sothe ye may haue sende hir home agayne menelay profre ferforth ye may restore within lytell whyle harmes done parys ile whiche men wont cythera calle rede afore alle yt worde vp rose amphymacus counsayle full contraryous shortly sayde shall nat anthenor hath rade degre euer thus without respyte spake hym hye despyte thou anthenor haue espyed wele may truste neuer adele v stonde great nede trouthe fayth nowe dede falshede hath slayne stabylnesse stede thy sykernesse fynde sothly varyaunce come fayth thy lygeaunce thy hestys made stande thy kynge thyne othes double menynge hyd thyne olde assuraunce come thy fayned false constaunce stede whiche mutabylyte hath take place lyke may se newe chaunge thou art remewable vpon groude thou mayst nat stande stable thy trouth gone olde affeccyowne shouldest haue stande wt towne fayth v lyue deye truste hope exyled aweye thy persone shortly wryte besy arte kynge excyte disencrease estat royall vnto grekes thrall seke pea drede thou shuldest rather thy manlyhede haue proferyd hym cyte diffende thy lyfe outtraunce dispende wherfore sothe assure rather shulde endure twenty thousande shall spere shelde vpon day slayne felde thy worde holde prophecye procedeth trecherye doubylnesse false treason vndermynynge prodicyon though thou outwarde shewe fayre venym hyd thy tale doth repayre lyke serpent styngynge vnder floures fele suche counsayllours wyse wordes despytous full bytyngly hathe amphymacus openly anthenor repreued counsayle agreued seynge treason wolde mene tyll eneas gan go betwene florysshed speche full flaterye gan tale modefye lyke mente trouthe entent therin double entendement spake one yet mentetwayne amphymacus oonly refrayne attempre hym melancolye oonly tyll myght tyme espye lyke purpose may procede execute fully vp dede whan founde hadde space vnder pretens trewe face tale gan breke oute many troyan standynge hym aboute shortly sayde conclusyowne touchynge diffence playnely towne henge hoolly balaunce bothe hope truste assuraunce cyte taken haue theyr flyght fynally manhode myght knyghthode togydre ago grekes haue stoutely fyght whiche hath lost many worthy knyght redy vpon v set dare nat gat vnshet ala supprysed drede semeth great nede good aduyse seke mene myschefe shall v demene parte sothfastly say knowe none redy way prudently pea trete pryam sodayne hete without abode chere face pale rancour gan interrupte tale attempre myght nat herte fretyngly treason made hym smerte myght hym selfe nat restrayne thus sayde vnto bothe twayne anthenor also enee wonder greatly ye hardy trouthe shame varye ye rebell contrarye oonly false collusyon v brynge desperacyon lyeges shall nat fayne false entent catche v trayne ala may ye herte fynde agayne nature vnkynde whylom counsayle chefe euery thynge brought prefe ye absent coude thynge fyne ala ye caste declyne away fro barayne left sooll remembre great adooll wyght ala chaunge shall truste man whan ye founde double entent ye nat thynke assent counsayle auys whylom sent forth parys grece full yore ago anthenor thou wotest thy selfe also thou firste made embassatour therupon chefe counsayllour touchynge sonde made exyon cause mocyon though soth parys shulde go grece thou wotest well ine durste presumpcyon haue sent parys vnto cytheron without aduyse auctoryte eneas playnely vpon grekes werre haue gonne trowe sothe neyther konne excuse hym selfe ye auysed euery thynge wrought deuysed execute counsayle tweyne whan parys went eleyne grounde roote speke specyall thou enee cause pryncypall present also whan euery thyng wrought grece whan hyder brought sothe regyowne neuer hadde come towne thou haddest therto contrayre albe thou woldest thy wordes fayre thyselfe excuse audyence thou knewe nought offence fully vnwyttynge dede sonnes euerychone dede ye mese alone destytute counsayle chefe refute pursewe grekes pee foryetell reckeles remembre infynyt outrage mortall werre slaughter damage cruelte destruccyowne haue wrought hereupon towne veryly whan recorde deed nat accorde treate lyke ye deuyse espye many sondry wyse entent right peryllous snare couertly vnder falsehede dare wyll confusyon ye acheue entencyon fynally ye haue shape impossyble escape shamefully myschefe dye without recure remedye fyne knowe doute treate ye aboute right anone troyan eneas ire rancoure ameued agayne kynge swellynge herte sodaynely dore sterte hadde wroke full many worde agayne kynge yspoke went way anthenor also pryamus ire wo sodaynely braste wepe myght hym selfe nat anguysshe kepe anger frat vpon hym sore within hym selfe conceyuynge euydence discrecyon couert gyle false treason hym cyte ishapen haue auysed dredynge aye ylke twayne engyne conspyred trayne grekes wolde hym betraye wherfore kynge caste wolde saye shape away theyr malys withstonde treason toke hande oonly right dede founde vpon selfe myght agayne rebounde full execucyon theyr contryued conspyracyon resorte agayne full dewe wyse oonly gan firste deuyse treason treason conuenyent falsehed guerdon pertynent shamefull deth fynall mede wherfore shape great nede remedye olde pryamus calleth sone amphymacus pyteously alone twayne terys drowned gan hym complayne anthenor eneas sayde sone take hede ca thynke thy fader dere yfere sone lefte lyue thou alone therfore blyue touchynge treason conspyred ysworne euer falle let v toforne oonly wysedome away make may firste trappe take puruey euen lyche iustly may falle oyche whiche haue made v ytreyned hast lette ordeyned mater close kept mewe fyne oonly nat eschewe slayne equyte ryght place euen towarde nyght purpose playnely theyr sake agayne houre counsayle make vnder coloure make calle thou vnwarely shalt vpon falle knyghtes sworne vnto mater secre right anone amphymacus assentyd vnto pryamus accomplysshe full secrete wyse fro poynt poynt ye haue herde deuyse bvt sothe sayde full yore agone olde wyse yt counsayle none worlde pryuely ycaste wyll platly laste people whiche rurall sayth yt secretes whiche nat knowen erthe wyll make mynde discure owne kynde nature vp caste disclose thynge men wont close let euery man beware gode counsayle go ferre abrode specyally lordes haue great nede men stonde moste drede great awayte vpon layde whan happeth thynge sayde one spoke lordes mouthe falleth ofte full kouthe reported ysprad full wyde many coste stonde asyde ware sodayne auenture hap dothe assure wyll first hym reporte amys therfore sothe beste beware kepe theyr tonge purpose caste shulde nat ronge spoke abrode amonge folkes rude gladly aye worste conclude euery thynge whyle newe reporte varyaunt vntrewe reason thynge expowne wyll folke towne lyke purpose whiche desyre fare wyspe fyre whan brenneth bryghtest blase sodaynely wasteth mase suche folke platly tryste fyre water holde theyr fyste beynge bothe ylke indifferent hote colde lyke theyr entent newe chaungeth theyr courage calme foloweth sodayne rage day loue tomorowe hate truste comon lasteth date lette nat lorde make secree counsayle ronne enee pryam wende hadde full close rumour wynde arose false reporte ferre blowe eneas anthenor well knowe ende gynnynge euery maner thynge hole counsayle pryamus kynge bothe two full one entent eke theyr assent conspyred togydre sworne couertly caste awaye aforne fynally troye cyte theyr engyne shall destroyed accorde caste playnely thus happe kynge pryamus sende shortly conclude wolde come suche multytude armyd men se nede hym shulde thynge drede eneas cyte great power auctoryte bothe blode kynred allyed golde greatly magnefyed thorugh cyte moste specyall myght power perygall sayth guydo vnto kynge anthenor almoste euery thynge vnto hym egall powere bothe twayne one herte entere conspyred haue sothe agayne towne fynally conclusyowne grekes myght haue surete theyr treasoure go lyberte theyr allyes borne troye towne whan brought destruccyowne lyfe good aufe without whiche tyme dauz anthenor eneas pryamus hath sent accomplysshe fyne entent haste great route came knyghtes stuffyd aboute therof astoned pryamus made sende amphymacus comaundynge hym chaunge purpose well wyste counsayle nat close sygnes gan well vnderstonde mater whiche hadde honde discured confusyon bothe murdre conspyracyon apparceyuynge warde syght great power troyan knyght fauoure eneas comon fostryd whiche proudely open audyence tofore kynge declareth sentence fully concludynge maugre sayth nay none mene way refute gayne remedye oonly pea denye escapynge playnely none therupon comons euerychone one voyce gan gale crye counsayle greatly magnefye albe kynge therto contrarye eneas lyste lenger tarye differre fyne purpose wonder irous see rose full vngoodly spake vnto kynge shortly sayde without tariynge befalle thou lefe lothe purpose pleased outher wrothe thou mayste well trust shall none fynally herken maugre thy wyll also thy myght day yet nyght pea grekes shall trete whan kynge sawe feruent hete bothe comon eneas gan anone dissymule caas prudence clerely gan se tyme may none wherfore sythe myght nat amende wysely gan condescende purpose platly enee sayde wolde goodly take gree accept lyst ordayne kynge lernyd fayne agayne conceyte platly herte otherwyse coude nat asterte coacte force vyolence whan sawe aduertence myght dyuerte syde fraude sowen wyde without grutchynge falsly gaue assent anthenor shulde forth sent comon choyse treate towne whiche tofore conclusyowne grekes accordyd fynally touchynge effect ambassatrye fro poynt poynt wolde stonde varyaunt fro toke honde hadde afore hym full conceyued better chere receyued whyle anthenor oute treate grekes stoute ye haue herde pea fynall towne aboute euery wall troye gan ascende blyue braunches many fresshe olyue token pea grekes eke agayne amyd felde endelonge playne shewed myght sene eke olyue lusty bowes grene conferme fro proynt poynt thynge stode disioynt worthy kynge great agamenon comytted hath hye discrecyon fully power auctoryte grekes playnely vnto thre firste pea trete vnto wyse worthy kynge crete vlixes dyomede mo thought nede wyll holde stably fynally nat varyable ende platly make therupon assuraunce take eyther parte bonde sacrament anthenor ywent asyde worthy lordes thre whan theyr lyberte tumulte alone pryuely anthenor full trechery replete falshode doubylnesse gan purpose vnto expresse behotynge trasshe cyte wolde make hym suerte firste hym selfe hym eneas shall fredam haue euery maner caas theyr allyes goodes euerychone lyste large gone theyr choyse dwellynge towne theyr rychesse possessyowne without harme damage lyke se auauntage theyr persones voyde abyde sworne grekes syde couenaunt holde party rehersed afore specyall theyr othes bounde varyaunce founde neyther partye platly stryfe behyght vp peryll theyr lyfe whan assuraunce thre charged kepe secre sayd thynge di curyd vnto tyme assuryd ende grosyd vp dede good toke hede lyst theyr purpose perturbyd shent comynge without auysement tonges longe large wherfore gan con oure charge wyse pryue wyghte thre none estate neyther hye lowe fully fyne theyr entent ne knowe couertly purpose hyde quod anthen vpon euery syde voyde away suspeccyowne myn aduyse troye towne wyse kynge called taltybyus shall go kynge pryamus hore yronne rage coy porte sleyghty right sage therwithall sadde demure stylle troyans thynge shall mysylle come treate pee assuryd wryte douteles troyans agree wyll therto euery thynge fynally anthenor grekes hath behyght thus shall deuoyded anone ryght thorugh comynge suspeccyon tyll haue conclusyon ye haue herde parfourmed euerydele whiche thynge grekes lyke wele apoynted vpon euery thynge wyll olde kynge anthenor shall troye go axed eke also pantasylle body haue cyte men myght graue dewe honour longynge hir estate voyde away suspeccyon debate anthenor drewe eue grekes taken hath leue kynge repeyreth towne wherof made anone relacyon kynge pryam without delay haste vpon next day made assemble cytesens secretely deuoydynge foreyns anthenor open audyence thorugh halle whan made sylence tale gan sugryd wordes swete makynge bawne outwarde flete rethoryk eloquence chere worde none offence shewynge circumspect man coude maner caas sygne outwarde countenaunce perceyue hym varyaunce harde treason espye effect declarynge embassatrye clere reporte answere agayne meanynge though nat playne vnderneth fraude fraught sleyghty wolf tyl pray hath caught close couert speche serpent tyll may wreche hydynge venym vnder floures longe bee styngeth tonge whan hath shad hony sote sugre crop venym rote right soth tonge scorpyon anthenor roote treason tale tolde face pleyne lyke sonne shyneth reyne fayre sheweth though weder wonder dyuers troubly se tygre full doubylnesse couertly treason dyde expresse nat mente trouthe towne fully affermynge conclusyowne grekes myghty stronge lykly eke abyde longe day day redy assayle also plente vytayle concludynge aye remedye agaynst holde chaumpartye stryue sayde hadde yet lyue theyr worthy knyghtes hardy lyon theyr manly men theyr champyons whiche theyr lyues platly iuparte cyte caste nat departe tyll theyr purpose acheued fynally nouther toure wall gate yren though ye shette grekes shall syde lette wyll v wynne laste wherfore nedeth mene way caste sythen myght fauour fortune may nat longe agaynst contune wherfore quod ye condescende right well thynge amende remedye ye nat varye saye contrarye mene shortly doute embassatoure whan oute grekes laste whan ye sent sayd goodly wolde assent vnto pea condycyon ye wyll make restytucyon harmes vyolences wronges done also offence parys wrought grece cytheron right semeth reason theyr request meynt equyte dryuen necessyte vnto theyr luste iustly enclyne maugre wyll werre fyne theyr eleccyon may nat make rebellyon mater fer ybrought stryue agayne soth helpeth nought may apeyre thynge auayle therfore beste counsayle prouerbe hath sayde yore man constrayned sore may nat flee falle trayne let hym chese lesse harme twayne gretter prudently eschewe let golde ye kept mewe saue lyfe make redempcyon better demeth reason spoyled oonly rychesse wylfully dye distresse lyfe better glode gode set nought sauynge blode foly man welfare thorugh couetyse golde spare lyfe dependeth balaunce let golde farewell go myschaunce may hereafter sort auenture golde grace good ynough recure sythen haue tolde may bye pea fynally golde treasour stynt eke werre foly playnely differre grekes vtterly accorde recorde ye assent without varyaunce may pea perturbaunce lyght recured soone assured iuste reporte entencyons wyll wryte oblygacyons couenauntes nat hynde ye shall faute fynde whan assuraunce outher parte hadde therupon endentures shalbe made fayth ye may nat repreue fully truste leue without fraude relacyon wyll make dylacyon signefye certayne hoolly effect ye wyll sayne people loude gan crye one voyse magnefye euer anthenor hath sayde vpon hym haue charge layde theyr answere entent fynall recorde reporte thynge forgetten caas haue assigned also eneas hym go thynge presence olde kynge taltybyus whiche also entent pwith anthenor troye sent whiche thre haue playnely vndertake ye haue herde fynall pea make albe couert treason mente theyr way forth anone wente playne power comytted towne kyng pryam hath ay suspeccyowne anthenor also enee shall destroye cytee hym selfe tryste hertely wo sayd ala beste myschefe falle yet worste alle nowe thorugh myn aduersyte bounde compelled necessyte maugre hede maner raunson lyfe make redempcyon vnto foon haue moste herte se right well may nat asterte must paye gayneth socoure good golde ryches treasoure moste foon dare nat denye yet stonde lyfe iupartye without refute hangynge balaunce ala constrayned thorugh wofull chaunce obeye theyr luste mortally hate dryuen therto byrthe thorugh fate parchas haue desteny yshape engyne may nat escape whyle pryam gan thus copleyne anthenor came quene eleyne besechynge hym embassatrye gentyllesse specefye thorugh prudent medyacyon fynde away conseruacyon hir estate fynally menelay may reconsyled falle treate holde hir lorde grace wolde restore hir vnto hir degre oonly mercy hye pyte anthenor vnto hir requeste gaue audyence makynge beheste wolde herte entere dylygent treate matere therwithall hym toke hir leue thus done eue anthenor pray god gyue hy sorowe grekes went next morowe oonly treate apeas fynall whyle feest funerall holde troye myn auctor wryteth thus lorde called glaucus manly knyght tofore lyuynge sone pryamus kynge ouer lyke sayth guydo kynge pryam besyed hym also pantasyllya body myght conseruyd fresshely syght loue worthy quene puryd golde stone shene lete make vessell full ryall fylde full bawne naturall kepe corp fro corrupcyowne tyll werre grekes towne thorugh treate ystynted clene kynge called phylymene deed quene myght affeccyon carye home hir regyon auncetres buryed lyke maner olde antiquyte custome vsed tyme vayne therof ryme passe ouer vnto tretee atwene grekes troye cytee partye grekes rede firste vlixes hym dyomede assigned kynge crete anthenor eneas mete yfere shortly sentence conduyt firste lycence noble wyse agamenowne entred troye towne conueyinge eneas whose comynge suche ioye comunes whiche thynges newe reioyse aye thoughe rewe wenynge full well theyr oppynyon good medyacyon vlixes kynge crete dyomede came eke trete thre shuld make faste fynall pea euer laste full ende theyr alder sorowe therupon erely next morowe pryam lette make conuocacyowne worthy within troye towne whan assembled one wyse vlixes rose vp anone tale gan suche wyse prudently wordes deuyse herken euery man hath ioye specyally troye inwarde menynge fraudelent full lytell wyste entent theyr pleasaunce coude fayne firste axeth thynges twayne one cyte wolde haue golde huge quantyte recompense harmes another thynge axed also without abode amphymacus sone kynge pryamus perpetuelly exyled neuer entre troye cyte golde prayer raunson done suggestyon anthenor false malycious oonly contraryous shulde treaty pee nat reckeles say trouthe amphymacus therfore sothe serpent enuyous hath founde tyme byte thought wolde cruelly hym quyte trouthe oonly entent ptherfore full expedyent prudence euery man charge tonge nat ouer large trouthes nat sayne wysedome somtyme fayne dissymule aduersyte specyally whan men trouble se theyr speche may nat auyle better theyr tonge fayle folyly theyr damage speke men must amonge kure ouer reke trouthe thynges oonly prudence humbly suffre pacyence false reporte folkes enuyous holde hym vertuous better whyle abyde say rancoure pryde sylence sothe hath ofte hasty stryfe hadde victorye prserogatyfe palme debate wonne well suffre konne speche nat presumptuous tolde amphymacus nat withstandynge trouthe mente yet worde exyle wente albe god full iustely afterwarde hath anthenor quyte rewarde hyt falsenesse duely syt say iniquyte exyle captyuyte iuged proscripcy owne relegat troye towne perpetuelly procurynge eneas loo right full kynge may se prouydence full iustly make recompence doubylnesse symulacyon suche contryued false treason auengeth falsehede parte shall hyt darte scapeth nat haue wounde falsehede aye wyll agayne rebounde rose firste orygenall resorte agayne right doth ball fraude euer doth hym caste truste right well wyll laste supplanteth shall supplanted good exaumple ye shall se anthenor storye ye rede whyles treaty procede touchynge exyle proscripcyon captyuyte relegacyon caste amphymacus herde noyse meruayllous great tumulte wonder sowne lyke lamentacyowne sondry folke playnynge distresse hertely wo warde heuynesse treate euen whan gone confuse crye gan anone pwherof vlixes eke dyomede sodaynely fylle drede supposynge theyr oppyowne rumoure falle towne amonge people como te hasty rancour auenged loue amphymacus causeles exyled thus volunte agayne trouthe ryght wherfore dradde whan drewe nyght murdred comons towne fraude conspyracyowne falsly compalsyd olde enmytee anthenor false enee sothly yet maner man coude wyt wherof began espye firste arose paleys thorugh close herde well lay nought wherof astoned theyr thought affrayde sodayne drede vlixes also dyomede lyste comons set anthenor without lenger let make sure tumulte cry grekes hath conueyed secretely whan assured theyr place vlixes firste chaunged face gan pynche sore selfe whyle anthenor treason gyle hestys fro day day sleyghte put delay semynge fully ought coude espye deceyt fraude trecherye couenauntes hath behyght one false troyan knyght sadde chere sobre countenaunce well auysed dalyaunce answerde agayne playnely dyde expresse wysse quod take vnto wytnesse hye goddes euery thynge may se without faynynge haue besy fro poynt poynt purpose acheue nat greue fynally ye lyste one thynge parturbeth matere whiche shall none offence playnely remembre presence say olde antyquyte firste byldynge troye cyte whylom ycalled yllyon cause oonly foundacyon kynge ylyus sythe go full longe founder walle stronge made mencyon called named yllyon whiche great besy charge pallas name made temple large passyngly reuerence whan phane moste excellence perfourmed masonry full wele saue rofe complete euerydele myghty stone byldynge well assured lede tymber cured agayne tempest obstacle fyll wonder oonly myracle dare well afferme certeyne suche another neuer seyne lyste se consydre meruayle celestyall came downe hye heuen plyades sterres seuen thorugh eyer holdynge passage lyke fayre meruaylous ymage worlde though men sought ne none halfe well ywrought trewely suppose pygmalyon remembred rose tyme hadde cunnynge graue peynte curyous thynge wrought dylygent laboure hande aungell heuenly toure thorugh goddes myght dyuyne ordyauce hyder sent thorugh puruyaunce relyke oonly grace prouyded place abyde proteccyon diffence sauacyon perpetuelly whyle worlde may dure agayne myschefe mysauenture euery trouble trybulacyon susteynynge releuacyon soueraygne helpe eke cyte whiche neuer may destroyed none engyne men may purchace goddes haue graunted suche grace suche vertue annexed eke therto troye sothe may neuer fordo tyll relyke stole away yet sothe man may place stere remewe preste dewe oonly offyce touche honde myghtely conserued bonde attempteth conclusyon remewe presumpcyon fyne platly shall fayle force none may hym nat auayle sothe wyll nat remeued except hym duete apperteyneth ye haue herde forne ouer man yet borne rede tell degree veryly stone tree deuysed ywrought wyght sotyll thought ceryously tell manere mynerua fresshe clere sterne goddesse thorugh hir great myght dredefull bothe loke syght whiche hir brest haueth cristall hir shelde egys goddesse inmortall ygraunted hath bokes lerne thorugh hir power whiche eterne holy relyke memoryall hir temple byldynge moste royall conserue assaute brede socoure euery maner nede agayne theyr foon vnto troye towne whyle kept deuociowne alway successyowne kynge kynge lyne downe iust tycle lynealy succede annexyd take hede prudently auoydynge neclygence conserue dewe reuerence bounde yholde ryght shall enmye power haue myght damage hyndrynge towne called palladyowne lyke clerkes wryte sayne pallas make hir towne certayne relyke sent fro heuen downe conclude shortly reasowne cause purpose let quod vlixes syth may beno bet labour ydell vayne without recure certayne thou haste sayde towne degre thorugh relyke may nat destroyed foly vndertake vnto grekes beheste make without thou haddest well sure quod anthenor yet recure haue hyght ye shall haue towne though dylacyowne maner anone shall telle ye lyste whyle dwelle without noyse outher perturbaunce preste whiche gouernaunce relyke shalbe spoke vnto good aduyse ytretyd shall full assent golde treasour shalbe blent accorde shall purpose brynge relyke whiche kept close place ye lyste assygne styll porte goodly benygne werkes tyll haue brought aboute fully thynge nothynge doute dare selfe take well honde whan menynge vnderstode toke leue went towne firste voyde suspecyowne theyr goynge anthenor hath hyght wolde go nyght pryamus make ordynaunce bondes assuraunce pea shulde ymaked knowe eke quantyte golde ye shall receyue thus shall beste purpose apparceyne kynge knowe eueryde e consente lyke wonder wele euery thynge anthenor hath fayde parte glad well apayde went theyr way made tariynge anthenor goth vnto kynge hym counsayllynge make delay calle lordes agayne next day lyeges assemble yfere fynally engroce matere syttynge expedyent whan kynge open lement crowned sat regalye anthenor gan specyfye audyence men myght knowe eche estate bothe hye lowe grekes wyll agree therto sume golde also whiche axe pea shall stande twenty thousande marke haue hande puryd god whiche must anone payed syluer may nat delayed muste eke haue quantyte ouer accorded certayne mesours couenaunt also whete floure theyr lyues saue theyr repayre large see whan sayle home theyr countree collect made anone good aduyse euerychone redy acercayne day man durste tho say nay contrarye anthern hath sayde well euyll payde full assent conclusyowne haste thorugh towne collatours gadered vp golde lyke sume haue tolde pore ryche sparyd none whiche tyme anthenor gone vnto preest called tonaunt myght wyse hym daunt make herte fully enclyne full craftely layde hoke lyne lusty eyte false coueytyse excycynge hym full secrete wyse wolde assent condescende vnto entent put hym possessyon relyke called palladyon without abode may delyueryd gaue hym golde huge quantyte hym blende moche behyght done full pryuely nyght shortly concludynge condescende wolde estate amende passyngly euer heyres shulde haue golde store plente ynough none indygence shulde haue power hym offence vnto vowe make quod anthenor platly vndertake golde good thou shalt haue suffysaunce treasour passynge habundaunce thou shalt sykernesse thy kyn excelle rychesse thou delyuer lyke myn axynge palladyon whiche thy kepynge behote thou mayste truste bonde shalbe secree lyst hyndrynge thy name thou drede shame esclaundred foule dede shape shall thou nede nat drede agaste maner wyse suche away sothe shall deuyse man shalbe suspecyous thy persone engenyous deme amysse mater goth well ware loth diffamed false thynge knowe therof assentynge maner towne shulde haue suspeccyowne lece let leuer hadde deye shall therfore caste another weye honour saue thou shall go quyte say vtterly neyther shall beholde ne parceyuere thefte stonde hole clere euer falle without shame vlixes shall bere blame dede thefe also men shall say whan ago engyne sleyghty wyle thorugh treynes false gyle hath stole away palladyowne temple lesynge twone fynally durynge lyue men shall hym falsehede ascryue gylte aretten offence thou oonly innocence thorugh worlde iniquyte shalbe excusyd platly go free nedeth nat tarye matere come attones lo thy golde thou ne shalte lenger delayed syth thou seest diffyculte parte pereyll reprefe shame drede scalundre myschefe delaye nat take thynge honde firste preest gan hym withstonde full myghtely sayde nothynge nouther prayer manasynge golde gode ne maner mede ne wolde assent foule dede thus answerde pryme face ofte sythe happeth men purchace gyfte good speke wordes playne trouth pouerte myght neuer attayne mede falshede may conquere tytle right men trouth lere gyftes great hertes enclyne golde maye stele marbyll myne prestes herte hath depe graue anthenor shall purpose haue possede palladyon thorugh false engyne conspyracyon preest called tonaunte whiche falshede myght hym best auaunte relyke fro temple rente vlixes anthenor sente towne haste myght seruaunt secretely nyght wherof troyans mortally dismayde thorugh treason fynally trayed wrought preest coueytyse blent false anthenor beynge assent phow grek made hors brasse wherin men armes vnder coloure pea brought troye whiche vtterly dystroyed euer cap xxxv troye ala well mayest yu morne wepe complaynynge wthertely syghes depe falsly defraudyd palladyon put euer possessyon myghty goddes worlde gouerne euery thyng thorugh myght coserne ryght deyte trouthe falshede may togydrese euery herte thorugh puruyaunce toke ye nat preest vengaunce traytoursly thorugh iniquyte golde good traysshed cyte troye ala without recure shall emforth sure place stonde sykerte syth holynesse hye degre may infect corrupt mede euery herte ought quake drede se ala false ypocrysye prestes shulde worlde exemplefye good doctryne perfeccyon make soone transmutacyon double entent daynely varye douteles seyntuarye pollut founde conuersacyon naked bare deuocyon shynynge theyr parfyt lyght yturned dyrkenesse vnto nyght vnto place shall men ferther go take example ought certys roote grounde euerydele coueytyse loke wele whiche greyne fer ysowe lyste auaryce knowe amonge prestes shall rathest fynde therwithall made blynde theyr estate may nat se sothnesse degre gredyer rauynous worldely good coueytous prestes catche may gone sythe many day theyr brest fyxhed rote coueytyse whiche syt sote man may arrace hym remewe theyr tayle euer doth sewe false worme moder noryce myschefe euery vyce golde nowe shynynge bryght persynge eke clere lyght prestes stemes blent sothnesse theyr entent coueytyse receptacle possede eke tabernacle theyr herte aye gredy enbrace auaryce hath lodgynge place myd theyr breste vyce vyces causeth vertue rather falle abyt supplaunte recorde take preest tonaunte treasour anthenor hath solde ryche relyke hadde holde palladyon whyle troye towne haue gaderyd vp aboute euyrowne ryche pore thorugh cyte golde syluer huge quantyte floure whete paye theyr raunson whiche sume entencyon made kepe wysely conserue temple longeth mynerue purposynge one affeccyowne cytesens thorugh towne hopynge therby fare bet vpon day assygned yset appollo theyr paynem wyse solempnely make sacryfyse slaughter bestes wt encense blode whiche day whan prestes stode compasse rounde aboute autere gan kyndle cole bryght clere vpon autere playnely rede offre vp bestes dede flawme great leuen appollo stellefyed heuen whan offre laboryous befell two thynges meruaylous firste sacryde fyre ne wolde brenne lyke hir desyre flawme vp ascende alofte albe assayed full ofte ten tymes yet ne wolde aye queynt ne myght se nought smoky resolucyons horryble blacke lyke exalacyons newe lyme whan meynt water colde hete queynt myght maner wyse lacke fyre theyr sacryfyce aye foude wonderfull obstacle next myracle theyr auter whan gan sprede entrayles bestes dede queme appollo wt flawmes bryght fayre came anone downe ayre royall egle full persynge loke clawes offrynge vp toke entrayles lyenge enuyrowne descence makynge suche sowne none hardy herte manhode astoned stode supprysed thorugh nerfe euery vayne meruayle case sodayne egle abydynge ouer towne full hye gan sore towarde grekes enhastynge myght theyr shypes sodaynely lyght entrayles bestes alle egle let fro clawes falle wherof troyans whan toke hede disamayed mortall drede sygnes haue clerely comprehendyd theyr goddes greatly offendyd agayne towne whan fyre went oute wolde put doute sure meruayle mente cassandra haste wente fully haue declaracyon therupon playne exposycyon tolde platly drede quenchynge theyr fyres rede vnto demonstracyon yre indignacyon appollo hath troye bore blode shad achylles temple slawe vengeably murdred ydrawe without maner reuerence honour done excellence appollo beynge present phane plate adiacent defoulyd pollut blode wherfore sayde shortly gode went prosessyon herte contryte deuocyon toumbe achylles nyght oonly fette theyr taprys lyght sacryd fyre brennynge wake fully purpose assent make murdre satissfaccyon whiche fyre none occacyon shall nat quenche flawmes holde thorugh none assaute stormy wyndes colde sacryfyce vpon autere tofore appollo brenne shall clere troye wrought hir rede egle badde take hede thynge token oftreason pronostycke declaracyon fynally troye ylyon shall tourne haste destruccyon flyenge fowle royall ouer towne myghty wall fethers maylyd bryght entrayles clawes kene troye fynall demonstraunce sothfaste shewynge sygnefyaunce grace ewer hap olde fortune lyklyhede myght nat contune perseuer theyr firste lyght attones haue take theyr flyght palladyon myght nat withholde stole lyke tolde man may fatall chaunce refuse grekes eke faste gan muse inwardly theyrwyttes sought entrayles egle brought therupon gan togydre rowne tyll yt calchas dyd euery thynge expowne vnto full gan assure fyne auenture conclude shulde vpon theyr welfare bad also coste spare perseuere herte stable fortune selfe enhable counsayllynge theyr besy payne solempnely haste ordayne certayne offrynge borne felde fayre pallas hir cristall shelde hir make ryche sacryfyse storye ordre shall deuyse bysshop calchas locke hore traytour forsworne syth go ful yore falsed hath trouth aliauce clerkes haue put remembraunce theyr locke letter olde newe exemplefye man vntrewe though yeres passe faste aweye rust sclaundre lyghtly wyll nat deye fret therof corrosyfe lasteth full many mannes lyfe full harde arrace awaye whose venym full selde made allaye reporte therof blowen wyde perpetuelly wyll abyde remembred newe fresshely mynde recorde hym coude away fynde olde calchas euyll mut sterue vnder colour offrynge mynerue make grekes entre towne sleyghty serpent fader patrowne fyndre vp treason gyle compassyd hath founde wyle grekes shall cyte wynne take pretendynge sacryfyce make vnto pallas shall expresse traytoure meroure falsenesse grekes bad theyr payne mynerua offrynge fayne haste shulde spede assent dyde make stede large wyde coper bra crafte synon contryued myght receyue large wele thousande knyghtes armed bryght stele thorugh sleyghte compassynge sotyll wytte meruayllous workynge wyse crafty greke synon whiche thorugh castynge discrecyon parformed hath ryche stede bra ye haue herde byddynge calchas aduyse appyus wyse holpe also stede deuyse fyne oonly deuocyowne grekes myght requere towne whan made graunte lycence presente reuerence myghty pallas stele armed bryght amyd hir temple large full lyght offrynge fynde occasyowne haue entre frely towne pylgrymage theyr vowes fulfylle whiche stede daren shall full stylle thousande knyghtes calchas deuyse ordayned hath slye wyse crafte synon appyus large stede makynge meruayllous vnder pretense oblacyon complete full perfeccyon werkemanshype tolde afore yere troye forlore whan sege sothly gan fyne cyte brought ruyne thorugh grekes myght wall stronge bete downe large thycke longe whiche yere made mencyowne alytell afore takynge towne kynges echone came fro ferre alyue lefte mortall werre pwhan sawe pryam couenaut vnto grekes vtterly made graunt haste possyble paye raunsowne toke leue went towne firste fynde kynge phylymene hym ladde body quene pantasyllia home hir countre full rychely buryed ij thousande knyghtes yt kynge brought vnto troye firste comynge mo fyfty home hym ladde woman quene eke hadde thousande storye sayth certayne foure hondred home agayne thus whan fro troye gone morowe nexte pryamus anone lordes rode towne acorde confirmacyowne pea fynall vpon outher syde felde grekes hym abyde relykes openly yborne outher party sworne forme afore recordyd anthenor grekes accordyd grekes firste swore dyomede troye takynge lytell hede othe condycyon curyd aboue vnder false treason sythe grekes tho theyr swerynge ne bounde selfe maner thynge stonde specyall holde kepe generall poyntes hole engrossyd thylke treate dauz anthenore grekes helde traytour fraudulent whiche full double entent meynt treason ye haue herde toforne whiche obserue oonly sworne fraude othe nat wordes playne theyr aduer saryes take trayne excludynge theyr meanynge ferre pea face herte werre openly confermed theyr honde inly treason assuraunce bonde though venym closyd wt wall nat hyd fro hym knoweth certaynely clerkes teche swereth falsly speche flourysshynge outwarde fayre coloure deceyue trewe neyghboure forsworne euer treason hyd though men may nat se worde away yborne swereth crafte crafte forsworne may made none excusacyon god knoweth entencyon demeth herte worde right nought wyll knoweth thought euery man nyghe eke fere therfore beware man hym forswere grekes dyde troyans deceyue fraude coude nat conceyue supposynge grekes hadde faythfull trewe theyr surete thynge herte thought whiche ende full dere abought whan founde fully reuerse theyr speche dede dyuerse vayne wryte theyr fayned othes theyr wordes whyte cherys coude fayne conclude quene eleyne durynge treate vpon day delyueryd kynge menelay payed raunsowne graunted tofore gaderyd towne golde syluer also floure theyr shyppes dylygent laboure full great haste euery thynge brought thorugh cyte came nought grekes symulacyon makynge coloure deuocyon thorugh holynesse vnder ypocrysye falsly fayned fraude flatery kynge haue prayed haue lyberte freely entre cyte make asseth oblacyon thefte palladyon offre vp ryche stede bra goddes called pallas pwhat kynge pryam lyketh assygne wyllnge benygne theyr repeyre saylynge see home grece towarde theyr countree whan quemyd large stede whiche ala pryam toke hede treason hyd coude nat aduerte graunted hole herte whan lyst brynge towne false entysynge suggestyowne anthenor also enee hauynge drede ambygnytee entent suspeccyon nouther fayngynge false treason right frendely lyke beheste condescendeth vnto theyr requeste theyr auowes myght obserue offre vp hors vnto mynerue grekes tho great dylygence full great honour huge reuerence haue shapen processyowne brynge stede troye towne men armes beynge aye thein calle troye wyn shorte tyme stode date whan hors brought gate narowe space stede towne pace albe assayed ouer whefore pryam bet downe wall make large right theyr deuyse whiche thynge ala vnwyse cause che e confusyowne hors came towne humbly forth gan procede temple large stede pallas mekely downe knelynge attones made offrynge fayned chere false deuocyowne wherof herte glad towne specyall troye sothe sayde aye fyne ioye occupyeth men full ofte se vnwarely cometh aduersyte gladnesse mysauenture whan men best wene ston de sure worldly blysshe none affyaunce dyuers vnhappy chaunce full deceyte euer meynt trouble truste varyaunt double selde one abydynge throwe worldly luste though blowe pompe pryde bost sowne anone passeth recorde troye towne wende well ryche stede haue sure deuoyde drede perpetuelly haue tolde tofore whan grekes haue hors ybore tofore pallas ye haue herde telle lyketh nat lenger dwelle boundes myghty towne purpose greke synowne haue comytted hole gouernayle stede whiche wyll nat fayle whan seeth best opportunyte engyne traysshe cyte grekes haue whyle founde newe sleyghte fully confounde say haue made theyr sonde kynge pryam wolde go fro londe vnto see towarde tenedowne thyder sayle conclusyowne eleyne good ysement secrete wyse thyder shalbe sent dradde vpon londe delyuered shortly theyr honde grekes wolde malys theyr payne party slee eleyne grounde gynnynge theyr wo roote cause also slaughter many worthy man sythen ryme sege firste began wherfore sayde stynte stryfe sure saue hir lyfe best lende hir syght secretely tenedowne nyght thus fayned full false treason pryam put suspeccyon alkaunce wolde neuer theyr lyue resorte agayne troye stryue thus made pryam wene honde deceyued clene theyr deceyte knowynge neuer adele herte thought nat wele grauntynge myght please whan hadde leyser good ease fro troyesayled vnto tenedowne pwith theyrnauye false greke synowne troye wakergan take kepe houre whan men theyr firste slepe haste sleyghty gynne many vyse many sotyll pynne stede made aboute gone crafty lokes vndoynge euerychone goth gan anone calle within hors worthy knyghtes alle secretely man myght espye traytoursly gan hym hye vpon walles selfe nyght towarde grekes gan shewe lyght lay tofore tenedowne redy armed falle vpon towne whan sodayne lyght espyed hors backe anone haue hyed towarde troye armed clene wente walle whiche hors late broke mortally wroke knyghtes eke stede bra haue met full sterne paas gan anone thorugh cyte euery halfe kylle slee blody swerde vpon euery syde made theyr woundes brode large wyde whyle ala thynge aduertynge mydnyght houre dedde lay slepynge full innocent thought nat gode bathed yrowne blode bothe man childe without excepcyon grekes sparynge condcyon olde yonge woman wyfe mayde crye pryamus abrayde llepe sodaynely woke whiche lay nyght hede ne toke daughter murdre towne tho wyste treasowne falsly compassyd vnto cytee anthenor also enee whose malys doute venym broken oute galle conspyracyon vnder sugre symulacyon hath louge closyd hyd dede execute kyd nowe fraude fully treason caste also false collusyon taked abrode yblowe autours openly yknowe hath enuye contryued hate theyr engyne sette abrode gate hath deceyte olde conspyracye fayned othes one allye openly shewed theyr falsenesse disclosed theyr doubylnesse ferre abrode geyne ala wylde fyre seyne toures hye wynde yblased wherof pryam astoned amased awapyd sterte bed comforteles temple fled appollo saue hym myght aye flawme fyres bryght brent towne cousumeth ryche byldynge whylom royall walles theyr rofes huge coueryd lede chefe refuge ala bare bareyne makyd grekes aye theyr swerdes nakyd murdre slee go twenty thousande nyght mo kylled haue longe day slaughter great affray spoyle robbe take fynde treasour good lefte nat behynde myghty honde sturdy vyolence temple without reuerence haue despoyled thorugh ye towne gredely rent racyd downe golde syluer ornamentes alle totore goddes foule mote falle kynge pryam aye deedly chere appolio makynge prayere furyously hertely wofull man soth rede ne wayte deth fatall eure cassandra holy creature warde wo desyrous sterue complaynynge ran vnto mynerue makynge hir lamentacyowne gentyll woman towne ala wolde dye full pyteously sobbe wepe crye theyr dooll lette dwelle theyr sorowes shulde telle storye theyr wo descryue penne shulde routhe ryue rehersynge eke euery strete theyr clothes blacke redy moyste wete ala bothe one alle theyr lordes downe aswowne falle theyr blode bedewed ysprent men may se cristall terys meynt theyr wepynge theyr woundes grene laye blede agayne sonne shene deedly iyen castynge vp whyte vayne wryte maner theyr mortall sorowe guydo wryt morowe anthenor hym false enee conueyued haue thorugh cyte myghty grekes vnto ylyon royall toure ryche mansyon whylom excellence whiche founde diffence hye lowe none estate lefte alone desolate golde rychesse twone shet enclosed chefe dongeowne man withstode brake locke raught away ye gode treasour shet within eche partye myght wyn gaue force lefe lothe pyrrus temple goth appollo great cruelte fyll pryam knelynge kne swerde furyously wode tofore auter shadde blode hye raughte lengthe brede stremes woundes rede statue golde borned bryght appollo great myght power sterne face defouled pollut place oonly deth worthy kynge pyrrus slayne whyle lay knelynge olde hatrede enuyous pryde whyle anthenor enee stode besyde routhe pyte beholde sehym lye stone colde pyteously tofore auter blede wherof ala whan eccuba toke hede hir doughter fayre polycene heer rent golde wyer shene inly supprysed sorowe herte whan began consydre aduerte noble kynge blody stremes rede drowned eyen dyrke dede pyrrus swerd gyrt thorugh outher syde mortall fere durste nat abyde inwardly thorugh darted syght rage toke flyght yet sothe thorugh cyte wyste neuer whytherwarde flee rescuse none remedye kynne frende none allye grekes swerde towne set hir flyght wofull quene hath met eneas causer wrake vnto rebukynge thus spake thou traytour moste malycyous thou false serpent adder enuyous crope roote fynder falsenesse soures well vnkyndenesse myghtest thou thy herte fynde vnto thy kynge vnkynde gynner grounde exaumple treason fynall cause destruccyon myghtest thou deuoyde pyte beholde ala thorugh thy cruelte kynge shedde blode euer hath ben gentyll good gracyous lorde specyally ouer thorugh hye bounte honoured ymagnefyed lyue may nat denyed lyeth deed temple ala thou nat oonly traytoure caas deth conspyrynge vukynde pyrrus conueyinge shuld hy fynde tofore appollo mydes cyte thou shuldest duete rather haue ben proteccyon myghty shelde sauacyon haste cyte towne ylorne whiche thou fostryd yborne grettest reputacyon lordes dwellynge towne thou haddest whylom pleasauce remembraunce pyet thy herte drope gentyllesse mercy pyte deedly rage full tene rewe doughter yonge polycene grekes swerde hir youthe saue thy herte may routhe haue manly pyte hir maydenhede diffende hir nowe kepe hir drede thou canste fynde weye wyse may nat deye hereafter whan men se rede false treason foule dede thou haste done vnto troye towne may partye proteccyowne thy fame venym allye treason whan men wyll assaye iuste reporte thy name accuse dede may helpe excuse agaynst tonges speke enee wyll say thou haddest yet pyte polycene oonly gentyllesse therwith sugre bytternesse thy decert blowe forth fame rehersayle foule blame shall thorugh worlde borne sklaundre infect whan yu art torne thou ne shalt shame mowe sustene shall doughter fayre polycene thy diffence agayne suche famous stryfe thou saue hir lyfe forse though thou make blyue swerde grekes thorugh herte ryue prayer wofull quene eneas toke hym polycene whose traytour herte cruelte hir youthe meued pyte oonly routhe breste arose secretely put hir vp close lyste grekes founde occasyon agaynst hym ayax thelamon toke warde andronomecha actor wyfe wyse cassandra temple longynge mynerue grekes swerde theyr lyues conserue menelay toke quene eleyne garde great payne bode herte many day toforne ala cyte lorne grekes aye besy theyr yre slee kylle cruelly fyre euery syde bete downe paleys house walles towne spare nought goth fyre feruent hate brent theyr desyre olde enuye auenged ne lefte within cyte thynge vnbrent also ylyowne rage tourned vp downe made none excepcyons oonly take possessyons anthenor euyll mote fate eneas grekes spare vounde theyr othe thus grekes furyous wrouthe haue day robbed ybrent tyll kynge agamenon hath sent lordes assemble yfere pallas temple oonly theyr wyse aduyse vpon thynges twayne firste wolde holde nat fayne hoolly theyr hope without excepcyowne wonne first towne ouer axed also touchynge goddes wolde golde treasour possessyowne haue thurgh hye renown answerd without tariynge wolde theyr fayth kepe euery thynge sworne hestys holde ouer sayde wolde golde treasour good cyte right requyreth also equyte iustly partyd dyuysyon euery wyght made distrybucyon lyke meryt hye lowe degre kynge eke reason se eche rewarde laboure longeth conqueroure man haue mater compleyne fylle spekynge eleyne eueryche oppynyon tofore ayax thelamon shortly sayde hath deserued deth many haue yelde vp breth playnely affermynge parlement rightwysnesse trewe iugement shulde nat escape lyfe gynnynge cause theyr stryfe rote grounde theyr sorowe wo sayde eke many nother mo noyse great affray agamenon kynge menelay ne durste worde hir party meue saue ye quene lyste grekes wold greue agaynst great rumour tyll vlixes chefely hir socour thorugh wyt eloquence deuer dyde dylygence saue hir lyfe fully purchace grekes gette hir grace guydo also doth v lere agamenon grekes gan requere graunte hym chefe guerdo cassandra haue possessyon hir lyfe hym abyde eke eneas anthenor besyde elenus grekes tolde werre neuer assent wolde prudent vertuous counsayllynge contraryous tho hye lowe estate troye firste began debate wixe grekes myghty towne eke helpe medyacyowne achylles buryed ygraue deed corp houndes saue whan slayne full cruell wyse nyght tyme ye haue herde deuyse sothly cassandra bothe murdre herte full wrothe sory eke many another thynge wrought towne wtout theyr wyttynge malys innocent grekes haue fully assent graunted prerogatyfe parlement haue theyr lyfe elenus firste teers drowned tofore kynge pyteously hath swowned abraydynge deedly face humble wyle besought hym grace knyghtly pyte haue aduertence spare swerde fro blode innocence mercy nat disdayne graunte lyfe sone twayne worthy ector brother entere eke rewe theyr moder dere oonly grace nat dede wydowe left alone rede wote nat whyther may dyuerte kynge ameued herte wordes wofull chere benygnely graunted prayere gaue eke lyfe fredam go moder hir child two ladyes gentyll woman alle mercy grace calle graunted eke compassyon safe conduyt fre pardon lyst towne abyde countre adiacent besyde put hole theyr eleccyowne thankynge hy fyll knee downe many tere dewed face kynge parteth fro place grekes right anone fully purpose shyp gone haste sayle towarde theyr countree suche tempest rose vp see wawe wynde also cloudes blake moneth dare nat take water salte drede neptunus ire also golus vnto euery thynge contrarye londe made longe tarye see aye fell bolyinge tyll grekes clachas enquerynge one assent myght euer one dyuerse see rage eue morowe answerd god gyue hym euyll sorowe olde shrewe prophesye well whan hym lyst lye tempest caused goddes furyes infernall neuer wolde appese stylle tyll murdre platly achylle auenged shedynge blode whiche sayde appollo eke wode temple hym consecrate thorugh deth troye vyolate blode agayne made satysfaccyon wherfore muste thorugh redempcyon hir roote specyall thorugh hir beaute orygynall cause deth yonge polycene gynnynge firste mortall tene therfore appollo myght vp offred sacryfyce please deyte deth agayne make recompence right deth firste offence grekes muste vtterly fulfyll desyre haue wyll large see sayle quyete pyrus tho furyous hete gan enquere aboute euery man polycene wyght tell hir worde shortly saufe sayde eneas anthornor hadde hyd hir pryuely wherof rose amonge sodaynely suche grutchynge grekes aboute theyr lyfe doute inwardly thynge toke grefe tyll anthenor god gyue hym euyll prefe may treason wardeyne bere ye keye shewe malys euery weye longe hath sought tyll chaumbre olde hath hir founde grekes tolde brought hir forth vnto theyr presence cruell force hatefull vyolence without pyte compassion hir delyueryd agamenon ala hasty iugement without respyte auysement shortly hath dempte shalbe dede flourynge hir maydenhede excepcyon assygned agamenon vnto pyrrus tyrannye ladde hir forth fast gan hym hye place shulde deye great prease weye gan croude shoue beholde sene yonge mayde fayre polycene hir beaute hir semlynesse hir womanhede excellent fayrenesse yfere whan toke hede hadde routhe shalbe dede without gylte trespace men may se vpon many face salte terys faste fall downe pyte compas yowne man childe none harde herte felte hir sake smerte hir goodly face whan beholde se fayne wolde myght haue delyuered hir force anone pyrrus hode wende echone without hir deth neuer haue repayre grece weder fayre calchas hadde made suggestyon brought oppynyon laste whan polycene dede wyll mayde clene graue achylles brought kneleth downe wt humble thought caste vp hir eye gan syghe ofte goddes humbly softe dredfull herte deuocyon made wyse hir lamentacyon oye almyghty yt worlde gouerne euery thynge consydre discerne worlde huge large rounde bothe eyer see heuen eke grounde deuyse worde wrought soth fastly knowe euery thought right euery maner wyght without lettynge persynge syght thynge concelyd ywrye beholdynge eternall eye euery thynge may attones se vpon soule haue mercy pyte grace benygne cure vpon woo pyteous auenture haue routhe shall deye wofull spirite lede conueye lyste nowe shall pace vnto selfe place confesse humylyte hethertowarde haue chastyte lade lyfe kept maydenhede seruyse bothe thought dede porte chere countenaunce feture dalyaunce one mysloke neuer yet abrayde sothe dye shall mayde ye well knowe synne innocent though nowe dempt iugement deed without gylte wytnesse inmortall clene entent accusyd yet ala may nat excusyd swerde vengeaunce mustebyte routheles whiche thynge wyte stonde clere pure offence discharged conscyence dare afferme fully gylteles touchynge murdre worthy achylles whiche slewe brother louyd nowe cause myne aduersyte yet wyll dede worde thought vnto deth assentaunt right nought therof right sory herte albe may nat asterte deed oonly sake alone vengeaunce shalbe take without mercy full cruell wyse blode make sacryfy e goddes theyr wrathe queme people blynde sothe amys ye deme agaynst herte cruell mercyles yrous fell without routhe mykell indurate slee mayde alone desolate herte ala pyte gone harder trouthe outher stocke stone cruell oppynyon forlacke pyte tygre lyon certes ye greatly blame oughte therof haue great shame assent foule dede slee mayde quakynge hir drede graunte hir none oportunyte wepe hir virgynyte cruell pyteous wreche blode gylte hereafter shall apeche accuse also great enuye goddes shall iustefye euery vnright bothe hye lowe full egally make knowe trouthe playnely spare degree make open secree saye nat selfe complayne haue reders fatall payne deth welcome vnto lyfe take gree sythen brether worthy renowne slayne buryed towne fader deed vn weldy age alone lefte rage haue abyde pyteously se fynall ruyne cyte whiche herte sytteth sore leuer haue wepe dye attones reles woo sythe kynne passed agoo longer lyue deth better yelde vp breth lad cyte amonge straungers lyue pouerte deth welcome longer lette thy dredefull darte fyle whette tendre herte therwith ryue agayne thy myght shall neuer stryue tyme kythe thy powere wyll herte entere clene mayde began without touche maner man lyfe day lytell auaunt make yet may myn ende goddes alle whose helpe clyppe calle theyr mercy mekely comende wofull spirite pray sende euery mayde better happe grace haue nowe longer space hertely ioye honour contune without assaute infortune lede theyr lyfe prosperyte maydens remembreth vpon take exaumple ye shall kepe ye wolde fewe terys wepe whan ye thynke vpon polycene age yeres grene whan slayne cruell auenture goddes haue cure dredfull goste hoolly betake eternally thus ende make yt worde hir hede gan enclyne full humbly whan shulde fyne hir eyen helde lede downe pyrrus wodder lyon dismembred hath sharpe swerde mayde yonge dredefull ferde ouer cruelte shewe peces smale hath hir hewe endelonge faders sepulture ala myght cruell herte endure mercyles foule adede astoned sothely whan rede hir deth dyde hym gode lyke tyraunt caste abrode hir blode tygre routhe haue rounde enuyrowne aboute faders graue sprent hate cruelte thou pyrrus thou mayste full well ybe achylles sone lyneall discent lyke hym herte entent thou sothe deuoyde pyte werse yet one degree thy fader lyuynge ne radde neuer yet foule thynge though wolde hatrede hym abrayde rancoure euer slewe amayde fynde well hadde parte whylom loue cupydes darte made hym sore lyue smerte whan wounded herte castynge oonly eye wenynge therby wystly deye myght nat sodayne stroke escape afterwarde fate hathe shape murdred loue polycene thou haste slayne thy cruell tene furyously without routhe shame whiche thynge foule hatefull fame thorugh al worlde hereafter shalbe sprede whan storye rehersyd rede shalbe sayde pyrrus routheles slewe yre mayde gyltles woryed shall thy name odyble dede passyngly horryble loue oonly fayre polycene deth whan eccuba quene hath seen ala besyde stode wo gan wexe wode sorowe hir wytte wente hir clothes hir heer rente rage wot nat doth gan anone hondes toth hir furye crache eke byte stone caste fystes smyte mette tyll grekes made hir bynde sente hir forth also fynde yle troye partynent slayne oonly iugement grekes stoned deth whan hadde yelde vp breth wofull quene cruell auenture grekes dyde make sepulture ceryously metall stone toke corp buryed anone great honour solempnyte longe men myght se ryche toumbe costfull royall set made memoryall eccuba whylom great fame gaue place name called longe mynde plocus festus guydo fynde thus quene oonly sorowe wode whan hir doughter hadde shadde hir blode grekes stone dyde hir ende make ye haue herde playnely sake polycene whylom calchas vnto appollo falsly offryde pyrrus swerde achylles auengynge make see calme blandysshynge goddes take vengeaunce vpon grekes euyll chaunce come false goddes euerychone theyr statue stockes stone whiche serpent olde snake sathan hym selfe gan dwellynge make fraudently folkes illude full sotyll hym selfe include ymages make holde forgyd syluer golde erroure false illusyon hath ybrought confusyon thorugh myscreauce ye worthy kynde man sythe tyme alder firste began false honour ydolatrye worshyp vnto maumetrye sacryfyse bestes blode apese whan wode queme bothe eue morowe pray god gyue sorowe within withoute none excepte false route saturne mar pallas iuno iubyter mercurius pluto nouther flora doth floures sprede nouther bachus grape whyte ede cupydo eyen blynde nouther daphne closyd vnder rynde thorugh tellus myght laurer tree thou dyane thy chastytee myghty venus cytherea thy dartes proserpyna lady arte depe downe helle belydes draweth welle ixyon thou zezyphus thyne appyll thou cruell tantalus furyes infernall ye spynne lyues threde fatall vpon rocke euery maner man mus synge wene coppys nysus cyrra vpon hylle besyde cyrrea cybele cere thy corne golus dredefull horne herde ferre whan thou lyst blowe ianus frons backe corbed lowe pryapys genyus preste curseth aye candellys feste thoechone frowarde kynde ymeneus whose power bynde hertes knet maryage tyll goddesse discorde rage disseuerth dyuysyon nouther maues haue theyr mansyon myd erthe dyrkenesse woo elues wont goo vndyrmeles whan phebus shene nouther fawny tendre greues grene water nymphes naydes satirye nouther dryad goddes woode wyldernesse goddes nouther lesse morpheus god slepe holde hym woode taketh kepe obseruaunce may nat fayle haue myschaunce ende playnely mede suche feyned falsenesse drede rose deuyll firste engyne sleyghty treynes serpentyne oonly mankynde whan made loute false ydoles whiche doute deuylles dauyd bereth wytnesse sautre wryt expresse confermeth endytes goddes paganysme rytes one excepteth none made golde syluer stone forged brasse metall tree eyen haue yet may nat se fendes dauyd sayth haueth fayth hope credence delyte drede wyll hym quyte suche guerdon soule sleeth perpetuelly fyne deth theyr seruyse whan men hense pace theyr lyfe vnhap euyll grace myschefe woo confusyowne men may se exaumple towne wende well assured haue haue stonde longe prospyryte agayne theyr foon thorugh helpe appollo venus eke fauour iuno thorugh pallas myght dyane mynerue wont honour serue cerymonyes sacryfyce ye tofore haue herde deuyse haue brought vnto ruyne cruell deth bed fyne may ye se venym byte ende suche olde rytes euydence noble towne may auayle palladyowne may nowe helpe theyr frauded fantasye theyr olde false ydolatrye ala ala bought sore farewell troye farewell euermore farewell ala cruell thy fall wryte shall thy sake forsothe whan take hede inwarde woo herte fele blede whan remembre thought ruyne thou arte brought nought whylom noble ryche worlde trowe none lyche perrygall speke fayrenesse speke knyghthode worthynesse clerkes say thy byldynge knewe worlde ought rewe thy pyteous waste walles wylde whylom royall whan men gan bylde thy toures hye kynge pryamus firste began moste ryche gloryous sette see noble ylyon wryte lamentacyon conuenyent troye thy sake thy great myschefe complayne crye certes trowe nat olde ieremye wepte captyuyte thylke noble royall chefe cyte ierusalem destruccyon hole transmygracyon iewes thou ezechyell tyme whan myschefe fell vnto kynge ycalled sedeclye babylon thy prophesye stone cruelly yslawe departyd sawe ye bothe two coude complayne danyell felte great payne kynges transmutacyon beste tyll thorugh oryson danyell restored mynde agayne ete nomore gras pyet veryly though ye thre wepynge hadde lyue present eke destruccyowne noble worthy royall towne haue bewayled myschefe wo slaughter sege outher partye full cruell wyse terys myght nat suffyse haue bewept theyr sorowes euerychone treason wrought aswell theyr sone hereof may nat auayle lyke gynneth sayle agayne wynde whan maste doth ryue right vayne stryue agayne face bytterer galle vengeaunce vpon troye falle presume theyr furyes sharpe whette ceryously boke sette great thynge dare nat vnder take euen pyteous ende make sege symplesse though style blotted rudenesse metre rusty vnfyled fourthe boke haue complyed humble honde drede doth quake vnto grace hoolly betake mercy thynge dispeyre makynge repeyre grekes lenger dwelle theyr auentures see telle theyr resorte home theyr countre receyued oonly supporte ye nat despyse fyfthe boke shortly shall deuyse phere begynneth fyfth boke troye whiche speketh howe grekes retourned grece dystruccyon howe perysshed almoste see escaped dyed myscheuously capitulo xxxvi whan eolus doth ye wydes rore apesed blewe stormys gouernor lorde also fully accorde whiche myghty iuno lady ayre tomake skye weder fayre clowde none heuen dyde appere neptunus blaundysshynge chere assent storye sayth sothe make see fro tempest calme smothe without boyllynge trouble wawe myghty grek shypward gan drawe repeyre home theyr countre hadde wonne cyte put theyr fomen fully werse fortune aye frowarde peruerse hath theyr merthe meynt aduersyte whan wende full assuryd haue stonde stedefaste quyete vlynde lady falsly made flete yrsugre galle discordaunce amonge selfe brynge varyaunce theyr hertes rancour pryde contagyously seueryne deuyde whan sat hyest theyr glorye palme conquest victorye fully reioysynge thorugh theyr hye renowne crowne laurer possessyowne hadde also theyr lust wonne whan bryghtest shone lusty fresshe sonne eest west theyr worthynesse clowdy skye vnwarely derkenesse eclypsed hath party theyr lyght diffacyd holsome bemys bryght theyr welfare prosperyte enuyous false contagyouste serpent pompouse ellat amonge selfe tomake debate indusynge rancoure discorde entre within shyppes borde agayne vlixes worthy thelamon presence kynge agamenon purposed hath playnely matere tofore grekes anone ye shall syres quod nat greue semeth iustly reaso may meue touchyng ye wynyng gettyng towne golde rychesse possessyowne fully delyuered taken honde treasoure founde londe thynketh inwarde syght ne hath nat ben departed halfe ryght amonge v iuste dyuysyon egall distrybusyon consydred firste tytle equyte euery wyght estate dignyte remembred eke sharpe shoure worthyest meryte laboure decertys mortall stryfe grauntynge eueryche prerogatyfe lyke fortune hath deseruyd ordre hath nat obseruyd amonges v without excepcyon delyueraunce palladyon whiche vlixes say without drede tofore vniustly doth possede hym vsurpynge false oppynyon merytorye retrybucyon apparence tytle grounde vnder pretense coloure falsly founde relyke reioyse shulde ryght sleyghte wonne rather myght vsurpeth maner vaunt gyuen hym graunt echone chefe guerdon wyll make replycacyon relyke nat hym mete whiche shall nat reioyse quyete may distourbe hym lette cleyme duely dette guerdon conuenyent ye lyste indifferent reason oonly doth seme atwene v two egally deme iustly firste euery circumstaunce outher meryte weyed ballaunce firste consydered forth fro day day whyle sege lay ye shulde plente vytayle syde fro myschefe fayle shall wtout auaunt breke knyghthode armes speke felde longe contynuaunce manly force seueraunce vpon foon fell kene day day armed clene nedeth nat make mencyon right honde slewe phylemon ye well knowe whiche kepynge yonge sone pryamus kynge fresshe lusty great fayrenesse hym hadde infynyte rychesse treasoure golde passyngly plente euerydele brought ye remembre lyst take hede ye quyte indigence nede occasyon great gode thorugh manhode shad nat blode mercyles full cruell wyse sake kynge fryse treasour cofres sought yfere sege ybrought knyghthode sythe go full yore haue nat eke augmented made grekes londe possessyons conquest oonly two regyons thorugh prudence labour wonne sythen ye sege firste begonne prouynces troye adiacent encrease dylygent achylles worthy warryoure ye experte full well laboure wrought auauntage sythen ye prudent sage nat foryetyll fully remembrynge nedeth nat reherse euery thynge dispreue manly knyght tytle cleyme hath ryght dome comyttynge oppynyons rehersayle condycyons nouther hath manhode prowesse force knyghode nouther hardynesse poynt haue rewarde dorynge preued cowarde experyence hath shewed dede whan cometh nede worde wynde sleyghty copassynge falshode euer ymagynynge euer yet daye preuyd thynge hym acheuyd whiche myght entytled laude ende medlyd fraude vnder coloure cure alle pretende fayre lyke paynted walle dyuerse hewed nouther hye lowe may man playne menyge knowe suche sleyghte copassyd treason troye gat palladyon whiche great shame sclaundre v alle conquest thus befalle treason haue cyte wonne knyghthode men reporte konne crop rote reherse shall vlixes grounde cause gynnynge firste vnhappy fame reboundeth alder shame syth trouthe platly knowen wyste tale endyde deme ye lyste vlixes aduertence conceyued hath great inpacyence thelamon great enuye feruent rancoure melancolye forbare hym firste full great aduyse full prudent right wyse thought wolde make therof iape worde haste shulde escape nouther none vnbrydled countenaunce outwarde conceyued regardaunce abraydynge stable face syres quod may haue grace vnder supporte hye presence tale may haue audyence nouther doute drede equyte shall possede palladyon durynge lyues day maugre myght say nay ye lyste reason se sege layde firste cyte haue selfe double wyse quyt well knyghthode sothly wyt thorugh counsayle besy cure ofte cause theyr discomfyture aye dylygent auauntage worught compassyd vnto theyr damage day sothe ne hadde hadde floured theyr felycyte theyr force contuned welfare trouthe shall nat spare dempt lokyd reason moste cause theyr confusyon euer agaynst replye ofte wente embassatrye importable costes dispense treate aye concludynge sentence forthrynge entencyowne disencrease hyndrynge towne whan sawe mene none myne aduyse wyttes euerychone force cyte wyn whyle hadde relyke within therupon sotelly ywrought vnto palladyon ybrought pwhiche thelamon malys stryueth olde hatrede vnto gylt ascryueth hoolly thynge haue worught ye prudent thought aduerteth wysely ende maketh honde quarell fully taketh palladyon iustly prouyde fauour let layde syde syth thynge ye platly vnderstonde let v demynge stonde one assent mater wende lo tale ende thelamon ire full feruent hate made inpacyent enuye inwardly ameued vlixes hath dispyteously repreued oonly malys hye disdayne vlixes rebukynge hym agayne full bytterly without abode anone twayne made full mortall fone presence agamenon furyously ayax thelamon melancolye pale nothynge rede thratte vlixes shalbe dede hondes shulde nat eschewe grekes tho rancour remewe quarell put arbytracyon menelay agamenon caused full mortall stryfe sentence anone diffynytyfe put vlixes possessyon perpetuelly palladyon hym confermynge abyde stable cause fauourable vlixes lyke guydo wryt goodly hath hym quyt vnto eleyne gettynge towne beynge cause hir auacyon dispeyred hir lyfe drede grekes wyllynge haue hir dede thorugh prudent medyacyon maugre myght thelamon hath quene fro deth preserued albe hadde well deserued grekes sayde theyr oppynyon thus defrauded palladyon ye haue herde worthy knyght manhode great myght thorugh gan herte brede passynge enuye full great hatrede thought wolde auenged day vpon vlixes menelay eke also vpon agamenon brake lyke wood lyon knyghtes aboute hym stronge sayde playnely great wronge deed wolde auenged specyally ylke thre therwithall furyous wrothe tournynge backe anone goth herte fret full mortall tene many greke quarell sustene herte sore gan
