disdayne agayne vlixes tother twayne full ware euer falle theyr knyghtes made aboute calle great stuffe wake slepe awayte manly kepe full good watche enuyron close full erely sonne arose worthy ayax bed vpryght ymurdred selfe nyght bledde morowe founde onpeces hewe many mortall wounde thynge cruell horryble god man lothsome odyble full many greke wofull morowe wepe se knyght murdred slepe crye noyse ran thorugh hoost one fro man man constreynt foule dede eueryche felte herte blede full desyrous make ordynaunce murdre vengeaunce hauynge therof great suspecyon menelay agamenon vlixes moste specyall comon voyce hym arrettynge foule fame myght nat asterte pyrrus moste toke thynge herte makynge vowe furyous wode venged playnely blode thelamon vpon vlixes hede hym manasynge shalbe dede sore hym fretynge sorowe vlixes erely morowe drede pyrrus taken hath see sheppes faste gan flee wente platly rede palladyon toke dyemede hauynge herte full great remors pyrrus taken hath cors thelamon loue specyall dyde make flawme funerall large great colys hoot rede amyddes feruent firy glede full many greke stondynge beholde lette brenne asshes colde storye tolde herlosed vrne golde full reuerently hath shette therupon hath prynt ysette armes curyously ygraue myschefe asshes saue sent home great affeccyon conserued regyon kynge whyle alyue euery thynge perfourmed blyue rytes tho dayes vsed euer one pyrrus hath ymused vpon murdre traytoursly ywrought caste shulde full dere abought pyteous deth thelamon hauynge aye herte agamenon hadde eke suspect olde menelay wayte eche lay makynge selfe wt theyr knyght stronge trye hath right wronge pyrrus ne wolde let lyghtly gone thus made mortall fone ylke thre platly deth thorugh false enuye whiche hertes sleeth whyle amonge self vntrewe stryfe vpon stryfe gan euery day renewe debate multeplye tyll anthenor gan thynge espye wysdome stynte disdayne reconcyled vnto pea agayne caused accorde made feste full royall besechynge full lowely thre graunt hym therat gentyllesse grekes myght echone outwarde conceyue alone feste manly made calle wryt guydo worthy grekes alle hye ne lowe none excepcyon shulde make descripcyon lordes estate sete sondry course gyftes grete anthenor gaue euery syde longe abyde plente great suffysaunce fynde fyll dalyaunce syttyng met speke enee brought hate enmyte disdayne shortely sentence put hym many great offence specyally theyr hasty tene whylom concyled polycene sleyghte made hir withdrawe whiche cause achylles slawe shortly concludynge one oppynyon fynall exyle troye towne nat withstandynge graunt lyberte gyuen hym abyde cyte also longe hym lyste deuyse grekes haue annullyd fraunchyse fro lowest vp vnto meste present hye feste douteles nat well espye brought conspyracye troye boke fynde saue hym selfe wytte anthenore ilyche false bothe one degre ye haue herde betraysshynge cyte lyke hadde spronge one roote wha knewe none boote eneas dome modefye prayed theyr courtesye leest graunte hym grace foure monthes myght haue space make stuffe apparayle hymselfe puruey vytayle eke graunt hym wolde assent thylke shyppes parys went cytheron vnto temple olde nombre two twenty tolde full graunt petycyowne retourned home troye towne tryste heuy se beholde waste cyte walles olde sorowe felte herte blede within hymselfe whan taketh hede remembred aduertence false treason great offence hym compassyd towne aforne howe sodaynely hath lorne grace grekes stode disconsolate whylom great estate herte fully dispayred vnwarely euyll apayred vnto grekes behynde backe beyng vngylty without lacke coude nat well deme saue sygnes dyde seme anthenor wyte caste playnely wold hym quyte thorugh towne made sende blyue thylke fewe lefte lyue comynge anone comaundement whan euerychone present syres quod ye se fortune towardes gynneth discontune aye vnstable hir eyen blynde ye experte selfe fynde whylom frowarde tourned werse clerkes called aduerse whan hir lyste hir cruelte shewe standeth ye fewe must parte ye stylle abyde ye wyll prouyde stondynge alone deuoyde socoure amonge selfe make gouernoure nat se ye shalbe acloyed euery parte fynally destroyed sely shepe ne rede disparpled whiche drede wherfore best dredfull thynge one assent chese kynge moste able estate occupye assaute manly guye anthenor knyghthode renowne accorde oppynyowne wherfore haste vnto entent without abode lete hym sent comynge playnely towne vpon hede let set crowne grauntynge hym sceptre regalye wysedome may guye assaute parturbaunce knyghthode prudent gouernaunce assent makynge delay neuer one lyketh say nay right gladde maner thynge ye haue herde make hym kynge full lytell sothly theyr sonde eneas menynge vnderstonde ne mente treason falsehede entrynge shalbe dede full traytoursly awayte liynge slee hym falsely comynge anthenor thynge ware dysarmed came wepen bare eneas huge route swerdes drawe set hym rounde aboute tyll troye yonge olde ran atwene manly hym holde theyr knee fyll mekely downe besechynge hym haue compassyowne worthynesse also manhede lyke knyght take hede left people bare besechynge hym dredfull swerde spare rancoure yre leue lest slaughtre wolde greue comon besought hym rewe quod eneas nat vntrewe nat double traytoure eke false worthy enhanged halse desceyte fraude welle amonge comon worthy dwelle hath nat chefe occasyon vndoynge destruccyon newe serpent whiche gothe vndisserued make grekes wrothe agayne false coll yowne myne exyle conspyred fro towne whiche may nat repellyd withdrawe swerde firste shalbe slawe falshede may fynally daunted right hath traytoursly supplaunted grekes menynge fer yle engyne playnely exyle caste myght haue bothe ioye aduersyte haue parte falle durynge lyfe amonge alle thurgh wronge kourbed desyre hath fyne perturbed whiche herte abydeth alway grene nat cause eke polycene yslawe achylles graue yet ye wolde hym saue vtterly shall mene gayne euer agaynst playne whose herte al treason hath compyled perpetuelly shall exyled towne shall man lette assent tyme sette whiche shulde raunson pace fyne gete none grace thus bothe false brother lyke brother eueryche hath exyled traytours bothe troye cytee anthenor hym eke enee anthenor gan hym redy make haste hath see ytake many troyan great apparayle wynde good began sayle many coste many sondry yles nedeth nat reherse myles perrelles playnely whiche great myschefe escaped see haue ioye therupon dwelle auentures telle shortly lytell whyle aryued vp noble yle whylom gorbodya ycalled bylt cyte strongly walled wryt guydo large wyde longe vpon roche whiche passyngly stronge whiche enuyron myn auctour telles woddes ryuers many lusty welles hadde plente maner thynge tethydes called kynge helde pea sceptre crowne fortune lyst nat frowne fauourable fully wylle conseruynge hym pea tranquylle without trouble many daye afore acceptyd anthenore right welcome storye sayth vnto hym confederate fayth fully assured came lege man whan tethydes euer worthy kynge dyde magnefye fro troye great nombre allye came soth vysyte hym se enhabyte myghty stronge cyte full curyously bylte lyme stone dayes called menelone whiche dyde great rychesse croche besyde see set vpon roche besy plente astore traytoure shulde wryte name penne cloyed whose falshede troye destroyed storye ye haue red seyne muste playnely resorte ageyne reherse besy cure cassandra tolde euery auenture grekes shulde falle tolde amonge alle prudent vertuous traytoursly within owne hous agamen shulde murdred fatall ende thynge myght fle let hym beware prudently prouyde lyfe shall nat longe abyde agayne fate none rede eke guydo wryt wha thelamon dede false murdre ye haue herde toforne two sone hadde ofsondry wyues borne comytted kepynge worthy tentre full manly kynge nourysshed ye storye sayth sothe tyll worthy knyghtes bothe tone called anthenycus tother hyght antissacus shape full semely wonder fayre face shortly guydo doth forth pace lyst lenger processe make bryngeth menelay hath take leue grekes agamenon eueryche sayle regyon many greke theyr companye though grekes firste gan denye laste instaunce payne hadde leue sayle bothe twayne see faste gan hye myd autumpne whiche colde drye melancolyke complexyon whan phebus passyd lyon heuenly beest beest royall halfe yronne sygne virgynall whiche somer naked bareyne whan cere hath full ryped euery grayne tyme yere straunge full dyuers sondry floures red whyte pers whiche may lusty glade vpon theyr stalke gan droupe fade enclyne theyr fresshe lusty cheres goynge canyculeres whan wycked humour inwardly habounde sodayne feuer folkes confounde make ax shake custome wyndes gynne wake bothe bough leef causynge falle tyme whan folke bachus calle fro storme rayne grape conserue hydous tempest make nat sterue duresse fretynge froste thorugh full ofte moche fruyte loste moysture cometh fro skyes euen also eke thondrynge leuen whiche vnwarely suche weders kene boyllynge vp many wawes grene rorynge rough frowarde manasse passyngly peryllous passe albe blandysshynge whyle dredful calme though smoth smyle trust wyll longe abyde recorde grekes suche lusty tyde see haue take began sayle theyr stuffe theyr apparayle home grece full many lusty man golde treasour wan sege infynyt rychesse dayes thre deuoyde distresse see obeyed fully theyr wyll deuoyde trouble wedres yll full lusty within shyppes borde foure wyndes beynge accorde conueye euery maner coste gladly euer whan men truste moste vnto fortune stonde hir grace shesodaynely chaunge hir face smyle afore mowe bake vnwarely tourned wrake chaunteresse stormye quene whan grekes effectuously best wene theyr passage fully assured vpon see called egee false goddes anone forsooke boreas fell wynde awooke hydous dredfull noyse sowne tourned theyr quyete vp downe made wawes grysely aryse storye shortly doth deuyse bryght daye tourned nyght heuen derke except dredfull lyght leuen whiche made sore gaste thondre seuered sayle maste theyr toppes smette peces smale water made lowe auale fyre lyghtnynge sodaynely therwith wolcanus forgeth styth hath borde fro borde flawme rent two twenty theyr shyppes brent without escape platly refuge thorughe rage fell deluge wrake wofull nauy goth whylom grek mynerua wroth dyde hir reuerence specyally great offence spytefully cylleus ayax wrought whiche tempest full dere abought whan shyppes almost ydrowned goddesse hath hym frowned vengeaunce felly hym awaked fayne swymme naked sayth myn auctour myschefe ye londe founde sonde almoste deth without remedye hym mynerua hath great enuye woodly hir temple wente cassandra tofore hir auter hente cruell force hatefull vyolence lo perell offence hye despyte holy place doute nat shall fayle grace euer vseth dede laste god wyll quyte mede rewarde hym lyke disserueth thyng many greke streueth bycause oonly suche occasyon exemplefye presumpcyon folyly atame haue tolde agayne god bolde shall repente sooner weneth many man harmene meneth suffreth vengeaunce trespasse one firste auctour goth nat quyte alone many offence abayth ceryously guydo wryt sayth suynge ordre wofull auenture euery greke homewarde dyde endure hye lowe sparynge none estate welfull infortunate bothe theyr woo theyr welfare right fyll storye shall declare grece whylom worthy kynge manly ryche prudent oflyuynge hadde sothe lyke wryt guydo tyme worthy sone two pallamydes eldest brother oetes called tother bothe twayne one moder borne storye reherseth hath toforne pallamydes noble knyght full famous eke power myght fer spoke many sondry coost hadde also grekes hoost wysedome whylom gouernayle ala slayne batayle thorugh vnhap martys cruell tene whan sonne shone bryght shene knyghthode worthynesse lyke tofore storye bereth wytnesse deth doth playnely specefye nowe malys hatrede enuye suche haue tunges infortunate make oonly kynge naulus debate grekes contryued haue newe hye treason false full vntrewe soth neuer wrought effect ymagyned thought false thynge yfeyned malyce kynge manly wyse prudent pallamydes shulde enuye god wot causeles sege troye cyte vpon nyght falsely murdred slaughter lothsome dede vlixes dyomede fully wrought ye haue herde deuyse whiche euery herte ought agryse false also tale haue fayned kyng naulus haue traytoursly coplayned albe dede neuer mente grekes also assente murdre conspyracyon menelay agamenon albe sothe euery ele false hanged hye halfe tale forge contryue make frendes causeles stryue thorugh fraude false collusyon kynge naulus put suspecyon grekes hadde conspyred douteles vpon murdre pallamydes makyng theyr groude dyd fayne fro troye sent lettres twayne pallamydes inmedyatly dyrect whiche concluded treason effect hye estat falsly allyed confederat troye sume golde haue fayned ytolde hadde cyte good receyued huge quantyte fyne oonly grekes betraye prolonge platly delaye sege gettynge towne engyne medyacyowne conferme sentence make naulus gyue full credence sayd playnely conclusyowne lettres whiche sent fro towne yfounde enclosed shelde vpon knyght yslayne felde comprehendynge hole trecherye treason full confederacye atwene towne pallamydes veryly though gylteles gyue open euydence make prefe great offence sayde vlixes affermynge certayne accorded chaumberlayne offyce pallamydes wonder secrete thynge reckeles assente conspyracye wrongly compassyd brennynge hote enuye behotynge hym guerdon great mede lyke deuyse execute dede take treasour sume gode full secretely knyt hode hyd whan voyded prees vnder bedde pallamydes put grekes suerte treasoure quantyte ne myght denyed lyke lettres hadde specyfyed whan founde knowe thorugh hoost noysed yblowe bothe lettres golde also fro poynt poynt accordynge bothe two whiche kynge assentynge treasowne receyued hadde troye towne assented ye haue herde telle grekes tho lenger wolde dwelle shope forth one entent haste came vnto tent kynge full innocent clene lytell knewe wolde mene vpon hym full knyghtly stode theyr ire furyously wode venged loude gan crye may man theyr malyce modefye hym mercyles fynde moste specyall kynge menelay agamenon oonly meued indignacyon wolde haue proceded vnto iugement hasty rancoure withoute auysement treason auenged bee nat withstandynge hye degree sothenesse whan worthy kynge conceyued hath malyce werkynge firste astoned inwarde syght sodaynely stert vp lyke knyght wyse worthy pallamydes hardy lyon amyd prees thynge agaste hym knyghtly gan expresse playnely sayde wolde nat refuse acquyte hym selfe horryble caas nat exceptynge worthy byrthe blode hye kynrede deuoydynge knyghthode mahede gaue lyfe deth fors tofore iuparde cors within felde lyste ordeyne lyke knyght quarell dareyne lyst durste vndertake excepcyon hym lyked none make hye lowe bolde preue reason haue tolde besechynge make delay prolonge hym day manly requerynge may haste falsly thynge compaste answere stoned echone hoost nat one hardy shall nat feyne chaump close quarell dareyne nouther vlixes nouther dyomede chefe worker foule dede pbut vlixes customable euery thynge deceyuable double werke full aye disceyte lyke serpent lyeth awayte whiche vnder floures glyde trace right vlixes fayned face whan sawe knyghtly hye prowesse manly chere hardynesse hye renowne pallamydes anone falshede put hym selfe prees lyke frende mente nat wele brotell glasse pretendynge outwarde stele one firste gan hym excuse counsayllynge longer muse matere theyr alder ease crafte gan appease touchynge rumoure hye treason hath voyded suspecyon theyr hertes concludynge tertayne accusynge made vayne conspyred oonly hatrede albe hym selfe roote dede pbut whan sawe myght nat acheue ye haue herde worthy kynge greue spot treason hym laye hehath anone founde another waye assent fully dyomede vnder pretense playnely frendelyhede comynge hym agayne certayne nyght vndersuraunce trewe knyght counsayle kepe outher sote soure enformynge hym great treasoure golde good infynyte ryches hym discured vnder secretenes whiche sothly man dyde knowe hyd enclosyd welle lowe within felde lytell syde whiche hym lyste fro hym nat hyde truste vnto hym discure wolde besy cure nyght hym go vnto welle thre mo fette away great sume gode sothe thynge vnderstode mente assentyd anone thre togydre gone vnto well lyke haue tolde moste manly bolde pallamydes lyke hym telle descended lowe welle supposynge haue treasour founde ala hym falsly confounde haue murdred hym wt stone great huge botome hauynge refuge wha acomplysshed entent repeyred eueryche tent tale storye telleth v feyned ye kynge naulus touchynge deth pallamydes desclaundre gylteles vlixes dyomede innocent platly rede grekes bothenygh ferre slayne knyghtly werre durynge sege parys arowe false fayne full narowe fynde tale neuer yet thought treason shuld haue wrought touchynge lettres sent towne suche conspyracyowne grekes wrought fable vnsoth falsly feyned make naulus wroth vlixes dyomede also agamenon grekes mo lette homewarde theyr waye hyndre also saye repeyre theyr regyons naulus occasyons oetes sone manly man accorded may one assent auenge mercyles cruell murdre pallamydes ordayne theyr home passage worke fully theyr damage grekes muste necessyte homewarde sayle foreby countre wherfore kynge shapen hath wyle hyl e hye lytell yle wynter season euery maner nyght make fyres sette vp lyght cause see erre grekes sawe fyre ferre vnware harme caste lande coude perell vnderstande shope theyr full myght aryue faste lyght wherwith ij hondred theyr shyppes brake amonge rockes fully go wrake drowned many worthy man thus vengaunce alderfirste began kynge naulus hath grekes take deedly hate sone sake great myschefe confusyon grekes nauye agamenon great perell deth escaped hadde almoste amonge beiaped erles duke worthy kynges crowned thorugh trayne see drowned menelay also dyomede escaped myschefe rede whan daunger gone oetes wood foryre one herte shope another wyle thought wolde agamenon begyle compassynge full mortall stryfe let sende lettre anone wyfe myghty great agamenon whiche included false treason euen lyke shall nat lye thus effect dyde specyfye firste hir lorde agamenon kynge hadde sege wrought wonder thynge preiudyce sclaundre hir name albe hir maner blame lyke wrote platly trespace knyghtly honoure foly difface say guydo telleth thus loued doughter kynge pryamus beaute hadde hir wyfe take hir herte fynally forsake worthy quene whylom great fame clemestra sothly hir name wonder semely right fayre descent borne stocke royall hir celly nge eke hir excellence albe neuer dyde offence yet hir lorde newe fangylnesse toke nother lettres dyde expresse fully purpose anone repayre though clemestra bothe good fayre sodaynely hir exyle londe many thousande myle warnynge hir prudent substaunce sentement oetes wrote vnto quene albe kynge innocent clene hir fore lyuynge louynge trewe maner thynge hir please passynge ententyfe worde dede durynge lyfe fer oughte reason desyred lettres falsly conspyred haue hir put parcas innocence gyue hasty credence thankynge firste oetes trouthe goodly hym lyst haue routhe vpon hir wronge hye compassyon yet storye maketh mencyon afterwarde shall descryue falsest one alyue vnto hir lorde longe absence haste made stronge ffence agayne thynge gan hir purueye suche fraude nat ne deye hir werke sothe wyte whiche ala muste anone endyte storye platly doth lere whiche dolefull mortall ovnsure truste worldly glorye wt sodayne chauge put memorye ioye vnstable vayne ambycyon vnware tourne reuersed vp downe ydell fame blowe vp skye ouer whelmyd twynclynge eye pompe boste tryumphe victorye lyke shadowe waste transytorye fortune false vnassured man neuer fully lured hye lowe maner estate bonde fayth conferate agayne whose myght man may hydiffende tourne shall discende whan syt hyest thyne vnstable whele thy brotyll fauour forged nat stele meynt allayed mutabylyte welfulnesse false felycyte sodayne sweygh frowarde yu canst auale fresshe chere anger pale hye disdayne thou sparest degree prynces duke hyest theyr see myghty kynges worthy emperours rychest reygne theyr royall floures sceptre crowne yu canst pull downe take wytnesse agamenowne noble myghty lyue sondry auctours hye renown descryue sothfastly excellence myght nat make diffence kynges baner sewe conspyred murdre voyde eschewe rescuse none coude make whiche ala penne fele quake doth myn ynke blotte boke myghty god thyne inwarde loke seest euery thynge thurgh thy eternal myght wylt thou nat equyte ryght punysshe chastyse horryble thynge specyally murdre kynge ala payne ixyon helle mane sathan dwelle nat egall equypolent venge murdre suffycyent excedeth comparyson felonye falshede treason wherfore lorde seest knowest thorugh thy power eternall suffre suche lyue vpon ye grounde worse tygre cerberus hounde chayned lyeth bounde helle gate whiche malyce playnely though hate berketh firste offence murdre gladly wrought sylence men aduerte take kepe ala prynce sle hym slepe pyllowe whan slepeth softe cryeth wreche hye god lofte axeth vengaunce take faste though abyde wyll laste ala kynge spoken ferre worthy outwarde werre cruell fate passynge odyous disposed hath owne hous mortall ende execute agaynst whiche refute right shyppe londe sette quene clemestra ye stronde hy mette humble chere loke full benygne shewed full many faythfull sygne wyfely trouthe hir countenauce albe herte varyaunce nat parceyued playnely hir face kynge goodly dyde enbrace soth trouthe mente paleyse hye way went nat aduertynge treason shape whiche ala myght nat escape falshede coude thynge fele ne may lenger concele agayne hir lorde clemestra wrought hir bonde wedlocke ne thought trewe loke sothly spousayle agayne hir malyce lytell myght auayle vnto hir lorde hir trouthe conserue newfangelnesse caused streue hir olde fayth hir assuraunce hir loue abode fykyll chaunce longe absence hadde hir herte appalled loued one egistus called whiche afore hir grace stode nouther byrthe blode lytell nought reputacyowne renowned manhode renowne knyghthode hye prowesse labour besynesse good awayte vpon hir nyght therfore best furthrede hir syght suche drede hadde lyue alone sorowles well coude grone nat say lyfe ladde except hym doughter hadde exyona guydo sayth hyght vnto hym clemestra behyght assurynge hym vpon payne hir hede shulde reygne whan hir lorde dede enhaste conclusyon hir worthy lorde kynge agamenon nexte nyght murdred yssayne false egistus quene full fayne lenger bode storye lere haste wedded yfere hir false sleyghty compassynge messene made hym crowned kynge put hym full possessyon ala synne hath domynacyon furthre wronge abate ryght worlde falshede hath myght full ofte sythe hath rightwysenesse estate sette worthynesse loo synne auoutrye brought murdre conspyracye synne vpon synne lynked twayne enbraced fendes chayne perpetuelly helle endure ala shall hymselfe full assure fro cruell murdre body withdrawe whan kynges theyr bed slawe whiche bryngeth alyenacyon extort tytle false successyon may coloure pretense seme full straytely god shall deme iustly venge dewe recompence intrusyon brought vyolence felly quyte suche horryble thynges sodayne slaughter specyally kynges greatly drede euery regyon fynde agamenon clemestra false double quene hadde sone passynge fayre sene right gracyous euery mannes syght horestes boke sayth hyght wonder semely yonge age great fere mortall rage lyste slayne drede anulle tytle nat succede hym preserue nat shent kynge taltybus power hath hym sent full secretely countre vnto kynge called ydume helde sceptre royall sete full myghtely lande crete carkasys named quene hadde doughter called eke clymene borne heyre regyon made eke mencyon horestes reken thynge quene also kynge cherysshed well storye lere clymen theyr owne doughter dere eke kept hadde cherte fro poynt poynt lyke degre attendaunce conuenyent dewe estate euer vpon hym sewe suche moste expert sage gouerne hym tyll came age reioyse god gaue hym myght herytage whiche hadde ryght clere discent happy chaunce thus leue hym vnder gouernaunce yonge lone agamenon muste make dygressyon pfro mater telle dyomede auentures guydo rede wofull fate paynes smerte whiche ala myght nat asterte remembred playnely wrytynge oeres sone ryche kynge called naulus ye haue herde toforne suche heuynesse herte hath borne vnto grekes repeyrynge home fro troye luste inwarde ioye hyndre bothe hye lowe cause nat vnknowe passynge enuyous wyll thought ylyke desyrous myght sothly le deth venge pallamydes lyke tofore stroye deuyse prudent wyse oetes malyce wrought traytoursly newe menes sought myght maner weye dyomedes vnwarely destroye thynge caste nat fayle ceryously make rehersayle grece kyngdome wyde large conyumpt one calydonye arge full habundaunt rychesse rente whiche kynge called pollente worthy man noble fame sone assandrus name doughter passynge fayre syght sothly egra fynde hyght hir fader lyke wryt guydo hadde nomo thyse childre two hath wysedome prouyded myghty reygne deuyded atwene two dissees eche parte lyue pee exclude fro indigence nede wyfe vnto dyomede albe tofore storye hym sayde whylom loued well crysayde nat say doublenesse well wot guydo bereth wytnesse boke sothely sayth none assandrus owne wyues brother full lusty fresshe full manlyhede troye wente dyomede see fordyuen vp downe ryued vp regyon called boece disconsolate tempest dryue wery full mate refresshe none thynge whiche lande thelephus kynge whose ryuayle whan herde sayne herte hadde hye disdayne bolde great offence entre grounde hauynge lycence yet sothe dyde damage hye lowe maner age nortoke nat myght disauayle vnto lande vytayle whiche payde iustly fyne flesshe fysshe brede wyne yet indignacyowne kynge thelephus descended downe great array harme myght gan bycker fyght assandrus full hye prowesse lyke lyon fomen gan oppresse wonder knyghtly ye feld vpon wan slewe day many worthy man hye courage manly pryde whan kynge whiche stode asyde sawe men slayne euery parte hye disdayne hent anone darte caste hym ala mortall fate cyd hath thurgh mayles thurgh plate assandrus felle downe dede soyle aboute blode rede deedly wounde began blede wood tygre tho came dyomede hym auenge bare hym lyke knyght sleeth kylleth put vnto flyght suche sorowe gan make knyghtly routhe brothres sake ne wyste best fynde myd wo beste foule deed corp saue lyke estate lette make graue buryed hym rytes olde oetes suster tolde slayne fraude dyomede fyne myght full possede reygne arge hole without stryfe purpartye annexed wyfe deth myght season take tolde hir eke forsake fayre egra hir womenhede hir lorde called dyomede tolde helle chayned ouermore forged hath fayned enuye assandrus lost lyfe howe hir lorde hath take nother wyfe hir dishonour shame passyngly great sclaundre hir name preiudyce ydone hir estate tolde make debate lyke wrote conclusyon clemestra agamenon whiche hir herte made sore greue put hir fully byleue treason ye haue herde tolde yre pale wexe colde vnkyndenesse hir herte sleeth heuynesse hir brothre deth neuer yet guydo doth assure woman loued better creature loued hym maner age firste nought sette hir herytage comparyson hir brothres lyfe loo oetes made newe stryfe ye haue herde storye rede gylteles worthy dyomede whan hath longe sege layne kyngdome wold haue come agayne myghty honde worthy quene hir lyeges assentyd bene exyled regyon may made medyacyon thus hym selfe mate dispeyred disconsolate agayne repeyred salerne londe great rychesse tenter thorugh worthynesse crowne sceptre hadde reygned longe lyeges knyghtes stronge brother apax thelamon murdred tofore made mencyon dyomede pore destytute may salerne fynde refute whan tenter firste gan hym espye sewed hym full great enuye hauynge hym aye suspecyon touchynge deth kynge thelamon dyomede certayne nyght full secretly hath taken hym flyght fro salerne faste gan hym hye hope fynde better remedye helpe socoure place fortune wolde graunte hym grace hymselfe ashamed confuse man forsake abiect refuse right fared wandrynge fro ne wyst best bvt fynde troyan eneas al whyle styll troye oonly routhe compassyowne supporte lefte towne beynge alway theyr lyfe doute theyr fomen rounde beset aboute lyued lacke hede contynuelly myschefe drede knowynge refute comforte caas tyll counsayle eneas supporte great nede sent haste dyomede knowynge full well desolacyon proscrip fro regyon besechynge hym manhode routhe hym enhaste without slouthe stuffe get souldeours also manly euery man without abode troye lede socoure great nede dyomede came taryed nought theyr request besought releue sharpe shoure hym brought many souldeoure eneas way hym mette frendely wyse towne hym fette hym made passyngly great chere gan comune yfere theyr auentures bothe lande see entermedlyd great aduersyte man may deuoyde eschewe take parte hym dewe sorte hap doth brydell lede storye shortly procede cely troyans almost shent theyr fomen yles adiacent besette aboute enuyrowne thorugh manhode hye renowne dyomede souldeours knyghtes noble werry reskued holpen vtterly foure dayes foughte knyghtly wyse deffendynge cyree thorugh prowesse also enee slewe toke withstode diffence troyanysshe blode suche fonde cyte false henge vp hye halse punysshed theyr great wronge dyomede thus gan wexe stronge longe processe made mencyowne chefe protectoure nowe troye towne enmye none large space durste abyde hadde grace lygaunce made loute thus name sprede gan aboute fame great oppynyon dylated vnto regyon swyfte reporte calydonye arg whiche quene greatly gan charge astoned whan taketh hede power gan myght drede lyste wolde hir londe vpon hir wynne knyghthode werre newe begynne secretely gan muse thynge hir lorde hir myghty kynge late exyled yput flyght hath grace founde fortune syght remounted hye estate wherof hir selfe chekmate wayes caste prudent hole aduyse hir parlement without grutchynge rebellyon hym reuoke regyon pand therupon hym lowly sent lettres messager forth went cause annullyng exyled fully reconcyled hole assente lyeges alle full lowly euerychone calle theyr offence theyr trespace without rygoure grace anone lyke manly knyght mercy sothly ryght whan hath theyr sonde well conceyued theyr menynge fully apparceyued stynte stryfe thought beste goodly wyse grauute theyr requeste reygne within certayne day repeyred full ryche array whose comynge full glad lyeges bene reconcyled bothe quene rancoure olde offence oonly wysdome put suspence one herte blysfull lyfe lede troye boke hym rede lette hym lyue felycytee agayne resortynge tell enee hath tyme spent whiche fro troye wt many troyan went shyppes stuffed meynee sayled forth many straunge see many daunger many strayte passage tofore aryued cartage ledynge hym fader anchyses way fynde le wyfe crewsa fatall auenture woo dyde endure lyste ceryously sene falsehede quene mene dido womanhede floure gaue hym hir rychesse treasoure iewellys golde myght hym please euery thynge myght hym ease vnkynde rede eneydos ye shall fynde falsely stale away nyght tyme whyle bedde lay conqueste also itaylle hadde many stronge bataylle auentures workes fyne hym fall ye may se full souerayne style fro poynt poynt compyled virgyle wryte made sythen go full yore troye boke speketh hym procedeth shall endyte horestes caste hym quyte fadres deth playnely nat spare ye lyste guydo shall declare requered equyte ryght iuge moste myght egally holdeth balaunce deth conspyred vengaunce voyse blode doth aye contune crye wreche clamour importune sothe iniustly shede murdre wrought wyll haue egal mede guerdon hath disseruyd may nat flee iugement reseruyd hym sytte hyest trone beholdeth hym selfe alone full rightfully noble myghty kynge though suffre foryet thynge consydereth inspeccyon murdre agamenon myghty lorde yt souerayne gode made mynystre blode pyonge horestes full hye prowesse execute dome ryght wysnesse gaue hym grace power myght anone toke ordre knyght lyke tolde whan foure twenty wynter olde fresshe lusty wonderly prudent wardely desyrous entent fortune wolde hym nat withsayne herytage recure agayne pwhiche egistus falsly hym denyeth crowne iustly occupyeth false tytle hir wyfe horestes wyll iuparde lyfe auenture whyle hym lasteth breth firste venged fadres deth vpon tho treason wrought alderfirste full lowely besought kynge ydumee goodlyhede forther hym great nede kynge benygnely anone assigned hath hym gone thousande knyghtes manly right stronge redresse great horryble wronge egistus wroughte vyolence wysedome dylygence horestes gan hym purueye within whyle seye hym gat store wyll nat lye another thousande companye worthy knyghtes one accorde go hym wt theyr souerayne lorde euery thynge byddynge obeye ye haue herde egistus werreye thus horestes full ryche array gan hoostey made delay lodgynge alderfirste gan chese cytee called troyese receyued great reuernece kynge named forence manly knyght bookes specefye bare herte passynge great enuye egistus double occasyon firste deth agamenon eke hadde doughter dere hym wardly entere good fayre yonge age whylom gyuen maryage egistus doubylnesse false treason new fangylnesse kynges doughter hath vtterly forsake haste dyd lybell make forge wryt repulsyon albe hadde trewe occasyon egistus hir forsoke saue falsly wyue toke quene clemestra agayne ryght lawe whan assent murdred haue slawe gamenon tofore tolde whylom myghty bolde hatefull false conspyracye well murdre auoutrye venge bothe dewe recompence worthy knyght myghty kyng forence offrede horestes make hym stronge go hym helpe venge wronge hym ladde armed bryght stele foure hondred knyghtes horsed wonder wele takynge felde manly chere horestes kynge yfere ryden forthe many manly man pbut horestes werre gan whan bryght phebus bole shone temple full lowely gone goddes best wyse humble herte dyde sacryfyse fully hope better fare bode lyfe deth spare without mercy remyssyon deth venge agamenon clemestra moste wyte make firste swerde byte moder hondes twayne ouer besy payne without pyte mercye shewe smale peces tyll hewe dismembred sonder ioynt fro ioynt eke foryet nat poynt iustly punysshe rygoure ryght egistus eke false vntrewe knyght nat slowe neclygent execute comaundement goddes lyst falle horestes knyghtes alle forensis myghty kynge also one herte sege go cyte called methene within whiche false quene clemestra god gyue hir harde grace whan horestes seged hath place knyghtes set rounde aboute false existus yryden oute gadre men wreke falle vpon sege breke myght maner syde great stuffe thus gan ryde takynge vp men euery coost tyll hym made full myghty hoost horeste whiche sege lay gouernaunce espyeth day day sent men full sage stoppe wayes lette passage made knyghtes full huge route pursue hym euery coste aboute sege man fully begonne assaute hath towne wonne entrede nyght full late sette wardes stronge euery gate doungeon moste strong pryncypall byldynge myghty royall horestes firste moder fonde quene clemestra lady londe whiche drede sore gan quake mercyles anone made hir take put chaynes tyll nexte morowe egistus god gyue hym euyll sorowe stuffe myght accroche towarde towne fast gan approche purpose full horestes greue within sodaynely releue sothe myght nat auayle cyte myght abayle horestes knyghtes vnwarely haue hym mette attones proudely hym sette firste slewe men put flyght taken hym maugre myght chaynes lyke hym fynde mercyles full faste hym bynde shet hym vp fetryd prysowne false founde towne assentyd wynynge helpynge murdre worthy kynge great werkers conspyratours agayne theyr lorde rysynge traytours take bounde rygoure nyght shet vp toure tyll morowe lyke lot drawe eueryche vnder fonge lawe lyke decerte excepcyon none whan nyght passed gone phebus role esswarde spere tour shone full bryght clere pwhan clemestra rote falsehede brought forthe quakynge hir drede horestes iugement yfet swerde sharpe kene whet lyke goddes charged hym toforne peces smale hath hir shorne made hir bere townes boundes vouryd bestes houndes pyte none breste reseruyd quyt hir fully hath disseruyd fro poynt poynt forgat right nought tha chayned egistus forth brought iustly dempt rygour lawe herdell naked drawe thorugh towne myght se hye hanged tree rot drye agayne sonne loo howe murdre hath guerdon wonne loo falsehede master awake traytours towne ytake galowes enhonged euerychone tyll seueryd sonder bone fro bone hye hylle agayne sterres shene thus towne fro treason purgyd clene trouthe augmentyd ymoryd reygne horestes full restoryd storye sewynge shall expowne daye whan toke crowne whan myste euery cloudy skye false treason conspyracye tryed vpon euery syde falsehede hadde place abyde storye sayth ordre rehersynge tyme menelay kynge see full wawes fro troyewarde aryued crete frely escapyd many drede peyne quene goodly fresshe eleyne cause famous fayre great prees meruayllous repayre fro euery parte hir beaute beholde troye walles nat full olde destroyed noble royall towne many man full worthy renowne hath loste lyfe may man say nay eleyne wyfe menelay whan thynge done may none wha kyng knew fully brother gamenon murdre euerydele full tryste lyked thynge wele inwardly felte full great smerte neuewe hadde also herte mene horestes mercyles lyke tyraunt graceles modre slewe pyte morrall yre cruelte fully caste wolde blyue sceptre crowne platly hym depryue full affermynge hatefull caas lawe vnworthy faders reygne heyre possede iustely consydred horryble dede attones furyous wrothe without abode vnto shyp gothe melancolyke great tene crete saylnge athene toke londe shyppes borde pwhere duke nestor gouernour lorde whiche receyueth lyke gentyll knyght power dylygence myght menelaye rancoure great hete gan duke secretely trete fynde mene inwarde syght depryue horestes ryght therupon haue iugement athene holde parlement lordes regyon gyue theron diffynycyon whiche shewed openly ynoughe horestes owne modre sloughe maner great offence hym selfe tho beynge presence whan thynge fully dyde espye partye gan agayne replye felte hym frely large hym allegynge hadde charge goddes shortly declare mortall swerde nat ne spare vpon clemestra roote false treason slewe hir lorde kynge agamenon murdre thorugh hir malys wrought wherfore horestes humbly besought lordes manly herte equyte consydre aduerte malyce rancoure rage hym depryue herytage syth sone agamenon borne heyre regyon ye haue herde called methene albe moder clemestra quene compassyd hadde destruccyon duke nestor ymeuyd reason susteynynge horestes ryght rose vp anone lyke manly knyght offrynge hym selfe proudely sake hye quarell vndertake body deth darreyne lyst tytle withseyne none companye durste worde agayne hym replye hoole stode oppynyon knyghtly medyacyon bare hym feynynge thynge horestes ycrowned kynge meneste beynge assent whan dissolued parlement horestes lyeges trewe receyued crowne newe treate lordes many one kynge menelay made atone gan theyr ire theyr rancourelete ydumee worthy kynge crete prudently gouerneth matere hermyone yonge doughter dere menelay quene eleyne yonge fresshe beaute souereyne yweddyd without tariynge horestes newe lusty kynge bycause allyaunce deuoyded rancour distaunce atwene kynges menelay olde horestes right tolde thus leue beste eche reygne lyue pea reste stryfe ceasyd caas erygona doughter egistus ye haue herde telle sorowe drede lyste lenger dwelle toke rope lyst thynge spare therwithall gan hir selfe gnare storye sayth hye vpon tree hir fyne ye gette wyll forth ceryously entreate storye telle greate ovlixes ordre wrytynge thyne auentures come rynge full wonderfull londe see entermedlyd great aduersytee guydo firste descryuynge thy repayre sayth thou founde weder foule fayre agreable thonder sowne stylle smothe wt clwdes frowne sayth also thou dyddest ordayne thy passage myghty shyppes twayne apparaylled marchaundyse thou myghtest moste secrete wyse euery myschefe see escape pbut thou haddest felle iape auctour thy resorte doth wryte sayth vlixes wordes whyte yrobbed rychesse gode contraryous wynde agayne hym stode dryue confusyon myghty stronge regyon thelamon reygned lyue hent take blyue pby myghty honde sesyd brest mercyles put vnder arest hym hadde suspect workynge touchynge murdre kynge wroughte sleyghty wyle tale sette suche style playnely hath iaped fro theyr honde freely escaped except queynt fare treasour ymade full bare passage hym vnkouthe fyll agayne wolfe mouthe veryly specyfyed kynge naulus men haue hym eft espyed take bounde chayned mercyles murdre kynge pallamydes storye reherseth certayne prudence scaped agayne bothe expert wyse olde though maner nat fully tolde escape thorugh besy payne daunger kynges twayne tyll thurgh fortune came fro myschefe fre presence kynge ydume symple array torne apparayle wherof kynge greatly gan meruayle tose pouert lowe manere made hym good chere though tyme infortunate hym receyueth lyke estate whan bothe twayne alone complaynynge vlixes made mone vnto kynge full sage ceryously sorte passage face sad sobre chere fro poynt poynt anone ye shall lorde quod shortly expresse truste haue gentyllesse shall myn auentures alle reherse right falle firste whan troye londe forsoke water shyppes toke anone wynde pesyble blowe yle whiche vnknowe called mirma great hab daunce thynge plesaunce may syluer golde bought redy founde wanted right nought abode full longe whyle ioye treasoure gat troye shyppes stuffed men hole sounde comodyte ylke gounde lyked countre enuyron disporte recreacyon tariynge thought nat full longe man dyde vnto v wronge tyll daye eyer styll wynde also fully wyll sayled forth quyete pee vnto porte called claustafages wherwith meyne longe many day founde thynge accordynge pay weder lusly agreable fayre may truste outher wynde ayre vpon fayth smothe skye agayne shyppe faste gan hye taryed nought toke anone see smothe calme endurynge dayes three weder founde lacke sodaynely heuen tourneth blacke hydous tempest wawes grene hope haue dispeyred clene troubled spirite made pensyfe without refute escape lyfe tossyd dryuen many sondry yle tyll laste caste vp cecyle recurynge londe great annoye payne tyme reygned kynges twayne remebre douteles tone called sorygenes whiche vnto full contraryous tother named coclopas bretherne byrthe conclusyon ylyke cruell condycyon though sorte hadde shape none bothe twayne fylle attones oppressynge full great distresse spoyled shyppes treasour rychesse pyte lyked nat spare tyll lefte destytute bare good ala mortall chaunce moste greuaunce whan golde may nomore restrayne sent downe myghty sone twayne alypham full large longe polypheme myghty gyaut stronge men auenge fayne haue hondred slayne disarayed stonde diffence malyce sodayne vyolence toke myschefe almost lorne alphenor myn owne brother sworne hatefully haue v founde chaynes caste stockes bounde ylocked pryson make platly mencyon myghty man great polypheme suster hadde shortly deme one fayrest euer yet borne myght beaute besette aforne nature hir gaue suche prerogatyfe clene mayde sothly wyfe flourynge bothe fayrenesse bounte alphenor whan dyde se albe fetred pryson loue loste wyt eke reason wexe mad narowe dyd hy bynde saue vpon hir alway mynde closed aye peryllous wounde syxe monthes thus lay bounde say platte trouthe tyll polypheme hadde vpon v outhe thorugh grace medyacyon quyt v fre pryson shewed v mercy pyte sorowe great humanyte alphenor ylyke one entent bronde cupyde brent felte parte many mortall fyt tyll wrought sotyll wyt nyght leef loth stale mayde way goth thorugh helpe men wt hym tyme morowe houre pryme polyphemus gan v sewe whose myghty honde myght nat eschewe suche assaute v gan make force haue mayde take alphenor mauge rage polypheme vnto damage knyghtes sore vpon lay myght vnneth scape away saue selfe compassyd enuyron deth pursued champyon whan sawe gayne fle deth shortly sayne whyle geaunt freesly sette swerde eye smette vnto shyp companye fledde haste man myght espye pwhere came alphenor fere whan wawes gan clere gracyous wynde gan v wake countre haue anone forsake nat holsome v abyde pbut man lyke wryt ouyde polyphemus geaunt drede hadde eye amyd forhede whiche vlixes smote stroke lyke browes braunched oke heer longe berde loke childre aferde whan hadde lost syght amonge hylles ronneth day nyght rage fynde hym refuge caste rockes great stone huge euery parte enuyron countre vlixes auenged thus sayth ouyde conclusyon boke transformacyon methamorphoseos ye may se whan euer leyser ce yously storye rede wrytynge forth wyll procede vlixes face deed pale ydumee tolde forth tale ersynge thus supprysed awaked fro polypheme whan escaped thorugh vnhappe infelycyte yle myddes see dryue whan gan nyght elodiu lytell kyngdome hyght pwhere circe great enchaunteresse thylke tyme lady goddesse th coude hir crafte wonderly forme sodaynely man transforme haue lykenesse lese reason horse bere tygre lyon wolfe fox hir lyste deuyse hir dredefull craft shapen suche wyse myghty hir straunge pocyons hir letuaryes confeccyons also fayre vpon se fro hir power man myght fle werke sorceresse founcyd vpon hir fayrenesse fynally thus stode yere hir abode playnely hadde power none myght departe nouther day nyght lusty lyfe ladde whiche tyme childe hadde right inly fayre goodly syght thelagonyus sothenesse hyght whiche afterwarde well reherse processe wexe manly man sotyle secrete prouydence hir crafte hadde experyence maugre hir enchauntementes olde stale away myght nat holde fynally fate conclude connynge hir crafte gan delude men scaped fro hir honde went large fre hir londe thynge lytell dyd auayle way gan sayle sleyghte lytell whyle yblowe vp yle pwhere calypha suster circe crowned quene helde hir sceptre pee whose craftes myghty stronge maugre wyll helde full longe sothe speke womanhede bounte fredome goodlyhede surely hadde souerayne excellence myne abode none offence euer crye clappe laste scaped fro hir trappe came yle right lyne whiche specyally thorugh hye power dyuyne ordeyned yore myracle spirituall oracle man haue temple sodayne answere hym lyst enquere questyons demaundes alle soules shall eke befalle whan men dede grauen vnderstone gan axe temple anone myn auentures shulde sewe man myght fate eschewe lyke myn entent hadde answere full conuenyent saue befalleth whan soule gone diffynycyon vnto none thyng assoyle accordeth nat ryght reseruyd vnto goddes myght excedeth reason wyt man fro thense forth sayle gan dryuen wynde parte socoured lyke haue deuoured karybdes profounde welle syrenes meremaydenes dwelle fro brest scale syluer shene theyr shape fysshes fresshe clene ouer kynde doth compasse appere femynyne face lyke virgyns nature without spot vndefouled pure custome wawes flete songe heuenly swete aungelyke full armonye veryly sugred melodye rauysshe wolde man lyue inly ioye almoste herte ryue make man sodayne hye plesaunce foryet hym selfe lese remembraunce deuoyde hym clene owne thought tyll vnwarely myschefe brought theyr songe take kepe shall brought mortall slepe anone may nat withdrawe wyll drenche shyp lowe vnder wawe thus swetnesse theyr heuenly sowne bryngeth man con fusyowne euer theyr boundes passe pbut lyfe scaped grace myn eres waxe gummes clere stopped ne myght touche werble theyr instrumentis wherby reason man blynded fynally thorugh sotylte men escaped fre saylynge forth mate werynesse tyll came vp full great distresse phenyce toke anone londe caste anker shyppes bonde sothly fyll v full vnfayre people cruell contrayre oonly malyce fyll anone slewe men almoste euerychone tresoure good lytell hadde berafte ladde fewe left lyue toke put pryson blyue thus hath fortune lad hir daunce lytell ioye plente myschaunce whose daunger lernyd experte fall mychefe pouerte great dole sorowe full breest see londe southe nat eest come vnto presence haue declaryd playnely sentence myn auentures worthynesse truste oonly faythfulnesse haue specyall haue rehersyd tolde hyghnesse beste wyse without dothe suffyse though hert constrayned sore thylke tyme vlixes spake helde pea full heuy lokynge ydumeus lyke gentyll kynge comforted hym euer myght besy herte lyght hym besought heuynesse lete longe hym lyste crete hym abyde made hym suerte shulde fare also well nat wante may hym ease whan sorowe gan apease cage drewe vnto ende leue toke sayde wolde wende tha londe home countre firste kynge fredome bounte gaue vnto hym great rychesse array euer pay golde treasour many thynges partynge thyse two kynges shyppes whan hym lyste sayle redy stuffyd meyne vytayle thus vlixes gan hym redy make whan hath leue fully take hasted hym toke anone see gan sayle towarde countree firste wente kynge alphenon whiche passyngly hadde affeccyon se vlixes home comynge desyrous ouer thynge haue hym newely aqueyntaunce vnto hym inly great plesaunce hym talke eloquence wysdome hye prudence smerte receyued playnely glad herte euer yet maner man sythen tyme worlde began encrease felycytee herde firste penolopee trewe wyfe without spot blame yet grene noble fame whiche hir lorde longe absence thought dede neuer dyde offence sothly bothe chere dede thorugh grece exaumple womanhede yet bokes lyste expresse thorugh world myrour fayrenesse amonge grekes borne hyest blode called auctours bothe fayre gode yet say bookes hir doutlees neuer none hadde great prees hir kept chaungynge newe vnto hir lorde euer ylyke trewe herte aye one nat parted twayne called quene souerayne wyfely trouthe bokes olde ofte fynde hir herte wolde colde tourne pale fro hir lorde ferre hir closet werre drede hadde fro fere eke quake fantasyes hir lordes sake absence bothe eue morowe deth vnto hir importable sorowe aye sothe ioye game whan fyll herde ectors name place anone fylle swowne gan hir selfe teres drowne womanhede ferde slaughter mortall swerde lyste hir lorde knyghtly surquedye hadde fortune falle ieopardye hap sorte mette worthy knyght selde neuer felte hir herte lyght many dreme nyghtes dyde hir gaste whyle sege laste euery play venym hir syght whan hir owne knyght worlde ioye hadde none hye lowe playnely one whose sake myrthe refuseth herte museth woman thynge gode melancolye meuyd blode let hym aduerte wysdome ysee remembre penolopee decert lyste blamyd guydo thou shuldest ashamyd say wyues thynge wele good fayth ferre fele though one two amonge offence good thorugh hir prouydence therof thynge wyte thoughe guydo boke endyte varyaunce eleyne creseyde medea sorowe deyde let agayne right equytee wyfely trouthe penolopee maydenhode yonge polycene goodnesse eccuba quene cassandra eke stedefastnesse take kyndenesse pantasylle without varyaunce put togydre balaunce ye shall fynde ye lyste accounte maugre grutcheth trouth shal surmoute dare afferme bere away pryse wyll man replye wyse feble oppynyon whyle vlixes alphenon hym made relacyon hatefull conspiracyon certayne lordes enuyron countree bauysshe wold quene penolopee maugre tho agayne albe euer ylyke playne hir trouthe stedfaste wall yet haue caste platly shall take force may nat eschewed haste reskewed caste tyme nat aiourne day nyght hir soiourne inly herte loue disamayde wysedome hath delayde none manly sage coude hir gette auauntage auyse hir werkynge whan vlixes conceyueth thynge fully knewe open euydence hadde also specyall credence sent vnto hym fro penolopee mater hole declarynge secretee owne sone thelamonyus wexe herte wood furyous wolde make dylacyon haste besoughte alphenon myghty kynge hye bounte releue hym aduersyte wolde thorugh myghty honde gentyllesse conueye hym londe graunteth hym say nat one nay bothe two full great array toke see whan wynde gode well fortuned thynge withstode aryued hadde lettynge vlixes ye haue herde kynge secretely nyght conueyed haue lygaunce disobeyed mercyles myght awake theyr beddes haue take makynge prolongynge tyll morowe hast wyght durst borowe smette theyr hedes jugement fynall sette vpon castell wall eueryche endelonge rowe vpon toure whan kocke gan crowe thus nyght kept selfe close tyll phebus meryly arose oryent whan larke songe tho kyng meyne stronge fresshely besene entre cytee pwho tho glad penolopee made ioye goodly quene full desyrous hir owne lorde sene shulde ordre sette great myrthe made whan mette make rehersayle complayntes olde gan theyr hertes vnfolde eche lyste thynge concele gladnesse inly fele shulde put memorye reioysynge hertely glorye lyeges made comynge costes eke hadde metynge gyftes great presentes ryche worlde cowe none ylyche longe tariynge boke newe assuraunce toke lordes lyeges alle grace falle chere made eke alphenowne gentyllesse thorugh hye renowne doughter inly debonayre alphenon nausica fayre vlixes medyacyon yweddyd vnto thelamon borne discent may man say nay reioyse crowne day thus came purueaunce two reygnes myghty allyaunce brought knotte men wolde deme playnely sotte presume oppynyon delate descripcyon sythen guydo touchynge chefe mater style brefe shortly rehersynge kynge alphenon repeyred home regyon vlixes chefe cytee abode stylle penolopee hym leue ioye solace tyll antropos lyketh purchace fychche fynally date threde vntwyne lyues fate phow translatoure wryteth stocke pyrrus lyncall dyscent fader hyght pelleus graunmoder called thetydes capitulo xxxvij muste full besy whyle directe tracy style descryuynge shortly entent stocke py u lyneal discet myn auctour folowe compendyous pwhose olde fader hyght pelleus graunmoder called therydes whiche two came worthy achylles troye treason loste lyfe dardanyca called wyfe pyrrus moder doughter rede vnto kynge called lychomede hauynge fader acastus hyght whiche sothnesse euer myght bare heuy herte kynge pelleus achylles also pyrrus kyn playnely syde malyce rancoure pryde enuye hatefull rage pwhan pelleus salie age berafte hym bothe sceptre crowne see lowe lyght hym downe exyle auayle way stryfe made hym go thetydes wyfe hye disdeyne gayne may grace herte gan day nyght compace deth pyrrus kepe hym therupon malycyously began shape away awayte lyinge hym sle home comynge pbut pyrrus treynes free many daunger escaped see many wawe many tempest wode great losse bothe men gode malasus alder firste gan londe stronge cyte lytell fro stronde refresshed wonder wele knewe grounde euerydele firste thexyle lyke men hym tolde therydes pelleus olde atastus bare hym hatrede vnto deth wherof gan drede thought wolde right wyse engyne eschewe malyse therupon besy payne nowhadde atastus sone twayne menalyppus polystenes adoughter ycalled thetydes whyle wofull pelleus castell olde ruynous thetydes full sorowe care drede deth day nyght gan dare disespeyred vnweldy age recure fynde mortall rage except hadde hope yore pyrrus shulde helpe hym restore repeyre whan falle whose comynge often gan calle tyme curse longe abode whan pyrrus vnderstode malasus relacyowne full faste gan haste towne toke see faste gan hym hye towarde londe called thesalye ofentent make ordynaunce atastus vengaunce alderfirste pyrrus full prudent espyes twayne tofore hath sent thesalye forth togydre gone crylyppus called tone adastrus named fere expert nedeth nat lere whose expleyte auauntage pyrrus hath direct massage thesalye cyteseyne called assandrus maner chaumberleyne pelleus whylom full secree whyle flourynge felycytee whan pyrrus conclusyon knewe sothe relacyon see londe hym ne lyste tarye albe founde wynde contrarye pbut caped many dredefull stoundes thesalye aprocheth boundes eolus luste obeyed fortune erly con eyed dryuen grace aryue place pelleus dolefull caue drede deth lay hym selfe saue sool saue wyfe withouten ferys enclosyd husshes brerys pyrrus went vp firste sonde sool hym selfe walkynge stronde pensyfe tryste way toke pwhere pelleus caue quoke hauynge hym tho none guyde saue swerde hangynge syde vn warely dredefull herte pelleus caue sterte disamayde lyfe doute whan behelde knyght walke aboute astoned abode stode full stylle ymagynynge sawe achylle pby pyrrus stondynge place sygnes shewed face nature without varyaunce made lyke chere countenaunce forme shape lymmes euerychone difference effect none pelleus without longer space gan anone pyrrus enbrace abrayde deedly thought ioye sette sorowe nought gan hym declare bothe exyle euyll fare pyteous lyfe pouerte myschaunce fortune false varyaunce atastus feruent hoote enuye cruelte tyrannye ceryously tolde pyrrus alle full sobre stode stylle walle face pale herte wrothe specheles shyp agayne gothe enformed douteles menalyppus polystenes atastus togydre thre huge array great meyne day full surquedous pryde hunte forest lytell besyde whan pyrrus therof toke good hede without abode chaunge gan wede full porely rent disarayed lyke man thought dismayed gyrte swerde made delay forest toke ryght way sool hym selfe without companye secretely man myght espye drowghe many dyuerse boundes herde horne vncouplynge houndes lyke man lyst make mone fro syght folke drewe hym aye alone casuelly disseueryd fro prees firste mette polystenes menalyppus rydynge syde bothe two pyrrus gan abyde boystously hym enquere fro se came also febly cladde pore estate walkynge desolate lowly chere countenaunce styll humble dalyaunce answerde agayne sayde fordyuen myschefe see affermed pale thynge rede felowshyp drowned dede fyue hondred wawes rage olde yonge medell age escaped tempest ryfe tolde vnneth lyfe ouer tolde platly eke touchynge byrthe greke went destytur ioye late come fro sege troye besought towarde lyuynge helpe hym refresshynge hym hadde catell loste gode lyke sawe naked stode prayinge also hope shulde auayle hym releue clothynge vytayle refute somewhat prouyde hym shulde abyde wyll wyt playnely whyle besyde ran full great harte downe ryuer menalyppus prycked courser sempte hym dewe thorugh thynne thycke onely pursewe spareth nat alway rode brother pyrrus stylle abode polystenes toke hede haste alyght fro stede grene reste hym besyde wery ryde without meyne beynge hym selfe sool lys ynge pyrrus complaynte dool sodaynely myght aduerte cruell pyrrus ran hym herte lefte hym dede lyinge playne whan menalyppus repeyred agayne seynge brother baskyn blode pyrrus efte furyous wode face coloure pale wan menalyppus yre ran slewe hym eke toke hede thus lay grounde blede bretherne two pyrrus swerd yslawe anone asyde gan hym drawe metynge aknyght sorte caas sayth storye called cynara pyrrus gan haste enquere whose man dyd answerde made tariynge seruaunt myghty kynge called atastus lorde countre pyrrus tho dedely enmyte cruell swerde fresshe rede blode ran hym thorugh lyon wode forest forsoke haste right way toke shyppe agayne pale blacke hewe gan anone array hym newe purpyll whiche clerkes telles kynges wyght elles pyrrus fresshe well deseyne forest repeyred ageyne sodaynely hap walkynge shorte whyle mette kynge olde atastus asked pyrrus man art thou thy selfe thus walkyst thus day fro certes quod pyrrus full sorowe wo inly supprysed hertely complaynynge one sone pryamus kynge whylom nowe put memorye whan troye flouryd glorye refutles myschefe brought walke sool full care thought exyle troye towne cruell pyrrus lyue prysowne bounde vnto hym though full lothe honde assured many full great othe obeye luste captyuyte loo thus standeth atastus tho entencyon many questyon enqueryd hym dalyaunce knewe ought pyrrus gouernaunce coude ought vnderstonde hym kept sythe came londe ywysse quod ye lyste hym haue kepeth hym close yonder caue amonge bruskayle shrowded face makynge sygne place done ydell mase whyle kynge thyderwarde gan gase hasty pyrrus gan swerde drawe purpose fully atastus haue slawe wonderly storye lere quene thetydes dyde anone appere rayned teres hir face gan swerde pyrrus enbrace prayinge hym deedly honde restrayne hast yu nat slayne yonge brother twayne ala fader hore gray mercyles fro wylt take away put vp swerde blode ne shede haue pyte vpon thy kynrede aduerte clerely fyne thou arte come lyne hatefull loke ryght vnkynde blode euery mannes syght pyrrus tho tygre wrothe gan afferme many full great othe grutche agaynst playne shall hym sle hondes twayne hath nat false extorsyon put pelleus regyon whiche lorde ye trewe wyfe fynally shall lese lyfe anone myn handes deye matere seye pelleus darynge caue grace oonly lyste lyfe saue helpe platly nought pelleus anone forth brought croked olde vnweldy eke se tofore pyrrus fyll downe kn besechynge hym apyteous face requeste take hym grace wolde manly herte goodly consydre deedly wo smerte atastus mortall payne hadde sone twayne whiche lay deed tofore hym grene slayne swerde sharpe kene whiche ne may recure wyse sorowe whiche ought ynough suffyse though ye hym vengaunce peysyd iustly balaunce syth hoolly submyttyd myght take hym mercy anone ryght let swerde age nat consume request dare presume pyrrus shortly sayne wha put vp swerde agayue seynge mercy myght moost auayle without wordes rehersayle firste tofore euerychone kynges made accorde one wysdome concludynge vp dede eche shulde right possede thesalye partyd twayne neyther hadde mater complayne eueryche reygne dewe see whyle togydre thre presence man atastus firste thus tale began syres quod nat vnknowe thorugh age brought lowe thorugh nature kyndely mocyon wexed feble wyt reson beynge vnweldy lymmes alle many yeres vpon falle vnneth thynge discerne feble sothe kyngdome gouerne lyfe deth takynge hede syth sone slayne dede sool lefte without heyre worldly luste fully dispeyre tyme passyd felycyte fortune tourne mutabylyte hath taught playnly dare wel expresse worldly ioye sykernesse truste whyle abyde wyll selfe prouyde haste prudent purueaunce discharge gouernaunce agayne sort lyste nat malygne sceptre crowne frely resygne thesalye lorshyp eke londe fre wyll hole thy honde shall man reclayme say nay interupte make delay touchynge thynge collusyon put possessyon hereupon euer sayde makynge full fayth honde layde quene thetydes syttynge present pelleus entent vnto pyrrus purpartye resygned eke right thesalye fully affermynge yore ago full desyre ioye also euer one neuewe succede rightfull heyre kyngdome possede vtterly without repentaunce longeth vnto lygeaunce sceptre swerde crowne dyademe kynge lyfe deth deme thy hande without longer date houre hooly translate whan knot conuencyon fully brought conclusyon perfourmed vp hole vnyte euermore atwene kynges thre atastus knyghtes disseueryd enuyrowne forest descendyd downe byddynge platly theyr lorde echone sworne accorde attones lusty companye thesalye faste gan hye pyrrus folke lyinge see sayled forthe streyght cytee atastus doth sette parlement openly gaue comaundement lyeges hye lowe estate without stryfe debate specyally gentyll blode yborne daye pyrrus sworne lyke theyr degree royall halle perseuere trewe lyeges alle durynge theyr lyfe ernest game pelleus comaundeth hath partye without fraude thus ioye solempne laude pyrrus euery maner age gladly accepted herytage day fortunat gode glad aspectis whan heuen stode well accordynge suche maner thynge worthy pyrrus ycrowned kynge thesalye ryche regyon vayne make mencyon theyr reuell theyr great array feste made day eke storye fynde nat sothe wyll passe ouer myn auctour dothe saue boke specefyed kyngdome fer magnefyed thesalye great myght pyrrus whylom gode knght se hym royall see tournynge agayne kynge ydumee whiche whyle graue vnder stone hym sone meryone storye sayth crowned kynge crete whyle reygnynge equyte deyed also wolde none haste leorica brother rightfull heyre successyon crowned kynge regyon whiche tyme atastus drede assent pyrrus rede full besy make specyall ryche toumbe passyngly royall buryed full huge prees menalyppus polystenes bothe two forest slawe thorugh pyrrus swerde full cruell lawe none processe make euen fully tale take bothe also eke yfere atastus theyr owne fader dere sothly locke hore troye boke rede pbut must agayne pyrrus wende wryte hym sory wofull ende whiche whan sat hyest see made full blynde vayne prosperyte gouernynge londe thesalye falsly fyll fantasye sette loue hermyon quene horestes wyfe reygnynge methene brent hote fyre fulfyllynge foule desyre purpose hole thus brought aboute hir rauysshynge whyle hir lorde oute ladde hir home helde hir wyfe semynge hym blysfull lyfe full relese paynes smerte whiche horestes bare full heuy herte caste hym playnely auengyd whan may haue opportunyte tyme though hadde wronge feble pyrrus stronge pwhiche helde also storye tolde andronomecha hym housholde ectors wyfe whylom hadde alytell childe whiche hir ladde sege complete destruccyowne whan brought troye towne lamedouta fynde name encreasynge full worthy fame pyrrus hadde sone also called achylleydos wryt guydo woman theyr great estate atwene selfe amonge debate hermyone hir yre hote complaynynge hir fader wrote hir fere hir hye degree andronomecha cherisshed better tha kynge pyrrus besechynge menelay enhaste hym euer may come hym selfe anone sle woman hir childe also abode nat faste gan hym hye hete towarde thesalye venged swerde stele vpon hir trespasseth neuer adele maugre hym cruelte reskewed amyd cyte thynge whiche hath nat herde woman kynge drawe swerde wyll mater dwelle maner shamed wryte telle done whyle pyrrus courage delos gone pylgrymage hauynge hym lytell route appollo knele loute soule praye achylle vowes also fulfylle thanke hym humble affeccyon god exployte hadde troye towne wreche also take cyte faders sake pbut thynge yspecefyed kynge horestes warely hath espyed delos gan haste hym full ryght ledynge hym many lusty knyght vnwarely pyrrus mette vengeably vpon hym sette fynally straunge londe horestes slewe hym owne honde fynde sothe made defence sodayne mortall vyolence enmye coude nat asterte myght swerde aduerte hym enuyron deset thylke tyme myght bet nouther socoure declyne thus pyrrus brought vnto fyne late crowned kynge thesalye loo guerdon anoutrye lo mede rewarde full ryfe mysse vse another mannes wyfe drede folowe shall vengaunce sodayne deth vnware myschaunce whiche euery man greatly ought charge delos temple large kynge pyrrus locked vnder stone horestes forth way gone force gat wyfe agayne wyght durst hym tho wtsayne methene proudely repeyred thesalye pyteously dispeyred destytute rede whan wyste worthy kyng dede heyre none successyon gouerne noble regyon saue achylleydos iytell aforne pyrrus absence grece borne fully age nat quarter clene youthe sothly grene lyste consydre rendre myght full many day reioyse ryght gouerne sceptre honde large boundes great londe yet childe lykely right feyre soth borne heyre pyrrus trouthe playne man lyste withsayne pbut fynde whan came age resygned hole herytage brother frely ryght lamedoute wonder manly knyght descended troy anysshe blode downe fro stocke hym gode floure knyghthode diffence frigya hym begat andromecha ordeyned nowe gru che frowne thesalye bere crowne whan made lorde londe frely resygned honde hath comaunded man dare replye thorugh kyngome thesalye captyuyte prysoners troye cyte loue hate excepcyon none shulde theyr large gone pby full assent achylleydos suche eke pryson cloos without raunson shall belyuered reioyse full lyberte custome vsed bothe borugh towne lyeges great regyon thus folke came thralle fro troye restored sodaynely ioye pby lamedoute ymade free eke reygneth royall see full myghtely haue made mynde troye boke hym fynde pyrrus kynrede fro hensforth processe rede pbut incydentes bere substaunce whiche vayne put remebrauce except myn auctor note entent impeth lytell incydent ywrought done full yore agon touchynge deth kynge menon whiche enuye cruell achylles slayne sothe amonge myrundones proudely gan pursewe vpon achylles troylus reskewe pwhom kynge pryam made buryed besyde troylus troye cyte temple ybylte marbyll olde fyne tale tolde chapitle shall reherse anon noble quene kynge menon tyme longe many day dede grauen vnder clay toumbe heuenly gan appere beset bryght sterres clere whose symylytude reken lyke thynge immortall man myght vtterly sustene beholde loke shene downe descendynge fro fyrmament full many man beynge present clade mantell full celestyall hir porte passyngly royall swetnesse fresshe rose made haste toumbe vnclose hir lorde taketh bone cheste made golde stone couched faste euer may disapered went anone hir way tofore certayne place neuer sayne affermynge lyklynesse outher aungell goodesse soule fate kynge nat deme suche heuenly thynge therm holde none oppynyon transcendeth shortly reson lyste nat suche mater diffyne resorte right lyne vlixes whyle dwelle ende surplus telle myght nat escape parodye hym shape parchas haue laste terme sette antropose mesured mette lyues threde rocke sponne diffende thy selfe vlixes thou konne shewe thy manhode nat aferde welfare thy sone swerde shall lyke wonte sha pe penne bothe rude blonte descryue fyne thy soioure vpon boundes set laboure almost wery feynt weyke ynough vestes ox plough longe day agayne hylle wende almost londes ende troye boke fychche wyll stake saue must spende fewe lynes blake laste chapitre shortly translate werke ympen date day deth sette hym arest full execute hym loued best lowe knee must loute god maketh men route causeth folke haue glad sweuenes bothe morowe lusty euenes whan mortheus slepy wonde whiche holdeth alway honde hath marked agayne derke nyght make men bothe mery lyght whyle haue gladnesse sodaynely falle heuynesse lyke gyueth euydence sondry sygnes apparence vnto lorde must mekely preye tyme style conueye vlixes dreme descryue laste hadde lyue declarynge hym token full notable sygnes demonstrable slepte agayne pale moone fatall day shulde folowe soone fy l thus bedde lay onyght tofore morowe gray hym thought sawe appere creature syght celestyall fygure none erthly thynge veryly dyuyne porte chere wonder femynyne hym sempte fantasye lyke thynge sent fayrye beaute hir goodly face recomforted playnely place surmountynge moste souerayne clerenesse hir eyen twayne sodaynely men myght aduerte perce wolde euen herte diffence none myght deuysed vlixes hir loke supprysed gan hir beholde alway slepe syghe sore persynge aye full besy payne hir enbrace armes twayne aye gan pursewe agaynewarde gan hym eschewe aye presed hir se aye hym gan flee contrayre hym fortune whan sawe importune axed hym shortly wolde hir platte trouthe tolde certys quod lyues emperesse ye woman goddesse nat deme iuge halfe ryght derked blynded syght dare well afferme place lyfe deth stande hoolly grace mercy requerynge ryght rewe whiche owne knyght pyte compassyon goodly se sauacyon desyre may fulfylle nyght haue wylle recure remedye lacke rouche must dye nowe haue atwyxe hope drede selfe declaryd womanhede kepte hir close whyle full sadly gan hym smyle put remembraunce sayde vnto hym sobre countenaunce sothly quod thyne affeccyon wolde fully tourne confusyon v bothe peryllous inly mortall contagyous vtterly gayne may rede one v must one dede fyne hatefull chaunce shulde folowe plesaunce vlixes gan nyghe nere beholdynge aye hir heuenly chere stode vpryght grounde sawe hir holde spere longe rounde hede therof borned stele forged newe grounde wonder wele therupon vysyowne sawe baner blasynge vp downe felde therof coloure ynde full fysshes beten fynde bokes lyke tolde myddes large crowne golde tourne gan hir face lykely anone parte place spake hym sayde wordes playne full token partynge v twayne euermore nouther soure swete daye neuer agayne mete disaperynge anone hir leue toke sodaynely woke gan muse fantalye thynge dreme myght sygnefye mente outher euell gode secretnesse nat vnderstode surmounted sothly reason therfore sente thorugh regyon suche sotell exposytours fate sorte crafty dyuynours clerkes soget crowne assemble one sweuen expowne whan knewe informacyon maner hole vysyon concluded accordynge one tyme approcheth shall come anone one next kynrede spere shulde make hym blede let se fate remewe syth harde destynero eschewe say tho folke theyr oppynyon werke truste constellacyon vlixes musynge tale chaungeth coloure gan wexe pale wonder dredefull full fantasyes gan hym selfe seke remedyes voyde away thynge wyll nat stareth brode may nat se warde loke cloude shent wenynge prudent made calle sone thelamon take shet vp pryson supposynge fully wytte myschefe therby go quyte nat aduerteth ne toke none hede sharpnesse speres hede fysshes baner beete see swymme flete quene called circe sygnes brought werre nat pee crowne token dignytee one shall holde royall see myd wawes bothe felle wode amonge fysshes large flode shall make dyuysyon tofore remembred auysyon agayne wyll ignoraunce execute fatall puruyaunce vp dreme spere stele whiche vlixes consydreth neuer adele wyght hath suspecyon sone called thelamon closed shet vp toure vlixes coste great laboure fro day day doth besynesse hym selfe make forteresse bylte rocke lyme square stone depe dyched aboute none man may entre syde casteth lyfe abyde certayne men chosen specyall nyght day watche vpon wall wyght shulde haue none entree falle secree knowen olde counsayle sworne storye rehersed hath forne olde fole dotarde vlixes sone hadde begoten cyrces fresshe lusty yonge coragyous called thelagonyus borne see amonge floddes rage also reken age fyue twenty yere aboute fader aye doute man myght beynge therof seurte tyll day desyrous knowe moder fyll knee lowe besechynge hir goodly nat spare fader trouthe declare shulde dwelle besought wolde telle sothly longe many dayes prudence put hym delayes tyll sawe myght haue reste importune requeste wha knewe none bote fro poynt poynt tolde crop rote vlixes kynge anone made lettynge toke leue may none sayde playnely wolde fader se pwherof quene gan herte colde whan saide myght hy nat wtholde hym besought chere debonayre wolde soone agayne repayre forthe sayleth onwarde way without abode selfe day many porte many fer countre tyll brought wolde achaya londe great renowne gan serche thorugh regyon place paleys pryncypall kynge helde see royall longe countre rode tyll taught kynge abode vlixes shytte vp mewe whiche place haste gan pursewe great party releuyd sorowe monday erely morowe vnto brydge ryght way toke founde porter deynous loke lowely firste gan hym praye wolde goodly hym conueye courte make tariynge message hadde kynge proudely denyed hym gate shortly sayde came late entre maner wyse vngoodly gan hym despyse frowarde speche malycyous haste thelagonyus herte nat aferde proude porter hente berde fyste rofe chawe bone fyll deed muet stone eke hym tho withstode made proudely lepe ye flode whan mo came make resystence hente swerde manly vyolence furyously irous tene storye sayth slewe fyftene hym selfe almoste wounded deth gan wery sothly fayle breth vlixes noyse sowne brydge descendyd downe fyndynge men entre gate deed slayne full mortall hate full irous hente anone darte auenture stondynge tho parte cruelly caste thelagon stroke conclucyon damageth nat glode asyde haste lenger wolde abyde hent vp darte without rest smote kynge lowe vnder brest thorugh rybbes shortly seye wounde must deye hauynge tho none oppynyon kynge suspecyon hadde owne fader slawe whiche faste gan ende drawe wounde deedly kene myght hym selfe nat sustene pale wan grounde gan glyde men aboute vpon euery syde besy helpe hym releue sore gan ake greue well felte must dede abraydynge lyfte vp hede hauynge yet mynde good reason remembre gan auysyon tolde hym drede one next kynrede descendyd downe owne lyne sweuene shall parfourme fyne accomplysshe darte stele coude nat conceyue wele shulde badde anone vnto meyne without harme vyolence fette anone vnto presence yonge man whiche gate stode hath day shad moche blode whan afore vlixes brought hym hath enqueryd sought firste kyn nexte countree certes quod borne see amonge fysshes myd wawes grene sayde also moder quene called circe name kouthe bothe est west right fer southe tolde also fader kynge hym begat home comynge fro troye towne towarde countre moder cyrces tolde secretely vlixes hyghte desyrous haue syghte entred myghty regyon haue pursewed vnto dongeon oonly hope fader haue seyne se well labour veyne sythe sothe lost trauayle may syde auayle foly lenger dwelle lo telle kynred axe pwith vlixes gan syghe sore lacke blode full pale sayde anone whan herde tale wot well wofull destyne fulfylled may none wot well late grutche stryue agayne pyteous fate sone clerkes whylom tolde hath made ende dayes olde theron expectant paynes full greuous worde thelagonyus whan wyste agayne nature lawe ala fader slawe whiche londe longe bare crowne without abode fylle anone swowne clothes rent yelowe heer torne ala quod euer borne cursed wofull destyne fortune whiche may nat fle cursed sort cursed myn auenture refuse euery creature forwaryed eke disposycyon cursed constellacyon cursed also infortunat houre whiche fader begat wolde god without lenger rede aquyte hym anone dede lay lyfe deth borowe whan kynge sawe great sorowe wyste sone cyrces borne many sygnes rehersed toforne vnto hym anone forgaue deth myght lacke want breth importable passyon sone called thelagon whiche hath pryson many daye shet presence haste fet whiche whan sawe fader suche poynt vpon deth stondynge disioynt knewe also trouth hath founde hadde laste deedly wounde swerde hente mortally irous wolde haue ronne thelagonyus hye despyte auenged vlixes faderly pyte made men holde hym restrayne amyd greuous payne prudence done anone made sone one gaue charge vnto thelamon enteernesse affeccyon hole herte fayned neuer adele lyfe loue brother wele parte hym treasour golde gode nexte borne blode tho sothe lenger taryed vlixes royally caryed achaya chefe cyte lyued dayes thre without tho gaue vp gost nat say playnely cost lyfe soule gone atoumbe metall stone body closed yshet made let thelamon great solempnytee ycrowned fadres see swerde sceptre delyueryd honde achaya full worthy londe ryght habundaunt treasour gode thelagon hym abode yere complet well cherysshed syght brother toke ordre knyght hym lyste lenger abyde kynge hym wysely gan prouyde golde great treasour plente repeyred home countre moder age wexe sad repeyre passyngly glad sawe hir sorcerye scapyd many iupardye many pereyll many great distress fylle sykenesse hir dette yelde vnto nature whiche escape may creature wolde lyuynge whose deth hir sone made kynge anlydos meruayllous countre haue tolde enclosed see amonge rockes many shyppes drowne syxty yere bare crowne manly man thelagonyus brother thelamonyus reygned also regyon seuenty wynter made mencyon made royall ende bothe two iubyter wende reygne amonge sterres bryght bvt lanterne clere lyght wasted frygyus darete whylom troye wryter poyete guyde haue none ferther passe euen selfe place fychched hath boundes style sege present whyle aye one dyde abyde dytes greke tother syde bothe two theyr wrytynge ne vary nat lytell thynge touchynge matere specyall notable hystoryall force incydentis smale whiche sothe lytell tale saue dytes maketh mencyowne nombre slayne towne lastynge sege affermynge drede eyght hondred thousade syx dede grekes syde vp right felde dare also behelde troye partye werre kene syxe hondred thousande seuenty syxtene slayne guydo ye may se came helpe cyte fro many coste many regyowne diffence reskus towne full ten yere caste syxe monthes myghty sege laste gette dare wryte hym selfe ouer complet dayes twelue grekes hadde full possessyon false engyne greke synon lyke tofore rehersyd late haue latyn translate dytes dare guydo adde therto myn auctours specefye seyn occupacyon sothly veyne lyke maner presumpcyon tyme complet translacyon iuste rekenynge countis clere thousande foure hondred yere twenty nere knowe drede criste receyued manhede hir emperesse quene heuen helle mayde clene eyghte yere computacyon suynge coronacyon hym gracyous werkynge herry fyfthe noble worthy kynge protectoure brutys albyowne called thorugh hyerenowne thorugh prowesse chyualrye also fer passeth cloude skye normadye myghty conquerour thorugh knyghthod dilygent labour maugre tho lyste hym withseyne hath conqueryd herytage ageyne myghty prudent gouernaunce recuryd eke trewe tytle fraunce lyste loke vnfolde pee de grewe cronycles olde sercheth bokes ywryt longe aforne shall fynde iustly borne reygne fraunce lyneall discent onwarde made regent thylke londe durynge faders lyfe goodnesse voyde werre stryfe reioyse without delay sceptre crowne kynges day clerely conclusyon enrolled vp conuencyon hope tyme fortunat olde
