worlde called aureat resorte shall influence grace cruell mar shall manace lookes furyous wode false aspectes shede blode atwene folkes thyse realmes twayne whiche euery wyght ought complayne truste myn oppynyon worthy kynge wysedome reson knyghthode shall payne make one longe hath twayne mene thus englonde fraunce may one without varyaunce hertes olde rancour enchace influence myghty grace called clerkes douteles soueraygne lorde prynce pee hope grace shall reygne set reste atwene thyse realmes twayne power sothly stondeth allyaunce blode royall knet vp bonde maryage werre shall voyde away rage make pea bryght bemes shyne one called katheryne named right good fayre also shalbe mene atwyxe bothe two grace emprynted hir womanhede complayne shall haue nede hope hir gracyous aryuaylle londe shall moche auaylle ioye honour prosperyte without trouble aduersyte repeyre shall hertely plesaunce plente welfare fulsome habundaunce pea quyete bothe nyghe ferre without stryfe debate werre myschefe pouert nede indigence full cessynge deth pestylence sothly hope ye shall sene come londe noble quene shall say herte feyne nought blessyd hath v brought hath thorugh myght werkyg knyghthode concludyd thyng suche meruayles armes done wrought purpose fully aboute brought hye wysedome set inwarde syght reioysynge longeth ryght hyest syt worthynesse glorye sceptre conquest victorye praye god oonly beste pwhan hath set pea reste full put clere possessyon longeth subieccyon sende hym home great honour euer yet hadde conquerour longe ioye quyete reygne royall sete thus shall aye saye daye nyght expleyt praye faythfull herte hole entent whylom gaue comaundement nat yore ago faders tyme sege troye maner ryme sake speke specyall though boystous rurall gaue charge storye translate rude connynge called iohn lydgate onke burye professyon vsynge habyte perfeccyon albe lyfe accorde nat therto feyne nat wot well nedeth nat wytnesse calle recorde take brother alle wyll nat fayle great nede shall noble storye rede beseche supporte grace offende maner place euer fynde errour gentyllesse shewe fauour benyngnely theyr payne correcte rather disdayne well wot moche thynge wronge falsely metryd bothe short longe shulde haue disdayne drede labour vayne let ignoraunce rudenesse excuse ye platly refuse certayne fautes whiche ye shall fynde doute nat thanke set behynde metrynge though ignoraunce yet storye ye fynde may plesaunce touchynge substauce myn auctour wryt though worde mysse syt amende chere debonayre errour hyndre appayre nat sayde purpose malyce worshyp hym wyse wyght gladly soon demeth lacke specyally behynde backe soth skylle gothe full hole neuer hadde fall nat fynde newe olde deme none bolde yblent vnconnynge blynde bayarde caste pereyll thynge tyll stumble myddes lake none redy vndertake sothe bolder say werse skylle prose verse suche nat stylle lytell forse say good ylle vnto boke nat dyrect suche haue effect symple folke full compassyon goodly correccyon amende thynge hyndre neuer adele custome aye redy say wele groude well sayinge lyfe hyndred makynge mayster chaucer founde full many spot hym lyst nat pynche grutche euery blot meue hym selfe parturbe reste haue herde tolde sayde alway beste suffrynge goodly gentyllesse full many thynge embraced rudenesse shall shortly hym descryue neuer none daye alyue reken bothe yonge olde worthy ynkehorne holde londe borugh towne vyllage cyte connynge hath tracy sewe go brode shet mewe hym make dyreccyon boke haue inspeccyon besechynge theyr prudent loke race scrape thorugh bok voyde adde semeth nede though nat ne rede boke rethorykes newe pyet hope shall fynde trewe storye playne clefly substaunce lyste se varyaunce worldly thynge wrought dayes olde boke may full well beholde chaunge fortune hir course mutable selde nat faythfull outher stable lordes prynces sfrom hir royalte sodaynely brought aduersyte kynges eke plounged pouerte drede darynge deserte vnware slaunghtre compassed enuy murdre execute conspyracye awayt leyinge falshede treason kyngdome sodayne euersyon bauysshynge woman delyte rote werre mortall despyte false mayntenaunce auoutrye many worthy causynge dye synne aye concludynge taketh hede vengaunce vnware fynall mede vo declare worldly luste loke right lytell truste boke exaumple ye shall fynde ye lyste enprente mynde passeth halt soiour wastynge away doth somer floure ryche pore euery maner age lyfe pylgrymage meynt labour moche woo men wolde take hede therto tofore prudently aduerte lytell ioye shulde haue theyr herte set theyr truste worldly thynge nouther prynce lorde kynge example troye lyke ye may se lyfe may haue full seurte therfore hym starfe vpon rode suffrynge deth aller gode lyfte vp hert thynke hym amonge ye neuer myghty stronge without hym may nat auayle gyue victorye batayle holde felde shortly conclude fewe agayne great multytude grace maketh prynces stronge worthy kynges reygne longe tyrantes sodaynely oppresse thorwe downe theyr great rychesse honde power reserueth eche aquyte lyke disserueth praye deuocyon myn herte hole affeccyon lyste graunte longe contynaunce prosperyte good perseueraunce helthe welfare victorye honoure vnto noble myghty conqueroure herry fyfther tofore yspecefyed name may magnefyed herein lyfe vp sterrys clere afterwarde aboue nynthe spere whan deed haue place praye god sende hym grace whose byddynge tolde late firste began sege translate haue hoolly honoure executed fyne laboure vnto shall storye se humble herte humylyte lytell booke lowely betake supporte thus ende make plaus deo pof moost noble excellent prynce kynge henry fyfthe moost worthy prynce knyghthode soures welle whose hye renowne thorugh worlde dothe shyne manhode doest excelle egall meryt worthy nyne borne also discent lyne rightfull heyre tytle attayne bere crowne worthy realme twayne also fer phebus spere eest west shedyth bemys bryght lucyna ashrouded chere gothe compasse rounde hir pale lyght thou art yrekened best knyght registred worthy name hyest place house fame holde palme knyghthod thy honde worthynesse hye victorye thou art drade see londe euermore laude honoure glorye iuste conquest put memorye crowne made laurer grene vpon thy heed tofore famous quene whylom ordeyned oonly conquerours stable herte longe perseueraunce gaue nat vp tyll victours empryses take sodayne chaunce whose name ay floureth wt newe remebrauce fadeth nat yeres yore agone amonges whiche thou mayste set one thorugh worlde many regyon reported fame flyeth wyde naturelly thy condycyon thynge begonne knyghtly abyde tyme manly set asyde rest ease cost theron spente tyll thou haue cheued fyne thyn entente moste circumspect passynge auysee thy werkes conueyed prudence sad demure lyke iosuee agayne whose swerde resystence hast also heuenly influence salamon wysely discerne oonly grace thy people gouerne mercy eke meynt thy magnyfycence oppressed haue pyte rebelles manly vyolence abate canste great cruelte dauyd thou haste kyngly pyt hye prowesse sesar iulyus tyme moost victoryous manly holdest thy hondes two beholde clere inspeccyon swerde knyghthode thy scepture also tone brynge subieccyon hertes made proude false rebellyon sceptre rewle best thy trewe people lyue rest thou haste manhode vertue grace attemperaunce fredome bounte lowly praye dredefull face disdayne nat benyngely se vpon boke rudely made fyne oonly agrene thyne hyghnesse rewe mercy vpon symplesse thy noble kyngly aduertence consydre se soueraygne lorde dere thyne inuat famous sapyence criste ihesu receyued good chere twey munytys herte entere wydowe whiche wyl thought gaue hir good kept hir selfe right nought whiche ensaumple nat offende thorugh myn vnconnyng thy hye noblesse let good wyll lytell gyfte amende thy mercy renowmed goodnesse haue disdayne bareyne rudenesse makynge though haue muse let trewe menynge surplus excuse good herte hath maner wyght present nouther god man parte ryght gyue hole ferforth aye perseuere fro tyme gan wyll thought thyne estate praye whiche conserue thus fynally saye firste almyghty god queme may plesaunce thy crowne thy dyademe grace good eure wt longe contynuaunce thy lyeges faythfull obeyssaunce eche vertue man may specefye praye god graunte vnto thy regalye pexplicit liber quintus vltimus plenuoye oo lytell boke put grace hym moste excellence nat hardy appere place without supporte magnyfycence euer fynde offence nat bolde presumpcyon thy selfe enarme aye pacyence submytte theyr correccyon pverba translatoris ad librum suum thou art enlymned flowres retoryke whyte blacke therfore thou muste abyde showres lyste set alacke whan thou art lykely go wracke agaynst thyne errour nat diffende humbly drawe go backe requerynge amysse amende endeth troye booke otherwyse called sege troye translated iohn lydgate monke monastery bery emprynted yere oure lorde mccccc xiij richard pynson prynter vnto kyng noble grace
